// 深淺調整：將 hex 顏色調亮（shade > 0）或調暗（shade < 0）
function adjustShade(hex, shade) {
  if (!hex || shade === 0) return hex;
  const h = hex.replace('#', '');
  const r = parseInt(h.slice(0, 2), 16);
  const g = parseInt(h.slice(2, 4), 16);
  const b = parseInt(h.slice(4, 6), 16);
  const adj = (v) => {
    if (shade > 0) return Math.round(v + (255 - v) * (shade / 100));
    return Math.round(v * (1 + shade / 100));
  };
  const toHex = (v) => Math.max(0, Math.min(255, v)).toString(16).padStart(2, '0');
  return '#' + toHex(adj(r)) + toHex(adj(g)) + toHex(adj(b));
}

// ============ 工具 ============

// 列表排序模式(明細/統計頁/單日詳細頁共用)
const LIST_SORT_KEY = 'ledger_list_sort_v1';
const DEFAULT_BUY_ACCOUNT_KEY = 'ledger_default_buy_account_v1';
const DEFAULT_SELL_ACCOUNT_KEY = 'ledger_default_sell_account_v1';
const LIST_SORT_OPTIONS = [
  { value: 'date_desc', label: '以日期排序(從近到遠)' },
  { value: 'date_asc',  label: '以日期排序(從遠到近)' },
  { value: 'amount_desc', label: '以金額排序(從大到小)' },
  { value: 'amount_asc',  label: '以金額排序(從小到大)' },
];
const DEFAULT_LIST_SORT = 'date_desc';
function loadListSort() {
  try {
    const v = localStorage.getItem(LIST_SORT_KEY);
    return LIST_SORT_OPTIONS.find((o) => o.value === v) ? v : DEFAULT_LIST_SORT;
  } catch { return DEFAULT_LIST_SORT; }
}
function sortTxnList(txns, mode) {
  const arr = [...txns];
  switch (mode) {
    case 'date_asc':
      arr.sort((a, b) => a.date.localeCompare(b.date) || (a.createdAt || 0) - (b.createdAt || 0));
      break;
    case 'amount_desc':
      // 金額為主、日期為輔(較近的優先)
      arr.sort((a, b) => b.amount - a.amount || b.date.localeCompare(a.date) || (b.createdAt || 0) - (a.createdAt || 0));
      break;
    case 'amount_asc':
      arr.sort((a, b) => a.amount - b.amount || b.date.localeCompare(a.date) || (b.createdAt || 0) - (a.createdAt || 0));
      break;
    case 'date_desc':
    default:
      arr.sort((a, b) => b.date.localeCompare(a.date) || (b.createdAt || 0) - (a.createdAt || 0));
      break;
  }
  return arr;
}
// 是否依日期分組(金額排序時不分組,只顯示扁平列表)
const isAmountSort = (mode) => mode === 'amount_desc' || mode === 'amount_asc';

// 全局列表排序模式監聽(明細頁/首頁共用 sortMode)
const listSortListeners = new Set();
const listSortBroadcast = (mode) => {
  listSortListeners.forEach((cb) => cb(mode));
};
function useListSort() {
  const [sortMode, setSortMode] = React.useState(loadListSort);
  React.useEffect(() => {
    listSortListeners.add(setSortMode);
    return () => { listSortListeners.delete(setSortMode); };
  }, []);
  // 包裝一層:set 的時候也廣播給其他 useListSort 訂閱者,並寫入 localStorage
  const setAndBroadcast = (mode) => {
    setSortMode(mode);
    try { localStorage.setItem(LIST_SORT_KEY, mode); } catch {}
    listSortBroadcast(mode);
  };
  return [sortMode, setAndBroadcast];
}

const fmt = (n) => {
  const num = Math.round(n);
  return Math.abs(num).toLocaleString('en-US');
};
// 帶正負號的格式化（用於結餘：可正可負）
const fmtSigned = (n) => {
  const num = Math.round(n);
  if (num < 0) return '-' + Math.abs(num).toLocaleString('en-US');
  return num.toLocaleString('en-US');
};
const todayStr = () => {
  const d = new Date();
  return `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}`;
};
// 格式化帳戶建立時間戳給 ⓘ toast 用 → 「2026/04/05 13:30 建立」
const formatCreatedAt = (ts) => {
  if (!ts) return '建立時間未知';
  const d = new Date(ts);
  const Y = d.getFullYear();
  const M = String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
  const D = String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
  const h = String(d.getHours()).padStart(2, '0');
  const m = String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0');
  return `${Y}/${M}/${D} ${h}:${m} 建立`;
};

// Module-scope 全域 toast(當 React 元件深層巢狀、不想傳 prop 時用)
// App mount 時會把實際 toast fn 注入這裡
let __globalToast = null;
let __globalToastRich = null;
const setGlobalToast = (fn) => { __globalToast = fn; };
const setGlobalToastRich = (fn) => { __globalToastRich = fn; };
const callGlobalToast = (msg) => { if (__globalToast) __globalToast(msg); };
const callGlobalToastRich = (data, ms) => { if (__globalToastRich) __globalToastRich(data, ms); };
const uid = () => 't_' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10) + Date.now().toString(36).slice(-4);

// 計算某帳戶的當前餘額 = 初始金額 + 所有收入 - 所有支出
const calcBalance = (account, transactions) => {
  const init = account.initAmount || 0;
  const delta = transactions.reduce((sum, t) => {
    if (t.accountId !== account.id) return sum;
    return sum + (t.type === 'income' ? t.amount : -t.amount);
  }, 0);
  return init + delta;
};

// ============ 持股相關計算(平均成本制) ============
// 算某 holding 目前持有股數(累計買進 - 累計賣出)
const holdingShares = (holding, trades) => {
  const buys = trades.filter((t) => t.holdingId === holding.id && t.type === 'buy');
  const sells = trades.filter((t) => t.holdingId === holding.id && t.type === 'sell');
  const bought = buys.reduce((s, t) => s + (t.shares || 0), 0);
  const sold = sells.reduce((s, t) => s + (t.shares || 0), 0);
  return bought - sold;
};

// 算某 holding 累計總投入成本(所有買進加總,不扣賣出)
const holdingTotalBought = (holding, trades) => {
  return trades
    .filter((t) => t.holdingId === holding.id && t.type === 'buy')
    .reduce((sum, t) => sum + (t.totalCost || 0), 0);
};

// 算累計買進股數
const holdingTotalBoughtShares = (holding, trades) => {
  return trades
    .filter((t) => t.holdingId === holding.id && t.type === 'buy')
    .reduce((sum, t) => sum + (t.shares || 0), 0);
};

// 平均成本(每股):累計買進總成本 / 累計買進股數(賣出不影響均價)
const holdingAvgCost = (holding, trades) => {
  const totalShares = holdingTotalBoughtShares(holding, trades);
  if (totalShares === 0) return 0;
  return holdingTotalBought(holding, trades) / totalShares;
};

// 算某 holding 目前持有的成本(剩餘股數 × 平均成本)
const holdingCost = (holding, trades) => {
  const shares = holdingShares(holding, trades);
  return shares * holdingAvgCost(holding, trades);
};

// 平均成本制下:賣 N 股對應成本 = N × 均價
const avgCostMatch = (holdingId, sellShares, trades, holdings) => {
  const holding = holdings.find((h) => h.id === holdingId);
  if (!holding) return { matchedCost: 0 };
  const avg = holdingAvgCost(holding, trades);
  return { matchedCost: sellShares * avg };
};

// 算某 holding 的浮動損益(市值 - 成本)
const holdingPnl = (holding, trades) => {
  const cost = holdingCost(holding, trades);
  const market = holding.marketValue || 0;
  return market - cost;
};

// 算投資帳戶總計:該帳戶下所有 holding 的市值/成本/浮動
// 沒有 holding 的舊投資帳戶,回傳 null(由呼叫方 fallback 回 calcBalance)
const investAccountSummary = (account, holdings, trades) => {
  const accountHoldings = holdings.filter((h) => h.accountId === account.id);
  if (accountHoldings.length === 0) return null;
  let totalMarket = 0, totalCost = 0;
  for (const h of accountHoldings) {
    const shares = holdingShares(h, trades);
    if (shares === 0) continue; // 已清倉的不計
    totalMarket += h.marketValue || 0;
    totalCost += holdingCost(h, trades);
  }
  return { totalMarket, totalCost, totalPnl: totalMarket - totalCost };
};

// 帳戶顯示名稱:純名稱(不加標示)。需要視覺標記時,由 JSX 旁邊加 <VirtualTag>。
// 純字串情境(如轉帳對方端、toast、dialog 訊息)需要顯示時,用 acctDisplayNameStr。
const acctDisplayName = (account) => {
  if (!account) return '';
  return account.name;
};

// 純字串顯示(無法塞 JSX 的場景):虛擬帳戶後接(虛)
const acctDisplayNameStr = (account) => {
  if (!account) return '';
  return account.virtual ? `${account.name}(虛)` : account.name;
};

// 用於統計時判斷:轉帳的 out/in 紀錄不算真實收支(錢只是搬位置),
// 但手續費 (transferRole === 'fee') 要算真實支出
// 代墊的 lend_out/lend_in/lend_collect_out/lend_collect_in 也都不算真實收支
// 股票結算:settle_out/settle_in 是本金歸還(不算),settle_pnl_in/settle_pnl_out 是真實損益(要算)
const isRealFlow = (t) => {
  const r = t.transferRole;
  if (r === 'out' || r === 'in') return false;
  if (r === 'lend_out' || r === 'lend_in') return false;
  if (r === 'lend_collect_out' || r === 'lend_collect_in') return false;
  if (r === 'settle_out' || r === 'settle_in') return false;
  // settle_pnl_in / settle_pnl_out / fee 都返回 true(算統計)
  return true;
};

// 偵測「將被刪除的紀錄」中含哪些股票買進影響,回傳警告訊息片段
// 用於 doBatchDelete 等批次刪除流程,確保使用者知道會連帶清掉哪些持股
// 回傳 { msg: string | null, anyHoldingDestroyed: boolean }
const detectStockBuyImpact = (state, actuallyDeleteIds) => {
  // 找出將被刪的 txn 中,有 tradeId 且對應 trade 是 buy 的
  const affectedBuyTradeIds = new Set();
  for (const tx of state.transactions) {
    if (!actuallyDeleteIds.has(tx.id) || !tx.tradeId) continue;
    const tr = state.trades.find((x) => x.id === tx.tradeId);
    if (tr && tr.type === 'buy') affectedBuyTradeIds.add(tr.id);
  }
  if (affectedBuyTradeIds.size === 0) return { msg: null, anyHoldingDestroyed: false, highlightWords: [] };
  // 對每個受影響的 buy,看它對應的 holding 在刪除後是否還有 buy
  // (透過 tradeId 反推 — 還活著的 buy txn 不在 actuallyDeleteIds 內就算)
  const aliveBuyTradeIds = new Set();
  for (const tx of state.transactions) {
    if (actuallyDeleteIds.has(tx.id) || !tx.tradeId) continue;
    const tr = state.trades.find((x) => x.id === tx.tradeId);
    if (tr && tr.type === 'buy') aliveBuyTradeIds.add(tr.id);
  }
  const destroyedHoldings = []; // { symbol, sellsCount }
  const visited = new Set();
  for (const buyId of affectedBuyTradeIds) {
    const buyTr = state.trades.find((x) => x.id === buyId);
    if (!buyTr) continue;
    const hId = buyTr.holdingId;
    if (visited.has(hId)) continue;
    visited.add(hId);
    // 該 holding 是否還有 buy 來源?
    const stillHasBuy = state.trades.some(
      (tr) => tr.holdingId === hId && tr.type === 'buy' && aliveBuyTradeIds.has(tr.id)
    );
    if (stillHasBuy) continue;
    // 該 holding 將完全消失
    const holding = state.holdings.find((h) => h.id === hId);
    if (!holding) continue;
    const sellsCount = state.trades.filter((tr) => tr.holdingId === hId && tr.type === 'sell').length;
    destroyedHoldings.push({ symbol: holding.symbol || '未知', sellsCount });
  }
  if (destroyedHoldings.length === 0) {
    return {
      msg: '⚠ 包含股票買進紀錄,刪除會影響該股票的成本計算。',
      anyHoldingDestroyed: false,
      highlightWords: [],
    };
  }
  // 有 holding 會完全消失
  let msg;
  let highlightWords = ['完全消失']; // 給 ConfirmDialog 的 highlightWords,讓「完全消失」染色
  if (destroyedHoldings.length === 1) {
    const h = destroyedHoldings[0];
    msg = `⚠ 「${h.symbol}」持股將 完全消失 。`;
    if (h.sellsCount > 0) {
      msg += `\n該持股已有 ${h.sellsCount} 筆 賣出紀錄\n結算與損益紀錄也會一併清除。`;
    }
  } else {
    const names = destroyedHoldings.map((h) => `「${h.symbol}」`).join('、');
    const totalSells = destroyedHoldings.reduce((sum, h) => sum + h.sellsCount, 0);
    msg = `⚠ ${names}持股將 完全消失 。`;
    if (totalSells > 0) {
      msg += `\n相關 ${totalSells} 筆 賣出結算與損益紀錄\n也會一併清除。`;
    }
  }
  return { msg, anyHoldingDestroyed: true, highlightWords };
};

// 把批次刪除的紀錄組成 preview 文字:主動選的在前、連動展開的在後並標 (連動)
// 主動選的: ・分類 › 子類  ±金額
// 連動展開的: ・(連動) 分類 › 子類  ±金額
// 超過 maxLines 用「以及其他 N 筆」
const buildBatchDeletePreview = (transactions, selectedIds, actuallyDeleteIds, maxLines = 5) => {
  const fmtAmt = (t) => `${t.type === 'expense' ? '-' : '+'}${t.amount.toLocaleString()}`;
  const labelOf = (t) => {
    if (t.transferRole === 'out') return '轉出';
    if (t.transferRole === 'in') return '轉入';
    if (t.transferRole === 'fee') return '手續費';
    return t.subCategory ? `${t.category || '未分類'} › ${t.subCategory}` : (t.category || '未分類');
  };
  const ordered = transactions.filter((t) => actuallyDeleteIds.has(t.id));
  // 排序:主動選的優先,內部按 date desc + createdAt desc;連動的也按同樣序
  const sortFn = (a, b) => b.date.localeCompare(a.date) || (b.createdAt || 0) - (a.createdAt || 0);
  const primary = ordered.filter((t) => selectedIds.has(t.id)).sort(sortFn);
  const cascade = ordered.filter((t) => !selectedIds.has(t.id)).sort(sortFn);
  const lines = [];
  for (const t of primary) lines.push(`・${labelOf(t)}  ${fmtAmt(t)}`);
  for (const t of cascade) lines.push(`・(連動) ${labelOf(t)}  ${fmtAmt(t)}`);
  if (lines.length <= maxLines) return lines.join('\n');
  const shown = lines.slice(0, maxLines);
  shown.push(`・以及其他 ${lines.length - maxLines} 筆`);
  return shown.join('\n');
};

// 預測「刪除 actuallyDeleteIds 後,股票買進連動會額外清掉的紀錄」
// 邏輯與 syncTradesAfterTxnDelete 第二輪 cascade 相同:
//   buy trade 被刪 → 該 holding 失去所有 buy → 殘存的 sell trade 跟對應的 settle 紀錄都要連動清
// 回傳要追加納入 actuallyDeleteIds 的 transaction id(避免警告漏列)
const expandStockBuyCascade = (state, actuallyDeleteIds) => {
  // 找被刪 txn 中含 buy tradeId 的
  const deletingBuyTradeIds = new Set();
  for (const tx of state.transactions) {
    if (!actuallyDeleteIds.has(tx.id) || !tx.tradeId) continue;
    const tr = state.trades.find((x) => x.id === tx.tradeId);
    if (tr && tr.type === 'buy') deletingBuyTradeIds.add(tr.id);
  }
  if (deletingBuyTradeIds.size === 0) return new Set();
  // 哪些 buy trade 還活著(對應的 txn 沒被刪)
  const aliveBuyTradeIds = new Set();
  for (const tx of state.transactions) {
    if (actuallyDeleteIds.has(tx.id) || !tx.tradeId) continue;
    const tr = state.trades.find((x) => x.id === tx.tradeId);
    if (tr && tr.type === 'buy') aliveBuyTradeIds.add(tr.id);
  }
  // 受影響的 holding(失去所有 buy)
  const orphanedHoldingIds = new Set();
  const visited = new Set();
  for (const buyId of deletingBuyTradeIds) {
    const buyTr = state.trades.find((x) => x.id === buyId);
    if (!buyTr) continue;
    const hId = buyTr.holdingId;
    if (visited.has(hId)) continue;
    visited.add(hId);
    const stillHasBuy = state.trades.some(
      (tr) => tr.holdingId === hId && tr.type === 'buy' && aliveBuyTradeIds.has(tr.id)
    );
    if (!stillHasBuy) orphanedHoldingIds.add(hId);
  }
  if (orphanedHoldingIds.size === 0) return new Set();
  // 找這些 holding 上殘存的 sell tradeIds
  const cascadeSellTradeIds = new Set();
  for (const tr of state.trades) {
    if (tr.type !== 'sell') continue;
    if (!orphanedHoldingIds.has(tr.holdingId)) continue;
    cascadeSellTradeIds.add(tr.id);
  }
  if (cascadeSellTradeIds.size === 0) return new Set();
  // 對應的 transactions(透過 tradeId)— settle_out / settle_in / settle_pnl_*
  const extraTxnIds = new Set();
  for (const tx of state.transactions) {
    if (!tx.tradeId) continue;
    if (actuallyDeleteIds.has(tx.id)) continue; // 已經要刪了不重複
    if (cascadeSellTradeIds.has(tx.tradeId)) extraTxnIds.add(tx.id);
  }
  return extraTxnIds;
};

// 計算某帳戶在特定年月的交易
const txnsInMonth = (account, transactions, ym) => {
  return transactions
    .filter((t) => t.accountId === account.id && t.date.startsWith(ym))
    .sort((a, b) => b.date.localeCompare(a.date) || (b.createdAt || 0) - (a.createdAt || 0));
};

const memStore = { data: null };
const storageGet = () => { try { return localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY); } catch { return memStore.data; } };
const storageSet = (v) => { try { localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, v); } catch { memStore.data = v; } };
const storageClear = () => { try { localStorage.removeItem(STORAGE_KEY); } catch { memStore.data = null; } };

// 全局 noteColor 監聽(供 TxnRow 等子元件讀取)
const noteColorListeners = new Set();
const noteColorBroadcast = (color) => {
  noteColorListeners.forEach((cb) => cb(color));
};
function useNoteColor() {
  const [color, setColor] = useState(() => {
    try { return localStorage.getItem(NOTE_COLOR_KEY) || ''; } catch { return ''; }
  });
  useEffect(() => {
    noteColorListeners.add(setColor);
    return () => { noteColorListeners.delete(setColor); };
  }, []);
  return color;
}

// 全局 NotePref 監聽(備註樣式偏好)
const notePrefListeners = new Set();
const notePrefBroadcast = (pref) => {
  notePrefListeners.forEach((cb) => cb(pref));
};
function loadNotePref() {
  try {
    const raw = localStorage.getItem(NOTE_PREF_KEY);
    if (!raw) return { ...DEFAULT_NOTE_PREF };
    return { ...DEFAULT_NOTE_PREF, ...JSON.parse(raw) };
  } catch { return { ...DEFAULT_NOTE_PREF }; }
}
function useNotePref() {
  const [pref, setPref] = useState(loadNotePref);
  useEffect(() => {
    notePrefListeners.add(setPref);
    return () => { notePrefListeners.delete(setPref); };
  }, []);
  return pref;
}

// ============ 滑動返回 hook（左右都可，阻擋系統手勢）============
function useSwipeBack(onBack, options = {}) {
  const { skipInPickerBackdrop = false } = options;
  const [dragX, setDragX] = useState(0);
  const onBackRef = React.useRef(onBack);
  React.useEffect(() => { onBackRef.current = onBack; }, [onBack]);

  // 用 callback ref：元素 mount 就綁 listener，unmount 自動清掉
  const cleanupRef = React.useRef(null);
  const setDragXRef = React.useRef(setDragX);
  setDragXRef.current = setDragX;

  const refCallback = React.useCallback((el) => {
    // 先清掉舊的 listener（舊元素已被拔掉）
    if (cleanupRef.current) {
      cleanupRef.current();
      cleanupRef.current = null;
    }
    if (!el) return;

    let startX = null, startY = null;
    let lastX = null, lastY = null;
    let isHorizontal = false;

    const onStart = (e) => {
      const target = e.target;
      if (target && (target.tagName === 'INPUT' && target.type === 'range' || target.closest?.('input[type="range"]'))) {
        startX = null;
        return;
      }
      // 自製拉桿:也跳過 swipe back
      if (target && target.closest?.('[data-slider="true"]')) {
        startX = null;
        return;
      }
      if (skipInPickerBackdrop && target && target.closest?.('[data-picker-backdrop]')) {
        startX = null;
        return;
      }
      // 如果正在拖曳排序,跳過 swipe back 邏輯
      if (document.body.hasAttribute('data-drag-active')) {
        startX = null;
        return;
      }
      const t = e.touches[0];
      startX = t.clientX;
      startY = t.clientY;
      lastX = t.clientX;
      lastY = t.clientY;
      isHorizontal = false;
    };

    const onMove = (e) => {
      if (startX == null) return;
      // 拖曳排序啟動後立即中止 swipe(避免拖曳中誤觸)
      if (document.body.hasAttribute('data-drag-active')) {
        startX = null;
        setDragXRef.current(0);
        return;
      }
      const t = e.touches[0];
      lastX = t.clientX;
      lastY = t.clientY;
      const dx = t.clientX - startX;
      const dy = Math.abs(t.clientY - startY);

      if (!isHorizontal && Math.abs(dx) > 10 && Math.abs(dx) > dy) {
        isHorizontal = true;
      }

      if (isHorizontal) {
        e.preventDefault();
        const clamped = Math.max(-200, Math.min(200, dx));
        setDragXRef.current(clamped);
      }
    };

    const onEnd = () => {
      if (startX != null && lastX != null) {
        const dx = lastX - startX;
        const dy = Math.abs(lastY - startY);
        if (Math.abs(dx) > 70 && Math.abs(dx) > dy) {
          onBackRef.current();
        }
      }
      setDragXRef.current(0);
      startX = null;
      startY = null;
      lastX = null;
      lastY = null;
      isHorizontal = false;
    };

    el.addEventListener('touchstart', onStart, { passive: true });
    el.addEventListener('touchmove', onMove, { passive: false });
    el.addEventListener('touchend', onEnd, { passive: true });
    el.addEventListener('touchcancel', onEnd, { passive: true });

    cleanupRef.current = () => {
      el.removeEventListener('touchstart', onStart);
      el.removeEventListener('touchmove', onMove);
      el.removeEventListener('touchend', onEnd);
      el.removeEventListener('touchcancel', onEnd);
    };
  }, [skipInPickerBackdrop]);

  return { ref: refCallback, dragX };
}

// ============ 滑動關閉（用於置中對話框/底部動作選單）============
// 回傳 handlers 給 backdrop；左右滑超過閾值就觸發 onClose
function useSwipeToClose(onClose, threshold = 50) {
  const startRef = React.useRef(null);
  return {
    onTouchStart: (e) => {
      const t = e.touches[0];
      startRef.current = { x: t.clientX, y: t.clientY };
    },
    onTouchMove: (e) => {
      if (!startRef.current) return;
      const t = e.touches[0];
      const dx = t.clientX - startRef.current.x;
      const dy = Math.abs(t.clientY - startRef.current.y);
      // 已經確認是水平滑動，阻止預設（避免頁面跟著滑）
      if (Math.abs(dx) > 10 && Math.abs(dx) > dy) {
        e.preventDefault?.();
      }
    },
    onTouchEnd: (e) => {
      if (!startRef.current) return;
      const t = e.changedTouches[0];
      const dx = t.clientX - startRef.current.x;
      const dy = Math.abs(t.clientY - startRef.current.y);
      startRef.current = null;
      if (Math.abs(dx) > threshold && Math.abs(dx) > dy) {
        onClose?.();
      }
    },
    onTouchCancel: () => { startRef.current = null; },
  };
}

// 計算機專用:支援左右滑 + 下滑關閉(下滑會即時帶動位移看到關閉動畫)
function useSwipeToCloseAny(onClose, threshold = 60) {
  const startRef = React.useRef(null);
  const onInputRef = React.useRef(false);  // 是否從 input/slider 開始(這類元件由自己處理)
  const [dragY, setDragY] = React.useState(0);
  return {
    dragY,
    setDragY,
    onTouchStart: (e) => {
      const tag = (e.target && e.target.tagName) ? e.target.tagName.toLowerCase() : '';
      // 只有 input/textarea/select 完全跳過(slider 拖拉、文字輸入要保留原本行為)
      onInputRef.current = (tag === 'input' || tag === 'textarea' || tag === 'select');
      const t = e.touches[0];
      startRef.current = { x: t.clientX, y: t.clientY };
    },
    onTouchMove: (e) => {
      if (onInputRef.current || !startRef.current) return;
      const t = e.touches[0];
      const dx = t.clientX - startRef.current.x;
      const dy = t.clientY - startRef.current.y;
      // 下滑時讓 sheet 跟著手指走(只下,不上)
      if (dy > 0 && Math.abs(dy) > Math.abs(dx)) {
        setDragY(dy);
        e.preventDefault?.();
      }
      // 水平滑也阻止預設
      else if (Math.abs(dx) > 10 && Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)) {
        e.preventDefault?.();
      }
    },
    onTouchEnd: (e) => {
      if (onInputRef.current) { onInputRef.current = false; startRef.current = null; return; }
      if (!startRef.current) return;
      const t = e.changedTouches[0];
      const dx = t.clientX - startRef.current.x;
      const dy = t.clientY - startRef.current.y;
      startRef.current = null;
      // 左右滑 ≥ threshold,或下滑 ≥ threshold
      if (Math.abs(dx) > threshold && Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy)) {
        setDragY(0);
        onClose?.();
        return;
      }
      if (dy > threshold && dy > Math.abs(dx)) {
        setDragY(0);
        onClose?.();
        return;
      }
      // 沒達門檻 → 彈回
      setDragY(0);
    },
    onTouchCancel: () => {
      startRef.current = null;
      onInputRef.current = false;
      setDragY(0);
    },
  };
}

// ============ 單色圖示元件 ============
function TypeIcon({ name, size = 22, color = '#fff' }) {
  const props = {
    width: size,
    height: size,
    viewBox: '0 0 24 24',
    fill: 'none',
    stroke: color,
    strokeWidth: 1.6,
    strokeLinecap: 'round',
    strokeLinejoin: 'round',
  };
  const f = { fill: color, stroke: 'none' };

  switch (name) {
    // 現金 / 紙鈔(共用同一個圖示)
    case 'bill':
    case 'cash': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="3" y="7" width="18" height="10" rx="2" />
        <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="2" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 銀行（希臘神殿形）
    case 'bank': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M4 10 L12 5 L20 10" />
        <line x1="4" y1="10" x2="20" y2="10" />
        <line x1="6" y1="10" x2="6" y2="17" />
        <line x1="12" y1="10" x2="12" y2="17" />
        <line x1="18" y1="10" x2="18" y2="17" />
        <line x1="3" y1="19" x2="21" y2="19" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 信用卡（簡潔長方形 + 單條線）
    case 'card': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="3" y="6" width="18" height="12" rx="2" />
        <line x1="3" y1="11" x2="21" y2="11" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 手機（圓角長方形 + 小點）
    case 'phone': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="7" y="3" width="10" height="18" rx="2" />
        <circle cx="12" cy="18" r="0.6" {...f} />
      </svg>
    );
    // 折線圖（單一向上箭頭線）
    case 'chart': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <polyline points="4 17 10 11 14 14 20 7" />
        <polyline points="15 7 20 7 20 12" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 箱子（立體感但簡潔）
    case 'box': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M3 8 L12 4 L21 8 L12 12 Z" />
        <path d="M3 8 L3 16 L12 20 L12 12" />
        <path d="M21 8 L21 16 L12 20" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 房子（屋頂 + 方塊）
    case 'home': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M4 11 L12 4 L20 11 L20 20 L4 20 Z" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 汽車
    case 'car': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M5 14 L6 9 L18 9 L19 14" />
        <rect x="4" y="14" width="16" height="5" rx="1" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 錢袋
    case 'bag': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M7 8 Q7 4 12 4 Q17 4 17 8 L19 20 L5 20 Z" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 鑽石
    case 'gem': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M6 4 L18 4 L21 10 L12 21 L3 10 Z" />
        <path d="M3 10 L21 10" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 靶心（兩層圓 + 中心點）
    case 'target': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="8" />
        <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="2" {...f} />
      </svg>
    );
    // 硬幣（₽符號風格）
    case 'coin': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="8" />
        <path d="M10 8 L10 16 M10 8 L13 8 Q15 8 15 10 Q15 12 13 12 L10 12" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 公事包
    case 'briefcase': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="3" y="8" width="18" height="12" rx="1.5" />
        <path d="M9 8 L9 6 Q9 5 10 5 L14 5 Q15 5 15 6 L15 8" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 購物車
    case 'cart': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M3 5 L5 5 L7 15 L18 15 L20 8 L7 8" />
        <circle cx="9" cy="19" r="1" {...f} />
        <circle cx="17" cy="19" r="1" {...f} />
      </svg>
    );
    // 加油槍
    case 'fuel': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="4" y="4" width="9" height="16" rx="1.5" />
        <path d="M13 10 L17 10 L17 17 Q17 19 18.5 19 Q20 19 20 17 L20 9 L18 7" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 醫院（方塊 + 十字）
    case 'hospital': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="4" y="4" width="16" height="16" rx="2" />
        <line x1="12" y1="9" x2="12" y2="15" />
        <line x1="9" y1="12" x2="15" y2="12" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 飛機（簡化成向上的樣子）
    case 'plane': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M12 3 L14 10 L21 12 L14 14 L12 21 L10 14 L3 12 L10 10 Z" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 禮物（方塊 + 十字緞帶）
    case 'gift': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="4" y="10" width="16" height="10" rx="1" />
        <line x1="4" y1="13" x2="20" y2="13" />
        <line x1="12" y1="10" x2="12" y2="20" />
        <path d="M8 10 Q6 8 7 6 Q9 5 12 10" />
        <path d="M16 10 Q18 8 17 6 Q15 5 12 10" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 長條圖（三根柱子）
    case 'barchart': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <line x1="6" y1="20" x2="6" y2="12" />
        <line x1="12" y1="20" x2="12" y2="6" />
        <line x1="18" y1="20" x2="18" y2="15" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 大樓
    case 'building': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="5" y="3" width="14" height="18" />
        <line x1="9" y1="7" x2="9" y2="7.5" />
        <line x1="15" y1="7" x2="15" y2="7.5" />
        <line x1="9" y1="11" x2="9" y2="11.5" />
        <line x1="15" y1="11" x2="15" y2="11.5" />
        <line x1="9" y1="15" x2="9" y2="15.5" />
        <line x1="15" y1="15" x2="15" y2="15.5" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 學士帽
    case 'cap': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M3 10 L12 5 L21 10 L12 15 Z" />
        <path d="M7 12 L7 16 Q7 18 12 18 Q17 18 17 16 L17 12" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 餐盤（圓圈）
    case 'plate': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="8" />
        <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="3" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 遊戲手把
    case 'game': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="3" y="8" width="18" height="10" rx="4" />
        <line x1="7" y1="13" x2="10" y2="13" />
        <line x1="8.5" y1="11.5" x2="8.5" y2="14.5" />
        <circle cx="15" cy="12" r="0.8" {...f} />
        <circle cx="17" cy="14" r="0.8" {...f} />
      </svg>
    );
    // 床/住宿
    case 'bed': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M3 17 L3 9 L10 9 L10 13 L21 13 L21 17" />
        <line x1="3" y1="19" x2="21" y2="19" />
        <circle cx="7" cy="11" r="1" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 購物袋
    case 'shopping': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M5 8 L7 20 L17 20 L19 8 Z" />
        <path d="M9 8 Q9 4 12 4 Q15 4 15 8" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 電影/娛樂（膠卷板）
    case 'movie': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="3" y="8" width="18" height="12" />
        <path d="M3 12 L21 12" />
        <path d="M6 4 L8 8 M10 4 L12 8 M14 4 L16 8 M18 4 L20 8" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 書本（教育）
    case 'book': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M4 5 L12 7 L12 20 L4 18 Z" />
        <path d="M20 5 L12 7 L12 20 L20 18 Z" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 寵物（爪印）
    case 'paw': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <circle cx="7" cy="9" r="1.5" />
        <circle cx="12" cy="7" r="1.5" />
        <circle cx="17" cy="9" r="1.5" />
        <circle cx="5" cy="14" r="1.5" />
        <circle cx="19" cy="14" r="1.5" />
        <path d="M8 19 Q8 15 12 15 Q16 15 16 19 Q16 21 12 21 Q8 21 8 19" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 閃電/水電費
    case 'bolt': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M13 3 L5 14 L11 14 L10 21 L19 9 L13 9 Z" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 咖啡
    case 'coffee': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M4 8 L4 17 Q4 20 8 20 L14 20 Q18 20 18 17 L18 8 Z" />
        <path d="M18 10 L20 10 Q22 10 22 12 L22 14 Q22 16 20 16 L18 16" />
        <path d="M8 4 Q8 6 10 6 M12 4 Q12 6 14 6" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 音符
    case 'music': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <circle cx="7" cy="18" r="2.5" />
        <circle cx="17" cy="16" r="2.5" />
        <line x1="9.5" y1="18" x2="9.5" y2="6" />
        <line x1="19.5" y1="16" x2="19.5" y2="4" />
        <path d="M9.5 6 L19.5 4" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 筆記/備註/其他
    case 'note': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M5 4 L15 4 L19 8 L19 20 L5 20 Z" />
        <path d="M15 4 L15 8 L19 8" />
        <line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12" />
        <line x1="8" y1="15" x2="14" y2="15" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 薪資錢袋
    case 'salary': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M7 8 Q7 4 12 4 Q17 4 17 8 L19 20 L5 20 Z" />
        <path d="M10 12 L14 12 M10 14 L14 14 M12 10 L12 16" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 火花/其他
    case 'spark': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M12 3 L13 10 L20 11 L13 12 L12 19 L11 12 L4 11 L11 10 Z" />
        <path d="M18 4 L18.5 6 L20 6.5 L18.5 7 L18 9 L17.5 7 L16 6.5 L17.5 6 Z" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 明細列表（剪貼板）
    case 'list': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="5" y="4" width="14" height="17" rx="2" />
        <path d="M9 4 L9 2 L15 2 L15 4" />
        <line x1="8.5" y1="10" x2="15.5" y2="10" />
        <line x1="8.5" y1="14" x2="15.5" y2="14" />
        <line x1="8.5" y1="17" x2="13" y2="17" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 日曆
    case 'calendar': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="4" y="5" width="16" height="16" rx="2" />
        <line x1="4" y1="10" x2="20" y2="10" />
        <line x1="8" y1="3" x2="8" y2="7" />
        <line x1="16" y1="3" x2="16" y2="7" />
        <circle cx="12" cy="15" r="1" {...f} />
      </svg>
    );
    // 鎖（關閉）
    case 'lock': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="5" y="11" width="14" height="10" rx="2" />
        <path d="M8 11 V7 a4 4 0 0 1 8 0 V11" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 鎖（開啟）
    case 'unlock': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="5" y="11" width="14" height="10" rx="2" />
        <path d="M8 11 V7 a4 4 0 0 1 8 0" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 統計（圓餅圖）
    case 'pie': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M12 3 A9 9 0 1 1 3 12 L12 12 Z" />
        <path d="M12 3 L12 12 L21 12 A9 9 0 0 0 12 3 Z" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 齒輪（設定）
    case 'gear': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="3" />
        <path d="M12 2 L12 5 M12 19 L12 22 M2 12 L5 12 M19 12 L22 12 M4.9 4.9 L7 7 M17 17 L19.1 19.1 M4.9 19.1 L7 17 M17 7 L19.1 4.9" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 鉛筆（編輯）
    case 'pencil': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M17 3 L21 7 L8 20 L3 21 L4 16 L17 3 Z" />
        <path d="M15 5 L19 9" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 星星(空心,標記為預設/常用)
    case 'star': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M12 3 L14.5 9 L21 9.5 L16 14 L17.5 20.5 L12 17 L6.5 20.5 L8 14 L3 9.5 L9.5 9 Z" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 星星(實心,已標記為預設)
    case 'star-filled': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M12 3 L14.5 9 L21 9.5 L16 14 L17.5 20.5 L12 17 L6.5 20.5 L8 14 L3 9.5 L9.5 9 Z" {...f} />
      </svg>
    );
    // 垃圾桶（刪除）
    case 'trash': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M4 7 L20 7" />
        <path d="M10 3 L14 3 L14 7 L10 7 Z" />
        <path d="M6 7 L7 21 L17 21 L18 7" />
        <path d="M10 11 L10 17 M14 11 L14 17" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 搜尋(放大鏡)
    case 'search': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <circle cx="10.5" cy="10.5" r="6.5" />
        <line x1="21" y1="21" x2="15.5" y2="15.5" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 下載（匯出 JSON — 向下箭頭進盒子）
    case 'download': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M12 3 L12 15" />
        <path d="M7 10 L12 15 L17 10" />
        <path d="M4 19 L20 19" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 上傳（匯入 — 向上箭頭出盒子）
    case 'upload': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M12 15 L12 3" />
        <path d="M7 8 L12 3 L17 8" />
        <path d="M4 19 L20 19" />
      </svg>
    );
    // CSV/試算表
    case 'sheet': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="4" y="3" width="16" height="18" rx="1" />
        <path d="M4 9 L20 9 M4 15 L20 15 M10 3 L10 21 M16 3 L16 21" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 資料夾
    case 'folder': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M3 6 L3 19 L21 19 L21 9 L12 9 L10 6 L3 6 Z" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 扳手（工具/設定）
    case 'wrench': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M14 6 L18 2 L22 6 L18 10 L14 6 Z" />
        <path d="M14 6 L4 16 L4 20 L8 20 L18 10" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 時鐘（提醒）
    case 'clock': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" />
        <path d="M12 7 L12 12 L16 14" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 連結鏈條
    case 'link': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M10 14 A4 4 0 0 1 10 8 L13 5 A4 4 0 0 1 19 11 L17 13" />
        <path d="M14 10 A4 4 0 0 1 14 16 L11 19 A4 4 0 0 1 5 13 L7 11" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 警告（三角驚嘆）
    case 'warning': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M12 3 L22 20 L2 20 Z" />
        <path d="M12 10 L12 15 M12 17.5 L12 18" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 筆記本（紀錄筆數）
    case 'clipboard': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <rect x="5" y="4" width="14" height="17" rx="1" />
        <path d="M9 4 L9 2 L15 2 L15 4" />
        <path d="M8 10 L16 10 M8 14 L16 14 M8 18 L12 18" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 盾牌（保險）
    case 'shield': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M12 3 L4 6 L4 12 C4 17 8 20 12 22 C16 20 20 17 20 12 L20 6 Z" />
        <path d="M9 12 L11 14 L15 10" />
      </svg>
    );
    // 標籤(分類)
    case 'tag': return (
      <svg {...props}>
        <path d="M3 12 L3 4 L11 4 L21 14 L13 22 Z" />
        <circle cx="7" cy="8" r="1" {...f} />
      </svg>
    );
    default: return (
      <svg {...props}><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="8" /></svg>
    );
  }
}

// ============ 主元件 ============
function App() {
  const [state, setState] = useState(() => {
    try {
      const raw = storageGet();
      if (raw) {
        const d = JSON.parse(raw);
        return {
          transactions: d.transactions || [],
          accounts: d.accounts?.length ? d.accounts : [...DEFAULT_ACCOUNTS],
          categories: d.categories || JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(DEFAULT_CATEGORIES)),
          accountTypes: d.accountTypes?.length ? d.accountTypes : [...DEFAULT_ACCOUNT_TYPES],
          holdings: d.holdings || [],
          trades: d.trades || [],
        };
      }
    } catch {}
    return {
      transactions: [],
      accounts: [...DEFAULT_ACCOUNTS],
      categories: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(DEFAULT_CATEGORIES)),
      accountTypes: [...DEFAULT_ACCOUNT_TYPES],
      holdings: [],
      trades: [],
    };
  });

  const [page, setPage] = useState('home');
  const [sheet, setSheet] = useState(null);
  const [sheetType, setSheetType] = useState('expense');
  const [editingTxn, setEditingTxn] = useState(null);
  const [toastMsg, setToastMsg] = useState('');
  const [currentMonth, setCurrentMonth] = useState(todayStr().slice(0, 7));
  const [selectedDate, setSelectedDate] = useState(todayStr());
  const [periodKey, setPeriodKey] = useState(null);
  const [detailDate, setDetailDate] = useState(null); // 點日期後看該日明細
  const [lendDetail, setLendDetail] = useState(null); // 代墊詳細頁(顯示某筆 lend_out 的詳細與收回操作)
  const [settleDetail, setSettleDetail] = useState(null); // 股票結算詳情頁(整組唯讀檢視)
  const [editMode, setEditMode] = useState(false);
  const [txnSelectMode, setTxnSelectMode] = useState(false); // 明細頁多選刪除模式(需要藏 bottom nav)
  const [homeSelectMode, setHomeSelectMode] = useState(false); // 首頁最近紀錄多選刪除模式
  const [settingsSubSheet, setSettingsSubSheet] = useState(false); // 設定頁內部子 sheet(清理/Drive 設定等,需要藏 bottom nav)
  // 備註顏色(全局)
  const [noteColor, setNoteColor] = useState(() => {
    try {
      return localStorage.getItem(NOTE_COLOR_KEY) || DEFAULT_NOTE_COLOR;
    } catch { return DEFAULT_NOTE_COLOR; }
  });
  useEffect(() => {
    try { localStorage.setItem(NOTE_COLOR_KEY, noteColor); } catch {}
    noteColorBroadcast(noteColor);
  }, [noteColor]);

  // [一次性遷移] 帳戶 / 已刪烙印紀錄補上 createdAt:
  // 沒紀錄時間的舊帳戶,用「10 天前隨機」(過去 10 天內某個時刻)填入,
  // 讓使用者點 ⓘ 時都能看到一個合理的建立時間。
  // 同時強制修正:debt 類型的 initAmount 一律存為負數
  // (避免某些使用者在編輯時誤改成正數,導致餘額計算反向)
  useEffect(() => {
    let migrated = false;
    setState((s) => {
      const now = Date.now();
      const tenDaysMs = 10 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
      const randomPastTime = () => now - Math.floor(Math.random() * tenDaysMs);

      const newAccounts = s.accounts.map((a) => {
        const patches = {};
        if (!a.createdAt) {
          patches.createdAt = randomPastTime();
          migrated = true;
        }
        // debt 類型強制 init 為負數
        if (a.type === 'debt' && (a.initAmount || 0) > 0) {
          patches.initAmount = -Math.abs(a.initAmount);
          migrated = true;
        }
        // invest 類型沒有 investSubType → 預設 stock(維持現有體驗)
        if (a.type === 'invest' && !a.investSubType) {
          patches.investSubType = 'stock';
          migrated = true;
        }
        return Object.keys(patches).length ? { ...a, ...patches } : a;
      });

      const newTxns = s.transactions.map((t) => {
        // 已刪虛擬帳戶烙印的紀錄:本端 + 對方端
        const patches = {};
        if (t._deletedAccountName && !t._deletedAccountCreatedAt) {
          patches._deletedAccountCreatedAt = randomPastTime();
          migrated = true;
        }
        if (t._deletedPeerName && !t._deletedPeerCreatedAt) {
          patches._deletedPeerCreatedAt = randomPastTime();
          migrated = true;
        }
        return Object.keys(patches).length ? { ...t, ...patches } : t;
      });

      // 雙向孤兒清理:
      //   方向 1:trade 對應的主帳本紀錄不存在 → 移除 trade(然後 holding 沒任何 trade 也移除)
      //   方向 2:主帳本紀錄帶 tradeId 但對應的 trade 不存在 → 移除這筆主帳本紀錄
      // 這修正兩種潛在不一致:
      //   - 用戶從持股詳情刪 trade,連動沒清乾淨主帳本
      //   - 用戶從主帳本刪交易,連動沒清乾淨 trade
      //   - 舊版資料(沒 tradeId 烙印)
      let newTrades = s.trades || [];
      let newHoldings = s.holdings || [];
      let newTxns2 = newTxns;

      // 方向 1: trade -> txn
      const txTradeIds = new Set();
      for (const tx of newTxns2) {
        if (tx.tradeId) txTradeIds.add(tx.tradeId);
      }
      const orphanedTradeIds = new Set();
      for (const tr of newTrades) {
        if (!txTradeIds.has(tr.id)) orphanedTradeIds.add(tr.id);
      }
      if (orphanedTradeIds.size > 0) {
        newTrades = newTrades.filter((tr) => !orphanedTradeIds.has(tr.id));
        migrated = true;
      }

      // 方向 2: txn -> trade
      const validTradeIds = new Set(newTrades.map((tr) => tr.id));
      const orphanedTxnsBefore = newTxns2.length;
      newTxns2 = newTxns2.filter((tx) => !tx.tradeId || validTradeIds.has(tx.tradeId));
      if (newTxns2.length !== orphanedTxnsBefore) {
        migrated = true;
      }

      // 方向 3: 失去所有 buy 來源的 holding,殘存 sell 也要連動清掉
      // (避免「沒買進但有賣出」的不平衡狀態,例如使用者曾經從主帳本刪買進轉帳但 sell 沒被清)
      const holdingIds = new Set(newHoldings.map((h) => h.id));
      const cascadeSellIds = new Set();
      for (const hId of holdingIds) {
        const buys = newTrades.filter((tr) => tr.holdingId === hId && tr.type === 'buy');
        if (buys.length > 0) continue; // 還有 buy → 正常
        const sells = newTrades.filter((tr) => tr.holdingId === hId && tr.type === 'sell');
        for (const s2 of sells) cascadeSellIds.add(s2.id);
      }
      if (cascadeSellIds.size > 0) {
        newTrades = newTrades.filter((tr) => !cascadeSellIds.has(tr.id));
        newTxns2 = newTxns2.filter((tx) => !tx.tradeId || !cascadeSellIds.has(tx.tradeId));
        migrated = true;
      }

      // 孤兒 holding(沒有任何 trade)
      const newHoldingsFiltered = newHoldings.filter((h) =>
        newTrades.some((tr) => tr.holdingId === h.id)
      );
      if (newHoldingsFiltered.length !== newHoldings.length) {
        newHoldings = newHoldingsFiltered;
        migrated = true;
      }

      if (!migrated) return s; // 不需要遷移就不觸發 re-render
      return { ...s, accounts: newAccounts, transactions: newTxns2, trades: newTrades, holdings: newHoldings };
    });
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, []); // 只在啟動時跑一次

  // 確保「代墊暫存」系統帳戶存在(代墊功能依賴)
  // [已停用]代墊功能入口已移除,改用一般「轉帳」處理代墊情境,
  // 因此不再需要自動建立此系統帳戶。如有舊資料仍會保留不會被刪。
  // useEffect(() => {
  //   if (!getLendBucketAccount(state.accounts)) {
  //     setState((s) => ({
  //       ...s,
  //       accounts: [
  //         ...s.accounts,
  //         {
  //           id: 'sys_lend_bucket',
  //           name: LEND_BUCKET_ACCOUNT_NAME,
  //           type: 'receivable',
  //           initAmount: 0,
  //           isSystem: 'lend_bucket',
  //         },
  //       ],
  //     }));
  //   }
  //   // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  // }, []);
  const [theme, setTheme] = useState(() => {
    try {
      return localStorage.getItem(THEME_KEY) || DEFAULT_THEME;
    } catch { return DEFAULT_THEME; }
  });
  useEffect(() => {
    try { localStorage.setItem(THEME_KEY, theme); } catch {}
  }, [theme]);
  const [manageCat, setManageCat] = useState(null); // { type, initialLabel? } | null
  const [editAccountId, setEditAccountId] = useState(null); // 直接編輯哪個帳戶
  const [accountsFromAddTxn, setAccountsFromAddTxn] = useState(false); // 從 AddTxnSheet 打開帳戶管理（關閉時回到 AddTxn 而不是首頁）
  const [detailAccount, setDetailAccount] = useState(null); // 帳戶明細頁
  const [sellSheet, setSellSheet] = useState(null); // 股票賣出 sheet { account } | null
  const [buyHoldingSheet, setBuyHoldingSheet] = useState(null); // 買進股票 sheet { account, prefillSymbol? } | null
  const [sellHoldingSheet, setSellHoldingSheet] = useState(null); // 新版賣出 sheet { holding } | null
  const [marketValueDialog, setMarketValueDialog] = useState(null); // 估市值 { holding } | null
  const [holdingDetailSheet, setHoldingDetailSheet] = useState(null); // 持股詳情 sheet { holding } | null
  const [showStockEntryPicker, setShowStockEntryPicker] = useState(false); // 從 + 進入股票時的投資帳戶選擇
  // 確認彈窗（通用）
  const [confirmDialog, setConfirmDialog] = useState(null); // { title, message, onConfirm, confirmText?, danger? } | null
  // 最後備份時間
  const [lastBackupAt, setLastBackupAt] = useState(() => {
    try { return parseInt(localStorage.getItem('ledger_last_backup') || '0'); } catch { return 0; }
  });
  // 備份提醒天數（預設 7 天）
  const [backupReminderDays, setBackupReminderDays] = useState(() => {
    try { return parseInt(localStorage.getItem('ledger_backup_reminder_days') || '7'); } catch { return 7; }
  });
  // Google Drive 資料夾連結
  const [driveFolderUrl, setDriveFolderUrl] = useState(() => {
    try { return localStorage.getItem('ledger_drive_folder') || ''; } catch { return ''; }
  });

  // 區塊排序狀態（每頁一組）
  const [blockOrder, setBlockOrder] = useState(() => {
    const defaults = {
      home: ['summary', 'dateStrip', 'actions', 'periods', 'recent', 'lendReminder'],
      txn: ['summary', 'period', 'list'],
      stats: ['summary', 'period', 'chart', 'compare', 'top5', 'transfer'],
      settings: ['backup-local', 'backup-ext', 'account', 'appearance', 'dataStat', 'cleanup', 'danger'],
      addTxn: ['amount', 'typeToggle', 'date', 'category', 'subCategory', 'note', 'account'],
    };
    // 每頁逐個驗證：過濾掉預設裡沒有的舊 key，保留順序，再把預設裡有但 saved 沒有的補到最後
    const merge = (savedPage, defPage) => {
      const defSet = new Set(defPage);
      const filtered = Array.isArray(savedPage) ? savedPage.filter((k) => defSet.has(k)) : [];
      const missing = defPage.filter((k) => !filtered.includes(k));
      return [...filtered, ...missing];
    };
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem(BLOCK_ORDER_KEY);
      if (raw) {
        const saved = JSON.parse(raw);
        const result = {};
        Object.keys(defaults).forEach((pageKey) => {
          result[pageKey] = merge(saved[pageKey], defaults[pageKey]);
        });
        return result;
      }
    } catch {}
    return defaults;
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    try { localStorage.setItem(BLOCK_ORDER_KEY, JSON.stringify(blockOrder)); } catch {}
  }, [blockOrder]);

  const moveBlock = (pageKey) => (blockKey, delta) => {
    setBlockOrder((o) => {
      const arr = [...(o[pageKey] || [])];
      const idx = arr.indexOf(blockKey);
      if (idx < 0) return o;
      const newIdx = idx + delta;
      if (newIdx < 0 || newIdx >= arr.length) return o;
      [arr[idx], arr[newIdx]] = [arr[newIdx], arr[idx]];
      return { ...o, [pageKey]: arr };
    });
  };

  // 拖曳完直接整頁重排
  const setPageOrder = (pageKey) => (newOrder) => {
    setBlockOrder((o) => ({ ...o, [pageKey]: newOrder }));
  };

  // 左右滑動切換頁面
  const PAGE_ORDER = ['home', 'txn', 'stats', 'settings'];
  const touchStartRef = React.useRef(null);
  const swipeLockRef = React.useRef(false); // 垂直滑動時鎖住橫向判定
  const pageWrapperRef = React.useRef(null);
  const [swipeDragX, setSwipeDragX] = useState(0); // 滑動中的即時位移
  const [isSwipeAnimating, setIsSwipeAnimating] = useState(false); // 是否正在過渡動畫

  const handleTouchStart = (e) => {
    if (editMode || isSwipeAnimating) return;
    // Sheet / Dialog / 浮層開啟時不處理 tab 滑動(避免跟內部手勢衝突)
    if (sheet || confirmDialog || manageCat || editAccountId ||
        accountsFromAddTxn || periodKey || detailDate || detailAccount ||
        txnSelectMode || homeSelectMode) return;
    // 若 touch 起源在任何 sheet 或 picker/dialog 內,跳過 tab 滑動(避免與內部手勢衝突)
    if (e.target && e.target.closest && (
      e.target.closest('[data-sheet="true"]') ||
      e.target.closest('[data-picker-backdrop]')
    )) return;
    const t = e.touches[0];
    touchStartRef.current = { x: t.clientX, y: t.clientY, time: Date.now() };
    swipeLockRef.current = false;
    // 若上次滑動有殘留位移，先清掉（安全網）
    if (swipeDragX !== 0) setSwipeDragX(0);
  };

  const handleTouchMove = (e) => {
    if (!touchStartRef.current || swipeLockRef.current) return;
    const t = e.touches[0];
    const dx = t.clientX - touchStartRef.current.x;
    const dy = t.clientY - touchStartRef.current.y;
    // 如果垂直位移明顯大於水平，鎖住（讓用戶正常上下捲動）
    if (Math.abs(dy) > Math.abs(dx) && Math.abs(dy) > 10) {
      swipeLockRef.current = true;
      setSwipeDragX(0);
      return;
    }
    // 水平位移要夠大才判為滑動（避免誤觸點擊）
    if (Math.abs(dx) > 20) {
      const idx = PAGE_ORDER.indexOf(page);
      // 如果是邊界頁（已在第一頁還要右滑、或最後一頁還要左滑）就加阻力
      const atLeftEdge = idx === 0 && dx > 0;
      const atRightEdge = idx === PAGE_ORDER.length - 1 && dx < 0;
      const resisted = (atLeftEdge || atRightEdge) ? dx * 0.3 : dx;
      setSwipeDragX(resisted);
    }
  };

  const handleTouchEnd = (e) => {
    if (!touchStartRef.current || swipeLockRef.current) {
      touchStartRef.current = null;
      setSwipeDragX(0);
      return;
    }
    const t = e.changedTouches[0];
    const dx = t.clientX - touchStartRef.current.x;
    const dy = t.clientY - touchStartRef.current.y;
    const dt = Date.now() - touchStartRef.current.time;
    touchStartRef.current = null;

    // 位移很小 → 視為點擊，完全不處理（讓 onClick 正常運作）
    if (Math.abs(dx) < 15 && Math.abs(dy) < 15) {
      if (swipeDragX !== 0) setSwipeDragX(0);
      return;
    }

    // 判定閾值：距離 > 70 或（速度快 + 距離 > 30）
    const velocity = Math.abs(dx) / Math.max(dt, 1);
    const isHorizontal = Math.abs(dx) > Math.abs(dy);
    const meetsDistance = Math.abs(dx) > 70;
    const meetsVelocity = velocity > 0.4 && Math.abs(dx) > 30;
    const idx = PAGE_ORDER.indexOf(page);

    if (isHorizontal && (meetsDistance || meetsVelocity)) {
      if (dx < 0 && idx < PAGE_ORDER.length - 1) {
        // 往左滑 → 下一頁：直接切換（不做滑出動畫避免黑畫面）
        setSwipeDragX(0);
        setPage(PAGE_ORDER[idx + 1]);
        return;
      } else if (dx > 0 && idx > 0) {
        setSwipeDragX(0);
        setPage(PAGE_ORDER[idx - 1]);
        return;
      }
    }
    // 沒滿足條件 → 動畫滑回原位
    setIsSwipeAnimating(true);
    setSwipeDragX(0);
    setTimeout(() => setIsSwipeAnimating(false), 200);
  };

  // 手勢被系統中斷（例：拉下通知欄、返回手勢）→ 強制回位
  const handleTouchCancel = () => {
    touchStartRef.current = null;
    swipeLockRef.current = false;
    if (swipeDragX !== 0) {
      setIsSwipeAnimating(true);
      setSwipeDragX(0);
      setTimeout(() => setIsSwipeAnimating(false), 200);
    }
  };

  // 安全網：當頁面切換時，強制重置 dragX（避免殘留位移）
  React.useEffect(() => {
    setSwipeDragX(0);
    setIsSwipeAnimating(false);
  }, [page]);

  // 安全網：visibilitychange（切到別的 App 回來）時重置
  React.useEffect(() => {
    const onVisibility = () => {
      if (document.visibilityState === 'visible') {
        touchStartRef.current = null;
        swipeLockRef.current = false;
        setSwipeDragX(0);
        setIsSwipeAnimating(false);
      }
    };
    document.addEventListener('visibilitychange', onVisibility);
    return () => document.removeEventListener('visibilitychange', onVisibility);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    storageSet(JSON.stringify(state));
  }, [state]);

  const toast = (msg, ms = 2400) => {
    setToastMsg(msg);
    try { if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(30); } catch {}
    setTimeout(() => setToastMsg(''), ms);
  };
  // 把 toast 注入 module-scope 全域,供深層元件不透過 prop 取用(例如 TxnRow 的 ⓘ icon)
  React.useEffect(() => { setGlobalToast(toast); }, []);

  // 中央警示彈窗(視覺強烈,給金額錯誤等重要提示)
  const [centerAlert, setCenterAlert] = useState('');
  const alertCenter = (msg, ms = 1600) => {
    setCenterAlert(msg);
    try { if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([30, 50, 30]); } catch {} // 雙震,更明顯
    setTimeout(() => setCenterAlert(''), ms);
  };

  // 結構化 toast：可傳 { type, title, detail }
  const toastRich = (data, ms = 1180) => {
    setToastMsg(data);
    setTimeout(() => setToastMsg(''), ms);
  };
  // 注入 toastRich 到 module-scope,供深層元件不透過 prop 取用
  React.useEffect(() => { setGlobalToastRich(toastRich); }, []);

  // 把 categories 攤平成 Map 以加速查詢(原 find O(N) → Map.get O(1))
  // 只在 categories 變動時重建,否則沿用上次結果
  const catIconMap = React.useMemo(() => {
    const map = new Map();
    for (const type of Object.keys(state.categories || {})) {
      for (const c of state.categories[type] || []) {
        map.set(`${type}:${c.label}`, c.icon);
      }
    }
    return map;
  }, [state.categories]);
  const catIcon = (type, label) => {
    const iconName = catIconMap.get(`${type}:${label}`) || (type === 'income' ? 'bag' : 'note');
    return <TypeIcon name={iconName} size={18} color="var(--text)" />;
  };

  const saveTxn = (txn) => {
    // 判斷是新增還是編輯(用於 toast)
    const isEditing = txn._transfer
      ? state.transactions.some((t) => t.transferId === txn._transfer.transferId)
      : txn._lend
      ? state.transactions.some((t) => t.lendId === txn._lend.lendId)
      : state.transactions.some((t) => t.id === txn.id);

    // 偵測是否有實際變更(僅編輯模式判斷)
    let isUnchanged = false;
    if (isEditing && !txn._transfer && !txn._lend) {
      const old = state.transactions.find((t) => t.id === txn.id);
      if (old) {
        const fields = ['type', 'amount', 'date', 'category', 'subCategory', 'accountId', 'note'];
        isUnchanged = fields.every((k) => (old[k] || '') === (txn[k] || ''));
      }
    } else if (isEditing && txn._transfer) {
      // 轉帳組:比對 fromId, toId, amount, date, fee, note
      const tr = txn._transfer;
      const oldGroup = state.transactions.filter((t) => t.transferId === tr.transferId);
      const oldOut = oldGroup.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'out');
      const oldIn = oldGroup.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'in');
      const oldFee = oldGroup.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'fee');
      if (oldOut && oldIn) {
        const sameCore =
          oldOut.accountId === tr.fromId &&
          oldIn.accountId === tr.toId &&
          oldOut.amount === tr.amount &&
          oldOut.date === tr.date &&
          (oldOut.note || '') === (tr.note || '');
        const sameFee = (oldFee?.amount || 0) === (tr.fee || 0);
        isUnchanged = sameCore && sameFee;
      }
    }

    setState((s) => {
      // 轉帳:存一組 2~3 筆關聯紀錄(out/in/fee),共用 transferId
      if (txn._transfer) {
        const tr = txn._transfer;
        const group = tr.transferId || ('tr_' + uid().slice(2, 10));
        const baseMeta = {
          transferId: group,
          transferPeer: { fromId: tr.fromId, toId: tr.toId },
          createdAt: tr.createdAt || Date.now(),
        };
        // 先移除這組裡的舊紀錄(編輯情境),但記住舊紀錄上的「已刪虛擬帳戶」烙印,儲存時要保留
        const oldGroup = s.transactions.filter((t) => t.transferId === group);
        const oldOut = oldGroup.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'out');
        const oldIn = oldGroup.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'in');
        const oldFee = oldGroup.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'fee');
        const pickStamps = (t) => {
          if (!t) return {};
          const stamps = {};
          if (t._deletedAccountName) stamps._deletedAccountName = t._deletedAccountName;
          if (t._deletedAccountVirtual) stamps._deletedAccountVirtual = t._deletedAccountVirtual;
          if (t._deletedPeerName) stamps._deletedPeerName = t._deletedPeerName;
          if (t._deletedPeerVirtual) stamps._deletedPeerVirtual = t._deletedPeerVirtual;
          return stamps;
        };
        let kept = s.transactions.filter((t) => t.transferId !== group);
        // 建 out 紀錄(保留舊 out 的已刪烙印)
        const outTxn = {
          id: 'to_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
          type: 'expense',
          amount: tr.amount,
          date: tr.date,
          note: tr.note || '[帳戶轉帳]',
          category: '轉帳',
          subCategory: '',
          accountId: tr.fromId,
          ...baseMeta,
          ...pickStamps(oldOut),
          transferRole: 'out',
        };
        // 建 in 紀錄(保留舊 in 的已刪烙印)
        const inTxn = {
          id: 'ti_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
          type: 'income',
          amount: tr.amount,
          date: tr.date,
          note: tr.note || '[帳戶轉帳]',
          category: '轉帳',
          subCategory: '',
          accountId: tr.toId,
          ...baseMeta,
          ...pickStamps(oldIn),
          transferRole: 'in',
        };
        const newTxns = [...kept, outTxn, inTxn];
        // 手續費(選填,從來源帳戶額外扣)
        if (tr.fee > 0) {
          newTxns.push({
            id: 'tf_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
            type: 'expense',
            amount: tr.fee,
            date: tr.date,
            note: '轉帳手續費',
            category: tr.feeCategory || '手續費用',
            subCategory: tr.feeSubCategory || '轉帳（手續費）',
            accountId: tr.fromId,
            ...baseMeta,
            ...pickStamps(oldFee),
            transferRole: 'fee',
          });
        }
        return { ...s, transactions: newTxns };
      }

      // 代墊:存一組 2 筆關聯紀錄(lend_out/lend_in),共用 lendId
      if (txn._lend) {
        const ld = txn._lend;
        const group = ld.lendId || ('ld_' + uid().slice(2, 10));
        const baseMeta = {
          lendId: group,
          createdAt: ld.createdAt || Date.now(),
        };
        // 確保「代墊暫存」帳戶存在
        const bucket = getLendBucketAccount(s.accounts);
        if (!bucket) {
          // 不應該發生(useEffect 啟動時會建),保險起見
          return s;
        }
        // 先移除這組舊紀錄
        let kept = s.transactions.filter((t) => t.lendId !== group);
        // lendMeta 只放在 out 上,串連狀態
        const lendMeta = {
          expectDate: ld.expectDate || '',
          debtor: ld.debtor || '',
          status: 'pending',  // pending / collected / partial
          collectedAmount: 0,
        };
        // 編輯時保留原有 collected 狀態
        const oldOut = s.transactions.find((t) => t.lendId === group && t.transferRole === 'lend_out');
        if (oldOut && oldOut.lendMeta) {
          lendMeta.status = oldOut.lendMeta.status || 'pending';
          lendMeta.collectedAmount = oldOut.lendMeta.collectedAmount || 0;
        }
        const lendOut = {
          id: 'lo_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
          type: 'expense',
          amount: ld.amount,
          date: ld.date,
          note: ld.note || '[代墊]',
          category: '代墊',
          subCategory: '',
          accountId: ld.fromId,
          ...baseMeta,
          transferRole: 'lend_out',
          lendMeta,
        };
        const lendIn = {
          id: 'li_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
          type: 'income',
          amount: ld.amount,
          date: ld.date,
          note: ld.note || '[代墊]',
          category: '代墊',
          subCategory: '',
          accountId: bucket.id,
          ...baseMeta,
          transferRole: 'lend_in',
        };
        return { ...s, transactions: [...kept, lendOut, lendIn] };
      }

      const idx = s.transactions.findIndex((t) => t.id === txn.id);
      const newTxns = idx >= 0 ? s.transactions.map((t) => (t.id === txn.id ? txn : t)) : [...s.transactions, txn];
      return { ...s, transactions: newTxns };
    });
    setSheet(null);
    setEditingTxn(null);

    // 編輯模式:依是否有變更顯示不同訊息
    if (isEditing) {
      if (isUnchanged) {
        toastRich({
          title: '未變更',
          amount: null,
          lines: [],
        }, 700);
      } else {
        // 更新時也顯示詳細(用徽章模式,與「已刪除紀錄」同款)
        let amount, lines, titleSuffix, badgeColor;
        if (txn._transfer) {
          const tr = txn._transfer;
          const fromName = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === tr.fromId)?.name || '';
          const toName = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === tr.toId)?.name || '';
          amount = fmt(tr.amount);
          lines = [amount, `${fromName} → ${toName}`, tr.fee > 0 ? `含手續費 ${fmt(tr.fee)}` : null].filter(Boolean);
          titleSuffix = '轉帳';
          badgeColor = 'var(--mint)';
        } else {
          const isInc = txn.type === 'income';
          const sign = isInc ? '+' : '-';
          const cat = txn.category || '';
          const subCat = txn.subCategory || '';
          const acctName = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === txn.accountId)?.name || '';
          amount = `${sign}${fmt(txn.amount)}`;
          lines = [amount, subCat ? `${cat} › ${subCat}` : cat, acctName].filter(Boolean);
          titleSuffix = isInc ? '收入' : '支出';
          badgeColor = 'var(--mint)';  // 成功徽章一律綠色
        }
        toastRich({
          title: txn._transfer ? '轉帳已更新' : `已更新${titleSuffix}`,
          amount: '✓',
          amountColor: badgeColor,
          lines,
        }, 1800);
      }
      return;
    }

    // 新增模式：顯示詳細資訊(徽章版型)
    if (txn._transfer) {
      const tr = txn._transfer;
      const fromName = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === tr.fromId)?.name || '';
      const toName = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === tr.toId)?.name || '';
      toastRich({
        title: '已新增轉帳',
        amount: '✓',
        amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
        lines: [
          fmt(tr.amount),
          `${fromName} → ${toName}`,
          tr.fee > 0 ? `含手續費 ${fmt(tr.fee)}` : null,
        ].filter(Boolean),
      }, 1800);
    } else {
      const isInc = txn.type === 'income';
      const sign = isInc ? '+' : '-';
      const cat = txn.category || '';
      const subCat = txn.subCategory || '';
      const acctName = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === txn.accountId)?.name || '';
      toastRich({
        title: `已新增${isInc ? '收入' : '支出'}`,
        amount: '✓',
        amountColor: isInc ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--pink)',
        lines: [
          `${sign}${fmt(txn.amount)}`,
          subCat ? `${cat} › ${subCat}` : cat,
          acctName,
        ].filter(Boolean),
      }, 1800);
    }
  };

  const deleteTxn = (id) => {
    const target = state.transactions.find((t) => t.id === id);
    const isTransfer = target && target.transferId;
    const isSettle = target && target.settleId && !isTransfer;

    if (isSettle) {
      // 股票結算:同 settleId 的所有紀錄整組刪
      const group = state.transactions.filter((t) => t.settleId === target.settleId);
      const actuallyDeleteIds = new Set(group.map((t) => t.id));
      const selectedIds = new Set([target.id]);
      const listText = buildBatchDeletePreview(state.transactions, selectedIds, actuallyDeleteIds);
      setConfirmDialog({
        title: '刪除股票結算',
        target: { label: '將刪除', name: listText, multiline: true },
        message: '本金歸還與損益屬同一組,將一併刪除。',
        warning: '此操作無法復原',
        confirmText: '全部刪除',
        danger: true,
        onConfirm: () => {
          setState((s) => syncTradesAfterTxnDelete(s, s.transactions.filter((t) => t.settleId !== target.settleId)));
          setSheet(null);
          setEditingTxn(null);
          toastRich({
            title: '已刪除股票結算',
            amount: '✓',
            amountColor: 'var(--pink-text)',
            lines: [`共移除 ${group.length} 筆關聯紀錄`],
          }, 2000);
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    if (isTransfer) {
      // 找到同組所有紀錄
      const group = state.transactions.filter((t) => t.transferId === target.transferId);
      // 偵測:這個轉帳組是不是某個股票買進?(group 中任一筆有 tradeId)
      const linkedTradeId = group.find((t) => t.tradeId)?.tradeId;
      const linkedTrade = linkedTradeId && state.trades.find((tr) => tr.id === linkedTradeId);
      const isStockBuy = !!(linkedTrade && linkedTrade.type === 'buy');
      // 算 actuallyDeleteIds:同組轉帳兩端 + 股票買進 cascade(若是)
      const actuallyDeleteIds = new Set(group.map((t) => t.id));
      const cascadeIds = expandStockBuyCascade(state, actuallyDeleteIds);
      for (const id of cascadeIds) actuallyDeleteIds.add(id);
      const selectedIds = new Set([target.id]); // 主動操作的:就是被點的這筆
      const listText = buildBatchDeletePreview(state.transactions, selectedIds, actuallyDeleteIds);
      // message:轉帳兩端是同組;若是股票買進加警告
      let linkMsg = '轉帳兩端紀錄屬同一組,將一併刪除。';
      const stockImpact = detectStockBuyImpact(state, actuallyDeleteIds);
      if (stockImpact.msg) {
        linkMsg += '\n\n' + stockImpact.msg;
      }
      setConfirmDialog({
        title: stockImpact.anyHoldingDestroyed || isStockBuy ? '刪除股票買進' : '刪除轉帳紀錄',
        target: { label: '將刪除', name: listText, multiline: true },
        message: linkMsg,
        warning: '此操作無法復原',
        confirmText: stockImpact.anyHoldingDestroyed ? '仍要刪除持股' : '全部刪除',
        highlightWords: stockImpact.highlightWords,
        danger: true,
        onConfirm: () => {
          setState((s) => syncTradesAfterTxnDelete(s, s.transactions.filter((t) => t.transferId !== target.transferId)));
          setSheet(null);
          setEditingTxn(null);
          // 轉帳包含多筆,用大 toast 顯示金額
          const outTxn = group.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'out');
          const inTxn = group.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'in');
          const nameOf = (txn) => {
            if (!txn) return '';
            const acct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === txn.accountId);
            if (acct) return acctDisplayNameStr(acct);
            if (txn._deletedAccountName) return `${txn._deletedAccountName}(已刪)`;
            return '';
          };
          const fromName = nameOf(outTxn);
          const toName = nameOf(inTxn);
          toastRich({
            title: '已刪除轉帳',
            amount: '✓',
            amountColor: 'var(--pink-text)',
            lines: [
              outTxn ? `金額:${outTxn.amount.toLocaleString()}` : null,
              fromName && toName ? `${fromName} → ${toName}` : null,
              `共移除 ${group.length} 筆關聯紀錄`,
            ].filter(Boolean),
          }, 2400);
        },
      });
      return;
    }

    // 構造刪除明細(用 items 結構顯示刪除線視覺)
    const isInc = target.type === 'income';
    const sign = isInc ? '+' : '-';
    const catText = target.subCategory ? `${target.category} › ${target.subCategory}` : (target.category || '');
    const liveAcct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === target.accountId);
    const isDeletedAcct = !liveAcct && !!target._deletedAccountName;
    const acctName = liveAcct?.name || target._deletedAccountName || '';
    const items = [
      {
        icon: isInc ? 'coin' : 'card',
        type: 'remove',
        label: '金額',
        detail: `${sign}${target.amount.toLocaleString()}`,
        // 已刪帳戶的紀錄:加說明告訴使用者只動統計、不動總資產
        sublabel: isDeletedAcct ? '僅影響收支統計,不影響總資產' : undefined,
      },
    ];
    if (catText) {
      items.push({ icon: 'tag', type: 'remove', label: '分類', detail: catText });
    }
    if (acctName) {
      items.push({
        icon: 'box',
        type: 'remove',
        label: '帳戶',
        detail: isDeletedAcct ? `${acctName}(帳號已刪)` : acctName,
      });
    }
    if (target.note && target.note.trim()) {
      items.push({ icon: 'note', type: 'remove', label: '備註', detail: target.note });
    }

    setConfirmDialog({
      title: '刪除紀錄',
      itemsHint: '以下內容將被移除:',
      items,
      message: '此動作無法復原。',
      confirmText: '刪除',
      danger: true,
      onConfirm: () => {
        setState((s) => syncTradesAfterTxnDelete(s, s.transactions.filter((t) => t.id !== id)));
        setSheet(null);
        setEditingTxn(null);
        // 刪除後顯示交易資訊
        if (target) {
          toastRich({
            title: '已刪除紀錄',
            amount: '✓',
            amountColor: 'var(--pink-text)',
            lines: [
              `${sign}${target.amount.toLocaleString()}`,
              catText || null,
              acctName || null,
            ].filter(Boolean),
          }, 2200);
        } else {
          toast('已刪除');
        }
      },
    });
  };

  // 代墊收回:從「代墊暫存」轉到指定帳戶,並更新 lendOut.lendMeta
  // amount = 收回金額,toAccountId = 收回到的真實帳戶
  const collectLend = (lendOut, amount, toAccountId) => {
    if (!lendOut || !lendOut.lendId) return;
    const bucket = getLendBucketAccount(state.accounts);
    if (!bucket) { toast('找不到代墊暫存帳戶'); return; }

    setState((s) => {
      const today = todayStr();
      const collectId = 'lc_' + uid().slice(2, 10);
      const baseMeta = {
        lendId: lendOut.lendId,
        createdAt: Date.now(),
      };
      const collectOut = {
        id: 'lco_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
        type: 'expense',
        amount,
        date: today,
        note: '代墊收回',
        category: '代墊',
        subCategory: '',
        accountId: bucket.id,
        ...baseMeta,
        transferRole: 'lend_collect_out',
      };
      const collectIn = {
        id: 'lci_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
        type: 'income',
        amount,
        date: today,
        note: '代墊收回',
        category: '代墊',
        subCategory: '',
        accountId: toAccountId,
        ...baseMeta,
        transferRole: 'lend_collect_in',
      };
      // 更新原 lendOut 的 lendMeta
      const newTxns = s.transactions.map((t) => {
        if (t.id === lendOut.id) {
          const newCollected = (t.lendMeta?.collectedAmount || 0) + amount;
          const newStatus = newCollected >= t.amount ? 'collected' : 'partial';
          return {
            ...t,
            lendMeta: {
              ...t.lendMeta,
              collectedAmount: newCollected,
              status: newStatus,
            },
          };
        }
        return t;
      });
      return { ...s, transactions: [...newTxns, collectOut, collectIn] };
    });

    const acct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === toAccountId);
    const isFullCollect = amount >= (lendOut.amount - (lendOut.lendMeta?.collectedAmount || 0));
    toastRich && toastRich({
      title: isFullCollect ? '已全額收回' : '已部分收回',
      amount: '✓',
      amountColor: 'var(--mint-text)',
      lines: [
        `收回 ${fmt(amount)} 到「${acct?.name || ''}」`,
        ...(isFullCollect ? ['代墊完成,將從首頁提醒中移除'] : [`仍有 ${fmt(lendOut.amount - (lendOut.lendMeta?.collectedAmount || 0) - amount)} 未收回`]),
      ],
    }, 2200);
  };

  // 刪除代墊:移除整組(lend_out + lend_in + 所有 lend_collect_*)
  const deleteLend = (lendOut) => {
    if (!lendOut || !lendOut.lendId) return;
    setState((s) => syncTradesAfterTxnDelete(s, s.transactions.filter((t) => t.lendId !== lendOut.lendId)));
    toastRich && toastRich({
      title: '已刪除代墊',
      amount: '✓',
      amountColor: 'var(--pink-text)',
      lines: [`金額 ${fmt(lendOut.amount)} 及所有相關紀錄已移除`],
    }, 1800);
  };

  // 股票結算(賣出):一次產生多筆紀錄
  // payload: { fromId, toId, principal, received, date, note, pnlCategory, pnlSubCategory }
  // - principal:本金(投入金額)
  // - received:實際拿回金額
  // - 損益 = received - principal
  // 紀錄拆解:
  //   1. settle_out:從投資帳戶扣 principal(本金歸還,不算統計)
  //   2. settle_in:進收款帳戶 principal(本金歸還,不算統計)
  //   3a. 若獲利 (received > principal):settle_pnl_in 進收款帳戶 (received-principal)(真實收入)
  //   3b. 若虧損 (received < principal):settle_pnl_out 從收款帳戶扣 (principal-received)(真實支出)
  //   3c. 若打平:不產生損益紀錄
  // 淨效果:投資 -principal,收款 +received(=principal±損益)
  // ============ 買進股票 ============
  // payload: { accountId, symbol, name?, currency?, shares, totalCost, fee, fromAccountId, date, note? }
  // 流程:
  //   1. 找/建 Holding(同 accountId + symbol 視為同一個)
  //   2. 新增 Trade(type='buy',記下原始 shares 跟 remainingShares,FIFO 用)
  //   3. 主帳本:fromAccount → investAccount 轉帳(總額 = totalCost + fee)
  //   4. 烙印 linkedTxnId 連結 Trade 跟主帳本紀錄
  // 註:totalCost 是「股票本身的金額」(不含手續費),fee 另算
  const saveBuyHolding = (p) => {
    if (!p || !p.accountId || !p.symbol || !p.shares || !p.totalCost || !p.fromAccountId) {
      toast && toast('參數不完整,無法儲存');
      return;
    }
    const shares = Number(p.shares);
    const totalCost = Number(p.totalCost);
    const fee = Number(p.fee) || 0;
    const grandTotal = totalCost + fee; // 從支出帳戶扣的總額
    const symbol = String(p.symbol).trim().toUpperCase();
    const name = (p.name || '').trim();
    const currency = p.currency || 'TWD';
    const date = p.date || todayStr();
    const note = (p.note || '').trim();

    setState((s) => {
      // 預設市值:使用者有填用使用者的;沒填用買進金額(totalCost,不含 fee)
      const defaultMarketValue = (p.marketValue !== undefined && p.marketValue !== null && p.marketValue > 0)
        ? Number(p.marketValue)
        : totalCost;

      // 找或建 Holding
      let holding = s.holdings.find((h) => h.accountId === p.accountId && h.symbol === symbol);
      let newHoldings = s.holdings;
      if (!holding) {
        // 新建持股 → 用 defaultMarketValue 當初始市值
        holding = {
          id: 'h_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
          accountId: p.accountId,
          symbol,
          name,
          currency,
          marketValue: defaultMarketValue,
          marketValueUpdatedAt: Date.now(),
          notes: '',
          createdAt: Date.now(),
        };
        newHoldings = [...s.holdings, holding];
      } else {
        // 既有持股加買:
        //   - 如果使用者「明確填了市值」→ 覆寫
        //   - 沒填 → 把這筆買進金額加到既有市值上(假設市場價沒變,新買進股票按帳面價計入)
        const userProvidedMV = (p.marketValue !== undefined && p.marketValue !== null && p.marketValue > 0);
        const newMV = userProvidedMV
          ? Number(p.marketValue)
          : (holding.marketValue || 0) + totalCost;
        newHoldings = s.holdings.map((h) => h.id === holding.id ? {
          ...h,
          marketValue: newMV,
          marketValueUpdatedAt: Date.now(),
          name: name && !h.name ? name : h.name, // 若這次補了名字,寫入
        } : h);
      }

      // 新增 Trade
      const tradeId = 'tr_' + uid().slice(2, 10);
      const newTrade = {
        id: tradeId,
        holdingId: holding.id,
        type: 'buy',
        date,
        shares,
        totalCost: totalCost + fee, // 把手續費算進成本(會反映在 FIFO 計算)
        fee,
        remainingShares: shares, // FIFO 用,初始 = shares
        note,
        createdAt: Date.now(),
      };

      // 主帳本:轉帳兩筆(支出帳戶 expense + 投資帳戶 income)
      const transferId = 'bt_' + uid().slice(2, 10);
      const baseMeta = { transferId, createdAt: Date.now(), tradeId };
      const outTxn = {
        id: 'bo_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
        type: 'expense',
        amount: grandTotal,
        date,
        note: `[買進 ${symbol}]${note ? ' ' + note : ''}`,
        category: '轉帳',
        subCategory: '',
        accountId: p.fromAccountId,
        ...baseMeta,
        transferRole: 'out',
      };
      const inTxn = {
        id: 'bi_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
        type: 'income',
        amount: grandTotal,
        date,
        note: `[買進 ${symbol}]${note ? ' ' + note : ''}`,
        category: '轉帳',
        subCategory: '',
        accountId: p.accountId,
        ...baseMeta,
        transferRole: 'in',
      };

      // 把 linkedTxnId 寫回 trade
      newTrade.linkedTxnId = inTxn.id;

      return {
        ...s,
        holdings: newHoldings,
        trades: [...s.trades, newTrade],
        transactions: [...s.transactions, outTxn, inTxn],
      };
    });
  };

  // ============ 賣出股票(走 FIFO) ============
  // payload: { holdingId, shares, totalReceived, fee, tax, toAccountId, date, note? }
  // 流程:
  //   1. FIFO 配對 → 算 matchedCost(對應的買進成本)
  //   2. 算實現損益 = totalReceived - matchedCost - fee - tax
  //   3. 新增 Trade(type='sell',記 matchedCost、realizedPnl)
  //   4. 更新對應 buy 批次的 remainingShares
  //   5. 主帳本:用 settle 機制(settle_out/settle_in/settle_pnl_in_out)
  //      - 投資帳戶 -matchedCost(本金歸還)
  //      - 收款帳戶 +matchedCost(本金歸還)
  //      - 收款帳戶 ±損益(實現損益)
  //      - 收款帳戶 -fee -tax(手續費跟交易稅,真實支出)
  const saveSellHolding = (p) => {
    if (!p || !p.holdingId || !p.shares || !p.totalReceived || !p.toAccountId) {
      toast && toast('參數不完整,無法儲存');
      return;
    }
    const sellShares = Number(p.shares);
    const totalReceived = Number(p.totalReceived);
    const fee = Number(p.fee) || 0;
    const tax = Number(p.tax) || 0;
    const date = p.date || todayStr();
    const note = (p.note || '').trim();

    // 配對前先檢查
    const holding = state.holdings.find((h) => h.id === p.holdingId);
    if (!holding) { toast && toast('找不到持股'); return; }
    const currentShares = holdingShares(holding, state.trades);
    if (sellShares > currentShares) {
      toast && toast(`賣出股數不能超過持有股數(${currentShares})`);
      return;
    }

    const match = avgCostMatch(p.holdingId, sellShares, state.trades, state.holdings);
    const matchedCost = match.matchedCost;
    const netReceived = totalReceived - fee - tax; // 扣掉手續費跟稅後實際拿回
    const realizedPnl = netReceived - matchedCost; // 實現損益(已扣手續費跟稅)

    setState((s) => {
      // 找賣出前的 holding marketValue,存進 trade 以便日後刪除時還原
      const targetHolding = s.holdings.find((h) => h.id === p.holdingId);
      const marketValueBefore = targetHolding?.marketValue || 0;

      // 新增 sell trade(不需要更新 buy 批次的 remainingShares,因為平均成本制不靠 batch tracking)
      const sellTradeId = 'tr_' + uid().slice(2, 10);
      const sellTrade = {
        id: sellTradeId,
        holdingId: p.holdingId,
        type: 'sell',
        date,
        shares: sellShares,
        totalReceived,
        fee,
        tax,
        matchedCost,
        realizedPnl,
        marketValueBefore, // 記住賣出前的市值,刪除這筆時用於還原
        note,
        createdAt: Date.now(),
      };

      // 主帳本:用 settle 機制
      const settleId = 'st_' + uid().slice(2, 10);
      const baseMeta = { settleId, createdAt: Date.now(), tradeId: sellTradeId };
      const newTxns = [];

      // 1. settle_out:投資帳戶歸還 matchedCost
      newTxns.push({
        id: 'so_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
        type: 'expense',
        amount: matchedCost,
        date,
        note: `[賣出 ${holding.symbol} - 本金]${note ? ' ' + note : ''}`,
        category: '股票結算',
        subCategory: '本金歸還',
        accountId: holding.accountId,
        ...baseMeta,
        transferRole: 'settle_out',
      });
      // 2. settle_in:收款帳戶 +matchedCost
      newTxns.push({
        id: 'si_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
        type: 'income',
        amount: matchedCost,
        date,
        note: `[賣出 ${holding.symbol} - 本金]${note ? ' ' + note : ''}`,
        category: '股票結算',
        subCategory: '本金歸還',
        accountId: p.toAccountId,
        ...baseMeta,
        transferRole: 'settle_in',
      });
      // 3. 損益(已含 fee/tax)
      if (realizedPnl > 0) {
        newTxns.push({
          id: 'sp_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
          type: 'income',
          amount: realizedPnl,
          date,
          note: `[賣出 ${holding.symbol} - 獲利]${note ? ' ' + note : ''}`,
          category: '股票相關',
          subCategory: '獲利了結',
          accountId: p.toAccountId,
          ...baseMeta,
          transferRole: 'settle_pnl_in',
        });
      } else if (realizedPnl < 0) {
        newTxns.push({
          id: 'sl_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
          type: 'expense',
          amount: -realizedPnl,
          date,
          note: `[賣出 ${holding.symbol} - 虧損]${note ? ' ' + note : ''}`,
          category: '投資失利',
          subCategory: '',
          accountId: p.toAccountId,
          ...baseMeta,
          transferRole: 'settle_pnl_out',
        });
      }
      // 註:fee 跟 tax 已併入 realizedPnl 內,不再另記

      // 賣出後調整 marketValue:
      // - 全賣完 → 歸 0
      // - 部分賣出 → 按剩餘股數比例調整(假設市場價格不變)
      let newHoldings = s.holdings;
      const newRemainingShares = currentShares - sellShares;
      if (newRemainingShares === 0) {
        newHoldings = s.holdings.map((h) => h.id === p.holdingId ? { ...h, marketValue: 0 } : h);
      } else if (currentShares > 0) {
        const ratio = newRemainingShares / currentShares;
        newHoldings = s.holdings.map((h) => {
          if (h.id !== p.holdingId) return h;
          const newMv = Math.round((h.marketValue || 0) * ratio);
          return { ...h, marketValue: newMv };
        });
      }

      return {
        ...s,
        trades: [...s.trades, sellTrade],
        transactions: [...s.transactions, ...newTxns],
        holdings: newHoldings,
      };
    });
  };

  // ============ 更新 holding 市值 ============
  const updateHoldingMarketValue = (holdingId, marketValue) => {
    const mv = Number(marketValue) || 0;
    setState((s) => ({
      ...s,
      holdings: s.holdings.map((h) =>
        h.id === holdingId ? { ...h, marketValue: mv, marketValueUpdatedAt: Date.now() } : h
      ),
    }));
  };

  // ============ 刪除 Trade(連動刪除主帳本紀錄) ============
  // 1. 找出這筆 Trade
  // 2. 刪除主帳本上 tradeId 標記為這筆 Trade 的所有紀錄
  // 3. 從 trades 陣列移除
  // 4. 如果該 Holding 沒有任何 Trade 了 → 一併移除 Holding
  const deleteTrade = (tradeId) => {
    setState((s) => {
      const t = s.trades.find((tr) => tr.id === tradeId);
      if (!t) return s;
      const holdingId = t.holdingId;
      // 刪主帳本上對應的紀錄(透過 tradeId 烙印關聯)
      const newTxns = s.transactions.filter((tx) => tx.tradeId !== tradeId);
      const newTrades = s.trades.filter((tr) => tr.id !== tradeId);
      // 該 Holding 還有沒有其他 trade?沒有就一起刪
      const remainingForHolding = newTrades.filter((tr) => tr.holdingId === holdingId);
      let newHoldings;
      if (remainingForHolding.length === 0) {
        newHoldings = s.holdings.filter((h) => h.id !== holdingId);
      } else if (t.type === 'sell' && typeof t.marketValueBefore === 'number') {
        // 刪除 sell trade:還原 marketValue 到賣出前的值
        newHoldings = s.holdings.map((h) =>
          h.id === holdingId
            ? { ...h, marketValue: t.marketValueBefore, marketValueUpdatedAt: Date.now() }
            : h
        );
      } else {
        newHoldings = s.holdings;
      }
      return { ...s, transactions: newTxns, trades: newTrades, holdings: newHoldings };
    });
  };

  // ============ 刪 transactions 時自動連動 Trade / Holding ============
  // 給定刪除後的 transactions 陣列(已經 filter 過),回傳同步調整 trades/holdings 後的新 state
  // 偵測:被刪掉的紀錄如果有 tradeId,且這個 tradeId 在新 transactions 中找不到 → 連動清理
  const syncTradesAfterTxnDelete = (s, newTransactions) => {
    const oldTxnIds = new Set(s.transactions.map((t) => t.id));
    const newTxnIds = new Set(newTransactions.map((t) => t.id));
