    // 找出被刪掉的紀錄中,帶 tradeId 的
    const orphanedTradeIds = new Set();
    for (const t of s.transactions) {
      if (oldTxnIds.has(t.id) && !newTxnIds.has(t.id) && t.tradeId) {
        // 這個 tradeId 是否還有其他 txn 綁著(避免一筆 trade 多筆 txn,只刪一筆就誤判)
        const stillHasOther = newTransactions.some((tx) => tx.tradeId === t.tradeId);
        if (!stillHasOther) orphanedTradeIds.add(t.tradeId);
      }
    }
    if (orphanedTradeIds.size === 0) {
      return { ...s, transactions: newTransactions };
    }
    // 找出要被刪的 trade 中,sell 類型且帶 marketValueBefore 的(用於還原 holding 市值)
    const restoreMap = new Map(); // holdingId -> marketValueBefore (取最新一筆即可)
    const sortedDeletedSells = s.trades
      .filter((tr) => orphanedTradeIds.has(tr.id) && tr.type === 'sell' && typeof tr.marketValueBefore === 'number')
      .sort((a, b) => (a.createdAt || 0) - (b.createdAt || 0));
    for (const tr of sortedDeletedSells) {
      // 取最早被刪的賣出,這樣還原到「最遠的賣出之前」(最完整還原)
      if (!restoreMap.has(tr.holdingId)) {
        restoreMap.set(tr.holdingId, tr.marketValueBefore);
      }
    }

    // 移除孤兒 trades(第一輪:由被刪 transactions 直接推導出的孤兒)
    const affectedHoldingIds = new Set();
    for (const tr of s.trades) {
      if (orphanedTradeIds.has(tr.id)) affectedHoldingIds.add(tr.holdingId);
    }
    let newTrades = s.trades.filter((tr) => !orphanedTradeIds.has(tr.id));

    // ============ 第二輪:buy trade 被刪導致 holding 失去所有買進來源 ============
    // 連動清理:該 holding 殘存的所有 sell trade + 它們對應的 settle 結算紀錄
    // 邏輯:如果一個 holding 沒有任何 buy 來源了,殘存的 sell 紀錄會造成帳目不平
    //      (例如投資帳戶會剩下「結算扣款」但沒有「買進進款」)
    const buyOrphans = s.trades.filter((tr) => orphanedTradeIds.has(tr.id) && tr.type === 'buy');
    const cascadeSellIds = new Set();
    for (const buyTr of buyOrphans) {
      const hId = buyTr.holdingId;
      // 該 holding 在 newTrades 中是否還有 buy?
      const stillHasBuy = newTrades.some((tr) => tr.holdingId === hId && tr.type === 'buy');
      if (stillHasBuy) continue;
      // 沒有了 → 該 holding 的所有 sell 都要連帶刪
      for (const tr of newTrades) {
        if (tr.holdingId === hId && tr.type === 'sell') {
          cascadeSellIds.add(tr.id);
          affectedHoldingIds.add(hId);
        }
      }
    }

    if (cascadeSellIds.size > 0) {
      // 從 newTrades 拿掉這些 sell
      newTrades = newTrades.filter((tr) => !cascadeSellIds.has(tr.id));
      // 從 newTransactions 拿掉所有帶這些 tradeId 的紀錄(settle_out / settle_in / settle_pnl_*)
      newTransactions = newTransactions.filter((tx) => !tx.tradeId || !cascadeSellIds.has(tx.tradeId));
      // 同時把連動刪的 sell 從 restoreMap 移除(對應 holding 整個要被刪了,還原市值沒意義)
      for (const sellId of cascadeSellIds) {
        const tr = s.trades.find((x) => x.id === sellId);
        if (tr) restoreMap.delete(tr.holdingId);
      }
    }

    // 對受影響的 holding,如果沒有任何 trade 了,連同 holding 一起刪;
    // 還在的 holding,如果有 marketValue 還原資料,套用還原
    const newHoldings = s.holdings
      .filter((h) => {
        if (!affectedHoldingIds.has(h.id)) return true;
        return newTrades.some((tr) => tr.holdingId === h.id);
      })
      .map((h) => {
        if (restoreMap.has(h.id)) {
          return { ...h, marketValue: restoreMap.get(h.id), marketValueUpdatedAt: Date.now() };
        }
        return h;
      });
    return { ...s, transactions: newTransactions, trades: newTrades, holdings: newHoldings };
  };

  // 包裝過的 setState:子元件用這個取代 setState 來刪 transactions,自動連動 trades/holdings
  const setStateWithSync = React.useCallback((updater) => {
    setState((s) => {
      const result = typeof updater === 'function' ? updater(s) : updater;
      // 如果 result 包含 transactions 異動,跑 sync 邏輯
      if (result && result.transactions && result.transactions !== s.transactions) {
        return syncTradesAfterTxnDelete(s, result.transactions);
      }
      return result;
    });
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, []);

  // ============ 舊版股票結算(保留,不再從新 UI 觸發) ============
  // payload: { fromId, toId, principal, received, date, note, pnlCategory, pnlSubCategory }
  const saveSettlement = (p) => {
    if (!p || !p.fromId || !p.toId || !p.principal) {
      toast && toast('參數不完整,無法儲存');
      return;
    }
    const principal = Number(p.principal);
    const received = Number(p.received);
    const pnl = received - principal;  // > 0 獲利,< 0 虧損,= 0 打平
    const settleId = 'st_' + uid().slice(2, 10);
    const baseMeta = {
      settleId,
      createdAt: Date.now(),
    };
    const newTxns = [];
    // 1. settle_out 本金從投資帳戶歸還
    newTxns.push({
      id: 'so_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
      type: 'expense',
      amount: principal,
      date: p.date,
      note: p.note || '[股票賣出 - 本金]',
      category: '股票結算',
      subCategory: '本金歸還',
      accountId: p.fromId,
      ...baseMeta,
      transferRole: 'settle_out',
    });
    // 2. settle_in 本金進收款帳戶
    newTxns.push({
      id: 'si_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
      type: 'income',
      amount: principal,
      date: p.date,
      note: p.note || '[股票賣出 - 本金]',
      category: '股票結算',
      subCategory: '本金歸還',
      accountId: p.toId,
      ...baseMeta,
      transferRole: 'settle_in',
    });
    // 3. 損益部分
    if (pnl > 0) {
      newTxns.push({
        id: 'sp_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
        type: 'income',
        amount: pnl,
        date: p.date,
        note: p.note ? `${p.note}(獲利)` : '股票賣出獲利',
        category: p.pnlCategory || '股票相關',
        subCategory: p.pnlSubCategory || '獲利了結',
        accountId: p.toId,
        ...baseMeta,
        transferRole: 'settle_pnl_in',
      });
    } else if (pnl < 0) {
      newTxns.push({
        id: 'sl_' + uid().slice(2, 10),
        type: 'expense',
        amount: -pnl,
        date: p.date,
        note: p.note ? `${p.note}(虧損)` : '股票賣出虧損',
        category: p.pnlCategory || '投資失利',
        subCategory: p.pnlSubCategory || '',
        accountId: p.toId,
        ...baseMeta,
        transferRole: 'settle_pnl_out',
      });
    }
    setState((s) => ({ ...s, transactions: [...s.transactions, ...newTxns] }));

    // toast 提示
    const fromName = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === p.fromId)?.name || '';
    const toName = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === p.toId)?.name || '';
    if (toastRich) {
      const lines = [
        `${fromName} → ${toName}`,
        `本金 ${fmt(principal)} · 拿回 ${fmt(received)}`,
      ];
      if (pnl > 0) lines.push(`獲利 +${fmt(pnl)}`);
      else if (pnl < 0) lines.push(`虧損 -${fmt(-pnl)}`);
      else lines.push('損益打平');
      toastRich({
        title: '已記錄股票賣出',
        amount: '✓',
        amountColor: pnl >= 0 ? 'var(--mint-text)' : 'var(--pink-text)',
        lines,
      }, 2400);
    }
  };

  const doReset = () => {
    setConfirmDialog({
      title: '清除所有資料',
      confirmText: '清除',
      danger: true,
      items: [
        { type: 'remove', icon: 'note', label: '移除', detail: '所有交易紀錄' },
        { type: 'remove', icon: 'bank', label: '移除', detail: '所有帳戶', resetTo: '恢復預設' },
        { type: 'remove', icon: 'bag', label: '移除', detail: '所有分類', resetTo: '恢復預設' },
        { type: 'keep', icon: 'clipboard', label: '保留', detail: '快照備份' },
        { type: 'keep', icon: 'gear', label: '保留', detail: '介面排序' },
      ],
      itemsFooter: '此動作無法復原',
      onConfirm: () => {
        // 記錄清除前的數量(拿來展示在 toast)
        const prevTxnCount = state.transactions.length;
        const prevAcctCount = state.accounts.length;
        storageClear();
        setState({
          transactions: [],
          accounts: [...DEFAULT_ACCOUNTS],
          categories: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(DEFAULT_CATEGORIES)),
          accountTypes: [...DEFAULT_ACCOUNT_TYPES],
        });
        toastRich({
          title: '已清除所有資料',
          amount: '✓',
          amountColor: 'var(--pink-text)',
          lines: [
            `已移除 ${prevTxnCount} 筆交易、${prevAcctCount} 個帳戶`,
            '帳戶 / 分類已重置為預設',
            '快照備份與介面排序已保留',
          ],
        }, 2800);
      },
    });
  };

  // 清理歷史紀錄:移除指定日期前的交易
  // cutoffDate = 'YYYY-MM-DD',移除所有 date < cutoffDate 的交易
  // preserveBalance = true 時,把被清除的金額轉為帳戶的起始餘額(openingBalance)
  const doCleanupHistory = (cutoffDate, preserveBalance) => {
    const oldTxns = state.transactions.filter((t) => t.date < cutoffDate);
    const keepTxns = state.transactions.filter((t) => t.date >= cutoffDate);
    if (oldTxns.length === 0) {
      toast('沒有早於該日期的資料可清理');
      return;
    }

    let newAccounts = state.accounts;
    if (preserveBalance) {
      // 計算每個帳戶在 cutoffDate 前的淨額(轉帳 out/in/fee 都已存為 expense/income/expense,直接用 type 即可)
      const deltaByAcct = new Map();
      for (const t of oldTxns) {
        if (!t.accountId) continue;
        const cur = deltaByAcct.get(t.accountId) || 0;
        if (t.type === 'income') deltaByAcct.set(t.accountId, cur + t.amount);
        else if (t.type === 'expense') deltaByAcct.set(t.accountId, cur - t.amount);
      }
      // 套用到每個帳戶的 initAmount
      newAccounts = state.accounts.map((a) => {
        const delta = deltaByAcct.get(a.id) || 0;
        if (delta === 0) return a;
        return { ...a, initAmount: (a.initAmount || 0) + delta };
      });
    }

    setState((s) => ({
      ...s,
      transactions: keepTxns,
      accounts: newAccounts,
    }));
    // 清理成功:用 toastRich 強化視覺
    const d = new Date(`${cutoffDate}T00:00:00`);
    const dateStr = `${d.getFullYear()}/${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}/${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}`;
    toastRich({
      title: '✓ 已清理歷史紀錄',
      amount: `${oldTxns.length} 筆`,
      amountColor: 'var(--mint-text)',
      lines: [
        `清除 ${dateStr} 之前的紀錄`,
        preserveBalance ? '帳戶餘額已保留(寫入起始餘額)' : '帳戶餘額依剩餘紀錄重新計算',
      ],
    }, 2800);
  };

  const openAddSheet = (type) => {
    setSheetType(type);
    setEditingTxn(null);
    setSheet('add');
  };

  const openEditSheet = (txn) => {
    // 代墊:只接收 lend_out,並改用 'lend' 類型
    if (txn.transferRole === 'lend_out') {
      setSheetType('lend');
    } else if (txn.transferRole === 'lend_in' || txn.transferRole === 'lend_collect_out' || txn.transferRole === 'lend_collect_in') {
      // 點到代墊的子紀錄,改成編輯主 lend_out
      const mainOut = state.transactions.find((t) => t.lendId === txn.lendId && t.transferRole === 'lend_out');
      if (mainOut) {
        // 直接打開代墊詳細頁,而不是編輯 sheet
        setLendDetail(mainOut);
        return;
      }
      setSheetType(txn.type);
    } else if (txn.transferId && (txn.transferRole === 'out' || txn.transferRole === 'in' || txn.transferRole === 'fee')) {
      // 點到轉帳的子紀錄(out/in/fee):切到「轉帳模式」編輯,讓使用者看到完整的轉出/轉入兩面
      setSheetType('transfer');
      // 統一以「out」為編輯主體,讓 from/to/amount/fee 完整顯示
      const outTxn = state.transactions.find((t) => t.transferId === txn.transferId && t.transferRole === 'out');
      if (outTxn) {
        setEditingTxn(outTxn);
        setSheet('add');
        return;
      }
      setEditingTxn(txn);
      setSheet('add');
      return;
    } else if (txn.transferRole === 'settle_out' || txn.transferRole === 'settle_in' || txn.transferRole === 'settle_pnl_in' || txn.transferRole === 'settle_pnl_out') {
      // 股票結算紀錄:開唯讀詳情頁(可以看完整內容,並提供整組刪除按鈕)
      const group = state.transactions
        .filter((t) => t.settleId && t.settleId === txn.settleId)
        .sort((a, b) => {
          const order = { settle_out: 0, settle_in: 1, settle_pnl_in: 2, settle_pnl_out: 2 };
          return (order[a.transferRole] ?? 99) - (order[b.transferRole] ?? 99);
        });
      setSettleDetail(group);
      return;
    } else {
      setSheetType(txn.type);
    }
    setEditingTxn(txn);
    setSheet('add');
  };

  return (
    <div
      style={styles.root}
      onTouchStart={handleTouchStart}
      onTouchMove={handleTouchMove}
      onTouchEnd={handleTouchEnd}
      onTouchCancel={handleTouchCancel}
    >
      <Style theme={theme} />

      {/* 頁面內容 */}
      <div
        className="page-fade"
        ref={pageWrapperRef}
        style={{
          ...(swipeDragX !== 0 || isSwipeAnimating ? {
            transform: `translateX(${swipeDragX}px)`,
            transition: isSwipeAnimating ? 'transform 0.2s cubic-bezier(0.2, 0.8, 0.2, 1)' : 'none',
            willChange: 'transform',
          } : {}),
          background: 'var(--bg)',
        }}
      >
        {page === 'home' && (
          <HomePage
            state={state}
            setState={setStateWithSync}
            catIcon={catIcon}
            currentMonth={currentMonth}
            setCurrentMonth={setCurrentMonth}
            selectedDate={selectedDate}
            setSelectedDate={setSelectedDate}
            onAdd={openAddSheet}
            onClickTxn={openEditSheet}
            onViewAll={() => setPage('txn')}
            onOpenPeriod={(key) => setPeriodKey(key)}
            onOpenAccount={() => setSheet('accounts')}
            onOpenDate={(date) => setDetailDate(date)}
            onOpenLend={(lendOut) => setLendDetail(lendOut)}
            editMode={editMode}
            setEditMode={setEditMode}
            blockOrder={blockOrder.home}
            moveBlock={moveBlock('home')}
            setPageOrder={setPageOrder('home')}
            setConfirmDialog={setConfirmDialog}
            toastRich={toastRich}
            toast={toast}
            onSelectModeChange={setHomeSelectMode}
          />
        )}
        {page === 'txn' && (
          <TxnListPage
            state={state}
            setState={setStateWithSync}
            setConfirmDialog={setConfirmDialog}
            toastRich={toastRich}
            toast={toast}
            catIcon={catIcon}
            currentMonth={currentMonth}
            setCurrentMonth={setCurrentMonth}
            onClickTxn={openEditSheet}
            editMode={editMode}
            setEditMode={setEditMode}
            onSelectModeChange={setTxnSelectMode}
            blockOrder={blockOrder.txn}
            moveBlock={moveBlock('txn')}
            setPageOrder={setPageOrder('txn')}
          />
        )}
        {page === 'stats' && (
          <StatsPage
            state={state}
            catIcon={catIcon}
            currentMonth={currentMonth}
            setCurrentMonth={setCurrentMonth}
            editMode={editMode}
            setEditMode={setEditMode}
            blockOrder={blockOrder.stats}
            moveBlock={moveBlock('stats')}
            setPageOrder={setPageOrder('stats')}
            onClickTxn={openEditSheet}
            onGoToTxn={(opts) => {
              if (opts?.month) setCurrentMonth(opts.month);
              setPage('txn');
              if (opts?.category && toast) toast(`已切到明細（${opts.category}${opts.subCategory ? ' › ' + opts.subCategory : ''}）`);
            }}
          />
        )}
        {page === 'settings' && (
          <SettingsPage
            state={state}
            setState={setStateWithSync}
            toast={toast}
            toastRich={toastRich}
            onReset={doReset}
            onCleanupHistory={doCleanupHistory}
            lastBackupAt={lastBackupAt}
            setLastBackupAt={setLastBackupAt}
            backupReminderDays={backupReminderDays}
            setBackupReminderDays={setBackupReminderDays}
            driveFolderUrl={driveFolderUrl}
            setDriveFolderUrl={setDriveFolderUrl}
            setConfirmDialog={setConfirmDialog}
            editMode={editMode}
            setEditMode={setEditMode}
            onSubSheetChange={setSettingsSubSheet}
            noteColor={noteColor}
            setNoteColor={setNoteColor}
            theme={theme}
            setTheme={setTheme}
            blockOrder={blockOrder.settings}
            moveBlock={moveBlock('settings')}
            setPageOrder={setPageOrder('settings')}
          />
        )}
      </div>

      {/* 底部 nav (多選模式時隱藏,讓刪除按鈕能錨到底部) */}
      {!txnSelectMode && !homeSelectMode && !settingsSubSheet && (
      <div style={styles.bottomnav}>
        {[
          { k: 'home', icon: 'home', label: '首頁' },
          { k: 'txn', icon: 'list', label: '明細' },
          { k: 'stats', icon: 'pie', label: '統計' },
          { k: 'settings', icon: 'gear', label: '設定' },
        ].map((p) => {
          const isActive = page === p.k;
          const color = isActive ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--text-faint)';
          return (
            <div
              key={p.k}
              style={{ ...styles.navItem, color }}
              onClick={() => setPage(p.k)}
            >
              <div style={styles.navIcon}>
                <TypeIcon name={p.icon} size={22} color={color} />
              </div>
              <div>{p.label}</div>
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
      )}

      {/* Sheet 背景 */}
      {sheet && (
        <div
          style={styles.backdrop}
          onClick={() => {
            setSheet(null);
            setEditingTxn(null);
          }}
        />
      )}

      {sheet === 'add' && (
        <AddTxnSheet
          state={state}
          type={sheetType}
          setType={setSheetType}
          editing={editingTxn}
          defaultDate={selectedDate}
          onSave={saveTxn}
          onDelete={deleteTxn}
          toast={toast}
          toastRich={toastRich}
          alertCenter={alertCenter}
          noteColor={noteColor}
          onClose={() => { setSheet(null); setEditingTxn(null); }}
          editMode={editMode}
          setEditMode={setEditMode}
          blockOrder={blockOrder.addTxn}
          moveBlock={moveBlock('addTxn')}
          onManageCategory={(t, initialLabel) => setManageCat({ type: t, initialLabel })}
          onManageAccount={(mode) => {
            if (mode === '__new__') setEditAccountId('__new__');
            setAccountsFromAddTxn(true);
          }}
          onEditAccountName={(acctId) => { setEditAccountId(acctId); setAccountsFromAddTxn(true); }}
          onAddSubCategory={(t, catLabel, subLabel) => {
            setState((s) => {
              const newCats = s.categories[t].map((c) =>
                c.label === catLabel
                  ? { ...c, subs: [...(c.subs || []), subLabel] }
                  : c
              );
              return { ...s, categories: { ...s.categories, [t]: newCats } };
            });
          }}
          setConfirmDialog={setConfirmDialog}
          onOpenStockEntry={() => {
            // 關閉新增收支 sheet,開啟投資帳戶選擇 picker
            setSheet(null);
            setEditingTxn(null);
            setShowStockEntryPicker(true);
          }}
        />
      )}

      {(sheet === 'accounts' || accountsFromAddTxn) && (
        <AccountsSheet
          state={state}
          setState={setStateWithSync}
          toast={toast}
          toastRich={toastRich}
          initialEditId={editAccountId}
          onClose={() => {
            if (accountsFromAddTxn) {
              // 從 AddTxnSheet 打開的，只關閉 AccountsSheet，保留 AddTxnSheet
              setAccountsFromAddTxn(false);
              setEditAccountId(null);
            } else {
              setSheet(null);
              setEditAccountId(null);
            }
          }}
          onOpenDetail={(a) => setDetailAccount(a)}
          setConfirmDialog={setConfirmDialog}
        />
      )}

      {detailAccount && (
        <AccountDetailSheet
          state={state}
          catIcon={catIcon}
          account={detailAccount}
          onClose={() => setDetailAccount(null)}
          onClickTxn={(t) => {
            // 不要關掉 detailAccount,讓編輯 sheet 蓋上來
            // 這樣關閉/左滑編輯 sheet 後會自然回到投資/帳戶詳情頁
            openEditSheet(t);
          }}
          onSell={(acct) => setSellSheet({ account: acct })}
          onBuyHolding={(acct, prefillSymbol) => setBuyHoldingSheet({ account: acct, prefillSymbol })}
          onSellHolding={(holding) => setSellHoldingSheet({ holding })}
          onUpdateMarketValue={(holding) => setMarketValueDialog({ holding })}
          onOpenHolding={(holding) => setHoldingDetailSheet({ holding })}
        />
      )}

      {sellSheet && (
        <SellSheet
          state={state}
          account={sellSheet.account}
          onClose={() => setSellSheet(null)}
          onConfirm={(payload) => {
            saveSettlement(payload);
            setSellSheet(null);
          }}
          toast={toast}
        />
      )}

      {buyHoldingSheet && (
        <BuyHoldingSheet
          state={state}
          account={buyHoldingSheet.account}
          prefillSymbol={buyHoldingSheet.prefillSymbol}
          onClose={() => setBuyHoldingSheet(null)}
          onConfirm={(payload) => {
            saveBuyHolding(payload);
            setBuyHoldingSheet(null);
            toastRich && toastRich({
              title: '已買進',
              amount: '✓',
              amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
              lines: [`${payload.symbol} ${payload.shares} 股`],
            }, 1800);
          }}
          toast={toast}
          toastRich={toastRich}
        />
      )}

      {sellHoldingSheet && (
        <SellHoldingSheet
          state={state}
          holding={sellHoldingSheet.holding}
          onClose={() => setSellHoldingSheet(null)}
          onConfirm={(payload) => {
            saveSellHolding(payload);
            setSellHoldingSheet(null);
            toastRich && toastRich({
              title: '已賣出',
              amount: '✓',
              amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
              lines: [`${sellHoldingSheet.holding.symbol} ${payload.shares} 股`],
            }, 1800);
          }}
          toast={toast}
          toastRich={toastRich}
        />
      )}

      {showStockEntryPicker && (() => {
        const investAccounts = state.accounts.filter((a) => a.type === 'invest' && !a.isSystem && (a.investSubType || 'stock') === 'stock');
        return (
          <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.centerDialogBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowStockEntryPicker(false)}>
            <div style={{ ...styles.centerDialogCard, maxHeight: '80vh', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' }} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
              <div style={{ padding: '14px 18px', borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border)' }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 600 }}>選擇投資帳戶</div>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginTop: 2 }}>
                  進入帳戶後可買進、賣出、估市值
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style={{ overflowY: 'auto', maxHeight: '60vh' }}>
                {investAccounts.length === 0 ? (
                  <div style={{ padding: 32, textAlign: 'center', color: 'var(--text-faint)', fontSize: 13 }}>
                    尚未建立投資帳戶<br />
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 11 }}>請先到「帳戶管理」新增投資類型帳戶</span>
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <div style={{ padding: 12, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 6 }}>
                    {investAccounts.map((a) => {
                      const summary = investAccountSummary(a, state.holdings, state.trades);
                      const myHoldings = state.holdings.filter((h) => h.accountId === a.id);
                      const activeCount = myHoldings.filter((h) => holdingShares(h, state.trades) > 0).length;
                      return (
                        <div
                          key={a.id}
                          onClick={() => {
                            setShowStockEntryPicker(false);
                            setDetailAccount(a);
                          }}
                          style={{
                            display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 12,
                            padding: '12px 14px', borderRadius: 12,
                            background: 'var(--bg-card)', border: '1.5px solid var(--border)',
                            cursor: 'pointer',
                          }}
                        >
                          <div style={{
                            width: 36, height: 36, borderRadius: 10,
                            background: '#9ae0d4',
                            display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
                          }}>
                            <TypeIcon name="chart" size={18} color="#fff" />
                          </div>
                          <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                            <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600 }}>{a.name}</div>
                            <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginTop: 2 }}>
                              {activeCount > 0 ? `持有 ${activeCount} 支股票` : '尚無持股'}
                            </div>
                          </div>
                          {summary && summary.totalMarket > 0 && (
                            <div style={{ textAlign: 'right' }}>
                              <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>市值</div>
                              <div style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 600 }}>{fmt(summary.totalMarket)}</div>
                            </div>
                          )}
                          <div style={{ fontSize: 18, color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>›</div>
                        </div>
                      );
                    })}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
              <div
                style={{ padding: '12px 20px', fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text-dim)', textAlign: 'center', cursor: 'pointer', borderTop: '1px solid var(--border)' }}
                onClick={() => setShowStockEntryPicker(false)}
              >取消</div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      })()}

      {holdingDetailSheet && (
        <HoldingDetailSheet
          state={state}
          holding={state.holdings.find((h) => h.id === holdingDetailSheet.holding.id)}
          onClose={() => setHoldingDetailSheet(null)}
          onUpdateMarketValue={(holding) => setMarketValueDialog({ holding })}
          onBuyMore={(holding) => {
            const acct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === holding.accountId);
            setHoldingDetailSheet(null);
            if (acct) setBuyHoldingSheet({ account: acct, prefillSymbol: holding.symbol });
          }}
          onSell={(holding) => {
            setHoldingDetailSheet(null);
            setSellHoldingSheet({ holding });
          }}
          onDeleteTrade={(tradeId) => {
            // 如果這次刪除導致 holding 整個消失,關閉 detail sheet
            const t = state.trades.find((tr) => tr.id === tradeId);
            const holdingTrades = t ? state.trades.filter((tr) => tr.holdingId === t.holdingId) : [];
            const isLastTrade = holdingTrades.length === 1; // 只剩這筆
            deleteTrade(tradeId);
            if (isLastTrade) {
              setHoldingDetailSheet(null);
              toastRich && toastRich({
                title: '已刪除持股',
                amount: '✓',
                amountColor: 'var(--pink-text)',
              }, 1400);
            } else {
              toastRich && toastRich({
                title: '已刪除紀錄',
                amount: '✓',
                amountColor: 'var(--pink-text)',
              }, 1400);
            }
          }}
          setConfirmDialog={setConfirmDialog}
        />
      )}

      {marketValueDialog && (() => {
        const h = marketValueDialog.holding;
        const shares = holdingShares(h, state.trades);
        return (
          <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.centerDialogBackdrop} onClick={() => setMarketValueDialog(null)}>
            <div style={styles.centerDialogCard} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
              <div style={{ padding: '14px 18px', borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border)' }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 600 }}>更新 {h.symbol} 目前市值</div>
                {h.name && <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginTop: 2 }}>{h.name}</div>}
              </div>
              <div style={{ padding: 18 }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 8 }}>
                  持有 {shares.toLocaleString()} 股 · 目前市值總額(NT$)
                </div>
                <input
                  type="number"
                  inputMode="decimal"
                  defaultValue={h.marketValue || ''}
                  placeholder="0"
                  autoFocus={false}
                  id="mv-input"
                  style={{
                    width: '100%', padding: '12px 14px', fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 600,
                    background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
                    border: '1.5px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 12,
                    outline: 'none', boxSizing: 'border-box',
                  }}
                  onKeyDown={(e) => {
                    if (e.key === 'Enter') {
                      const mv = parseFloat(e.target.value) || 0;
                      updateHoldingMarketValue(h.id, mv);
                      setMarketValueDialog(null);
                    }
                  }}
                />
                <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 6 }}>
                  系統會根據此金額顯示浮動損益
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8, padding: '0 14px 14px' }}>
                <button
                  onClick={() => setMarketValueDialog(null)}
                  style={{
                    flex: 1, padding: '12px',
                    background: 'transparent', color: 'var(--pink-text)',
                    border: '1.5px solid var(--pink)', borderRadius: 12,
                    fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer',
                  }}
                >取消</button>
                <button
                  onClick={() => {
                    const input = document.getElementById('mv-input');
                    const mv = parseFloat(input?.value) || 0;
                    updateHoldingMarketValue(h.id, mv);
                    setMarketValueDialog(null);
                  }}
                  style={{
                    flex: 1, padding: '12px',
                    background: 'var(--mint)', color: '#fff',
                    border: 'none', borderRadius: 12,
                    fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer',
                  }}
                >確認</button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      })()}

      {periodKey && (
        <PeriodDetailSheet
          state={state}
          setState={setStateWithSync}
          catIcon={catIcon}
          periodKey={periodKey}
          onClose={() => setPeriodKey(null)}
          onClickTxn={(t) => {
            setPeriodKey(null);
            openEditSheet(t);
          }}
          setConfirmDialog={setConfirmDialog}
          toastRich={toastRich}
          toast={toast}
        />
      )}

      {detailDate && (
        <DayDetailSheet
          state={state}
          catIcon={catIcon}
          date={detailDate}
          onClose={() => setDetailDate(null)}
          onClickTxn={(t) => {
            setDetailDate(null);
            openEditSheet(t);
          }}
          onAdd={(type, date) => {
            setDetailDate(null);
            setSelectedDate(date);
            openAddSheet(type);
          }}
        />
      )}

      {lendDetail && (
        <LendDetailSheet
          state={state}
          lendOut={state.transactions.find((t) => t.id === lendDetail.id) || lendDetail}
          onClose={() => setLendDetail(null)}
          onCollect={collectLend}
          onEdit={(t) => {
            setLendDetail(null);
            // 直接打開編輯 sheet,類型設為 lend
            setSheetType('lend');
            setEditingTxn(t);
            setSheet('add');
          }}
          onDelete={deleteLend}
          setConfirmDialog={setConfirmDialog}
          toast={toast}
          toastRich={toastRich}
        />
      )}

      {settleDetail && (
        <SettleDetailSheet
          state={state}
          settleGroup={
            // 即時從 state 取最新紀錄,避免 sheet 開啟期間 state 變動造成不同步
            (() => {
              const settleId = settleDetail[0]?.settleId;
              const fresh = state.transactions
                .filter((t) => t.settleId && t.settleId === settleId)
                .sort((a, b) => {
                  const order = { settle_out: 0, settle_in: 1, settle_pnl_in: 2, settle_pnl_out: 2 };
                  return (order[a.transferRole] ?? 99) - (order[b.transferRole] ?? 99);
                });
              return fresh.length > 0 ? fresh : settleDetail;
            })()
          }
          onClose={() => setSettleDetail(null)}
          onDeleteGroup={(group) => {
            // 走現有 deleteTxn 流程(會跳 ConfirmDialog 三層警告 + 整組刪 + 還原市值)
            setSettleDetail(null);
            deleteTxn(group[0].id);
          }}
        />
      )}

      {manageCat && (
        <CategoryManageSheet
          state={state}
          setState={setStateWithSync}
          toast={toast}
          toastRich={toastRich}
          catType={manageCat.type}
          initialLabel={manageCat.initialLabel}
          onClose={() => setManageCat(null)}
          setConfirmDialog={setConfirmDialog}
        />
      )}

      {/* 通用確認彈窗 */}
      {confirmDialog && (
        <ConfirmDialogRenderer dialog={confirmDialog} onClose={() => setConfirmDialog(null)} />
      )}

      {/* 中央警示彈窗(金額錯誤等重要提示) */}
      {centerAlert && (
        <div
          style={styles.centerAlertBackdrop}
          onClick={() => setCenterAlert('')}
          onTouchStart={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
          onTouchMove={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); e.preventDefault(); }}
        >
          <div style={styles.centerAlertCard} onClick={() => setCenterAlert('')}>
            <div style={styles.centerAlertIcon}>
              <TypeIcon name="warning" size={28} color="var(--pink-text)" />
            </div>
            <div style={styles.centerAlertText}>{centerAlert}</div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {toastMsg && (
        typeof toastMsg === 'string'
          ? <div style={styles.toast}>{toastMsg}</div>
          : (
            <>
              <div
                style={{
                  ...styles.toastBackdrop,
                  pointerEvents: toastMsg.variant === 'info_card' ? 'auto' : (styles.toastBackdrop.pointerEvents || 'auto'),
                  cursor: toastMsg.variant === 'info_card' ? 'pointer' : 'default',
                }}
                onClick={(e) => {
                  if (toastMsg.variant === 'info_card') {
                    setToastMsg('');
                  } else {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                  }
                }}
                onTouchStart={(e) => { if (toastMsg.variant !== 'info_card') e.stopPropagation(); }}
                onTouchMove={(e) => { if (toastMsg.variant !== 'info_card') { e.stopPropagation(); e.preventDefault(); } }}
              />
              <div
                style={{
                  ...styles.toastRich,
                  pointerEvents: toastMsg.variant === 'info_card' ? 'auto' : styles.toastRich.pointerEvents,
                  cursor: toastMsg.variant === 'info_card' ? 'pointer' : 'default',
                }}
                onClick={() => { if (toastMsg.variant === 'info_card') setToastMsg(''); }}
              >
                {(() => {
                  const isCheckmark = toastMsg.amount === '✓';
                  const isInfoBadge = toastMsg.variant === 'info_badge';
                  const isInfoCard = toastMsg.variant === 'info_card';
                  const hasDetails = toastMsg.amount || (toastMsg.lines && toastMsg.lines.length > 0);

                  // info_card 模式:中性卡片,三行配色不同(用於 ⓘ 點擊查看資訊)
                  // titleSegments:[{text, color, weight}...]  highlightLine:string  bottomLine:string
                  if (isInfoCard) {
                    return (
                      <div style={{
                        animation: 'toastInfoSlideIn 0.32s cubic-bezier(0.2, 0.8, 0.2, 1)',
                        textAlign: 'center',
                      }}>
                        {/* 第一行:帳戶名等主標(粗體大字) */}
                        {(toastMsg.title || Array.isArray(toastMsg.titleSegments)) && (
                          <div style={{
                            fontSize: 16,
                            fontWeight: 700,
                            color: 'var(--text)',
                            lineHeight: 1.3,
                            marginBottom: 6,
                          }}>
                            {Array.isArray(toastMsg.titleSegments)
                              ? toastMsg.titleSegments.map((seg, i) => (
                                  <span key={i} style={{
                                    color: seg.color || 'var(--text)',
                                    fontWeight: seg.weight || 700,
                                  }}>{seg.text}</span>
                                ))
                              : toastMsg.title}
                          </div>
                        )}
                        {/* 第二行:說明(淡色小字) */}
                        {toastMsg.subtitle && (
                          <div style={{
                            fontSize: 12,
                            fontWeight: 400,
                            color: 'var(--text-faint)',
                            lineHeight: 1.3,
                            marginBottom: 4,
                          }}>{toastMsg.subtitle}</div>
                        )}
                        {/* 第三行:重點資料(顏色強調) */}
                        {toastMsg.highlight && (
                          <div style={{
                            fontSize: 15,
                            fontWeight: 600,
                            color: toastMsg.highlightColor || 'var(--blue)',
                            lineHeight: 1.3,
                            letterSpacing: '0.3px',
                          }}>{toastMsg.highlight}</div>
                        )}
                        {/* 底部關閉提示 */}
                        <div style={{
                          fontSize: 10,
                          color: 'var(--text-faint)',
                          marginTop: 12,
                          opacity: 0.7,
                        }}>(點選畫面任何一處關閉)</div>
                      </div>
                    );
                  }
                  // info_badge 模式:小圓徽章在左 + 標題 + 金額 + 分層 lines(用於新增/更新)
                  if (isInfoBadge) {
                    const badgeColor = toastMsg.badgeColor || toastMsg.amountColor || 'var(--mint)';
                    const isPink = badgeColor.includes('pink') || badgeColor.includes('f5b') || badgeColor.includes('d96');
                    const isAccent = badgeColor.includes('accent') || badgeColor.includes('8f7') || badgeColor.includes('6b5');
                    const shadowColor = isPink ? 'rgba(245,181,192,0.45)' : isAccent ? 'rgba(143,127,240,0.45)' : 'rgba(126,224,192,0.5)';
                    // 同色系極淺底色(支出微粉、收入微綠、轉帳微紫)— 4-5% 不透明
                    // 成功感:統一用綠色色條 + 微綠色底,不論交易類型
                    const tintBg = 'rgba(126,224,192,0.06)';
                    const barColor = 'var(--mint)';
                    return (
                      <div style={{
                        display: 'flex', alignItems: 'stretch', gap: 0,
                        position: 'relative', overflow: 'hidden',
                        borderRadius: 14,
                        animation: 'toastInfoSlideIn 0.32s cubic-bezier(0.2, 0.8, 0.2, 1)',
                      }}>
                        {/* 左側 3px 同色直條 */}
                        <div style={{
                          width: 3, flexShrink: 0,
                          background: barColor,
                          borderRadius: '3px 0 0 3px',
                          animation: 'toastInfoBarGrow 0.4s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1) 0.05s both',
                          transformOrigin: 'top',
                        }} />
                        {/* 同色系微淺底 */}
                        <div style={{
                          flex: 1,
                          padding: '12px 14px',
                          background: tintBg,
                        }}>
                          {/* 右側資訊區 */}
                          <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
                            <div style={{
                              fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--mint-text)',
                              letterSpacing: '0.2px', marginBottom: 4,
                              textTransform: 'none',
                              animation: 'toastInfoTitleRise 0.35s cubic-bezier(0.2, 0.8, 0.2, 1) 0.08s both',
                              textAlign: 'center',
                            }}>
                              {toastMsg.title}
                            </div>
                            {toastMsg.amount && toastMsg.amount !== '✓' && (
                              <div style={{
                                fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 500,
                                color: 'var(--text-faint)',
                                letterSpacing: '0px', lineHeight: 1.3, marginBottom: 4,
                                animation: 'toastInfoAmountFade 0.5s ease-out 0.1s both',
                              }}>
                                {toastMsg.amount}
                              </div>
                            )}
                            {toastMsg.lines && toastMsg.lines.length > 0 && (
                              <div>
                                {toastMsg.lines.map((line, i) => {
                                  const isFirst = i === 0;
                                  // 第一行(分類)— 子分類部分用更深字色
                                  if (isFirst && typeof line === 'string' && line.includes(' › ')) {
                                    const [main, sub] = line.split(' › ');
                                    return (
                                      <div key={i} style={{
                                        fontSize: 12.5, lineHeight: 1.5,
                                        overflow: 'hidden', textOverflow: 'ellipsis', whiteSpace: 'nowrap',
                                      }}>
                                        <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>{main}</span>
                                        <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)', margin: '0 5px' }}>›</span>
                                        <span style={{ color: 'var(--text)', fontWeight: 600 }}>{sub}</span>
                                      </div>
                                    );
                                  }
                                  return (
                                    <div key={i} style={{
                                      fontSize: 12,
                                      color: isFirst ? 'var(--text)' : 'var(--text-faint)',
                                      fontWeight: isFirst ? 500 : 400,
                                      lineHeight: 1.55,
                                      overflow: 'hidden', textOverflow: 'ellipsis', whiteSpace: 'nowrap',
                                    }}>
                                      {line}
                                    </div>
                                  );
                                })}
                              </div>
                            )}
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    );
                  }
                  // 勾勾模式:大圓徽章 + 標題 + 副資訊
                  if (isCheckmark) {
                    const badgeColor = toastMsg.amountColor || 'var(--mint)';
                    const badgeShadowColor = badgeColor.includes('pink') || badgeColor.includes('f5b5')
                      ? 'rgba(245,181,192,0.4)'
                      : badgeColor.includes('faint') || badgeColor.includes('dim')
                      ? 'rgba(160,160,160,0.35)'
                      : 'rgba(126,224,192,0.45)';
                    // 預設勾勾,但若 toastMsg.icon === 'info' 用驚嘆號等不同符號
                    const customIcon = toastMsg.icon;
                    return (
                      <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', padding: '4px 16px 6px' }}>
                        <div style={{
                          width: 56, height: 56, borderRadius: '50%',
                          background: badgeColor,
                          display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
                          boxShadow: `0 6px 20px ${badgeShadowColor}, 0 0 0 6px rgba(255,255,255,0.04)`,
                          marginBottom: 14,
                          animation: 'toastBadgePop 0.45s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1)',
                        }}>
                          {customIcon === 'info' ? (
                            <svg width="32" height="32" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="#1a1a1a" strokeWidth="2.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
                              <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9" />
                              <line x1="12" y1="11" x2="12" y2="17" />
                              <circle cx="12" cy="7.5" r="0.6" fill="#1a1a1a" stroke="none" />
                            </svg>
                          ) : customIcon === 'warn' ? (
                            // 警告:三角形 + 中間驚嘆號(直線+點)
                            <svg width="34" height="34" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="#1a1a1a" strokeWidth="2.4" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
                              <path d="M12 3 L22 20 L2 20 Z" />
                              <line x1="12" y1="10" x2="12" y2="14.5" />
                              <circle cx="12" cy="17.2" r="0.7" fill="#1a1a1a" stroke="none" />
                            </svg>
                          ) : customIcon === 'minus' ? (
                            <svg width="32" height="32" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="#1a1a1a" strokeWidth="3.2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
                              <line x1="6" y1="12" x2="18" y2="12" />
                            </svg>
                          ) : (
                            <svg width="32" height="32" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="#1a1a1a" strokeWidth="3.2" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
                              <polyline points="5 12 10 17 19 8" />
                            </svg>
                          )}
                        </div>
                        <div style={{ fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--text)', letterSpacing: '0.5px', marginBottom: toastMsg.lines?.length > 0 ? 12 : 0, whiteSpace: 'pre-line', textAlign: 'center', lineHeight: 1.35 }}>
                          {Array.isArray(toastMsg.titleSegments) ? (() => {
                            // 第一行(換行前)= 主標 fontSize 19,之後 = 副標 fontSize 14
                            let line = 0;
                            return toastMsg.titleSegments.map((seg, i) => {
                              if (seg === '\n') {
                                line += 1;
                                return <br key={i} />;
                              }
                              const fs = line === 0 ? 19 : 14;
                              if (typeof seg === 'string') {
                                return <span key={i} style={{ fontSize: fs }}>{seg}</span>;
                              }
                              return (
                                <span key={i} style={{
                                  fontSize: fs,
                                  color: seg.color || 'var(--text)',
                                  fontWeight: seg.weight || 700,
                                }}>{seg.text}</span>
                              );
                            });
                          })() : <span style={{ fontSize: 17 }}>{toastMsg.title}</span>}
                        </div>
                        {toastMsg.lines && toastMsg.lines.length > 0 && (
                          <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 2, alignItems: 'center' }}>
                            {toastMsg.lines.map((line, i) => {
                              const renameMatch = typeof line === 'string'
                                ? line.match(/^「(.+?)」\s*→\s*「(.+?)」$/)
                                : null;
                              if (renameMatch) {
                                const oldName = renameMatch[1];
                                const newName = renameMatch[2];
                                return (
                                  <div key={i} style={{
                                    position: 'relative',
                                    width: '100%',
                                    height: 28,
                                    marginTop: 4,
                                    marginBottom: 6,
                                  }}>
                                    {/* 舊名:劃線 → 飛走 */}
                                    <div style={{
                                      position: 'absolute',
                                      top: 0,
                                      left: 0,
                                      right: 0,
                                      display: 'flex',
                                      justifyContent: 'center',
                                      animation: 'toastRenameOldFly 1.4s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.4, 1) 0.45s forwards',
                                    }}>
                                      <span style={{
                                        position: 'relative',
                                        display: 'inline-block',
                                        fontSize: 13,
                                        color: 'var(--text-dim)',
                                        whiteSpace: 'nowrap',
                                      }}>
                                        {oldName}
                                        <span style={{
                                          position: 'absolute',
                                          left: 0,
                                          top: '50%',
                                          height: 1.5,
                                          background: 'var(--pink)',
                                          borderRadius: 1,
                                          pointerEvents: 'none',
                                          animation: 'toastRenameStrike 1.3s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1) 0.55s forwards',
                                        }} />
                                      </span>
                                    </div>
                                    {/* 新名:從下方淡入飄上 */}
                                    <div style={{
                                      position: 'absolute',
                                      top: 0,
                                      left: 0,
                                      right: 0,
                                      display: 'flex',
                                      justifyContent: 'center',
                                      opacity: 0,
                                      animation: 'toastRenameNewFloat 0.9s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.4, 0.5, 1) 1.4s forwards',
                                    }}>
                                      <span style={{
                                        fontSize: 16,
                                        fontWeight: 700,
                                        whiteSpace: 'nowrap',
                                      }}>
                                        <span style={{ color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>{newName}</span>
                                      </span>
                                    </div>
                                  </div>
                                );
                              }
                              return (
                                <div key={i} style={{
                                  fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text-dim)', lineHeight: 1.4, textAlign: 'center',
                                  wordBreak: 'keep-all',
                                  overflowWrap: 'anywhere',
                                }}>
                                  {line}
                                </div>
                              );
                            })}
                          </div>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    );
                  }
                  if (hasDetails) {
                    return <div style={styles.toastRichTitle}>{toastMsg.title}</div>;
                  }
                  // 簡短模式（舊的兼容路徑）：大綠色勾勾 + 大字
                  return (
                    <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10, padding: '8px 20px' }}>
                      <div style={{
                        width: 48, height: 48, borderRadius: '50%',
                        background: 'var(--mint)',
                        display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
                        boxShadow: '0 4px 16px rgba(126,224,192,0.4)',
                      }}>
                        <svg width="28" height="28" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="#1a1a1a" strokeWidth="3" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
                          <polyline points="5 12 10 17 19 8" />
                        </svg>
                      </div>
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 22, fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--text)', letterSpacing: '1px' }}>
                        {toastMsg.title}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  );
                })()}
                {toastMsg.variant !== 'info_badge' && toastMsg.amount && toastMsg.amount !== '✓' && (
                  <div style={{ ...styles.toastRichAmount, color: toastMsg.amountColor || 'var(--text)' }}>
                    {toastMsg.amount}
                  </div>
                )}
                {toastMsg.variant !== 'info_badge' && toastMsg.amount !== '✓' && toastMsg.lines && toastMsg.lines.length > 0 && (
                  <div style={styles.toastRichLines}>
                    {toastMsg.lines.map((line, i) => {
                      // 第一行是名稱時(被「」包住)放大強調;
                      // 第一行是金額(+/- 開頭+數字)時更大字 + 用 amountColor
                      // 最後一行(如果超過2行)則淡化當 footer
                      // 改名格式:「舊名」 → 「新名」 — 觸發劃線+漂浮動畫
                      const renameMatch = typeof line === 'string'
                        ? line.match(/^「(.+?)」\s*→\s*「(.+?)」$/)
                        : null;
                      if (renameMatch) {
                        const oldName = renameMatch[1];
                        const newName = renameMatch[2];
                        return (
                          <div key={i} style={{
                            ...styles.toastRichLine,
                            position: 'relative',
                            width: '100%',
                            marginTop: 4,
                            marginBottom: 6,
                            height: 26,
                          }}>
                            {/* 舊名:黑色 → 劃紅線 → 飄走(往上飛走) */}
                            <div style={{
                              position: 'absolute',
                              top: 0,
                              left: 0,
                              right: 0,
                              display: 'flex',
                              justifyContent: 'center',
                              animation: 'toastRenameOldFly 1.4s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.4, 1) 0.45s forwards',
                            }}>
                              <span style={{
                                position: 'relative',
                                display: 'inline-block',
                                fontSize: 15,
                                fontWeight: 600,
                                color: 'var(--text)',
                                whiteSpace: 'nowrap',
                              }}>
                                {oldName}
                                {/* 紅色劃線 */}
                                <span style={{
                                  position: 'absolute',
                                  left: 0,
                                  top: '50%',
                                  height: 2,
                                  background: 'var(--pink)',
                                  borderRadius: 1,
                                  pointerEvents: 'none',
                                  animation: 'toastRenameStrike 1.3s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1) 0.55s forwards',
                                }} />
                              </span>
                            </div>
                            {/* 新名:從下方淡入飄上,結束時與舊名同位置 */}
                            <div style={{
                              position: 'absolute',
                              top: 0,
                              left: 0,
                              right: 0,
                              display: 'flex',
                              justifyContent: 'center',
                              opacity: 0,
                              animation: 'toastRenameNewFloat 0.9s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.4, 0.5, 1) 1.4s forwards',
                            }}>
                              <span style={{
                                fontSize: 15,
                                fontWeight: 600,
                                whiteSpace: 'nowrap',
                              }}>
                                <span style={{ color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>{newName}</span>
                              </span>
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        );
                      }
                      const isQuoted = typeof line === 'string' && line.startsWith('「') && line.endsWith('」');
                      const isAmount = typeof line === 'string' && /^[+\-]\d[\d,]*(\.\d+)?$/.test(line.trim());
                      const isFirst = i === 0;
                      const isLast = i === toastMsg.lines.length - 1 && toastMsg.lines.length > 2;
                      let lineStyle = styles.toastRichLine;
                      if (isFirst && isAmount) {
                        // 依「動作類型」決定金額色:
                        // 新增:用 +/- 自動配色(粉=扣錢、綠=進錢)— 強調「新支出」感
                        // 更新/刪除/清除/移除:中性灰(錢已扣過或已消失,不需再強調金額)
                        const titleStr = toastMsg.title || '';
                        const isAdd = /新增/.test(titleStr);
                        const isDeleted = /刪除|清除|移除/.test(titleStr);
                        const trimmed = line.trim();
                        const sign = trimmed.charAt(0);
                        let amtColor;
                        if (isAdd) {
                          amtColor = sign === '-' ? 'var(--pink-text)'
                                   : sign === '+' ? 'var(--mint-text)'
                                   : 'var(--text)';
                        } else {
                          amtColor = 'var(--text-dim)';
                        }
                        // 刪除類:金額消失動畫(淡出 + 縮小 + 模糊)
                        if (isDeleted) {
                          return (
                            <div key={i} style={{
                              ...styles.toastRichLine,
                              fontSize: 32,
                              fontWeight: 700,
                              letterSpacing: '-0.8px',
                              lineHeight: 1.1,
                              marginBottom: 4,
                              marginTop: 0,
                              alignSelf: 'center',
                              color: 'var(--pink-text)',
                              animation: 'toastDeletedFadeOut 0.7s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.4, 1) 0.25s forwards',
                            }}>
                              {line}
                            </div>
                          );
                        }
                        lineStyle = {
                          ...styles.toastRichLine,
                          fontSize: 32,
                          fontWeight: 700,
                          color: amtColor,
                          letterSpacing: '-0.8px',
                          lineHeight: 1.1,
                          marginBottom: 4,
                          marginTop: 0,
                        };
                      } else if (isFirst && isQuoted) {
                        lineStyle = { ...styles.toastRichLine, fontSize: 15, color: 'var(--text)', fontWeight: 500, marginBottom: 2 };
                      } else if (isLast) {
                        lineStyle = { ...styles.toastRichLine, fontSize: 11.5, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 4 };
                      }
                      return <div key={i} style={lineStyle}>{line}</div>;
                    })}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </>
          )
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 通用區塊包裝 ============
// ============ 確認彈窗(危險操作自動加鎖) ============
function ConfirmDialogRenderer({ dialog, onClose }) {
  // danger 操作預設鎖定,避免誤觸
  const [locked, setLocked] = useState(!!dialog.danger);
  const isDanger = !!dialog.danger;
  // 結構化變更：陣列，每筆 { icon, label, from, to, changed, diff? }
  const hasChanges = Array.isArray(dialog.changes);
  // items 格式:每筆 { icon, iconColor, label, detail, type: 'remove'|'keep' }
  const hasItems = Array.isArray(dialog.items);
  // 左右滑返回
  const swipe = useSwipeToClose(onClose);

  return (
    <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={onClose}>
      <div style={styles.pickerCard} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()} {...swipe}>
        <div style={{ ...styles.pickerTitle, fontSize: 17, fontWeight: 700, padding: '14px 16px 12px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', gap: 12 }}>
          <span style={{ color: 'var(--text)' }}>
            {(() => {
              // 關鍵動詞染色:破壞性 = 粉,還原/恢復 = 綠,其餘白
              // 若 title 含空格,視為多段層次:[動作] [類型] [欄位] — 動作染色,類型淡色,欄位粗體
              const title = dialog.title || '';
              const dangerWords = ['刪除', '清除', '移除'];
              const safeWords = ['還原', '恢復'];

              // 多段標題:支援「刪除 子分類 名稱」這樣的層次表達
              if (title.includes(' ')) {
                const segments = title.split(/\s+/).filter(Boolean);
                return (
                  <>
                    {segments.map((seg, idx) => {
                      const isDangerSeg = dangerWords.includes(seg);
                      const isSafeSeg = safeWords.includes(seg);
                      let color = 'var(--text)';
                      let fontWeight = 700;
                      if (isDangerSeg) {
                        color = 'var(--pink)';
                      } else if (isSafeSeg) {
                        color = 'var(--mint)';
                      } else if (idx > 0 && idx < segments.length - 1) {
                        // 中間段(類型描述):藍色,中性提示,跟動作色與欄位色都區分開
                        color = 'var(--blue)';
                        fontWeight = 600;
                      }
                      return (
                        <span key={idx} style={{ color, fontWeight, marginRight: idx < segments.length - 1 ? 6 : 0 }}>
                          {seg}
                        </span>
                      );
                    })}
                  </>
                );
              }

              const allWords = [...dangerWords, ...safeWords];
              // 找第一個命中的關鍵詞
              let matchWord = null;
              let matchIdx = -1;
              for (const w of allWords) {
                const i = title.indexOf(w);
                if (i !== -1 && (matchIdx === -1 || i < matchIdx)) {
                  matchWord = w;
                  matchIdx = i;
                }
              }
              if (!matchWord) return title;
              const isDangerWord = dangerWords.includes(matchWord);
              const before = title.slice(0, matchIdx);
              const after = title.slice(matchIdx + matchWord.length);
              return (
                <>
                  {before && <span style={{ marginRight: 6 }}>{before}</span>}
                  <span style={{ color: isDangerWord ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--mint)' }}>
                    {matchWord}
                  </span>
                  {after && <span style={{ marginLeft: 6 }}>{after}</span>}
                </>
              );
            })()}
          </span>
          {isDanger && (
            <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8, flexShrink: 0 }}>
              <span style={{ ...styles.lockLabel, color: locked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--pink)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 4 }}>
                <TypeIcon name={locked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'} size={12} color={locked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--pink)'} />
                {locked ? '鎖定中' : '已解鎖'}
              </span>
              <div
                style={{ ...styles.toggleTrack, background: locked ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--pink)' }}
                onClick={() => setLocked((v) => !v)}
              >
                <div style={{ ...styles.toggleThumb, transform: locked ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(18px)' }} />
              </div>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* 目標物件強調顯示(例如被刪除/還原的名稱) - 共用,hasChanges 或純文字都可用 */}
        {dialog.target && (
          <div style={{
            margin: '12px 16px 8px',
            padding: '10px 14px',
            background: isDanger ? 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.10)' : 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.10)',
            border: `1px solid ${isDanger ? 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.25)' : 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.25)'}`,
            borderRadius: 10,
            display: 'flex',
            alignItems: dialog.target.multiline ? 'flex-start' : 'center',
            gap: 10,
          }}>
            {dialog.target.label && (
              <div style={{
                fontSize: 11,
                color: isDanger ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--mint)',
                fontWeight: 600,
                letterSpacing: 0.5,
                flexShrink: 0,
                marginTop: dialog.target.multiline ? 2 : 0,
              }}>
                {dialog.target.label}
              </div>
            )}
            <div style={{
              fontSize: dialog.target.multiline ? 13 : 15,
              color: 'var(--text)',
              fontWeight: dialog.target.multiline ? 500 : 600,
              flex: 1,
              overflow: 'hidden',
              textOverflow: dialog.target.multiline ? 'clip' : 'ellipsis',
              whiteSpace: dialog.target.multiline ? 'pre-line' : 'nowrap',
              lineHeight: dialog.target.multiline ? 1.7 : 1.3,
            }}>
              {dialog.target.name}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {hasChanges ? (
          <>
            {dialog.changesHint && (
              <div style={{ padding: '0 20px 8px', fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', lineHeight: 1.6 }}>
                {dialog.changesHint}
              </div>
            )}
            <div style={{ padding: '0 16px 6px' }}>
              {dialog.changes.map((c, i) => {
                const unchanged = !c.changed;
                return (
                  <div
                    key={i}
                    style={{
                      display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10,
                      padding: '8px 4px',
                      borderBottom: i < dialog.changes.length - 1 ? '1px solid var(--border)' : 'none',
                      opacity: unchanged ? 0.45 : 1,
                    }}
                  >
                    <div style={{
                      width: 28, height: 28, borderRadius: 8,
                      background: unchanged ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'rgba(126,224,192,0.12)',
                      display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
                      flexShrink: 0,
                    }}>
                      <TypeIcon name={c.icon} size={15} color={unchanged ? 'var(--text-faint)' : 'var(--mint)'} />
                    </div>
                    <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginBottom: 2 }}>{c.label}</div>
                      {unchanged ? (
                        <div style={{ fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text-dim)', overflow: 'hidden', textOverflow: 'ellipsis', whiteSpace: 'nowrap' }}>
                          {c.from}
                          <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginLeft: 6 }}>（未變更）</span>
                        </div>
                      ) : (
                        <div style={{ fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text)', lineHeight: 1.35 }}>
                          <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)', textDecoration: 'line-through' }}>{c.from}</span>
                          <span style={{ color: 'var(--mint-text)', margin: '0 6px' }}>→</span>
                          <span style={{ fontWeight: 600 }}>{c.to}</span>
                          {c.diff && (
                            <span style={{ marginLeft: 6, fontSize: 12, color: c.diff.startsWith('+') ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--pink)' }}>
                              ({c.diff})
                            </span>
                          )}
                        </div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                );
              })}
              {dialog.changes.every((c) => !c.changed) && (
                <div style={{ padding: '10px 4px 2px', fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-faint)', textAlign: 'center' }}>
                  所有欄位均無更改
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </>
        ) : hasItems ? (
          <>
            {dialog.itemsHint && (
              <div style={{ padding: '10px 20px 0', fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text-dim)', lineHeight: 1.5 }}>
                {dialog.itemsHint}
              </div>
            )}
            <div style={{ padding: '8px 16px 6px' }}>
              {dialog.items.map((it, i) => {
                const isRemove = it.type === 'remove';
                const isKeep = it.type === 'keep';
                const accentColor = isRemove ? 'var(--pink)' : isKeep ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--text-dim)';
                const bgColor = isRemove ? 'rgba(232,141,141,0.12)' : isKeep ? 'rgba(126,224,192,0.12)' : 'var(--bg-card)';
                return (
                  <div
                    key={i}
                    style={{
                      display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10,
                      padding: '10px 4px',
                      borderBottom: i < dialog.items.length - 1 ? '1px solid var(--border)' : 'none',
                    }}
                  >
                    <div style={{
                      width: 30, height: 30, borderRadius: 8,
                      background: bgColor,
                      display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
                      flexShrink: 0,
                    }}>
                      <TypeIcon name={it.icon} size={16} color={accentColor} />
                    </div>
                    <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
                      {it.label && (
                        <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: accentColor, marginBottom: 2, fontWeight: 600, letterSpacing: 0.3 }}>
                          {it.label}
                        </div>
                      )}
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 14, color: 'var(--text)', lineHeight: 1.35 }}>
                        {isRemove ? (
                          <>
                            <span style={{
                              color: 'var(--text-dim)',
                              textDecoration: 'line-through',
                              textDecorationColor: 'var(--pink)',
                              textDecorationThickness: 1.5,
                            }}>{it.detail}</span>
                            {it.resetTo && (
                              <>
                                <span style={{ color: 'var(--mint-text)', margin: '0 6px' }}>→</span>
                                <span style={{ fontWeight: 600 }}>{it.resetTo}</span>
                              </>
                            )}
                          </>
                        ) : (
                          it.detail
                        )}
                      </div>
                      {it.sublabel && (
                        <div style={{
                          fontSize: 11,
                          color: 'var(--text-faint)',
                          marginTop: 3,
                          lineHeight: 1.4,
                        }}>{it.sublabel}</div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                );
              })}
            </div>
            {dialog.itemsFooter && (
              <div style={{ padding: '6px 20px 0', fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-faint)', lineHeight: 1.5 }}>
                {dialog.itemsFooter}
              </div>
            )}
          </>
        ) : (
          <>
            {dialog.bigNumber && (
              <div style={{
                padding: '8px 20px 14px',
                display: 'flex',
                flexDirection: 'column',
                alignItems: 'center',
                gap: 4,
              }}>
                <div style={{
                  fontSize: 44,
                  fontWeight: 700,
                  color: 'var(--pink-text)',
                  letterSpacing: 1,
                  lineHeight: 1.1,
                  fontVariantNumeric: 'tabular-nums',
                }}>
                  {dialog.bigNumber.value}
                </div>
                {dialog.bigNumber.label && (
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-faint)', letterSpacing: 0.5 }}>
                    {dialog.bigNumber.label}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            )}
            {/* messageList 模式:中段以左側豎線清單呈現項目 */}
            {dialog.messageList && (
              <div style={{
                padding: '4px 20px 14px',
                fontSize: 14,
                color: 'var(--text-dim)',
                lineHeight: 1.6,
                whiteSpace: 'pre-wrap',
              }}>
                {dialog.messageList.before && (
                  <div style={{ marginBottom: 10 }}>{dialog.messageList.before}</div>
                )}
                {Array.isArray(dialog.messageList.items) && dialog.messageList.items.length > 0 && (
                  <div style={{
                    margin: '0 0 10px',
                    paddingLeft: 12,
                    borderLeft: '2px solid var(--text-faint)',
                    display: 'flex',
                    flexDirection: 'column',
                    gap: 4,
                  }}>
                    {dialog.messageList.items.map((it, i) => (
                      <div key={i} style={{ color: 'var(--text)', fontWeight: 500 }}>
                        {it}
                      </div>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                )}
                {dialog.messageList.after && (
                  <div>{dialog.messageList.after}</div>
                )}
              </div>
            )}
            {dialog.message && !dialog.messageList && (() => {
              // 自動拆解 message:把「警告類」句子拆出來變成警告區塊,
              //                  把跟 title 同義的「確定要刪除...嗎」拆掉避免重複
              const rawText = dialog.message;
              const lines = rawText.split('\n').map((l) => l.trim()).filter(Boolean);
              const warningPatterns = [
                /^[•·・]?\s*此動作無法復原[。.]?$/,
                /^[•·・]?\s*無法復原[。.]?$/,
                /^[•·・]?\s*.*無法還原[。.]?$/,
                /^[•·・]?\s*.*無法復原[,,].*$/,
              ];
              // 重複偵測:title「刪除 XXX」+ message 第一句「確定要刪除...嗎?」 → 拿掉第一句
              const titleHasDelete = (dialog.title || '').includes('刪除') ||
                                     (dialog.title || '').includes('清除') ||
                                     (dialog.title || '').includes('移除');
              const dedupePattern = /^確定要(刪除|清除|移除).*嗎[?？]?$/;
              const filteredLines = [];
              const extractedWarnings = [];
              lines.forEach((line, idx) => {
                if (warningPatterns.some((re) => re.test(line))) {
                  // 抽出警告文,去掉前面的 bullet 符號
                  extractedWarnings.push(line.replace(/^[•·・]\s*/, '').replace(/[。.]$/, ''));
                } else if (idx === 0 && titleHasDelete && dedupePattern.test(line)) {
                  // skip 重複句
                } else {
                  filteredLines.push(line);
                }
              });
              const effectiveMessage = filteredLines.join('\n');
              const autoWarning = extractedWarnings.length > 0 ? extractedWarnings.join('、') : null;

              return (
                <>
                  {effectiveMessage && (() => {
                    // 將 message 拆成「主標(第一行)」+「bullet 列」+「結尾段」
                    // 主標 = 沒以 • 開頭的第一行(通常是疑問句或結論句)
                    // bullet 列 = 連續以 • 開頭的行
                    // 結尾段 = bullet 之後若還有非 bullet 行
                    const msgLines = effectiveMessage.split('\n');
                    const headline = [];
                    const bullets = [];
                    const trailing = [];
                    let phase = 'head';
                    msgLines.forEach((line) => {
                      const trimmed = line.trim();
                      const isBullet = /^[•·・]\s/.test(trimmed);
                      if (isBullet) {
                        phase = 'bullet';
                        bullets.push(trimmed.replace(/^[•·・]\s*/, ''));
                      } else if (phase === 'head') {
                        if (trimmed) headline.push(trimmed);
                      } else {
                        if (trimmed) trailing.push(trimmed);
                      }
                    });

                    // highlight 邏輯共用函式
                    const renderHighlighted = (text) => {
                      const quantRe = /\d+(?:,\d+)*\s*(?:筆|個|項|張|次|天|月|年)/;
                      const virtualRe = /\(已刪\)|\(虛\)/;
                      const userWords = Array.isArray(dialog.highlightWords) ? dialog.highlightWords.filter(Boolean) : [];
                      const esc = (s) => s.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&');
                      const sortedUserWords = [...userWords].sort((a, b) => b.length - a.length);
                      const userRe = sortedUserWords.length > 0 ? sortedUserWords.map(esc).join('|') : null;
                      const fullRe = userRe
                        ? new RegExp(`(${quantRe.source}|${virtualRe.source}|${userRe})`, 'g')
                        : new RegExp(`(${quantRe.source}|${virtualRe.source})`, 'g');
                      const parts = text.split(fullRe);
                      const quantTest = new RegExp(`^${quantRe.source}$`);
                      const virtualTest = new RegExp(`^${virtualRe.source}$`);
                      const userTest = userRe ? new RegExp(`^(?:${userRe})$`) : null;
                      return parts.map((part, i) => {
                        if (!part) return null;
                        if (virtualTest.test(part)) {
                          // (虛) → 「虛擬」膠囊(綠);(已刪) → 「帳號已刪」膠囊(灰)
                          const isDeleted = part === '(已刪)';
                          const label = isDeleted ? '帳號已刪' : '虛擬';
                          return (
                            <span key={i} style={{
                              color: isDeleted ? 'var(--text-faint)' : 'var(--mint)',
                              fontSize: 11,
                              fontWeight: 500,
