                              marginLeft: 4,
                              padding: '1px 6px',
                              borderRadius: 4,
                              background: isDeleted ? 'rgba(140, 140, 140, 0.12)' : 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.12)',
                              verticalAlign: 'middle',
                              display: 'inline-block',
                            }}>{label}</span>
                          );
                        }
                        if (quantTest.test(part)) {
                          // 把 "1 筆" 拆成 "1" + "筆",中間用較大間距
                          const m = part.match(/^(\d+(?:,\d+)*)\s*(.+)$/);
                          if (m) {
                            return (
                              <span key={i} style={{ color: 'var(--pink)', fontWeight: 700, marginRight: 2 }}>
                                {m[1]}<span style={{ marginLeft: 4 }}>{m[2]}</span>
                              </span>
                            );
                          }
                          return (
                            <span key={i} style={{ color: 'var(--pink)', fontWeight: 700, marginRight: 2 }}>
                              {part}
                            </span>
                          );
                        }
                        if (userTest && userTest.test(part)) {
                          return (
                            <span key={i} style={{
                              color: isDanger ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--highlight)',
                              fontWeight: 700,
                            }}>
                              {part}
                            </span>
                          );
                        }
                        return <React.Fragment key={i}>{part}</React.Fragment>;
                      });
                    };

                    // 沒 bullet 的退化情況 → 沿用舊風格(避免破壞其他對話框)
                    if (bullets.length === 0) {
                      return (
                        <div style={{
                          padding: dialog.bigNumber ? '0 20px 14px' : (dialog.target ? '0 20px 10px' : '4px 20px 8px'),
                          fontSize: 14,
                          color: 'var(--text-dim)',
                          lineHeight: 1.6,
                          whiteSpace: 'pre-wrap',
                          textAlign: dialog.bigNumber ? 'center' : 'left',
                        }}>
                          {renderHighlighted(effectiveMessage)}
                        </div>
                      );
                    }

                    // 結構化呈現:主標(若有)+ bullet 列 + 結尾段(若有)
                    return (
                      <div style={{
                        padding: dialog.target ? '4px 20px 6px' : '14px 20px 6px',
                      }}>
                        {/* 主標:大字、深色,有焦點 */}
                        {headline.length > 0 && (
                          <div style={{
                            fontSize: 15,
                            color: 'var(--text)',
                            fontWeight: 600,
                            lineHeight: 1.5,
                            marginBottom: 10,
                          }}>
                            {renderHighlighted(headline.join('\n'))}
                          </div>
                        )}
                        {/* bullet 列:卡片化,每條獨立一行,有層次 */}
                        <div style={{
                          background: 'var(--bg)',
                          borderRadius: 10,
                          padding: '4px 14px',
                          display: 'flex',
                          flexDirection: 'column',
                        }}>
                          {bullets.map((b, i) => (
                            <div key={i} style={{
                              fontSize: 13,
                              color: 'var(--text-dim)',
                              lineHeight: 1.55,
                              display: 'flex',
                              gap: 8,
                              padding: '10px 0',
                              borderTop: i > 0 ? '1px solid var(--text-faint)' : 'none',
                              opacity: 1,
                            }}>
                              <span style={{
                                color: 'var(--text-faint)',
                                flexShrink: 0,
                                marginTop: 1,
                              }}>•</span>
                              <span>{renderHighlighted(b)}</span>
                            </div>
                          ))}
                        </div>
                        {/* 結尾段(若有) */}
                        {trailing.length > 0 && (
                          <div style={{
                            fontSize: 14,
                            color: 'var(--text-dim)',
                            lineHeight: 1.6,
                            marginTop: 10,
                          }}>
                            {renderHighlighted(trailing.join('\n'))}
                          </div>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    );
                  })()}
                  {/* 自動拆出來的警告(若 caller 沒明確設 dialog.warning,且偵測到警告句) */}
                  {!dialog.warning && autoWarning && (
                    <div style={{
                      margin: effectiveMessage ? '0 16px 4px' : '4px 16px 4px',
                      padding: '8px 12px',
                      background: 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.08)',
                      borderRadius: 6,
                      fontSize: 12.5,
                      color: 'var(--pink-text)',
                      fontWeight: 500,
                      display: 'flex',
                      alignItems: 'center',
                      gap: 8,
                    }}>
                      <TypeIcon name="warning" size={13} color="var(--pink-text)" />
                      <span>{autoWarning}</span>
                    </div>
                  )}
                </>
              );
            })()}
            {/* 警告字句(粉色 + icon) */}
            {dialog.warning && (
              <div style={{
                margin: '0 16px 14px',
                padding: '8px 12px',
                background: 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.08)',
                borderRadius: 6,
                fontSize: 13,
                color: 'var(--pink-text)',
                fontWeight: 500,
                display: 'flex',
                alignItems: 'center',
                gap: 8,
              }}>
                <TypeIcon name="warning" size={14} color="var(--pink-text)" />
                <span>{dialog.warning}</span>
              </div>
            )}
          </>
        )}

        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8, padding: '8px 16px 16px' }}>
          {!dialog.singleAction && (
            <button
              style={{
                flex: 1,
                border: '1px solid var(--pink)',
                borderRadius: 12,
                padding: '11px 0',
                fontSize: 15,
                fontWeight: 600,
                background: 'transparent',
                color: 'var(--pink-text)',
                cursor: 'pointer',
                boxSizing: 'border-box',
              }}
              onClick={onClose}
            >取消</button>
          )}
          <button
            style={{
              ...styles.saveBtn,
              flex: 1,
              padding: '12px 0',
              background: isDanger && hasChanges ? 'var(--mint)' : (isDanger ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--mint)'),
              color: 'var(--on-mint)',
              marginTop: 0,
              opacity: locked ? 0.4 : 1,
              cursor: locked ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
              boxSizing: 'border-box',
            }}
            onClick={async () => {
              if (locked) return;
              const fn = dialog.onConfirm;
              const before = dialog.beforeConfirm;
              if (before) {
                // 先關閉 dialog,等動畫,再執行 onConfirm
                onClose();
                try { await before(); } catch {}
                if (fn) fn();
              } else {
                onClose();
                if (fn) fn();
              }
            }}
          >{dialog.confirmText || '確定'}</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 編輯排序共用元件 ============
function EditOrderButton({ editMode, setEditMode }) {
  if (editMode) return null;
  return (
    <button style={styles.editOrderBtn} onClick={() => setEditMode && setEditMode(true)}>
      編輯排序
    </button>
  );
}

// 列表排序控制(chip + sheet),用於明細頁/統計頁/單日詳細頁
function ListSortControl({ sortMode, setSortMode }) {
  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false);
  const current = LIST_SORT_OPTIONS.find((o) => o.value === sortMode) || LIST_SORT_OPTIONS[0];
  // chip 上短標
  const shortLabel = sortMode === 'date_desc' ? '日期↓'
    : sortMode === 'date_asc' ? '日期↑'
    : sortMode === 'amount_desc' ? '金額↓'
    : '金額↑';
  return (
    <>
      <span
        style={{
          fontSize: 11,
          padding: '6px 4px 6px 8px',
          color: 'var(--text-dim)',
          cursor: 'pointer',
          WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
          userSelect: 'none',
          display: 'inline-flex',
          alignItems: 'center',
          justifyContent: 'center',
          gap: 2,
          lineHeight: 1,
          opacity: 0.85,
        }}
        onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); setOpen(true); }}
      >
        {shortLabel}
        <span style={{ fontSize: 9, opacity: 0.7 }}>▾</span>
      </span>
      {open && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setOpen(false)}>
          <div style={{ ...styles.pickerCard, maxWidth: 320 }} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>資料排序方式</div>
            <div style={{ padding: '4px 8px 12px' }}>
              {LIST_SORT_OPTIONS.map((opt) => {
                const active = opt.value === sortMode;
                return (
                  <button
                    key={opt.value}
                    style={{
                      width: '100%',
                      display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 12,
                      padding: '12px 14px', borderRadius: 10,
                      background: active ? 'rgba(126,224,192,0.10)' : 'transparent',
                      border: active ? '1.5px solid var(--mint)' : '1.5px solid transparent',
                      color: 'var(--text)', cursor: 'pointer', textAlign: 'left',
                      marginBottom: 4,
                    }}
                    onClick={() => {
                      setSortMode(opt.value);
                      setOpen(false);
                    }}
                  >
                    {/* radio */}
                    <span style={{
                      width: 18, height: 18, borderRadius: '50%',
                      border: active ? '5px solid var(--mint)' : '1.5px solid var(--border)',
                      flexShrink: 0,
                      background: active ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'transparent',
                      transition: 'all 0.15s',
                    }} />
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: active ? 600 : 400 }}>{opt.label}</span>
                  </button>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </>
  );
}

function EditModeBanner({ editMode, setEditMode }) {
  if (!editMode) return null;
  return (
    <div style={styles.editModeBannerFloat}>
      <span>編輯排序模式</span>
      <button style={styles.editDoneBtn} onClick={() => setEditMode(false)}>完成</button>
    </div>
  );
}

function Block({ blockKey, title, headerRight, editMode, isFirst, isLast, onMoveUp, onMoveDown, onReorder, children, inline, compactInline, disableReorder }) {
  const elRef = React.useRef(null);
  const [, forceUpdate] = React.useReducer((x) => x + 1, 0);

  // 把 onReorder 存進 ref,這樣它變化時不會觸發 useEffect 重跑(避免拖曳中被中斷)
  const onReorderRef = React.useRef(onReorder);
  React.useEffect(() => { onReorderRef.current = onReorder; }, [onReorder]);

  // 拖曳邏輯：只在 editMode 啟用,disableReorder 也跳過
  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (!editMode || disableReorder) return;
    const el = elRef.current;
    if (!el) return;

    // 進入 useEffect 時兜底:清掉任何殘留的拖曳樣式(克隆法只會留下 display)
    el.style.removeProperty('display');

    let draggedEl = null;
    let placeholder = null;
    let dragOffsetY = 0;
    let startY = null;
    let startX = null;
    let moved = false;
    let lastBoundary = null; // 'top' | 'bottom' | null,避免重複觸發 toast
    let boundaryToastEl = null;
    let boundaryToastTimer = null;

    // 顯示邊界 toast(薄荷綠風格 + 精緻微調)
    const showBoundaryToast = (type) => {
      if (boundaryToastEl) boundaryToastEl.remove();
      if (boundaryToastTimer) clearTimeout(boundaryToastTimer);

      const isTop = type === 'top';
      // 精簡箭頭 + 底線,但線條更細緻(2.2 不是 3)
      const arrow = isTop
        ? '<svg width="23" height="23" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><line x1="12" y1="19" x2="12" y2="6"/><polyline points="5 13 12 6 19 13"/><line x1="5" y1="4" x2="19" y2="4" opacity="0.6"/></svg>'
        : '<svg width="23" height="23" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><line x1="12" y1="5" x2="12" y2="18"/><polyline points="19 11 12 18 5 11"/><line x1="5" y1="20" x2="19" y2="20" opacity="0.6"/></svg>';
      const text = isTop ? '已到頂端' : '已到底端';

      boundaryToastEl = document.createElement('div');
      boundaryToastEl.style.cssText = `
        position:fixed;
        top:50%;left:50%;
        transform:translate(-50%,-50%) scale(0.88);
        background:linear-gradient(135deg, #8be8cc 0%, #7ee0c0 100%);
        color:#0a1410;
        padding:14px 23px;
        border-radius:17px;
        font-size:17px;
        font-weight:600;
        letter-spacing:0.4px;
        z-index:10000;
        pointer-events:none;
        box-shadow:
          0 14px 38px rgba(0,0,0,0.45),
          0 0 0 1px rgba(255,255,255,0.15) inset,
          0 1px 0 rgba(255,255,255,0.3) inset,
          0 0 60px rgba(126,224,192,0.35);
        display:flex;
        align-items:center;
        gap:10px;
        opacity:0;
        transition:transform 0.22s cubic-bezier(0.2, 0.8, 0.2, 1), opacity 0.18s ease-out;
      `;
      boundaryToastEl.innerHTML = `<span style="display:flex;align-items:center;opacity:0.85;">${arrow}</span><span>${text}</span>`;
      document.body.appendChild(boundaryToastEl);

      // 下一幀觸發進場
      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        if (boundaryToastEl) {
          boundaryToastEl.style.transform = 'translate(-50%,-50%) scale(1)';
          boundaryToastEl.style.opacity = '1';
        }
      });

      boundaryToastTimer = setTimeout(() => {
        if (boundaryToastEl) {
          // 淡出離場
          boundaryToastEl.style.opacity = '0';
          boundaryToastEl.style.transform = 'translate(-50%,-50%) scale(0.95)';
          const toRemove = boundaryToastEl;
          boundaryToastEl = null;
          setTimeout(() => toRemove.remove(), 180);
        }
        boundaryToastTimer = null;
      }, 700);

      if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([20, 40, 20]);
    };

    let dragClone = null; // 浮起的克隆副本

    // 清除畫面上所有殘留的 placeholder 和 clone
    const cleanupStray = () => {
      document.querySelectorAll('[data-placeholder="true"]').forEach((n) => n.remove());
      document.querySelectorAll('[data-drag-clone="true"]').forEach((n) => n.remove());
    };

    let dragScroller = null; // cache 住拖曳時的 scroll 容器

    const startDragging = (clientX, clientY) => {
      // 開始前先清理所有殘留(兜底,避免前一次拖曳失敗留下 DOM)
      cleanupStray();
      // 也清掉可能殘留的 display:none on 其他 Block
      document.querySelectorAll('[data-block-key]').forEach((n) => {
        if (n !== el && n.style.display === 'none') n.style.removeProperty('display');
      });

      draggedEl = el;
      const rect = el.getBoundingClientRect();
      dragOffsetY = clientY - rect.top;

      // 預先查找 scroll 容器(拖曳中不再每幀查找,避免 lag)
      dragScroller = el.closest('[data-scroll-container]');
      if (!dragScroller) {
        let node = el.parentNode;
        while (node && node !== document.body) {
          const os = getComputedStyle(node).overflowY;
          if ((os === 'auto' || os === 'scroll') && node.scrollHeight > node.clientHeight) {
            dragScroller = node;
            break;
          }
          node = node.parentNode;
        }
      }

      // 建立佔位符 — 高度精準對齊被拖卡片,不複製 margin 避免疊加
      // 中央放「放在這裡」文字提示(薄荷綠);依卡片寬高動態調整字級,過小則改顯示三個圓點
      placeholder = document.createElement('div');
      placeholder.setAttribute('data-placeholder', 'true');
      placeholder.style.cssText = `height:${rect.height}px;margin:0;border-radius:12px;background:rgba(126,224,192,0.18);border:2px dashed rgba(126,224,192,0.85);box-sizing:border-box;transition:none;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;overflow:hidden;`;
      const labelEl = document.createElement('div');
      // 字級候選(由大到小),挑出寬高都裝得下的最大級
      const sizeCandidates = [18, 15, 13, 11];
      // 「放在這裡」+ letterSpacing 1px,單字寬約 fontSize+1,左右安全留白 24px
      const charCount = 4;
      const horizontalPadding = 24;
      // 高度需求:字級 + 上下呼吸 8px
      const minHeightFor = (fs) => fs + 8;
      // 寬度需求:字數 × (字級 + letterSpacing) + 兩側留白
      const minWidthFor = (fs) => charCount * (fs + 1) + horizontalPadding;
      let chosen = null;
      for (const fs of sizeCandidates) {
        if (rect.height >= minHeightFor(fs) && rect.width >= minWidthFor(fs)) {
          chosen = fs;
          break;
        }
      }
      const showText = chosen !== null;
      const fontSize = chosen ?? 11;
      labelEl.style.cssText = `color:var(--mint, #7ee0c0);font-size:${fontSize}px;font-weight:600;letter-spacing:1px;opacity:0.85;pointer-events:none;white-space:nowrap;`;
      labelEl.textContent = showText ? '放在這裡' : '• • •';
      placeholder.appendChild(labelEl);
      el.parentNode.insertBefore(placeholder, el);

      // 建立克隆副本用於浮起顯示
      dragClone = el.cloneNode(true);
      dragClone.setAttribute('data-drag-clone', 'true');
      // 讀取原元素 computed 圓角(可能是 "12px" 或 "12px 12px 12px 12px"),
      // 套到 dragClone 讓陰影/描邊跟著彎角走
      const elRadius = getComputedStyle(el).borderRadius || '12px';
      dragClone.style.cssText = `position:fixed;top:${rect.top}px;left:${rect.left}px;width:${rect.width}px;z-index:9998;opacity:0.55;transform:scale(1.03) rotate(-0.5deg);box-shadow:0 16px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.6), 0 0 0 2px rgba(126,224,192,0.4);pointer-events:none;margin:0;border-radius:${elRadius};`;
      document.body.appendChild(dragClone);

      // 原元素用 visibility:hidden 保留佔位空間,但因為有 placeholder 接替,改用 display:none 讓 placeholder 接管
      el.style.display = 'none';

      // 鎖定 body 的 touch 行為,防止瀏覽器發送 touchcancel 中斷拖曳
      document.body.style.touchAction = 'none';
      document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';
      document.body.style.webkitUserSelect = 'none';
      // 設置 flag 讓 useSwipeBack 等手勢機制跳過本次
      document.body.setAttribute('data-drag-active', 'true');

      if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(30);
    };

    // 邊緣自動捲動：用 requestAnimationFrame 取得與螢幕同步的平滑捲動
    let autoScrollRaf = null;
    let autoScrollSpeed = 0; // 正值=向下捲，負值=向上捲

    const autoScrollTick = () => {
      if (autoScrollSpeed === 0) {
        autoScrollRaf = null;
        return;
      }
      if (dragScroller && dragScroller !== document.body) {
        dragScroller.scrollTop += autoScrollSpeed;
      } else {
        window.scrollBy(0, autoScrollSpeed);
      }
      autoScrollRaf = requestAnimationFrame(autoScrollTick);
    };

    const startAutoScroll = () => {
      if (autoScrollRaf) return;
      autoScrollRaf = requestAnimationFrame(autoScrollTick);
    };

    const stopAutoScroll = () => {
      if (autoScrollRaf) {
        cancelAnimationFrame(autoScrollRaf);
        autoScrollRaf = null;
      }
      autoScrollSpeed = 0;
    };

    const moveDragging = (clientY) => {
      if (!draggedEl || !placeholder || !dragClone) return;

      // auto-scroll:頂端觸發範圍更大(因為狀態列/標題擋住手指難以觸及),底端保持
      const EDGE_TOP = 120;
      const EDGE_BOTTOM = 80;
      const MAX_SPEED = 14;
      const viewportH = window.innerHeight;
      if (clientY < EDGE_TOP) {
        const ratio = (EDGE_TOP - clientY) / EDGE_TOP;
        autoScrollSpeed = -Math.max(2, Math.ceil(ratio * ratio * MAX_SPEED));
        startAutoScroll();
      } else if (clientY > viewportH - EDGE_BOTTOM) {
        const ratio = (clientY - (viewportH - EDGE_BOTTOM)) / EDGE_BOTTOM;
        autoScrollSpeed = Math.max(2, Math.ceil(ratio * ratio * MAX_SPEED));
        startAutoScroll();
      } else {
        stopAutoScroll();
      }

      // 找同父層的其他 block 節點,決定插入位置
      const parent = placeholder.parentNode;
      if (!parent) return;
      const siblings = Array.from(parent.children).filter(
        (c) => c !== draggedEl && c !== placeholder && c.hasAttribute('data-block-key')
      );
      // 找第一個中點大於 clientY 的 sibling,插到它前面
      let insertedBefore = null;
      for (const sib of siblings) {
        const r = sib.getBoundingClientRect();
        const mid = r.top + r.height / 2;
        if (clientY < mid) {
          insertedBefore = sib;
          break;
        }
      }
      if (insertedBefore) {
        parent.insertBefore(placeholder, insertedBefore);
      } else {
        // 沒找到 → 放最後
        const last = siblings[siblings.length - 1];
        if (last) parent.insertBefore(placeholder, last.nextSibling);
      }

      // 邊界回饋:若 placeholder 已在最頂/最底,且手指繼續往外推,加阻力位移 + 視覺提示
      // 判斷方式:檢查 placeholder 在 parent.children 裡的位置相對於 siblings
      const allChildren = Array.from(parent.children);
      const phIdx = allChildren.indexOf(placeholder);
      // 檢查 placeholder 之前/之後還有沒有其他 data-block-key 節點
      let hasBlockBefore = false;
      let hasBlockAfter = false;
      for (let i = 0; i < allChildren.length; i++) {
        const c = allChildren[i];
        if (c === placeholder || c === draggedEl) continue;
        if (!c.hasAttribute('data-block-key')) continue;
        if (i < phIdx) hasBlockBefore = true;
        else hasBlockAfter = true;
      }
      const atTop = !hasBlockBefore;
      const atBottom = !hasBlockAfter;

      // 剛觸及邊界時觸發 toast(只觸發一次,離開再回來才會再觸發)
      const currentBoundary = atTop ? 'top' : atBottom ? 'bottom' : null;
      if (currentBoundary !== lastBoundary) {
        if (currentBoundary === 'top') showBoundaryToast('top');
        else if (currentBoundary === 'bottom') showBoundaryToast('bottom');
        lastBoundary = currentBoundary;
      }

      const phRect = placeholder.getBoundingClientRect();
      // 橡皮筋阻力:到頂/底後,clone 位置會"拉不動",只能用 1/3 速度跟隨
      // 原 top = clientY - dragOffsetY,超出邊界後改為阻尼計算
      let finalTop = clientY - dragOffsetY;
      if (atTop && clientY < phRect.top) {
        // placeholder 頂邊 = phRect.top,這是理論上能到的最高點
        // 對應的 clone top = phRect.top - dragOffsetY
        const maxTop = phRect.top - dragOffsetY;
        const overshoot = maxTop - finalTop; // 越過的量
        finalTop = maxTop - overshoot / 3;    // 只讓 clone 跟隨 1/3,剩下 2/3 是阻力
      } else if (atBottom && clientY > phRect.bottom) {
        const minTop = phRect.bottom - dragOffsetY - (dragClone.offsetHeight || 60);
        // 其實是 clone 底邊到 phRect.bottom 就該停,但因為 height 難取,簡化直接用 clientY 阻尼
        const maxClientY = phRect.bottom;
        const overshoot = clientY - maxClientY;
        finalTop = (maxClientY - dragOffsetY) + overshoot / 3;
      }
      dragClone.style.top = finalTop + 'px';
    };

    const endDragging = () => {
      if (!draggedEl) return;
      stopAutoScroll();
      // 讀取新順序
      const parent = placeholder ? placeholder.parentNode : null;
      let newOrder = null;
      if (parent) {
        const keys = [];
        Array.from(parent.children).forEach((c) => {
          if (c === placeholder) {
            keys.push(blockKey);
          } else if (c !== draggedEl && c.hasAttribute('data-block-key')) {
            keys.push(c.getAttribute('data-block-key'));
          }
        });
        newOrder = keys;
      }
      // 清理 — 克隆方案下,原元素沒有被加 inline style,只需恢復 display/visibility
      if (placeholder) { placeholder.remove(); placeholder = null; }
      if (dragClone) { dragClone.remove(); dragClone = null; }
      if (draggedEl) {
        draggedEl.style.removeProperty('display');
        draggedEl.style.removeProperty('visibility');
      }
      draggedEl = null;
      lastBoundary = null;
      if (boundaryToastEl) { boundaryToastEl.remove(); boundaryToastEl = null; }
      if (boundaryToastTimer) { clearTimeout(boundaryToastTimer); boundaryToastTimer = null; }

      // 解鎖 body touch
      document.body.style.removeProperty('touch-action');
      document.body.style.removeProperty('user-select');
      document.body.style.removeProperty('-webkit-user-select');
      document.body.removeAttribute('data-drag-active');

      if (newOrder && onReorderRef.current) onReorderRef.current(newOrder);
    };

    let longPressTimer = null;

    const onTouchStart = (e) => {
      // 忽略可互動元素
      if (e.target.closest('input, select, textarea, button')) return;
      const t = e.touches[0];
      startX = t.clientX;
      startY = t.clientY;
      moved = false;
      // 長按 400ms 才進入拖曳，期間手指移動（捲動）則取消
      longPressTimer = setTimeout(() => {
        longPressTimer = null;
        startDragging(startX, startY);
      }, 400);
    };

    const onTouchMove = (e) => {
      const t = e.touches[0];
      // 尚未啟動拖曳：如果手指移動超過 10px，取消長按計時器，讓頁面自然捲動
      if (longPressTimer) {
        if (Math.abs(t.clientX - startX) > 10 || Math.abs(t.clientY - startY) > 10) {
          clearTimeout(longPressTimer);
          longPressTimer = null;
        }
        return;
      }
      if (!draggedEl) return;
      if (Math.abs(t.clientX - startX) > 3 || Math.abs(t.clientY - startY) > 3) moved = true;
      moveDragging(t.clientY);
      if (e.cancelable) e.preventDefault();
    };

    const onTouchEnd = () => {
      if (longPressTimer) {
        clearTimeout(longPressTimer);
        longPressTimer = null;
      }
      if (draggedEl) endDragging();
    };

    // touchcancel 只在尚未拖曳時清長按計時器,已進入拖曳則忽略(避免瀏覽器誤發中斷拖曳)
    const onTouchCancel = () => {
      if (longPressTimer) {
        clearTimeout(longPressTimer);
        longPressTimer = null;
      }
      // 拖曳中的 touchcancel 故意忽略,等 touchend 才結束
    };

    let mouseLongPressTimer = null;

    const onMouseDown = (e) => {
      if (e.target.closest('input, select, textarea, button')) return;
      startX = e.clientX;
      startY = e.clientY;
      moved = false;
      mouseLongPressTimer = setTimeout(() => {
        mouseLongPressTimer = null;
        startDragging(startX, startY);
      }, 400);
    };

    const onMouseMove = (e) => {
      if (mouseLongPressTimer) {
        if (Math.abs(e.clientX - startX) > 10 || Math.abs(e.clientY - startY) > 10) {
          clearTimeout(mouseLongPressTimer);
          mouseLongPressTimer = null;
        }
        return;
      }
      if (!draggedEl) return;
      moveDragging(e.clientY);
    };

    const onMouseUp = () => {
      if (mouseLongPressTimer) {
        clearTimeout(mouseLongPressTimer);
        mouseLongPressTimer = null;
      }
      if (draggedEl) endDragging();
    };

    el.addEventListener('touchstart', onTouchStart, { passive: true });
    document.addEventListener('touchmove', onTouchMove, { passive: false });
    document.addEventListener('touchend', onTouchEnd);
    document.addEventListener('touchcancel', onTouchCancel);
    el.addEventListener('mousedown', onMouseDown);
    document.addEventListener('mousemove', onMouseMove);
    document.addEventListener('mouseup', onMouseUp);

    return () => {
      if (longPressTimer) clearTimeout(longPressTimer);
      if (mouseLongPressTimer) clearTimeout(mouseLongPressTimer);
      el.removeEventListener('touchstart', onTouchStart);
      document.removeEventListener('touchmove', onTouchMove);
      document.removeEventListener('touchend', onTouchEnd);
      document.removeEventListener('touchcancel', onTouchCancel);
      el.removeEventListener('mousedown', onMouseDown);
      document.removeEventListener('mousemove', onMouseMove);
      document.removeEventListener('mouseup', onMouseUp);
      // 清理殘留樣式
      if (autoScrollRaf) cancelAnimationFrame(autoScrollRaf);
      if (dragClone && dragClone.parentNode) {
        dragClone.remove();
      }
      if (draggedEl) {
        draggedEl.style.removeProperty('display');
        draggedEl.style.removeProperty('visibility');
      }
      if (placeholder && placeholder.parentNode) {
        placeholder.remove();
      }
      // 保險:解鎖 body
      document.body.style.removeProperty('touch-action');
      document.body.style.removeProperty('user-select');
      document.body.style.removeProperty('-webkit-user-select');
      document.body.removeAttribute('data-drag-active');
      if (boundaryToastEl) boundaryToastEl.remove();
      if (boundaryToastTimer) clearTimeout(boundaryToastTimer);
    };
  }, [editMode, blockKey]);

  if (inline && !editMode) {
    // inline 模式：標題在左，內容在右（並排）。若沒 title 就不 render title 欄位
    return (
      <div style={{ ...styles.blockInline, ...(compactInline ? { marginBottom: 0 } : {}) }}>
        {title && <div style={styles.blockInlineTitle}>{title}</div>}
        <div style={styles.blockInlineContent}>{children}</div>
        {headerRight && <div style={styles.blockInlineRight}>{headerRight}</div>}
      </div>
    );
  }
  // compactInline + editMode:不顯示控制列,只用拖曳排序(節省空間)
  const isCompactEditMode = editMode && compactInline;
  // compactInline + 非 editMode:扁平樣式(無外框、無 padding、無底距),靠 children 自帶卡片做視覺分隔
  const isCompactView = !editMode && compactInline;

  return (
    <div
      ref={elRef}
      data-block-key={blockKey}
      style={{
        ...styles.block,
        ...(editMode ? styles.blockEdit : {}),
        ...(editMode ? { cursor: 'grab' } : {}),
        ...(isCompactEditMode ? { padding: '3px 6px', marginBottom: 2 } : {}),
        ...(isCompactView ? { padding: 0, marginBottom: 0, border: 'none' } : {}),
      }}
    >
      {(title || editMode) && !isCompactEditMode && (
        <div style={styles.blockHeader}>
          <div style={styles.blockTitle}>
            {editMode && <span style={styles.blockHandle}>☰</span>}
            <span>{title}</span>
          </div>
          {editMode && !disableReorder ? (
            <div style={styles.blockMoveBtns}>
              <button
                style={{ ...styles.moveBtn, opacity: isFirst ? 0.3 : 1 }}
                onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); if (!isFirst) onMoveUp(); }}
                disabled={isFirst}
              >↑</button>
              <button
                style={{ ...styles.moveBtn, opacity: isLast ? 0.3 : 1 }}
                onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); if (!isLast) onMoveDown(); }}
                disabled={isLast}
              >↓</button>
            </div>
          ) : headerRight}
        </div>
      )}
      <div style={editMode ? { pointerEvents: 'none' } : {}}>
        {children}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 首頁 ============
// ============ 代墊詳細頁(收回操作 / 編輯) ============
function LendDetailSheet({ state, lendOut, onClose, onCollect, onEdit, onDelete, setConfirmDialog, toast, toastRich }) {
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(onClose);
  const [showCollectSheet, setShowCollectSheet] = useState(false);
  const [collectMode, setCollectMode] = useState('full'); // 'full' | 'partial'
  const [collectAccountId, setCollectAccountId] = useState(state.accounts.find((a) => !a.isSystem)?.id || '');
  const [partialAmount, setPartialAmount] = useState('');

  const fromAcct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === lendOut.accountId);
  const remaining = lendOut.amount - (lendOut.lendMeta?.collectedAmount || 0);
  const expDate = lendOut.lendMeta?.expectDate;
  const debtor = lendOut.lendMeta?.debtor;
  const isPartial = lendOut.lendMeta?.status === 'partial';
  const today = todayStr();
  const overdue = expDate && expDate < today;

  // 已收回紀錄(partial 時可能有多筆 collect_out 紀錄)
  const collectRecords = state.transactions
    .filter((t) => t.lendId === lendOut.lendId && t.transferRole === 'lend_collect_in')
    .sort((a, b) => b.date.localeCompare(a.date));

  const handleConfirmCollect = () => {
    const amt = collectMode === 'full' ? remaining : parseFloat(partialAmount);
    if (!amt || isNaN(amt) || amt <= 0) {
      toast && toast('請輸入有效金額');
      return;
    }
    if (amt > remaining) {
      toast && toast(`金額超過未收回餘額(${fmt(remaining)})`);
      return;
    }
    if (!collectAccountId) {
      toast && toast('請選擇收回到的帳戶');
      return;
    }
    onCollect(lendOut, amt, collectAccountId);
    setShowCollectSheet(false);
    onClose();
  };

  return (
    <div
      data-sheet="true"
      style={{
        ...styles.sheet,
        transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
        transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
      }}
      ref={swipe.ref}
    >
      <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
        <div style={{ width: 80 }} />
        <div style={{ ...styles.sheetTitle, color: 'var(--text)' }}>代墊詳細</div>
        <div style={{ minWidth: 80, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'flex-end', paddingRight: 12 }}>
          <button
            style={{
              background: 'transparent', border: 'none', color: 'var(--text-dim)',
              fontSize: 22, cursor: 'pointer', padding: 4,
            }}
            onClick={onClose}
          >×</button>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div style={styles.sheetScroll}>
        {/* 主資訊卡 */}
        <div style={{
          margin: '8px 16px 16px', padding: 20, borderRadius: 16,
          background: 'rgba(126,224,192,0.08)', border: '1.5px solid var(--mint)',
        }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 4 }}>未收回餘額</div>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 36, fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--mint-text)', letterSpacing: '-0.5px' }}>
            {fmt(remaining)}
          </div>
          {isPartial && (
            <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginTop: 6 }}>
              原代墊 {fmt(lendOut.amount)},已收回 {fmt(lendOut.lendMeta.collectedAmount)}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* 詳細欄位 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 16px', borderRadius: 12, background: 'var(--bg-card-2, rgba(127,127,127,0.05))', overflow: 'hidden' }}>
          {debtor && (
            <div style={{ padding: '12px 16px', borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border-soft)', display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontSize: 13 }}>對方</span>
              <span style={{ fontWeight: 500 }}>{debtor}</span>
            </div>
          )}
          <div style={{ padding: '12px 16px', borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border-soft)', display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
            <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontSize: 13 }}>付款帳戶</span>
            <span style={{ fontWeight: 500 }}>{fromAcct?.name || '(未知)'}</span>
          </div>
          <div style={{ padding: '12px 16px', borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border-soft)', display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
            <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontSize: 13 }}>代墊日期</span>
            <span style={{ fontWeight: 500 }}>{lendOut.date.replace(/-/g, '/')}</span>
          </div>
          <div style={{ padding: '12px 16px', borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border-soft)', display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
            <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontSize: 13 }}>預計收回</span>
            <span style={{ fontWeight: 500, color: overdue ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--text)' }}>
              {expDate ? `${expDate.replace(/-/g, '/')}${overdue ? ' (逾期)' : ''}` : '未設定'}
            </span>
          </div>
          <div style={{ padding: '12px 16px', display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'flex-start', gap: 12 }}>
            <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontSize: 13, flexShrink: 0 }}>備註</span>
            <span style={{ fontWeight: 500, textAlign: 'right', wordBreak: 'break-word' }}>
              {lendOut.note || '—'}
            </span>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 已收回紀錄(若有) */}
        {collectRecords.length > 0 && (
          <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 16px' }}>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', padding: '0 4px 6px' }}>已收回紀錄</div>
            <div style={{ borderRadius: 12, background: 'var(--bg-card-2, rgba(127,127,127,0.05))', overflow: 'hidden' }}>
              {collectRecords.map((r, i) => {
                const acc = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === r.accountId);
                return (
                  <div
                    key={r.id}
                    style={{
                      padding: '10px 16px', display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between',
                      borderBottom: i === collectRecords.length - 1 ? 'none' : '1px solid var(--border-soft)',
                    }}
                  >
                    <div>
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 13 }}>{r.date.replace(/-/g, '/')}</div>
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>收回到 {acc?.name || '(未知)'}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600, color: 'var(--mint-text)' }}>+{fmt(r.amount)}</div>
                  </div>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* 動作按鈕 */}
        <div style={{ padding: '0 16px 16px', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 10 }}>
          <button
            style={{
              padding: '14px', borderRadius: 12, border: 'none', cursor: 'pointer',
              background: 'var(--mint)', color: 'var(--on-mint)',
              fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 600,
            }}
            onClick={() => { setCollectMode('full'); setShowCollectSheet(true); }}
          >
            全額收回({fmt(remaining)})
          </button>
          <button
            style={{
              padding: '14px', borderRadius: 12, border: '1.5px solid var(--mint)', cursor: 'pointer',
              background: 'transparent', color: 'var(--mint-text)',
              fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 600,
            }}
            onClick={() => { setCollectMode('partial'); setPartialAmount(''); setShowCollectSheet(true); }}
          >
            部分收回
          </button>
          <button
            style={{
              padding: '12px', borderRadius: 12, border: 'none', cursor: 'pointer',
              background: 'transparent', color: 'var(--text-dim)',
              fontSize: 14,
            }}
            onClick={() => onEdit(lendOut)}
          >編輯代墊資訊</button>
          <button
            style={{
              padding: '12px', borderRadius: 12, border: 'none', cursor: 'pointer',
              background: 'transparent', color: 'var(--pink)',
              fontSize: 14,
            }}
            onClick={() => {
              setConfirmDialog && setConfirmDialog({
                title: '刪除代墊紀錄',
                message: '確定要刪除這筆代墊嗎?\n相關的收回紀錄也會一併移除。',
                confirmText: '刪除',
                danger: true,
                onConfirm: () => {
                  onDelete(lendOut);
                  onClose();
                },
              });
            }}
          >刪除這筆代墊</button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 收回對話框 */}
      {showCollectSheet && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowCollectSheet(false)}>
          <div style={{ ...styles.pickerCard, maxWidth: 360 }} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>
              {collectMode === 'full' ? '確認全額收回' : '部分收回'}
            </div>
            <div style={{ padding: '12px 20px 20px' }}>
              {/* 金額 */}
              <div style={{ marginBottom: 16 }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6 }}>收回金額</div>
                {collectMode === 'full' ? (
                  <div style={{
                    fontSize: 28, fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--mint-text)',
                    padding: '8px 12px', borderRadius: 10,
                    background: 'rgba(126,224,192,0.10)',
                  }}>
                    {fmt(remaining)}
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <input
                    type="number"
                    inputMode="decimal"
                    value={partialAmount}
                    onChange={(e) => setPartialAmount(e.target.value)}
                    placeholder={`最多 ${fmt(remaining)}`}
                    style={{
                      width: '100%', padding: '10px 12px', fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 600,
                      background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
                      border: '1.5px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 10,
                      outline: 'none', boxSizing: 'border-box',
                    }}
                  />
                )}
              </div>
              {/* 收回到哪個帳戶 */}
              <div style={{ marginBottom: 16 }}>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6 }}>收回到</div>
                <select
                  value={collectAccountId}
                  onChange={(e) => setCollectAccountId(e.target.value)}
                  style={{
                    width: '100%', padding: '10px 12px', fontSize: 14,
                    background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
                    border: '1.5px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 10,
                    outline: 'none', boxSizing: 'border-box',
                  }}
                >
                  {state.accounts.filter((a) => !a.isSystem).map((a) => (
                    <option key={a.id} value={a.id}>{a.name}</option>
                  ))}
                </select>
              </div>
              {/* 按鈕 */}
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 10 }}>
                <button
                  style={{
                    flex: 1, padding: '12px', borderRadius: 10, border: '1.5px solid var(--border)',
                    background: 'transparent', color: 'var(--text)', cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: 14,
                  }}
                  onClick={() => setShowCollectSheet(false)}
                >取消</button>
                <button
                  style={{
                    flex: 1, padding: '12px', borderRadius: 10, border: 'none',
                    background: 'var(--mint)', color: 'var(--on-mint)', cursor: 'pointer',
                    fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600,
                  }}
                  onClick={handleConfirmCollect}
                >確認收回</button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}


// ============ 股票賣出 Sheet ============
function SellSheet({ state, account, onClose, onConfirm, toast }) {
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(onClose);
  const currentBalance = calcBalance(account, state.transactions);

  const [principal, setPrincipal] = useState(String(currentBalance > 0 ? currentBalance : 0));
  const [received, setReceived] = useState('');
  const [date, setDate] = useState(todayStr());
  const [showDatePicker, setShowDatePicker] = useState(false);
  const [note, setNote] = useState('');
  // 收款帳戶:預設第一個非投資、非系統的帳戶
  const defaultToAcct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id !== account.id && a.type !== 'invest' && !a.isSystem);
  const [toAccountId, setToAccountId] = useState(defaultToAcct?.id || '');
  const [showToSheet, setShowToSheet] = useState(false);
  // 損益分類(自動推測,但可改)
  // 美股 → 美股失利,台股 → 台股失利;其他 → 留空讓使用者選
  const guessPnlSubLoss = () => {
    if (account.name.includes('美股')) return '美股失利';
    if (account.name.includes('台股') || account.name.includes('股票')) return '台股失利';
    return '';
  };

  const principalNum = parseFloat(principal) || 0;
  const receivedNum = parseFloat(received) || 0;
  const pnl = receivedNum - principalNum;

  const toAcct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === toAccountId);

  const handleSubmit = () => {
    if (!principalNum) { toast && toast('請輸入本金'); return; }
    if (principalNum > currentBalance) {
      toast && toast(`本金不能超過投資帳戶餘額(${fmt(currentBalance)})`);
      return;
    }
    if (!received || isNaN(receivedNum)) { toast && toast('請輸入實際拿回金額'); return; }
    if (receivedNum < 0) { toast && toast('拿回金額不能為負'); return; }
    if (!toAccountId) { toast && toast('請選擇收款帳戶'); return; }
    onConfirm({
      fromId: account.id,
      toId: toAccountId,
      principal: principalNum,
      received: receivedNum,
      date,
      note: note.trim(),
      pnlCategory: pnl >= 0 ? '股票相關' : '投資失利',
      pnlSubCategory: pnl >= 0 ? '獲利了結' : guessPnlSubLoss(),
    });
  };

  // 日期選擇器
  if (showDatePicker) {
    return (
      <DatePicker
        value={date}
        onChange={setDate}
        onClose={() => setShowDatePicker(false)}
      />
    );
  }

  const wd = ['日','一','二','三','四','五','六'][new Date(date).getDay()];

  return (
    <div
      data-sheet="true"
      style={{
        ...styles.sheet,
        transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
        transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
      }}
      ref={swipe.ref}
    >
      <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
        <button
          style={{
            background: 'transparent', border: 'none', color: 'var(--text-dim)',
            fontSize: 22, cursor: 'pointer', padding: '6px 12px',
          }}
          onClick={onClose}
        >×</button>
        <div style={{ ...styles.sheetTitle, color: 'var(--text)' }}>賣出 / 結算</div>
        <div style={{ width: 50 }} />
      </div>

      <div style={styles.sheetScroll}>
        {/* 從哪裡賣 — 固定資訊卡 */}
        <div style={{
          margin: '8px 16px 12px', padding: 14, borderRadius: 12,
          background: 'rgba(126,224,192,0.08)', border: '1.5px solid var(--mint)',
        }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 4 }}>賣出來源</div>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 600 }}>{account.name}</div>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginTop: 4 }}>
            目前餘額:{fmt(currentBalance)}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 本金 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>本金(投入金額)</div>
          <input
            type="number"
            inputMode="decimal"
            value={principal}
            onChange={(e) => setPrincipal(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="0"
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '12px 14px', fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 600,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
              border: '1.5px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 12,
              outline: 'none', boxSizing: 'border-box',
            }}
          />
          <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 4, paddingLeft: 4 }}>
            預設帶入投資帳戶當前餘額;部分賣出時請手動輸入
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 實際拿回 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>實際拿回</div>
          <input
            type="number"
            inputMode="decimal"
            value={received}
            onChange={(e) => setReceived(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="0"
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '12px 14px', fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 600,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
              border: '1.5px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 12,
              outline: 'none', boxSizing: 'border-box',
            }}
          />
        </div>

        {/* 損益預覽 */}
        {received !== '' && !isNaN(receivedNum) && principalNum > 0 && (
          <div style={{
            margin: '0 16px 14px', padding: '12px 16px', borderRadius: 12,
            background: pnl > 0 ? 'rgba(126,224,192,0.10)' :
                        pnl < 0 ? 'rgba(229,129,138,0.10)' :
                        'var(--bg-card-2, rgba(127,127,127,0.05))',
            border: pnl > 0 ? '1.5px solid var(--mint)' :
                    pnl < 0 ? '1.5px solid var(--pink)' :
                    '1.5px solid var(--border)',
            display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center',
          }}>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>
              {pnl > 0 ? '獲利' : pnl < 0 ? '虧損' : '損益'}
            </div>
            <div style={{
              fontSize: 22, fontWeight: 700,
              color: pnl > 0 ? 'var(--mint-text)' : pnl < 0 ? 'var(--pink-text)' : 'var(--text-dim)',
            }}>
              {pnl > 0 ? '+' : pnl < 0 ? '-' : ''}{fmt(Math.abs(pnl))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* 收款帳戶 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>收款帳戶(錢進到哪)</div>
          <div
            style={{
              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10,
              padding: '12px 14px', borderRadius: 12,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', border: '1.5px solid var(--border)',
              cursor: 'pointer',
            }}
            onClick={() => setShowToSheet(true)}
          >
            {toAcct ? (
              <>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 500, flex: 1 }}>{toAcct.name}</div>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>{fmt(calcBalance(toAcct, state.transactions))}</div>
              </>
            ) : (
              <div style={{ fontSize: 14, color: 'var(--text-faint)', flex: 1 }}>選擇收款帳戶</div>
            )}
            <div style={{ fontSize: 18, color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>›</div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 日期 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>日期</div>
          <div
            style={{
              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', padding: '12px 14px', borderRadius: 12,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', border: '1.5px solid var(--border)',
              cursor: 'pointer',
            }}
            onClick={() => setShowDatePicker(true)}
          >
            <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 500, flex: 1 }}>
              {date.replace(/-/g, '/')}
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginLeft: 6, fontSize: 13 }}>({wd})</span>
            </div>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 18, color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>›</div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 備註 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 14px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>備註</div>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={note}
            onChange={(e) => setNote(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="選填(例如:賣鴻海)"
            maxLength={100}
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '12px 14px', fontSize: 14,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
              border: '1.5px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 12,
              outline: 'none', boxSizing: 'border-box',
            }}
          />
        </div>

        {/* 確認按鈕 */}
        <div style={{ padding: '0 16px 16px' }}>
          <button
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '14px', borderRadius: 12, border: 'none',
              background: 'var(--mint)', color: 'var(--on-mint)',
              fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer', letterSpacing: 0.3,
            }}
            onClick={handleSubmit}
          >
            確認賣出
          </button>
        </div>

        {/* 說明文字 */}
        <div style={{
          margin: '0 16px 24px', padding: '12px 14px', borderRadius: 10,
          background: 'var(--bg-card-2, rgba(127,127,127,0.05))',
          fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', lineHeight: 1.6,
        }}>
          ℹ️ 系統會自動處理:
          <br/>· 本金部分(投資 → 收款帳戶)不算進收支統計
          <br/>· 損益部分(獲利或虧損)才會進收入/支出統計
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 收款帳戶選擇 sheet */}
      {showToSheet && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowToSheet(false)}>
          <div style={{ ...styles.pickerCard, maxWidth: 360, maxHeight: '70vh', overflow: 'hidden', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column' }} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>選擇收款帳戶</div>
            <div style={{ overflow: 'auto', padding: '4px 8px 12px' }}>
              {state.accounts.filter((a) => a.id !== account.id && !a.isSystem).map((a) => {
                const meta = state.accountTypes.find((t) => t.value === a.type);
                const active = a.id === toAccountId;
                return (
                  <button
                    key={a.id}
                    style={{
                      width: '100%', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10,
                      padding: '12px 14px', borderRadius: 10, marginBottom: 4,
                      background: active ? 'rgba(126,224,192,0.10)' : 'transparent',
                      border: active ? '1.5px solid var(--mint)' : '1.5px solid transparent',
                      color: 'var(--text)', cursor: 'pointer', textAlign: 'left',
                    }}
                    onClick={() => { setToAccountId(a.id); setShowToSheet(false); }}
                  >
                    <div style={{
                      width: 32, height: 32, borderRadius: 8, background: meta?.color || '#f5c29c',
                      display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', flexShrink: 0,
                    }}>
                      <TypeIcon name={meta?.icon || 'box'} size={16} color="#fff" />
                    </div>
                    <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: active ? 600 : 500 }}>{a.name}</div>
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>
                        餘額 {fmt(calcBalance(a, state.transactions))}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </button>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}


// ============ 股票買進 Sheet(新版,有 holding/trade 機制) ============
function BuyHoldingSheet({ state, account, prefillSymbol, onClose, onConfirm, toast, toastRich }) {
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(onClose);
  const [symbol, setSymbol] = useState(prefillSymbol || '');
  const [shares, setShares] = useState('');
  const [totalAmount, setTotalAmount] = useState('');
  const [marketValue, setMarketValue] = useState(''); // 目前市值(選填)
  const [date, setDate] = useState(todayStr());
  const [showDatePicker, setShowDatePicker] = useState(false);
  const [note, setNote] = useState('');
  // 預設扣款帳戶:優先讀 localStorage(且帳戶仍存在且非 invest/debt)
  const [defaultBuyAccountId, setDefaultBuyAccountId] = useState(() => {
    try { return localStorage.getItem(DEFAULT_BUY_ACCOUNT_KEY) || ''; } catch { return ''; }
  });
  const initialFromId = (() => {
    if (defaultBuyAccountId) {
      const a = state.accounts.find((x) => x.id === defaultBuyAccountId);
      if (a && a.type !== 'invest' && a.type !== 'debt' && !a.isSystem) return a.id;
    }
    const fallback = state.accounts.find((a) => a.type !== 'invest' && a.type !== 'debt' && !a.isSystem);
    return fallback?.id || '';
  })();
  const [fromAccountId, setFromAccountId] = useState(initialFromId);
  const [showFromSheet, setShowFromSheet] = useState(false);

  const sharesNum = parseFloat(shares) || 0;
  const totalCost = parseFloat(totalAmount) || 0;
  const marketValueNum = parseFloat(marketValue) || 0;
  const fromAcct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === fromAccountId);
  const symbolUpper = symbol.trim().toUpperCase();
  const existingHolding = state.holdings.find((h) => h.accountId === account.id && h.symbol === symbolUpper);

  const handleSubmit = () => {
    if (!symbolUpper) { toast && toast('請輸入代號'); return; }
    if (!sharesNum || sharesNum <= 0) { toast && toast('請輸入股數'); return; }
    if (!totalCost || totalCost <= 0) { toast && toast('請輸入金額'); return; }
    if (!fromAccountId) { toast && toast('請選擇扣款帳戶'); return; }
    onConfirm({
      accountId: account.id,
      symbol: symbolUpper,
      name: '',
      currency: 'TWD',
      shares: sharesNum,
      totalCost,
      fee: 0, // 已併入金額
      fromAccountId,
      date,
      note: note.trim(),
      marketValue: marketValueNum > 0 ? marketValueNum : null, // 有填才傳;沒填讓 saveBuyHolding 用買進金額
    });
  };

  if (showDatePicker) {
    return (
      <DatePicker value={date} onChange={setDate} onClose={() => setShowDatePicker(false)} />
    );
  }

  if (showFromSheet) {
    return (
      <AccountPickerSheet
        state={state}
        currentId={fromAccountId}
        excludeIds={[account.id]}
        onPick={(id) => { setFromAccountId(id); setShowFromSheet(false); }}
        onClose={() => setShowFromSheet(false)}
        title="選擇扣款帳戶"
      />
    );
  }

  return (
    <div
      data-sheet="true"
      style={{
        ...styles.sheet,
        transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
        transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
      }}
      ref={swipe.ref}
    >
      <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
        <button
          style={{
            background: 'transparent', border: 'none', color: 'var(--text-dim)',
            fontSize: 22, cursor: 'pointer', padding: '6px 12px',
          }}
          onClick={onClose}
        >×</button>
        <div style={{ ...styles.sheetTitle, color: 'var(--text)' }}>
          {existingHolding ? `加買 ${symbolUpper}` : '買進股票'}
        </div>
        <div style={{ width: 50 }} />
      </div>

      <div style={styles.sheetScroll}>
        {/* 代號 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '12px 16px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>代號</div>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={symbol}
            onChange={(e) => setSymbol(e.target.value.toUpperCase())}
            placeholder="例:RKLB、2330"
            maxLength={20}
            disabled={!!prefillSymbol}
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '12px 14px', fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 600,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
              border: '1.5px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 12,
              outline: 'none', boxSizing: 'border-box',
              textTransform: 'uppercase',
              opacity: prefillSymbol ? 0.7 : 1,
            }}
          />
          {existingHolding && (
            <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--mint-text)', marginTop: 4, paddingLeft: 4 }}>
              已持有 · 此筆視為加買
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* 股數 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>股數</div>
          <input
            type="number"
            inputMode="decimal"
            value={shares}
            onChange={(e) => setShares(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="0"
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '12px 14px', fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 600,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
              border: '1.5px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 12,
              outline: 'none', boxSizing: 'border-box',
            }}
          />
        </div>

        {/* 金額 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>
            金額
          </div>
          <input
            type="number"
            inputMode="decimal"
            value={totalAmount}
            onChange={(e) => setTotalAmount(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="0"
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '12px 14px', fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 600,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
              border: '1.5px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 12,
              outline: 'none', boxSizing: 'border-box',
            }}
          />
        </div>

        {/* 目前市值(選填) */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>
            目前市值 <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>(選填,空白 = 用買進金額)</span>
          </div>
          <input
            type="number"
            inputMode="decimal"
            value={marketValue}
            onChange={(e) => setMarketValue(e.target.value)}
            placeholder={totalCost > 0 ? totalCost.toString() : '0'}
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '12px 14px', fontSize: 16,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
              border: '1.5px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 12,
              outline: 'none', boxSizing: 'border-box',
            }}
          />
        </div>

        {/* 扣款帳戶 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{
            display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between',
            marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4, paddingRight: 4,
          }}>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>扣款帳戶</div>
            <span
              onClick={(e) => {
                e.stopPropagation();
                if (!fromAccountId) {
                  toast && toast('請先選擇扣款帳戶');
                  return;
                }
                const curName = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === fromAccountId)?.name || '';
                if (fromAccountId === defaultBuyAccountId) {
                  // 已是預設 → info toast
                  if (toastRich) {
                    toastRich({
                      title: '已是預設扣款帳戶',
                      amount: '✓',
                      icon: 'info',
                      amountColor: 'var(--text-faint)',
                      lines: [`「${curName}」`],
                    }, 1500);
                  } else {
                    toast && toast(`「${curName}」已是預設`);
                  }
                  return;
                }
                // 設為預設
                const oldId = defaultBuyAccountId;
                const oldName = oldId ? state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === oldId)?.name : '';
                try { localStorage.setItem(DEFAULT_BUY_ACCOUNT_KEY, fromAccountId); } catch {}
                setDefaultBuyAccountId(fromAccountId);
                if (toastRich) {
                  if (oldName) {
                    toastRich({
                      title: '已更新預設扣款帳戶',
                      amount: '✓',
                      amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
                      lines: [`原「${oldName}」 → 「${curName}」`],
                    }, 1800);
                  } else {
                    toastRich({
                      title: '已設為預設扣款帳戶',
                      amount: '✓',
                      amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
                      lines: [`「${curName}」`],
                    }, 1800);
                  }
                } else {
                  toast && toast(`已設「${curName}」為預設`);
                }
              }}
              style={{
                display: 'inline-flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
                width: 28, height: 28,
                cursor: 'pointer',
                WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
              }}
              title={fromAccountId === defaultBuyAccountId ? '目前是預設扣款帳戶' : '設為預設扣款帳戶'}
            >
              {fromAccountId && fromAccountId === defaultBuyAccountId ? (
                <TypeIcon name="star-filled" size={18} color="var(--mint)" />
              ) : (
                <TypeIcon name="star" size={18} color="var(--text-faint)" />
              )}
            </span>
          </div>
          <div
            onClick={() => setShowFromSheet(true)}
            style={{
              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10,
              padding: '12px 14px', borderRadius: 12,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', border: '1.5px solid var(--border)',
              cursor: 'pointer',
            }}
          >
            {fromAcct ? (
              <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 500, flex: 1 }}>{fromAcct.name}</div>
            ) : (
              <div style={{ fontSize: 14, color: 'var(--text-faint)', flex: 1 }}>選擇帳戶</div>
            )}
            <div style={{ fontSize: 18, color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>›</div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 日期 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>日期</div>
          <div
            onClick={() => setShowDatePicker(true)}
            style={{
              padding: '12px 14px', borderRadius: 12,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', border: '1.5px solid var(--border)',
              cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: 14,
            }}
          >
            {date} ({['日','一','二','三','四','五','六'][new Date(date).getDay()]})
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 備註 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>
            備註 <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>(選填)</span>
          </div>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={note}
            onChange={(e) => setNote(e.target.value)}
            maxLength={100}
            placeholder=""
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '12px 14px', fontSize: 14,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
              border: '1.5px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 12,
              outline: 'none', boxSizing: 'border-box',
            }}
          />
        </div>

        {/* 儲存按鈕 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '16px 16px 24px' }}>
          <button
            onClick={handleSubmit}
            disabled={!symbolUpper || !sharesNum || !totalCost || !fromAccountId}
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '14px',
              background: (!symbolUpper || !sharesNum || !totalCost || !fromAccountId) ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--mint)',
              color: (!symbolUpper || !sharesNum || !totalCost || !fromAccountId) ? 'var(--text-faint)' : '#fff',
              border: 'none', borderRadius: 12,
              fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 600,
              cursor: (!symbolUpper || !sharesNum || !totalCost || !fromAccountId) ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
            }}
          >確認買進</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


// ============ 自製拉桿(5% 一格,有頓點 + 浮動 % 標籤) ============
function CustomSlider({ currentShares, sharesNum, onChange }) {
  const trackRef = React.useRef(null);
  const [dragging, setDragging] = React.useState(false);

  const pctRaw = currentShares > 0 ? (sharesNum / currentShares) * 100 : 0;
  const pctClamp = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, pctRaw));
  const pctSnapped = Math.round(pctClamp / 5) * 5;
  const isOver = sharesNum > currentShares;
  const accent = isOver ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--mint)';

  const handleMove = (clientX) => {
    const rect = trackRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect();
    if (!rect) return;
    const ratio = (clientX - rect.left) / rect.width;
    let pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, ratio * 100));
    // snap 到 5%
    pct = Math.round(pct / 5) * 5;
    const newShares = Math.round((currentShares * pct) / 100);
    onChange(newShares);
  };

  const onPointerDown = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();
    setDragging(true);
    const x = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
    handleMove(x);
    // haptic 起始
    try { if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(8); } catch {}
  };

  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (!dragging) return;
    let lastSnapped = pctSnapped;
    const onMove = (e) => {
      // 阻止外層 sheet 的 swipe back / 頁面滾動
      if (e.cancelable) e.preventDefault();
      const x = e.touches ? e.touches[0].clientX : e.clientX;
      const rect = trackRef.current?.getBoundingClientRect();
      if (!rect) return;
      const ratio = (x - rect.left) / rect.width;
      let pct = Math.max(0, Math.min(100, ratio * 100));
      pct = Math.round(pct / 5) * 5;
      if (pct !== lastSnapped) {
        try { if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(8); } catch {}
        lastSnapped = pct;
      }
      const newShares = Math.round((currentShares * pct) / 100);
      onChange(newShares);
    };
    const onUp = () => setDragging(false);
    window.addEventListener('mousemove', onMove);
    window.addEventListener('mouseup', onUp);
    window.addEventListener('touchmove', onMove, { passive: false });
    window.addEventListener('touchend', onUp);
    window.addEventListener('touchcancel', onUp);
    return () => {
      window.removeEventListener('mousemove', onMove);
      window.removeEventListener('mouseup', onUp);
      window.removeEventListener('touchmove', onMove);
      window.removeEventListener('touchend', onUp);
      window.removeEventListener('touchcancel', onUp);
    };
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, [dragging, currentShares]);

  // pctSnapped 顯示用,定位用 pctClamp(輸入超出時固定 100)
  const fillWidth = `${pctClamp}%`;
  const labelText = isOver ? '超出' : pctSnapped === 0 ? '0%' : pctSnapped === 100 ? '全部' : `${pctSnapped}%`;
  // 膠囊置中於拇指,但靠近邊緣時夾住,避免被切掉
  // 膠囊寬約 50px(含 padding),取 25 為半寬;軌道內距離兩側 12px
  const knobPos = pctClamp / 100; // 0..1

  return (
    <div data-slider="true" style={{ marginTop: 16, padding: '0 2px', userSelect: 'none', touchAction: 'none' }}>
      {/* 拉桿區(含浮動標籤、軌道、拇指圓) */}
      {/* 結構:總高 56px = 膠囊 22 + 留白 12 + 軌道區 22 */}
      <div style={{ position: 'relative', height: 56, padding: '0 12px' }}>
        {/* 浮動百分比膠囊(top: 0,高 22) */}
        {/* 邊緣保護:膠囊左/右最多貼近父容器 padding 邊界,避免被切掉 */}
        <div style={{
          position: 'absolute', top: 0,
          left: `calc(12px + (100% - 24px) * ${knobPos})`,
          transform: knobPos < 0.08 ? 'translateX(0)' :
                     knobPos > 0.92 ? 'translateX(-100%)' :
                     'translateX(-50%)',
          minWidth: 38, // 固定最小寬,避免「40%」「100%」「全部」切換時跳動
          textAlign: 'center',
          padding: '3px 9px', borderRadius: 999,
          background: accent, color: '#fff',
          fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 700, lineHeight: 1.3,
          whiteSpace: 'nowrap', pointerEvents: 'none',
          transition: dragging ? 'none' : 'left 0.15s ease-out',
          boxShadow: '0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,0.12)',
        }}>{labelText}</div>

        {/* 軌道感應區(top: 34,高 22 — 膠囊下方留 12px 間隔) */}
        <div
          ref={trackRef}
          onMouseDown={onPointerDown}
          onTouchStart={onPointerDown}
          style={{
            position: 'absolute', top: 34, left: 12, right: 12, height: 22,
            cursor: 'pointer',
            display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center',
          }}
        >
          {/* 視覺軌道(細,3px) */}
          <div style={{
            position: 'relative', width: '100%', height: 3,
            background: 'var(--border)',
            borderRadius: 999,
          }}>
            {/* 已填充段 */}
            <div style={{
              position: 'absolute', top: 0, left: 0, height: '100%',
              width: fillWidth, background: accent,
              borderRadius: 999,
              transition: dragging ? 'none' : 'width 0.15s ease-out',
            }} />
            {/* 拇指圓(18px,白底深綠/粉紅描邊) */}
            <div style={{
              position: 'absolute', top: '50%', left: fillWidth,
              transform: 'translate(-50%, -50%)',
              width: 18, height: 18, borderRadius: '50%',
              background: '#fff',
              border: `2px solid ${accent}`,
              boxShadow: '0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,0.18)',
              transition: dragging ? 'none' : 'left 0.15s ease-out',
              pointerEvents: 'none',
            }} />
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      {/* 兩端標籤(0 / 全部) */}
      <div style={{
        display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between',
        fontSize: 10, color: 'var(--text-faint)',
        padding: '0 14px', marginTop: 6,
      }}>
        <span>0</span>
        <span>全部</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


// ============ 股票賣出 Sheet(新版,走 FIFO) ============
function SellHoldingSheet({ state, holding, onClose, onConfirm, toast, toastRich }) {
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(onClose);
  const account = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === holding.accountId);
  const currentShares = holdingShares(holding, state.trades);
  const investedCost = holdingCost(holding, state.trades); // 目前持股對應成本
  const avgCostPerShare = currentShares > 0 ? investedCost / currentShares : 0;

  const [shares, setShares] = useState(String(currentShares));
  const [totalReceived, setTotalReceived] = useState('');
  const [date, setDate] = useState(todayStr());
  const [showDatePicker, setShowDatePicker] = useState(false);
  const [note, setNote] = useState('');
  // 預設收款帳戶:優先讀 localStorage(且帳戶仍存在且非 invest/debt)
  const [defaultSellAccountId, setDefaultSellAccountId] = useState(() => {
    try { return localStorage.getItem(DEFAULT_SELL_ACCOUNT_KEY) || ''; } catch { return ''; }
  });
  const initialToId = (() => {
    if (defaultSellAccountId) {
      const a = state.accounts.find((x) => x.id === defaultSellAccountId);
      if (a && a.type !== 'invest' && a.type !== 'debt' && !a.isSystem) return a.id;
    }
    const fallback = state.accounts.find((a) => a.type !== 'invest' && a.type !== 'debt' && !a.isSystem);
    return fallback?.id || '';
  })();
  const [toAccountId, setToAccountId] = useState(initialToId);
  const [showToSheet, setShowToSheet] = useState(false);

  const sharesNum = parseFloat(shares) || 0;
  const receivedNum = parseFloat(totalReceived) || 0;
  const toAcct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === toAccountId);

  const handleSubmit = () => {
    if (!sharesNum || sharesNum <= 0) { toast && toast('請輸入股數'); return; }
    if (sharesNum > currentShares) { toast && toast(`股數不能超過持有(${currentShares})`); return; }
    if (!receivedNum || receivedNum <= 0) { toast && toast('請輸入售出金額'); return; }
    if (!toAccountId) { toast && toast('請選擇收款帳戶'); return; }
    onConfirm({
      holdingId: holding.id,
      shares: sharesNum,
      totalReceived: receivedNum,
      fee: 0, tax: 0, // 已併入金額
      toAccountId,
      date,
      note: note.trim(),
    });
  };

  if (showDatePicker) {
    return (
      <DatePicker value={date} onChange={setDate} onClose={() => setShowDatePicker(false)} />
    );
  }

  if (showToSheet) {
    return (
      <AccountPickerSheet
        state={state}
        currentId={toAccountId}
        excludeIds={[holding.accountId]}
        onPick={(id) => { setToAccountId(id); setShowToSheet(false); }}
        onClose={() => setShowToSheet(false)}
        title="選擇收款帳戶"
      />
    );
  }

  return (
    <div
      data-sheet="true"
      style={{
        ...styles.sheet,
        transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
        transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
      }}
      ref={swipe.ref}
    >
      <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
        <button
          style={{
            background: 'transparent', border: 'none', color: 'var(--text-dim)',
            fontSize: 22, cursor: 'pointer', padding: '6px 12px',
          }}
          onClick={onClose}
        >×</button>
        <div style={{ ...styles.sheetTitle, color: 'var(--text)' }}>賣出 {holding.symbol}</div>
        <div style={{ width: 50 }} />
      </div>

      <div style={styles.sheetScroll}>
        {/* 持股資訊卡(精簡) */}
        <div style={{
          margin: '8px 16px 12px', padding: 14, borderRadius: 12,
          background: 'rgba(126,224,192,0.08)', border: '1.5px solid var(--mint)',
        }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 600 }}>{holding.symbol}</div>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginTop: 4 }}>
            持有 {currentShares.toLocaleString()} 股
            {investedCost > 0 && (
              <> · 投入 {fmt(investedCost)}</>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 股數 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{
            fontSize: 12, marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4,
            display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between',
          }}>
            <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>賣出股數</span>
            {sharesNum > currentShares && (
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--pink-text)', fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 600 }}>
                超過持有 {currentShares} 股
              </span>
            )}
          </div>
          <input
            type="number"
            inputMode="decimal"
            value={shares}
            onChange={(e) => setShares(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="0"
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '12px 14px', fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 600,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)',
              color: sharesNum > currentShares ? 'var(--pink-text)' : 'var(--text)',
              border: `1.5px solid ${sharesNum > currentShares ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--border)'}`,
              borderRadius: 12,
              outline: 'none', boxSizing: 'border-box',
            }}
          />
          {sharesNum > currentShares && (
            <div
              onClick={() => setShares(String(currentShares))}
              style={{
                marginTop: 6,
                padding: '8px 12px',
                background: 'rgba(217,104,119,0.08)',
                border: '1px solid var(--pink)',
                borderRadius: 8,
                fontSize: 12,
                color: 'var(--pink-text)',
                display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between',
                cursor: 'pointer',
              }}
            >
              <span>最多只能賣 {currentShares.toLocaleString()} 股</span>
              <span style={{ fontWeight: 600 }}>點此修正</span>
            </div>
          )}
          {/* 自製拉桿:5% 一格,共 21 個節點(0%, 5%, ... 100%) */}
          {currentShares > 0 && (
            <CustomSlider
              currentShares={currentShares}
              sharesNum={sharesNum}
              onChange={(newShares) => setShares(String(newShares))}
            />
          )}
        </div>

        {/* 售出金額 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>
            售出金額(實收)
          </div>
          <input
            type="number"
            inputMode="decimal"
            value={totalReceived}
            onChange={(e) => setTotalReceived(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="0"
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '12px 14px', fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 600,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
              border: '1.5px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 12,
