              outline: 'none', boxSizing: 'border-box',
            }}
          />
          {/* 保本價/損益提示(僅當有股數且有成本資料時) */}
          {sharesNum > 0 && sharesNum <= currentShares && investedCost > 0 && (() => {
            const matchedCost = sharesNum * avgCostPerShare;
            if (receivedNum <= 0) {
              return (
                <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>
                  保本價 {fmt(matchedCost)} · 高於此價有獲利
                </div>
              );
            }
            const pnl = receivedNum - matchedCost;
            const isProfit = pnl >= 0;
            return (
              <div style={{
                marginTop: 6, paddingLeft: 4,
                fontSize: 11,
                color: isProfit ? 'var(--mint-text)' : 'var(--pink-text)',
                fontWeight: 500,
              }}>
                {isProfit ? '預估獲利' : '預估虧損'} {isProfit ? '+' : ''}{fmt(pnl)}
                <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginLeft: 6, fontWeight: 400 }}>
                  (對應成本 {fmt(matchedCost)})
                </span>
              </div>
            );
          })()}
        </div>

        {/* 收款帳戶 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{
            display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between',
            marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4, paddingRight: 4,
          }}>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>收款帳戶</div>
            <span
              onClick={(e) => {
                e.stopPropagation();
                if (!toAccountId) {
                  toast && toast('請先選擇收款帳戶');
                  return;
                }
                const curName = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === toAccountId)?.name || '';
                if (toAccountId === defaultSellAccountId) {
                  if (toastRich) {
                    toastRich({
                      title: '已是預設收款帳戶',
                      amount: '✓',
                      icon: 'info',
                      amountColor: 'var(--text-faint)',
                      lines: [`「${curName}」`],
                    }, 1500);
                  } else {
                    toast && toast(`「${curName}」已是預設`);
                  }
                  return;
                }
                const oldId = defaultSellAccountId;
                const oldName = oldId ? state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === oldId)?.name : '';
                try { localStorage.setItem(DEFAULT_SELL_ACCOUNT_KEY, toAccountId); } catch {}
                setDefaultSellAccountId(toAccountId);
                if (toastRich) {
                  if (oldName) {
                    toastRich({
                      title: '已更新預設收款帳戶',
                      amount: '✓',
                      amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
                      lines: [`原「${oldName}」 → 「${curName}」`],
                    }, 1800);
                  } else {
                    toastRich({
                      title: '已設為預設收款帳戶',
                      amount: '✓',
                      amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
                      lines: [`「${curName}」`],
                    }, 1800);
                  }
                } else {
                  toast && toast(`已設「${curName}」為預設`);
                }
              }}
              style={{
                display: 'inline-flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
                width: 28, height: 28,
                cursor: 'pointer',
                WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
              }}
              title={toAccountId === defaultSellAccountId ? '目前是預設收款帳戶' : '設為預設收款帳戶'}
            >
              {toAccountId && toAccountId === defaultSellAccountId ? (
                <TypeIcon name="star-filled" size={18} color="var(--mint)" />
              ) : (
                <TypeIcon name="star" size={18} color="var(--text-faint)" />
              )}
            </span>
          </div>
          <div
            onClick={() => setShowToSheet(true)}
            style={{
              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10,
              padding: '12px 14px', borderRadius: 12,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', border: '1.5px solid var(--border)',
              cursor: 'pointer',
            }}
          >
            {toAcct ? (
              <>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 500, flex: 1 }}>{toAcct.name}</div>
              </>
            ) : (
              <div style={{ fontSize: 14, color: 'var(--text-faint)', flex: 1 }}>選擇帳戶</div>
            )}
            <div style={{ fontSize: 18, color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>›</div>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 日期 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>日期</div>
          <div
            onClick={() => setShowDatePicker(true)}
            style={{
              padding: '12px 14px', borderRadius: 12,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', border: '1.5px solid var(--border)',
              cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: 14,
            }}
          >
            {date} ({['日','一','二','三','四','五','六'][new Date(date).getDay()]})
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 備註 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>
            備註 <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>(選填)</span>
          </div>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={note}
            onChange={(e) => setNote(e.target.value)}
            maxLength={100}
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '12px 14px', fontSize: 14,
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
              border: '1.5px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 12,
              outline: 'none', boxSizing: 'border-box',
            }}
          />
        </div>

        {/* 儲存按鈕 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '8px 16px 24px' }}>
          <button
            onClick={handleSubmit}
            disabled={!sharesNum || !receivedNum || !toAccountId || sharesNum > currentShares}
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '14px',
              background: (!sharesNum || !receivedNum || !toAccountId || sharesNum > currentShares) ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--pink)',
              color: (!sharesNum || !receivedNum || !toAccountId || sharesNum > currentShares) ? 'var(--text-faint)' : '#fff',
              border: 'none', borderRadius: 12,
              fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 600,
              cursor: (!sharesNum || !receivedNum || !toAccountId || sharesNum > currentShares) ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
            }}
          >確認賣出</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


// ============ 已清倉持股區(摺疊) ============
function ClosedHoldingsSection({ holdings, trades }) {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);
  return (
    <div style={{ marginTop: 10 }}>
      <div
        onClick={() => setExpanded(!expanded)}
        style={{
          display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between',
          padding: '10px 12px',
          background: 'var(--bg-card)',
          border: '1px solid var(--border)',
          borderRadius: 10, cursor: 'pointer',
          fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)',
        }}
      >
        <span>已清倉 ({holdings.length})</span>
        <span>{expanded ? '▾' : '▸'}</span>
      </div>
      {expanded && (
        <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 6, marginTop: 6 }}>
          {holdings.map((h) => {
            // 算這支股票的累計實現損益
            const sells = trades.filter((t) => t.holdingId === h.id && t.type === 'sell');
            const totalPnl = sells.reduce((s, t) => s + (t.realizedPnl || 0), 0);
            return (
              <div key={h.id} style={{
                padding: '10px 12px',
                background: 'var(--bg-card-2, rgba(127,127,127,0.04))',
                border: '1px solid var(--border)',
                borderRadius: 10, opacity: 0.8,
              }}>
                <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'baseline' }}>
                  <span style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600 }}>{h.symbol}</span>
                  <span style={{
                    fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600,
                    color: totalPnl >= 0 ? 'var(--mint-text)' : 'var(--pink-text)',
                  }}>
                    累計 {totalPnl >= 0 ? '+' : ''}{fmt(totalPnl)}
                  </span>
                </div>
                {h.name && <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginTop: 2 }}>{h.name}</div>}
              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}



// ============ 股票結算詳情 Sheet(唯讀檢視 + 整組刪除) ============
function SettleDetailSheet({ state, settleGroup, onClose, onDeleteGroup }) {
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(onClose);
  // settleGroup 是同 transferId 的 settle 紀錄陣列(2-3 筆)
  // 從中取出 tradeId,反查 trade + holding
  const tradeId = settleGroup[0]?.tradeId;
  const trade = state.trades.find((tr) => tr.id === tradeId);
  const holding = trade ? state.holdings.find((h) => h.id === trade.holdingId) : null;

  const settleOut = settleGroup.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'settle_out');
  const settleIn = settleGroup.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'settle_in');
  const pnlIn = settleGroup.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'settle_pnl_in');
  const pnlOut = settleGroup.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'settle_pnl_out');

  const investAcct = settleOut ? state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === settleOut.accountId) : null;
  const recvAcct = settleIn ? state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === settleIn.accountId) : null;

  const date = settleGroup[0]?.date || trade?.date || '';
  const principal = settleOut?.amount || trade?.matchedCost || 0;
  const realizedPnl = pnlIn ? pnlIn.amount : (pnlOut ? -pnlOut.amount : (trade?.realizedPnl || 0));
  const totalReceived = principal + (pnlIn ? pnlIn.amount : 0) - (pnlOut ? pnlOut.amount : 0);
  const fee = trade?.fee || 0;
  const tax = trade?.tax || 0;
  const shares = trade?.shares || 0;

  // 從 trade.note 抽出純使用者備註(去掉系統前綴)
  const userNote = (() => {
    const n = settleGroup[0]?.note || '';
    // 系統 note 格式:「[賣出 SYMBOL - 本金] 使用者備註」或「[賣出 SYMBOL - 獲利] ...」
    const m = n.match(/^\[賣出 [^\]]+\]\s*(.*)$/);
    return m ? m[1] : n;
  })();

  return (
    <div
      data-sheet="true"
      style={{
        ...styles.sheet,
        transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
        transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
      }}
      ref={swipe.ref}
    >
      <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
        <button
          style={{
            background: 'transparent', border: 'none', color: 'var(--text-dim)',
            fontSize: 22, cursor: 'pointer', padding: '6px 12px',
          }}
          onClick={onClose}
        >‹</button>
        <div style={{ ...styles.sheetTitle, color: 'var(--text)' }}>股票結算詳情</div>
        <div style={{ width: 50 }} />
      </div>

      <div style={styles.sheetScroll}>
        {/* 主資訊卡:賣出 SYMBOL + 損益 */}
        <div style={{
          margin: '12px 16px', padding: '20px 16px',
          borderRadius: 14,
          background: 'var(--bg-card)',
          border: '1px solid var(--border)',
          textAlign: 'center',
        }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 4 }}>
            賣出 <span style={{ fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--text)' }}>{holding?.symbol || '(已刪除)'}</span>
          </div>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginBottom: 12 }}>
            {shares.toLocaleString()} 股 · {date}
          </div>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>實現損益</div>
          <div style={{
            fontSize: 28, fontWeight: 700, marginTop: 4,
            color: realizedPnl > 0 ? 'var(--mint-text)' : realizedPnl < 0 ? 'var(--pink-text)' : 'var(--text)',
          }}>
            {realizedPnl > 0 ? '+' : ''}{fmt(realizedPnl)}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 明細列 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>明細</div>
          <div style={{
            background: 'var(--bg-card)',
            border: '1px solid var(--border)',
            borderRadius: 12,
            overflow: 'hidden',
          }}>
            {[
              { label: '售出金額', value: fmt(totalReceived) },
              { label: '配對成本', value: fmt(principal) },
              ...(fee > 0 ? [{ label: '手續費', value: fmt(fee) }] : []),
              ...(tax > 0 ? [{ label: '證交稅', value: fmt(tax) }] : []),
              { label: '投資帳戶', value: investAcct?.name || '(已刪除)' },
              { label: '收款帳戶', value: recvAcct?.name || '(已刪除)' },
              ...(userNote ? [{ label: '備註', value: userNote }] : []),
            ].map((row, i, arr) => (
              <div
                key={i}
                style={{
                  display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center',
                  padding: '12px 14px',
                  borderBottom: i < arr.length - 1 ? '1px solid var(--border)' : 'none',
                  fontSize: 14,
                }}
              >
                <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>{row.label}</span>
                <span style={{ color: 'var(--text)', fontWeight: 500 }}>{row.value}</span>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 主帳本關聯紀錄 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 12px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 6, paddingLeft: 4 }}>
            主帳本關聯紀錄({settleGroup.length} 筆)
          </div>
          <div style={{
            background: 'var(--bg-card)',
            border: '1px solid var(--border)',
            borderRadius: 12,
            overflow: 'hidden',
          }}>
            {settleGroup.map((t, i) => {
              const acct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === t.accountId);
              const roleLabel = t.transferRole === 'settle_out' ? '本金歸還(支出)'
                : t.transferRole === 'settle_in' ? '本金歸還(收款)'
                : t.transferRole === 'settle_pnl_in' ? '獲利了結'
                : t.transferRole === 'settle_pnl_out' ? '投資失利'
                : '';
              const isInc = t.type === 'income';
              return (
                <div
                  key={t.id}
                  style={{
                    padding: '10px 14px',
                    borderBottom: i < settleGroup.length - 1 ? '1px solid var(--border)' : 'none',
                  }}
                >
                  <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text)', fontWeight: 500 }}>{roleLabel}</span>
                    <span style={{
                      fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600,
                      color: isInc ? 'var(--mint-text)' : 'var(--pink-text)',
                    }}>
                      {isInc ? '+' : '-'}{fmt(t.amount)}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 2 }}>
                    {acct?.name || '(已刪除)'}
                  </div>
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 編輯說明 */}
        <div style={{
          margin: '8px 16px 12px', padding: '10px 12px',
          background: 'var(--bg-card)', border: '1px solid var(--border)',
          borderRadius: 10,
          fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', lineHeight: 1.5,
        }}>
          股票結算紀錄包含本金歸還與損益,彼此關聯。如需修改,請刪除整組後重新建立。
        </div>

        {/* 刪除整組按鈕 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 24px' }}>
          <button
            onClick={() => onDeleteGroup && onDeleteGroup(settleGroup)}
            style={{
              width: '100%', padding: '12px',
              background: 'transparent', color: 'var(--pink-text)',
              border: '1.5px solid var(--pink)',
              borderRadius: 12,
              fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600,
              cursor: 'pointer',
            }}
          >
            刪除整組結算紀錄
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


// ============ 持股詳情 Sheet ============
function HoldingDetailSheet({ state, holding, onClose, onUpdateMarketValue, onBuyMore, onSell, onDeleteTrade, setConfirmDialog }) {
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(onClose);
  const longPressTimerRef = React.useRef(null);
  const longPressTriggeredRef = React.useRef(false);

  if (!holding) return null;
  const shares = holdingShares(holding, state.trades);
  const cost = holdingCost(holding, state.trades);
  const market = holding.marketValue || 0;
  const pnl = market - cost;
  const trades = state.trades
    .filter((t) => t.holdingId === holding.id)
    .sort((a, b) => (b.date || '').localeCompare(a.date || ''));

  const account = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === holding.accountId);

  const handleLongPress = (trade) => {
    longPressTriggeredRef.current = true;
    if (!setConfirmDialog || !onDeleteTrade) return;
    const isBuy = trade.type === 'buy';
    const amt = isBuy ? trade.totalCost : trade.totalReceived;
    setConfirmDialog({
      title: '刪除紀錄',
      messageList: {
        before: `將永久刪除這筆${isBuy ? '買進' : '賣出'}紀錄:`,
        items: [
          `${(trade.date || '').replace(/-/g, '/')}  ${isBuy ? '買進' : '賣出'} ${trade.shares.toLocaleString()} 股  ${isBuy ? '-' : '+'}${fmt(amt)}`,
          ...(isBuy ? ['同時會刪除主帳本上的扣款紀錄'] : ['同時會刪除主帳本上的收款 + 損益紀錄']),
        ],
        after: '此動作無法復原',
      },
      confirmText: '刪除',
      danger: true,
      onConfirm: () => {
        onDeleteTrade(trade.id);
      },
    });
  };

  const startLongPress = (trade) => {
    longPressTriggeredRef.current = false;
    longPressTimerRef.current = setTimeout(() => handleLongPress(trade), 500);
  };
  const cancelLongPress = () => {
    if (longPressTimerRef.current) {
      clearTimeout(longPressTimerRef.current);
      longPressTimerRef.current = null;
    }
  };

  return (
    <div
      data-sheet="true"
      style={{
        ...styles.sheet,
        transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
        transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
      }}
      ref={swipe.ref}
    >
      <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
        <button
          style={{
            background: 'transparent', border: 'none', color: 'var(--text-dim)',
            fontSize: 22, cursor: 'pointer', padding: '6px 12px',
          }}
          onClick={onClose}
        >‹</button>
        <div style={{ ...styles.sheetTitle, color: 'var(--text)' }}>{holding.symbol}</div>
        <div style={{ width: 50 }} />
      </div>

      <div style={styles.sheetScroll}>
        {/* 主資訊卡 */}
        <div style={{
          margin: '12px 16px', padding: '20px 16px',
          borderRadius: 14,
          background: 'var(--bg-card)',
          border: '1px solid var(--border)',
          textAlign: 'center',
        }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 4 }}>
            {shares.toLocaleString()} 股 · 投入 {fmt(cost)}
          </div>

          <div style={{ marginTop: 12, fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>目前市值</div>
          <div
            onClick={() => onUpdateMarketValue && onUpdateMarketValue(holding)}
            style={{
              fontSize: 32, fontWeight: 700, marginTop: 4,
              cursor: 'pointer',
              display: 'inline-flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8,
            }}
          >
            {market > 0 ? fmt(market) : <span style={{ color: 'var(--mint-text)', fontSize: 18 }}>點此編輯</span>}
            <TypeIcon name="pencil" size={16} color="var(--text-faint)" />
          </div>
          {market > 0 && cost > 0 && (
            <div style={{
              marginTop: 6, fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600,
              color: pnl >= 0 ? 'var(--mint-text)' : 'var(--pink-text)',
            }}>
              {pnl >= 0 ? '+' : ''}{fmt(pnl)}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* 操作按鈕 */}
        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8, margin: '0 16px 16px' }}>
          <button
            onClick={() => onBuyMore && onBuyMore(holding)}
            style={{
              flex: 1, padding: '12px',
              background: 'var(--mint)', color: '#fff',
              border: 'none', borderRadius: 12,
              fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600,
              cursor: 'pointer',
            }}
          >+ 加買</button>
          <button
            onClick={() => onSell && onSell(holding)}
            disabled={shares === 0}
            style={{
              flex: 1, padding: '12px',
              background: shares === 0 ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--pink)',
              color: shares === 0 ? 'var(--text-faint)' : '#fff',
              border: 'none', borderRadius: 12,
              fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600,
              cursor: shares === 0 ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
            }}
          >賣出</button>
        </div>

        {/* 買賣紀錄 */}
        <div style={{ margin: '0 16px 16px' }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 8, paddingLeft: 4, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
            <span>買賣紀錄({trades.length})</span>
            {trades.length > 0 && (
              <span style={{ fontSize: 10, color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>長按可刪除</span>
            )}
          </div>
          {trades.length === 0 ? (
            <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-faint)', padding: 16, textAlign: 'center' }}>
              尚無紀錄
            </div>
          ) : (
            <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 6 }}>
              {trades.map((t) => {
                const isBuy = t.type === 'buy';
                const amt = isBuy ? t.totalCost : t.totalReceived;
                const pnlPart = !isBuy && t.realizedPnl !== undefined ? t.realizedPnl : null;
                return (
                  <div
                    key={t.id}
                    onTouchStart={() => startLongPress(t)}
                    onTouchEnd={cancelLongPress}
                    onTouchMove={cancelLongPress}
                    onTouchCancel={cancelLongPress}
                    onMouseDown={() => startLongPress(t)}
                    onMouseUp={cancelLongPress}
                    onMouseLeave={cancelLongPress}
                    onContextMenu={(e) => { e.preventDefault(); handleLongPress(t); }}
                    style={{
                      padding: '10px 12px',
                      borderRadius: 10,
                      background: 'var(--bg-card)',
                      border: '1px solid var(--border)',
                      userSelect: 'none',
                      WebkitUserSelect: 'none',
                    }}
                  >
                    <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'baseline' }}>
                      <span style={{
                        fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 600,
                        color: isBuy ? 'var(--mint-text)' : 'var(--pink-text)',
                      }}>
                        {isBuy ? '買進' : '賣出'} {t.shares.toLocaleString()} 股
                      </span>
                      <span style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600 }}>
                        {isBuy ? '-' : '+'}{fmt(amt)}
                      </span>
                    </div>
                    <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginTop: 4 }}>
                      <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>
                        {(t.date || '').replace(/-/g, '/')}
                      </span>
                      {pnlPart !== null && (
                        <span style={{
                          fontSize: 11, fontWeight: 500,
                          color: pnlPart >= 0 ? 'var(--mint-text)' : 'var(--pink-text)',
                        }}>
                          損益 {pnlPart >= 0 ? '+' : ''}{fmt(pnlPart)}
                        </span>
                      )}
                    </div>
                    {t.note && (
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginTop: 4 }}>
                        {t.note}
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}


function AccountPickerSheet({ state, currentId, excludeIds, onPick, onClose, title }) {
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(onClose);
  const filtered = state.accounts.filter((a) =>
    !excludeIds?.includes(a.id) && !a.isSystem
  );

  return (
    <div
      data-sheet="true"
      style={{
        ...styles.sheet,
        transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
        transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
      }}
      ref={swipe.ref}
    >
      <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
        <button
          style={{
            background: 'transparent', border: 'none', color: 'var(--text-dim)',
            fontSize: 22, cursor: 'pointer', padding: '6px 12px',
          }}
          onClick={onClose}
        >×</button>
        <div style={{ ...styles.sheetTitle, color: 'var(--text)' }}>{title || '選擇帳戶'}</div>
        <div style={{ width: 50 }} />
      </div>
      <div style={styles.sheetScroll}>
        <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 6, padding: 12 }}>
          {filtered.map((a) => {
            const typeMeta = state.accountTypes.find((t) => t.value === a.type);
            const bal = calcBalance(a, state.transactions);
            const isSelected = a.id === currentId;
            return (
              <div
                key={a.id}
                onClick={() => onPick(a.id)}
                style={{
                  display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 12,
                  padding: '12px 14px', borderRadius: 12,
                  background: 'var(--bg-card)',
                  border: isSelected ? '2px solid var(--mint)' : '1.5px solid var(--border)',
                  cursor: 'pointer',
                }}
              >
                <div style={{
                  width: 30, height: 30, borderRadius: 8,
                  background: typeMeta?.color || '#f5c29c',
                  display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
                }}>
                  <TypeIcon name={typeMeta?.icon || 'box'} size={16} color="#fff" />
                </div>
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 500 }}>{a.name}</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>
                    {typeMeta?.label || '其他'}
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div style={{ fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>
                  {bal.toLocaleString()}
                </div>
              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}



function HomePage({ state, setState, catIcon, currentMonth, setCurrentMonth, selectedDate, setSelectedDate, onAdd, onClickTxn, onViewAll, onOpenPeriod, onOpenAccount, onOpenDate, onOpenLend, editMode, setEditMode, blockOrder, moveBlock, setPageOrder, setConfirmDialog, toastRich, toast, onSelectModeChange }) {
  // 最近紀錄篩選：all / expense / income / transfer
  const [recentFilter, setRecentFilter] = useState(() => {
    try { return localStorage.getItem('ledger_recent_filter') || 'all'; } catch { return 'all'; }
  });
  // 列表排序模式(與明細頁共用,改一邊另一邊也跟著變)
  const [sortMode, setSortMode] = useListSort();
  // 鎖定「最近紀錄」內容區最小高度，避免切換篩選時整頁高度變化
  // 在「全部」模式下量一次高度，其他篩選沿用該高度當 minHeight
  const recentContentRef = React.useRef(null);
  const [recentMinHeight, setRecentMinHeight] = useState(0);
  // 多選刪除模式
  const [selectMode, setSelectMode] = useState(false);
  const [selectedIds, setSelectedIds] = useState(() => new Set());
  React.useEffect(() => { if (onSelectModeChange) onSelectModeChange(selectMode); }, [selectMode]); // eslint-disable-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  const exitSelectMode = () => { setSelectMode(false); setSelectedIds(new Set()); };
  const toggleSelect = (id) => {
    setSelectedIds((prev) => {
      const next = new Set(prev);
      if (next.has(id)) next.delete(id); else next.add(id);
      return next;
    });
  };
  const enterSelectModeWith = (id) => { setSelectMode(true); setSelectedIds(new Set([id])); };
  const changeRecentFilter = (v) => {
    if (v === recentFilter) return;
    setRecentFilter(v);
    try { localStorage.setItem('ledger_recent_filter', v); } catch {}
  };

  const shiftMonth = (delta) => {
    const [y, m] = currentMonth.split('-').map(Number);
    const d = new Date(y, m - 1 + delta, 1);
    setCurrentMonth(`${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}`);
  };

  // 「全部」模式渲染後量最近紀錄內容區高度，作為其他篩選的 minHeight
  React.useLayoutEffect(() => {
    if (recentFilter === 'all' && recentContentRef.current) {
      const h = recentContentRef.current.offsetHeight;
      if (h > 0 && h !== recentMinHeight) setRecentMinHeight(h);
    }
  }, [recentFilter, state.transactions]);

  // 本月收支
  let monthInc = 0, monthExp = 0;
  for (const t of state.transactions) {
    if (!t.date.startsWith(currentMonth)) continue;
    if (!isRealFlow(t)) continue;
    if (t.type === 'income') monthInc += t.amount;
    else if (t.type === 'expense') monthExp += t.amount;
  }

  // 期間花費（支出）
  const today = todayStr();
  const now = new Date();
  const dayOfWeek = now.getDay();
  const weekStartDate = new Date(now);
  weekStartDate.setDate(now.getDate() - dayOfWeek);
  const weekEndDate = new Date(weekStartDate);
  weekEndDate.setDate(weekStartDate.getDate() + 6);
  const toIso = (d) => `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}`;
  const weekStart = toIso(weekStartDate);
  const weekEnd = toIso(weekEndDate);
  const thisMonth = today.slice(0, 7);
  const thisYear = today.slice(0, 4);

  // 一次掃過 transactions 算完 today/week/month/year × income/expense 8 個累加
  // (原本 8 次 reduce 全表 → 改成 1 次 reduce,效能提升 8 倍)
  // useMemo 確保只在 transactions / 日期變動時重算
  const totals = React.useMemo(() => {
    const t = { todayInc: 0, todayExp: 0, weekInc: 0, weekExp: 0, monthIncP: 0, monthExpP: 0, yearInc: 0, yearExp: 0 };
    for (const tx of state.transactions) {
      if (!isRealFlow(tx)) continue;
      const d = tx.date;
      const isToday = d === today;
      const isThisWeek = d >= weekStart && d <= weekEnd;
      const isThisMonth = d.startsWith(thisMonth);
      const isThisYear = d.startsWith(thisYear);
      if (tx.type === 'income') {
        if (isToday) t.todayInc += tx.amount;
        if (isThisWeek) t.weekInc += tx.amount;
        if (isThisMonth) t.monthIncP += tx.amount;
        if (isThisYear) t.yearInc += tx.amount;
      } else if (tx.type === 'expense') {
        if (isToday) t.todayExp += tx.amount;
        if (isThisWeek) t.weekExp += tx.amount;
        if (isThisMonth) t.monthExpP += tx.amount;
        if (isThisYear) t.yearExp += tx.amount;
      }
    }
    return t;
  }, [state.transactions, today, weekStart, weekEnd, thisMonth, thisYear]);
  const { todayInc, todayExp, weekInc, weekExp, monthIncP, monthExpP, yearInc, yearExp } = totals;

  // 今年第一天 ~ 今年最後一天
  const thisYearStart = `${thisYear}/01/01`;
  const thisYearEnd = `${thisYear}/12/31`;

  // 本月區間
  const monthEndDay = new Date(parseInt(thisMonth.slice(0, 4)), parseInt(thisMonth.slice(5, 7)), 0).getDate();
  const monthStartStr = `${thisMonth.replace('-', '/')}/01`;
  const monthEndStr = `${thisMonth.replace('-', '/')}/${String(monthEndDay).padStart(2, '0')}`;

  // 最近紀錄：依日期排序（新的在上），最多 15 筆，並按日期分組
  // 同一筆轉帳的時序：先付手續費 → 轉出 → 轉入
  // 新到舊顯示（由上到下）：轉入 → 轉出 → 手續費
  const roleOrder = { in: 0, out: 1, fee: 2 };
  // 最近紀錄計算(useMemo:只在 transactions / 篩選 / 排序 變動時重算)
  const { recent, recentGroups, recentGroupKeys } = React.useMemo(() => {
    // 套用篩選
    const filtered = state.transactions.filter((t) => {
      if (recentFilter === 'all') return true;
      if (recentFilter === 'transfer') return !!t.transferRole;
      if (recentFilter === 'expense') return t.type === 'expense' && !t.transferRole;
      if (recentFilter === 'income') return t.type === 'income' && !t.transferRole;
      return true;
    });
    let result;
    if (isAmountSort(sortMode)) {
      result = sortTxnList(filtered, sortMode).slice(0, 15);
    } else {
      result = [...filtered]
        .sort((a, b) => {
          const cmp = sortMode === 'date_asc'
            ? a.date.localeCompare(b.date)
            : b.date.localeCompare(a.date);
          if (cmp !== 0) return cmp;
          const cmp2 = sortMode === 'date_asc'
            ? (a.createdAt || 0) - (b.createdAt || 0)
            : (b.createdAt || 0) - (a.createdAt || 0);
          if (cmp2 !== 0) return cmp2;
          const ra = roleOrder[a.transferRole] ?? 99;
          const rb = roleOrder[b.transferRole] ?? 99;
          return ra - rb;
        })
        .slice(0, 15);
    }
    // 按日期分組
    const groups = {};
    const keys = [];
    for (const t of result) {
      if (!groups[t.date]) {
        groups[t.date] = [];
        keys.push(t.date);
      }
      groups[t.date].push(t);
    }
    return { recent: result, recentGroups: groups, recentGroupKeys: keys };
  }, [state.transactions, recentFilter, sortMode]);

  // 批量刪除
  const selectableCount = recent.length;
  const allSelected = selectableCount > 0 && selectedIds.size === selectableCount;

  // 選擇模式下的左右滑取消手勢(跟 TxnListPage 一致)
  const exitSwipe = useSwipeToClose(selectMode ? exitSelectMode : null);
  const toggleAll = () => {
    if (allSelected) setSelectedIds(new Set());
    else setSelectedIds(new Set(recent.map((t) => t.id)));
  };
  const doBatchDelete = () => {
    const ids = Array.from(selectedIds);
    if (ids.length === 0) return;
    const sel = state.transactions.filter((t) => ids.includes(t.id));
    const transferIds = new Set();
    const settleIds = new Set();
    sel.forEach((t) => {
      if (t.transferId) transferIds.add(t.transferId);
      if (t.settleId) settleIds.add(t.settleId);
    });
    const actuallyDeleteIds = new Set(ids);
    state.transactions.forEach((t) => {
      if (t.transferId && transferIds.has(t.transferId)) actuallyDeleteIds.add(t.id);
      if (t.settleId && settleIds.has(t.settleId)) actuallyDeleteIds.add(t.id);
    });
    // 預測股票買進 cascade 連動清掉的 sell + settle 紀錄,加入 actuallyDeleteIds 一起顯示
    const cascadeIds = expandStockBuyCascade(state, actuallyDeleteIds);
    if (cascadeIds.size > 0) {
      for (const id of cascadeIds) actuallyDeleteIds.add(id);
    }
    const delCount = actuallyDeleteIds.size;
    const includesTransfer = transferIds.size > 0;
    const includesSettle = settleIds.size > 0;
    const expandedCount = delCount - ids.length;
    const listText = buildBatchDeletePreview(state.transactions, selectedIds, actuallyDeleteIds);
    if (!setConfirmDialog) return;
    // message:只有「為什麼會多刪幾筆」的提示,不再寫總數(target list 已表達)
    let linkMsg;
    if (expandedCount > 0) {
      if (includesTransfer && includesSettle) {
        linkMsg = '同組轉帳與股票結算將一併刪除。';
      } else if (includesSettle) {
        linkMsg = '本金歸還與損益屬同一組,將一併刪除。';
      } else if (includesTransfer) {
        linkMsg = '轉帳兩端紀錄屬同一組,將一併刪除。';
      }
    }
    // 偵測股票買進影響:若刪除會讓某 holding 完全消失,加警告
    const stockImpact = detectStockBuyImpact(state, actuallyDeleteIds);
    if (stockImpact.msg) {
      linkMsg = (linkMsg ? linkMsg + '\n\n' : '') + stockImpact.msg;
    }
    setConfirmDialog({
      title: stockImpact.anyHoldingDestroyed ? '刪除股票買進'
        : includesSettle && includesTransfer ? '刪除多筆紀錄'
        : includesSettle ? '刪除股票結算'
        : includesTransfer ? '刪除轉帳'
        : `刪除 ${ids.length} 筆交易`,
      target: { label: '將刪除', name: listText, multiline: true },
      message: linkMsg,
      warning: '此操作無法復原',
      confirmText: stockImpact.anyHoldingDestroyed ? '仍要刪除持股' : '刪除',
      highlightWords: stockImpact.highlightWords,
      danger: true,
      onConfirm: () => {
        setState && setState((s) => ({
          ...s,
          transactions: s.transactions.filter((t) => !actuallyDeleteIds.has(t.id)),
        }));
        if (toastRich) {
          toastRich({ title: `已刪除 ${delCount} 筆`, amount: '✓', amountColor: 'var(--pink-text)' }, 1200);
        } else if (toast) {
          toast(`已刪除 ${delCount} 筆`);
        }
        exitSelectMode();
      },
    });
  };

  return (
    <div style={styles.page} {...(selectMode ? exitSwipe : {})}>
      {/* 頂部：只保留 App 名稱（selectMode 時顯示已選資訊） */}
      <div style={styles.topBar}>
        {selectMode ? (
          <>
            <div style={styles.topBarMain}>
              <div style={styles.appName}>
                <span style={{ color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>已選</span>
                <span style={{ marginLeft: 6, fontVariantNumeric: 'tabular-nums' }}>{selectedIds.size}</span>
                <span style={{ marginLeft: 4, fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 500, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>/{selectableCount}</span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <span
              style={{
                fontSize: 14,
                fontWeight: 600,
                color: 'var(--pink-text)',
                cursor: 'pointer',
                padding: '6px 14px',
                borderRadius: 16,
                border: '1.5px solid var(--pink)',
                background: 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.08)',
                userSelect: 'none',
                WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
              }}
              onClick={exitSelectMode}
            >取消</span>
          </>
        ) : (
          <>
            <div style={styles.topBarMain}>
              <div style={styles.appName}>記帳軟體</div>
            </div>
            <EditOrderButton editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />
          </>
        )}
      </div>

      <EditModeBanner editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />

      <div style={styles.pageScroll}>
      {/* 本月收支 - 常駐釘選在頂端（sticky），不參與排序 */}
      <div style={{
        ...styles.stickySummary,
        ...(editMode ? { position: 'static' } : {}),
      }}>
        <Block
          editMode={false}
          blockKey="summary"
          isFirst={true}
          isLast={false}
          title="本月收支"
        >
          <div style={styles.summaryRow}>
            <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
              <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>收入</div>
              <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: 'var(--mint-text)' }}>{fmt(monthInc)}</div>
            </div>
            <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
              <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>支出</div>
              <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>{fmt(monthExp)}</div>
            </div>
            <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
              <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>結餘</div>
              <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: (monthInc - monthExp) < 0 ? 'var(--pink)' : (monthInc - monthExp) > 0 ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--text)' }}>{fmtSigned(monthInc - monthExp)}</div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Block>
      </div>

      {/* 可排序區塊列表 */}
      {blockOrder.filter((k) => k !== 'summary').map((blockKey, idx, arr) => {
        const blockProps = {
          onReorder: setPageOrder,
          key: blockKey,
          blockKey,
          editMode,
          isFirst: idx === 0,
          isLast: idx === arr.length - 1,
          onMoveUp: () => moveBlock(blockKey, -1),
          onMoveDown: () => moveBlock(blockKey, 1),
        };

        if (blockKey === 'summary') {
          return null;
        }

        if (blockKey === 'dateStrip') {
          return (
            <Block {...blockProps} title="日期">
              <Calendar
                state={state}
                currentMonth={currentMonth}
                selectedDate={selectedDate}
                setSelectedDate={setSelectedDate}
                onOpenDate={onOpenDate}
                editMode={editMode}
              />
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'actions') {
          return (
            <Block {...blockProps} title="快速動作">
              <div style={styles.addRow}>
                <button style={styles.recordBtn} onClick={() => !editMode && onAdd('expense')}>
                  <span style={styles.recordBtnIcon}>
                    <TypeIcon name="cash" size={20} color="#1a1a1a" />
                  </span>
                  <span>記一筆</span>
                </button>
                <button style={styles.addAcctBtn} onClick={() => !editMode && onOpenAccount()}>
                  <span style={styles.recordBtnIcon}>
                    <TypeIcon name="bank" size={18} color="var(--text-dim)" />
                  </span>
                  <span>帳戶</span>
                </button>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'lendReminder') {
          // 找出所有未收回(pending 或 partial)的代墊
          const lendOuts = state.transactions
            .filter((t) => t.transferRole === 'lend_out' && (t.lendMeta?.status === 'pending' || t.lendMeta?.status === 'partial'))
            .sort((a, b) => {
              // 有預計日的優先,且越近越前面
              const ad = a.lendMeta?.expectDate || '9999-12-31';
              const bd = b.lendMeta?.expectDate || '9999-12-31';
              return ad.localeCompare(bd);
            });
          // 沒未收回代墊就完全不顯示這個 block(連標題都不顯示)
          if (lendOuts.length === 0) return null;
          const today = todayStr();
          const totalRemaining = lendOuts.reduce((s, t) => s + (t.amount - (t.lendMeta?.collectedAmount || 0)), 0);
          return (
            <Block {...blockProps} title={`代墊提醒 · ${lendOuts.length} 筆未收回`}>
              <div style={{
                background: 'var(--bg-card-2, rgba(127,127,127,0.05))',
                borderRadius: 12, padding: 4,
              }}>
                {/* 摘要列 */}
                <div style={{
                  display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between',
                  padding: '8px 12px', borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border-soft)',
                  fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text-dim)',
                }}>
                  <span>未收回總額</span>
                  <span style={{ color: 'var(--mint-text)', fontWeight: 700, fontSize: 15 }}>
                    {fmt(totalRemaining)}
                  </span>
                </div>
                {/* 每筆代墊 */}
                {lendOuts.map((t, i) => {
                  const remaining = t.amount - (t.lendMeta?.collectedAmount || 0);
                  const isPartial = t.lendMeta?.status === 'partial';
                  const expDate = t.lendMeta?.expectDate;
                  const overdue = expDate && expDate < today;
                  const debtor = t.lendMeta?.debtor;
                  return (
                    <div
                      key={t.id}
                      onClick={() => !editMode && onOpenLend && onOpenLend(t)}
                      style={{
                        padding: '10px 12px', cursor: 'pointer',
                        borderBottom: i === lendOuts.length - 1 ? 'none' : '1px solid var(--border-soft)',
                        display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10,
                      }}
                    >
                      <div style={{ flex: 1, minWidth: 0 }}>
                        <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 500, color: 'var(--text)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 6 }}>
                          {debtor && <span style={{ color: 'var(--mint-text)', fontWeight: 600 }}>{debtor}</span>}
                          <span style={{
                            overflow: 'hidden', textOverflow: 'ellipsis', whiteSpace: 'nowrap',
                            color: debtor ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--text)',
                          }}>{t.note || '[代墊]'}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 3, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8 }}>
                          <span>{t.date.replace(/-/g, '/')}</span>
                          {expDate && (
                            <span style={{ color: overdue ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--text-faint)' }}>
                              預計 {expDate.slice(5).replace('-', '/')}{overdue ? ' (逾期)' : ''}
                            </span>
                          )}
                          {isPartial && (
                            <span style={{
                              fontSize: 10, padding: '1px 6px', borderRadius: 8,
                              background: 'rgba(245,216,74,0.18)', color: 'var(--highlight)',
                            }}>已收回 {fmt(t.lendMeta.collectedAmount)}</span>
                          )}
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      <div style={{ textAlign: 'right', flexShrink: 0 }}>
                        <div style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--mint-text)' }}>
                          {fmt(remaining)}
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      <div style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)', fontSize: 18 }}>›</div>
                    </div>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }


        if (blockKey === 'periods') {
          return (
            <Block {...blockProps} title="期間花費">
              <div style={styles.periodCard}>
                {[
                  { key: 'today', label: '本日花費', range: today.replace(/-/g, '/'), inc: todayInc, exp: todayExp },
                  { key: 'week', label: '本週花費', range: `${weekStart.replace(/-/g, '/')} ~ ${weekEnd.replace(/-/g, '/')}`, inc: weekInc, exp: weekExp },
                  { key: 'month', label: '本月花費', range: `${monthStartStr} ~ ${monthEndStr}`, inc: monthIncP, exp: monthExpP },
                  { key: 'year', label: '本年花費', range: `${thisYearStart} ~ ${thisYearEnd}`, inc: yearInc, exp: yearExp },
                ].map((p, i, arr) => (
                  <div
                    key={p.key}
                    style={{ ...styles.periodRow, borderBottom: i === arr.length - 1 ? 'none' : '1px solid var(--border-soft)' }}
                    onClick={() => !editMode && onOpenPeriod(p.key)}
                  >
                    <div style={styles.periodLeft}>
                      <div style={styles.periodLabel}>{p.label}</div>
                      <div style={styles.periodRange}>{p.range}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div style={styles.periodRight}>
                      <div style={styles.periodIncAmt}>+{fmt(p.inc)}</div>
                      <div style={styles.periodExpAmt}>-{fmt(p.exp)}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div style={styles.periodArrow}>›</div>
                  </div>
                ))}
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'recent') {
          const filterOpts = [
            { key: 'transfer', label: '轉帳' },
            { key: 'income', label: '收入' },
            { key: 'expense', label: '支出' },
            { key: 'all', label: '全部' },
          ];
          // 只有非「全部」模式才套用 minHeight
          const contentStyle = recentFilter !== 'all' && recentMinHeight > 0
            ? { minHeight: recentMinHeight }
            : {};
          return (
            <Block key={blockKey} {...blockProps} title="最近紀錄" headerRight={!editMode ? (
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8, marginTop: 6 }}>
                <div style={styles.recentFilterBar}>
                  {filterOpts.map((opt) => (
                    <span
                      key={opt.key}
                      style={{
                        ...styles.recentFilterChip,
                        ...(recentFilter === opt.key ? styles.recentFilterChipActive : {}),
                      }}
                      onClick={() => changeRecentFilter(opt.key)}
                    >
                      {opt.label}
                    </span>
                  ))}
                  <ListSortControl sortMode={sortMode} setSortMode={setSortMode} />
                </div>
              </div>
            ) : null}>
              <div ref={recentContentRef} style={contentStyle}>
              {recent.length ? (
                <div style={styles.txnList}>
                  {isAmountSort(sortMode) ? (
                    // 金額排序:不分組,扁平輸出
                    recent.map((t) => (
                      <TxnRow
                        key={t.id}
                        txn={t}
                        state={state}
                        catIcon={catIcon}
                        selectMode={selectMode}
                        selected={selectedIds.has(t.id)}
                        onClick={() => {
                          if (editMode) return;
                          if (selectMode) toggleSelect(t.id);
                          else onClickTxn(t);
                        }}
                        onLongPress={() => {
                          if (editMode || selectMode) return;
                          enterSelectModeWith(t.id);
                        }}
                      />
                    ))
                  ) : (
                    recentGroupKeys.map((date) => {
                      const days = recentGroups[date];
                      const wd = ['日', '一', '二', '三', '四', '五', '六'][new Date(date).getDay()];
                      return (
                        <React.Fragment key={date}>
                          <div style={styles.groupDate}>
                            <span>{date.replace(/-/g, '/')} · 週{wd}</span>
                          </div>
                          {days.map((t) => (
                            <TxnRow
                              key={t.id}
                              txn={t}
                              state={state}
                              catIcon={catIcon}
                              selectMode={selectMode}
                              selected={selectedIds.has(t.id)}
                              onClick={() => {
                                if (editMode) return;
                                if (selectMode) toggleSelect(t.id);
                                else onClickTxn(t);
                              }}
                              onLongPress={() => {
                                if (editMode || selectMode) return;
                                enterSelectModeWith(t.id);
                              }}
                            />
                          ))}
                        </React.Fragment>
                      );
                    })
                  )}
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div style={styles.empty}>
                  {recentFilter === 'all' ? '還沒有紀錄' : `沒有符合「${filterOpts.find(o => o.key === recentFilter)?.label}」的紀錄`}
                  <br />
                  {recentFilter === 'all' ? '點上方按鈕開始記一筆' : '試試切換其他篩選'}
                </div>
              )}
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        return null;
      })}

      {/* 版本號：首頁底部置中 */}
      <div style={styles.versionFooter}>版本{APP_VERSION}</div>
      </div>

      {selectMode && (
        <div style={{
          position: 'fixed', bottom: 0, left: 0, right: 0,
          maxWidth: 480, margin: '0 auto',
          padding: '10px 14px calc(12px + env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0px))',
          background: 'rgba(20, 22, 25, 0.96)',
          backdropFilter: 'blur(20px)',
          WebkitBackdropFilter: 'blur(20px)',
          borderTop: '1px solid var(--border)',
          display: 'flex', gap: 8, zIndex: 60,
          boxShadow: '0 -12px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',
        }}>
          <button
            style={{
              flex: '0 0 auto', padding: '10px 16px',
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
              border: '1px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 10,
              fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer',
              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 6,
            }}
            onClick={toggleAll}
            disabled={selectableCount === 0}
          >
            <div style={{
              width: 18, height: 18, borderRadius: 9,
              border: `1.5px solid ${allSelected ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--text-faint)'}`,
              background: allSelected ? 'var(--mint)' : 'transparent',
              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
            }}>
              {allSelected && (
                <svg width="10" height="10" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="#1a1a1a" strokeWidth="4" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
                  <polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12" />
                </svg>
              )}
            </div>
            <span>{allSelected ? '取消全選' : '全選'}</span>
          </button>
          <button
            style={{
              flex: 1, padding: '10px 16px',
              background: selectedIds.size > 0 ? 'var(--pink)' : 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.25)',
              color: selectedIds.size > 0 ? '#1a1a1a' : 'var(--text-faint)',
              border: 'none', borderRadius: 10,
              fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700,
              cursor: selectedIds.size > 0 ? 'pointer' : 'default',
              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', gap: 6,
              transition: 'background 0.15s, color 0.15s',
            }}
            onClick={() => selectedIds.size > 0 && doBatchDelete()}
            disabled={selectedIds.size === 0}
          >
            <TypeIcon name="trash" size={14} color={selectedIds.size > 0 ? '#1a1a1a' : 'var(--text-faint)'} />
            <span>刪除 {selectedIds.size > 0 ? `(${selectedIds.size})` : ''}</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 日期條（前3天 + 今天 + 後3天）============
function Calendar({ state, currentMonth, selectedDate, setSelectedDate, onOpenDate, editMode }) {
  // 以「今天」為基準，往前 3 天、往後 3 天 = 7 格
  const today = todayStr();
  const todayDate = new Date(today);
  const cells = [];
  for (let offset = -3; offset <= 3; offset++) {
    const d = new Date(todayDate);
    d.setDate(todayDate.getDate() + offset);
    const iso = `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}`;
    cells.push({
      iso,
      day: d.getDate(),
      weekday: ['日', '一', '二', '三', '四', '五', '六'][d.getDay()],
      isToday: iso === today,
    });
  }

  // 每日收支 flags（用於顯示點點）
  const dayFlags = {};
  for (const t of state.transactions) {
    if (!isRealFlow(t)) continue;
    if (!dayFlags[t.date]) dayFlags[t.date] = { inc: false, exp: false };
    if (t.type === 'income') dayFlags[t.date].inc = true;
    else if (t.type === 'expense') dayFlags[t.date].exp = true;
  }

  const handleClick = (iso) => {
    if (editMode) return;
    setSelectedDate(iso);
    if (onOpenDate) onOpenDate(iso);
  };

  return (
    <div style={styles.dateStripCard}>
      <div style={styles.dateStripRow}>
        {cells.map((c) => {
          const flags = dayFlags[c.iso];
          const isSelected = c.iso === selectedDate;
          return (
            <div
              key={c.iso}
              style={{
                ...styles.dateCell,
                ...(c.isToday ? styles.dateCellToday : {}),
                ...(isSelected && !c.isToday ? styles.dateCellSelected : {}),
                ...(isSelected && c.isToday ? styles.dateCellTodaySelected : {}),
              }}
              onClick={() => handleClick(c.iso)}
            >
              <div style={{
                ...styles.dateCellWeekday,
                color: c.isToday ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--text-faint)',
              }}>{c.weekday}</div>
              <div style={{
                ...styles.dateCellDay,
                color: c.isToday ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--text)',
                fontWeight: c.isToday ? 700 : 500,
              }}>{c.day}</div>
              {flags ? (
                <div style={styles.dateCellDots}>
                  {flags.inc && <div style={{ ...styles.dot, background: 'var(--mint)' }} />}
                  {flags.exp && <div style={{ ...styles.dot, background: 'var(--pink)' }} />}
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div style={styles.dateCellDotsPlaceholder} />
              )}
            </div>
          );
        })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 明細頁 ============
function TxnListPage({ state, setState, setConfirmDialog, toastRich, toast, catIcon, currentMonth, setCurrentMonth, onClickTxn, editMode, setEditMode, onSelectModeChange, blockOrder, moveBlock, setPageOrder }) {
  const [scope, setScope] = useState('month'); // day | month | year
  // 日模式用獨立 state（month 模式維持原本 currentMonth 同步）
  const [currentDate, setCurrentDate] = useState(todayStr());
  // 多選刪除模式
  const [selectMode, setSelectMode] = useState(false);
  const [selectedIds, setSelectedIds] = useState(() => new Set());

  // 進階篩選(啟用後取代 scope/月份/年份邏輯)
  const [filterMode, setFilterMode] = useState(false);
  const [showFilter, setShowFilter] = useState(false);
  const [fStart, setFStart] = useState(todayStr().slice(0, 7) + '-01');
  const [fEnd, setFEnd] = useState(todayStr());
  const [fType, setFType] = useState('all'); // all | income | expense
  const [fKeyword, setFKeyword] = useState('');
  const [fEditField, setFEditField] = useState(null); // 'start' | 'end' | null
  const filterSwipe = useSwipeToClose(() => setShowFilter(false));
  // 列表類型篩選(非進階篩選模式下使用): all | income | expense | transfer
  const [listFilter, setListFilter] = useState('all');
  const [sortMode, setSortMode] = useListSort();

  const applyFilter = () => {
    if (fStart > fEnd) {
      if (toast) toast('起始日期不能晚於結束日期');
      return;
    }
    setFilterMode(true);
    setShowFilter(false);
  };
  const clearFilter = () => {
    setFilterMode(false);
    setShowFilter(false);
    setFKeyword('');
    setFType('all');
  };

  // 把 selectMode 同步給父層(用來控制 bottom nav 顯示)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (onSelectModeChange) onSelectModeChange(selectMode);
  }, [selectMode, onSelectModeChange]);

  // 切換頁面或 unmount 時自動退出選擇模式
  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      if (onSelectModeChange) onSelectModeChange(false);
    };
  }, [onSelectModeChange]);

  const exitSelectMode = () => {
    setSelectMode(false);
    setSelectedIds(new Set());
  };

  const toggleSelect = (id) => {
    setSelectedIds((prev) => {
      const next = new Set(prev);
      if (next.has(id)) next.delete(id); else next.add(id);
      return next;
    });
  };

  const enterSelectModeWith = (id) => {
    setSelectMode(true);
    setSelectedIds(new Set([id]));
  };

  const shiftDay = (delta) => {
    const d = new Date(currentDate + 'T00:00:00');
    d.setDate(d.getDate() + delta);
    const iso = `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}`;
    setCurrentDate(iso);
  };

  const shiftMonth = (delta) => {
    const [y, m] = currentMonth.split('-').map(Number);
    const d = new Date(y, m - 1 + delta, 1);
    setCurrentMonth(`${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}`);
  };

  const shiftYear = (delta) => {
    const [y, m] = currentMonth.split('-').map(Number);
    setCurrentMonth(`${y + delta}-${String(m).padStart(2, '0')}`);
  };

  // 依 scope 決定過濾 prefix
  const prefix = scope === 'day' ? currentDate
    : scope === 'month' ? currentMonth
    : currentMonth.slice(0, 4);

  // filterMode 啟用時用進階篩選取代 scope 模式
  // 篩選 + 累加 + 排序 + 分組 — 全部用 useMemo 緩存
  // (僅在 transactions / 篩選條件 / 排序模式 變動時重算)
  const { monthTxns, inc, exp, sorted, groups, groupKeys } = React.useMemo(() => {
    const _monthTxns = filterMode
      ? state.transactions
          .filter((t) => t.date >= fStart && t.date <= fEnd)
          .filter((t) => fType === 'all' ? true : t.type === fType)
          .filter((t) => {
            if (!fKeyword.trim()) return true;
            const kw = fKeyword.trim().toLowerCase();
            return (t.category || '').toLowerCase().includes(kw)
                || (t.subCategory || '').toLowerCase().includes(kw)
                || (t.note || '').toLowerCase().includes(kw);
          })
      : state.transactions.filter((t) => t.date.startsWith(prefix));
    let _inc = 0, _exp = 0;
    for (const t of _monthTxns) {
      if (!isRealFlow(t)) continue;
      if (t.type === 'income') _inc += t.amount;
      else if (t.type === 'expense') _exp += t.amount;
    }
    const sortedAll = sortTxnList(_monthTxns, sortMode);
    const _sorted = filterMode
      ? sortedAll
      : sortedAll.filter((t) => {
          if (listFilter === 'all') return true;
          if (listFilter === 'transfer') return t.type === 'transfer' || t.transferId;
          return t.type === listFilter;
        });
    const _groups = {};
    _sorted.forEach((t) => {
      (_groups[t.date] ||= []).push(t);
    });
    const _groupKeys = isAmountSort(sortMode)
      ? []
      : Object.keys(_groups).sort((a, b) => sortMode === 'date_asc' ? a.localeCompare(b) : b.localeCompare(a));
    return { monthTxns: _monthTxns, inc: _inc, exp: _exp, sorted: _sorted, groups: _groups, groupKeys: _groupKeys };
  }, [state.transactions, filterMode, fStart, fEnd, fType, fKeyword, prefix, sortMode, listFilter]);

  const order = blockOrder || ['summary', 'period', 'list'];

  // 批量刪除觸發
  const doBatchDelete = () => {
    const ids = Array.from(selectedIds);
    if (ids.length === 0) return;
    const txns = state.transactions.filter((t) => ids.includes(t.id));
    // 展開連動的轉帳對(如果有選到轉帳筆,同 transferId 的要一起刪除)
    // 同時:展開股票結算組(同 settleId 的也一起)
    const transferIds = new Set();
    const settleIds = new Set();
    txns.forEach((t) => {
      if (t.transferId) transferIds.add(t.transferId);
      if (t.settleId) settleIds.add(t.settleId);
    });
    const actuallyDeleteIds = new Set(ids);
    state.transactions.forEach((t) => {
      if (t.transferId && transferIds.has(t.transferId)) actuallyDeleteIds.add(t.id);
      if (t.settleId && settleIds.has(t.settleId)) actuallyDeleteIds.add(t.id);
    });
    // 預測股票買進 cascade 連動清掉的 sell + settle 紀錄,加入 actuallyDeleteIds 一起顯示
    const cascadeIds = expandStockBuyCascade(state, actuallyDeleteIds);
    if (cascadeIds.size > 0) {
      for (const id of cascadeIds) actuallyDeleteIds.add(id);
    }
    const delCount = actuallyDeleteIds.size;
    const includesTransfer = transferIds.size > 0;
    const includesSettle = settleIds.size > 0;
    const expandedCount = delCount - ids.length;

    const listText = buildBatchDeletePreview(state.transactions, selectedIds, actuallyDeleteIds);

    // message:只在有連動展開時提示原因(target list 已表達總數)
    let linkMsg;
    if (expandedCount > 0) {
      if (includesTransfer && includesSettle) {
        linkMsg = '同組轉帳與股票結算將一併刪除。';
      } else if (includesSettle) {
        linkMsg = '本金歸還與損益屬同一組,將一併刪除。';
      } else if (includesTransfer) {
        linkMsg = '轉帳兩端紀錄屬同一組,將一併刪除。';
      }
    }
    // 偵測股票買進影響:若刪除會讓某 holding 完全消失,加警告
    const stockImpact = detectStockBuyImpact(state, actuallyDeleteIds);
    if (stockImpact.msg) {
      linkMsg = (linkMsg ? linkMsg + '\n\n' : '') + stockImpact.msg;
    }

    setConfirmDialog({
      title: stockImpact.anyHoldingDestroyed ? '刪除股票買進'
        : includesSettle && includesTransfer ? '刪除多筆紀錄'
        : includesSettle ? '刪除股票結算'
        : includesTransfer ? '刪除轉帳'
        : `刪除 ${ids.length} 筆交易`,
      target: {
        label: '將刪除',
        name: `${listText}`,
        multiline: true,
      },
      message: linkMsg,
      warning: '此操作無法復原',
      confirmText: stockImpact.anyHoldingDestroyed ? '仍要刪除持股' : '刪除',
      highlightWords: stockImpact.highlightWords,
      danger: true,
      onConfirm: () => {
        setState((s) => ({
          ...s,
          transactions: s.transactions.filter((t) => !actuallyDeleteIds.has(t.id)),
        }));
        if (toastRich) {
          toastRich({
            title: `已刪除 ${delCount} 筆`,
            amount: '✓',
            amountColor: 'var(--pink-text)',
          }, 1200);
        } else if (toast) {
          toast(`已刪除 ${delCount} 筆`);
        }
        exitSelectMode();
      },
    });
  };

  const selectableCount = sorted.length;
  const allSelected = selectableCount > 0 && selectedIds.size === selectableCount;
  const toggleAll = () => {
    if (allSelected) {
      setSelectedIds(new Set());
    } else {
      setSelectedIds(new Set(sorted.map((t) => t.id)));
    }
  };

  // 選擇模式下的左右滑返回手勢
  const exitSwipe = useSwipeToClose(selectMode ? exitSelectMode : null);

  return (
    <div
      style={styles.page}
      {...(selectMode ? exitSwipe : {})}
    >
      <div style={styles.pageHeader}>
        <h1 style={styles.pageTitle}>
          {selectMode ? (
            <span>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>已選</span>
              <span style={{ marginLeft: 6, fontVariantNumeric: 'tabular-nums' }}>{selectedIds.size}</span>
              <span style={{ marginLeft: 4, fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 500, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>/{selectableCount}</span>
            </span>
          ) : (
            <span>明細</span>
          )}
        </h1>
        {selectMode ? (
          <div
            style={{
              fontSize: 14,
              fontWeight: 600,
              color: 'var(--pink-text)',
              cursor: 'pointer',
              padding: '6px 14px',
              borderRadius: 16,
              border: '1.5px solid var(--pink)',
              background: 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.08)',
              userSelect: 'none',
              WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
            }}
            onClick={exitSelectMode}
          >
            取消
          </div>
        ) : (
          <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 6, alignItems: 'center' }}>
            {!editMode && (
              <button
                style={{
                  background: filterMode ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--bg-card)',
                  border: `1px solid ${filterMode ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--border)'}`,
                  borderRadius: 10,
                  padding: '6px 8px',
                  cursor: 'pointer',
                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  color: filterMode ? '#1a1a1a' : 'var(--text-dim)',
                }}
                onClick={() => setShowFilter(true)}
                aria-label="搜尋"
              >
                <TypeIcon name="search" size={16} color={filterMode ? '#1a1a1a' : 'var(--text-dim)'} />
              </button>
            )}
            <EditOrderButton editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />
          </div>
        )}
      </div>

      <EditModeBanner editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />

      <div style={styles.pageScroll}>
      {order.map((blockKey, idx) => {
        const blockProps = {
          onReorder: setPageOrder,
          blockKey,
          editMode,
          isFirst: idx === 0,
          isLast: idx === order.length - 1,
          onMoveUp: () => moveBlock && moveBlock(blockKey, -1),
          onMoveDown: () => moveBlock && moveBlock(blockKey, 1),
        };

        if (blockKey === 'period') {
          // 導航標題
          const navTitle = scope === 'day'
            ? (() => {
                const [y, m, d] = currentDate.split('-');
                const wd = ['日', '一', '二', '三', '四', '五', '六'][new Date(currentDate + 'T00:00:00').getDay()];
                return `${y}/${m}/${d} (${wd})`;
              })()
            : scope === 'month'
              ? `${currentMonth.slice(0, 4)}年 ${parseInt(currentMonth.slice(5, 7))}月`
              : `${currentMonth.slice(0, 4)}年`;
          const onNavPrev = () => {
            if (editMode) return;
            setSelectedIds(new Set());
            if (scope === 'day') shiftDay(-1);
            else if (scope === 'month') shiftMonth(-1);
            else shiftYear(-1);
          };
          const onNavNext = () => {
            if (editMode) return;
            setSelectedIds(new Set());
            if (scope === 'day') shiftDay(1);
            else if (scope === 'month') shiftMonth(1);
            else shiftYear(1);
          };
          return (
            <Block key="period" {...blockProps} title="時間範圍">
              {/* 日/月/年 切換 */}
              <div style={styles.scopeToggle}>
                <button
                  style={{ ...styles.scopeBtn, ...(scope === 'day' ? styles.scopeBtnActive : {}) }}
                  onClick={() => { if (editMode) return; setScope('day'); setSelectedIds(new Set()); }}
                >日</button>
                <button
                  style={{ ...styles.scopeBtn, ...(scope === 'month' ? styles.scopeBtnActive : {}) }}
                  onClick={() => { if (editMode) return; setScope('month'); setSelectedIds(new Set()); }}
                >月</button>
                <button
                  style={{ ...styles.scopeBtn, ...(scope === 'year' ? styles.scopeBtnActive : {}) }}
                  onClick={() => { if (editMode) return; setScope('year'); setSelectedIds(new Set()); }}
                >年</button>
              </div>
              <div style={styles.monthHeader}>
                <div style={styles.monthNav} onClick={onNavPrev}>‹</div>
                <div style={styles.monthTitle}>{navTitle}</div>
                <div style={styles.monthNav} onClick={onNavNext}>›</div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'summary') {
          const scopeChar = scope === 'day' ? '日' : scope === 'month' ? '月' : '年';
          const scopeLabel = scope === 'day' ? '' : scope === 'month' ? '份' : '度';
          return (
            <Block key="summary" {...blockProps} title={
              <span><span style={{ color: 'var(--mint-text)', fontWeight: 700 }}>{scopeChar}</span>{scopeLabel}總覽</span>
            }>
              <div style={styles.summaryRow}>
                <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
                  <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>收入</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: 'var(--mint-text)' }}>{fmt(inc)}</div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
                  <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>支出</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>{fmt(exp)}</div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
                  <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>結餘</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: (inc - exp) < 0 ? "var(--pink)" : (inc - exp) > 0 ? "var(--mint)" : "var(--text)" }}>{fmtSigned(inc - exp)}</div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'list') {
          const scopeChar = scope === 'day' ? '日' : scope === 'month' ? '月' : '年';
          return (
            <Block
              key="list"
              {...blockProps}
              title={
                filterMode ? (
                  <span>
                    <span style={{ color: 'var(--accent-text)', fontWeight: 700 }}>篩選結果</span>
                    <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginLeft: 8, fontSize: 12, fontWeight: 500 }}>
                      {sorted.length} 筆
                    </span>
                  </span>
                ) : (
                  <span>全<span style={{ color: 'var(--mint-text)', fontWeight: 700 }}>{scopeChar}</span>交易列表</span>
                )
              }
              headerRight={filterMode ? (
                <div
                  style={{
                    fontSize: 11,
                    color: 'var(--text-dim)',
                    cursor: 'pointer',
                    padding: '4px 9px',
                    borderRadius: 8,
                    border: '1px solid var(--border)',
                    marginTop: 6,
                  }}
                  onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); clearFilter(); }}
                >
                  清除
                </div>
              ) : !editMode ? (
                <div style={{ ...styles.recentFilterBar, marginTop: 6 }} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
                  {[
                    { key: 'transfer', label: '轉帳' },
                    { key: 'income', label: '收入' },
                    { key: 'expense', label: '支出' },
                    { key: 'all', label: '全部' },
                  ].map((opt) => (
                    <span
                      key={opt.key}
                      style={{
                        ...styles.recentFilterChip,
                        ...(listFilter === opt.key ? styles.recentFilterChipActive : {}),
                      }}
                      onClick={() => { setSelectedIds(new Set()); setListFilter(opt.key); }}
                    >
                      {opt.label}
                    </span>
                  ))}
                  <ListSortControl sortMode={sortMode} setSortMode={setSortMode} />
                </div>
              ) : null}
            >
              {filterMode && (
                <div
                  style={{
                    display: 'flex',
                    flexWrap: 'wrap',
                    gap: 6,
                    padding: '4px 8px 10px',
                    fontSize: 11,
                  }}
                  onClick={() => setShowFilter(true)}
                >
                  <span style={{
                    padding: '3px 8px',
                    borderRadius: 6,
                    background: 'rgba(143, 127, 240, 0.15)',
                    color: 'var(--accent-text)',
                    fontWeight: 500,
                  }}>
                    {fStart.replace(/-/g, '/')} ~ {fEnd.replace(/-/g, '/')}
                  </span>
                  {fType !== 'all' && (
                    <span style={{
                      padding: '3px 8px',
                      borderRadius: 6,
                      background: fType === 'income' ? 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.15)' : 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.15)',
                      color: fType === 'income' ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--pink)',
                      fontWeight: 500,
                    }}>
                      {fType === 'income' ? '收入' : '支出'}
                    </span>
                  )}
                  {fKeyword.trim() && (
                    <span style={{
                      padding: '3px 8px',
                      borderRadius: 6,
                      background: 'var(--bg-card)',
                      color: 'var(--text-dim)',
                      fontWeight: 500,
                    }}>
                      「{fKeyword.trim()}」
                    </span>
                  )}
                </div>
              )}
              {sorted.length ? (
                <div style={styles.txnList}>
                  {isAmountSort(sortMode) ? (
                    // 金額排序:扁平列表(不分組)
                    sorted.map((t) => (
                      <TxnRow
                        key={t.id}
                        txn={t}
                        state={state}
                        catIcon={catIcon}
                        selectMode={selectMode}
                        selected={selectedIds.has(t.id)}
                        onClick={() => {
                          if (editMode) return;
                          if (selectMode) {
                            toggleSelect(t.id);
                          } else {
                            onClickTxn(t);
                          }
                        }}
                        onLongPress={() => {
                          if (editMode || selectMode) return;
                          enterSelectModeWith(t.id);
                        }}
                      />
                    ))
                  ) : (
                    groupKeys.map((date) => {
                    const days = groups[date];
                    const wd = ['日', '一', '二', '三', '四', '五', '六'][new Date(date).getDay()];
                    return (
                      <React.Fragment key={date}>
                        <div style={styles.groupDate}>
                          <span>{date.replace(/-/g, '/')} · 週{wd}</span>
                        </div>
                        {days.map((t) => (
                          <TxnRow
                            key={t.id}
                            txn={t}
                            state={state}
                            catIcon={catIcon}
                            selectMode={selectMode}
                            selected={selectedIds.has(t.id)}
                            onClick={() => {
                              if (editMode) return;
                              if (selectMode) {
                                toggleSelect(t.id);
                              } else {
                                onClickTxn(t);
                              }
                            }}
                            onLongPress={() => {
                              if (editMode || selectMode) return;
                              enterSelectModeWith(t.id);
                            }}
                          />
                        ))}
                      </React.Fragment>
                    );
                  })
                  )}
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div style={styles.empty}>這個月還沒有紀錄</div>
              )}
            </Block>
          );
        }

        return null;
      })}
      </div>

      {/* 多選模式 sticky footer:全選 + 刪除按鈕 */}
      {selectMode && (
        <div style={{
          position: 'fixed',
          bottom: 0,
          left: 0,
          right: 0,
          maxWidth: 480,
          margin: '0 auto',
          padding: '10px 14px calc(12px + env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0px))',
          background: 'rgba(20, 22, 25, 0.96)',
          backdropFilter: 'blur(20px)',
          WebkitBackdropFilter: 'blur(20px)',
          borderTop: '1px solid var(--border)',
          display: 'flex',
          gap: 8,
          zIndex: 60,
          boxShadow: '0 -12px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',
        }}>
          <button
            style={{
              flex: '0 0 auto',
              padding: '10px 16px',
              background: 'var(--bg-card)',
              color: 'var(--text)',
              border: '1px solid var(--border)',
              borderRadius: 10,
              fontSize: 13,
              fontWeight: 600,
              cursor: 'pointer',
              display: 'flex',
              alignItems: 'center',
              gap: 6,
            }}
            onClick={toggleAll}
            disabled={selectableCount === 0}
          >
            <div style={{
              width: 18, height: 18, borderRadius: 9,
              border: `1.5px solid ${allSelected ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--text-faint)'}`,
              background: allSelected ? 'var(--mint)' : 'transparent',
              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
            }}>
              {allSelected && (
