                <svg width="10" height="10" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="#1a1a1a" strokeWidth="4" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
                  <polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12" />
                </svg>
              )}
            </div>
            <span>{allSelected ? '取消全選' : '全選'}</span>
          </button>
          <button
            style={{
              flex: 1,
              padding: '10px 16px',
              background: selectedIds.size > 0 ? 'var(--pink)' : 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.25)',
              color: selectedIds.size > 0 ? '#1a1a1a' : 'var(--text-faint)',
              border: 'none',
              borderRadius: 10,
              fontSize: 14,
              fontWeight: 700,
              cursor: selectedIds.size > 0 ? 'pointer' : 'default',
              display: 'flex',
              alignItems: 'center',
              justifyContent: 'center',
              gap: 6,
              transition: 'background 0.15s, color 0.15s',
            }}
            onClick={() => selectedIds.size > 0 && doBatchDelete()}
            disabled={selectedIds.size === 0}
          >
            <TypeIcon name="trash" size={14} color={selectedIds.size > 0 ? '#1a1a1a' : 'var(--text-faint)'} />
            <span>刪除 {selectedIds.size > 0 ? `(${selectedIds.size})` : ''}</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 篩選條件彈窗 */}
      {showFilter && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.actionMenuBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowFilter(false)} {...filterSwipe}>
          <div style={styles.filterCard} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
            <div style={styles.actionMenuTitle}>
              <span style={{ display: 'inline-flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8 }}>
                <TypeIcon name="search" size={18} color="var(--accent-text)" />
                <span style={{ color: 'var(--accent-text)' }}>搜尋</span>
                <span style={{ marginLeft: 2 }}>交易</span>
              </span>
            </div>

            <div style={styles.fieldLabel}>起始日期</div>
            <button
              style={{ ...styles.field, textAlign: 'left', cursor: 'pointer' }}
              onClick={() => setFEditField('start')}
            >
              {fStart.replace(/-/g, '/')}
            </button>

            <div style={styles.fieldLabel}>結束日期</div>
            <button
              style={{ ...styles.field, textAlign: 'left', cursor: 'pointer' }}
              onClick={() => setFEditField('end')}
            >
              {fEnd.replace(/-/g, '/')}
            </button>

            <div style={styles.fieldLabel}>類型</div>
            <div style={styles.typeToggle}>
              {[
                { v: 'all', l: '全部' },
                { v: 'expense', l: '支出' },
                { v: 'income', l: '收入' },
              ].map((opt) => (
                <button
                  key={opt.v}
                  onClick={() => setFType(opt.v)}
                  style={{
                    ...styles.typeBtn,
                    ...(fType === opt.v
                      ? opt.v === 'income' ? { background: 'var(--mint)', color: 'var(--on-mint)' }
                      : opt.v === 'expense' ? { background: 'var(--pink)', color: 'var(--on-pink)' }
                      : { background: 'var(--accent)', color: '#fff' }
                      : {}),
                  }}
                >{opt.l}</button>
              ))}
            </div>

            <div style={styles.fieldLabel}>關鍵字（非必填）</div>
            <input
              type="text"
              style={styles.field}
              value={fKeyword}
              onChange={(e) => setFKeyword(e.target.value)}
              placeholder="搜尋分類或備註"
            />

            <button style={{ ...styles.saveBtn, background: 'var(--mint)', color: 'var(--on-mint)', marginTop: 20 }} onClick={applyFilter}>套用</button>
            {filterMode && (
              <button style={{ ...styles.deleteBtn, marginTop: 6 }} onClick={clearFilter}>清除篩選</button>
            )}
            <button style={{ ...styles.cancelBtn || styles.deleteBtn, marginTop: 6, background: 'transparent', border: '1px solid var(--border)', color: 'var(--text-dim)' }} onClick={() => setShowFilter(false)}>取消</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 日期選擇器(搜尋彈窗的起/結日期) */}
      {fEditField && (
        <DatePicker
          value={fEditField === 'start' ? fStart : fEnd}
          onChange={(d) => {
            if (fEditField === 'start') setFStart(d);
            else setFEnd(d);
          }}
          onClose={() => setFEditField(null)}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 統計頁 ============
function StatsPage({ state, catIcon, currentMonth, setCurrentMonth, editMode, setEditMode, blockOrder, moveBlock, setPageOrder, onClickTxn, onGoToTxn }) {
  const [scope, setScope] = useState('month'); // day | month | year
  const [chartType, setChartType] = useState('expense'); // expense | income（D）
  const [selectedCat, setSelectedCat] = useState(null); // 選中分類高亮（C）
  const [drillCat, setDrillCat] = useState(null); // 下鑽：查看某大類的子類佔比（I）
  const [currentDate, setCurrentDate] = useState(todayStr());

  const shiftDay = (delta) => {
    const d = new Date(currentDate + 'T00:00:00');
    d.setDate(d.getDate() + delta);
    const iso = `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}`;
    setCurrentDate(iso);
  };

  const shiftMonth = (delta) => {
    const [y, m] = currentMonth.split('-').map(Number);
    const d = new Date(y, m - 1 + delta, 1);
    setCurrentMonth(`${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}`);
  };

  const shiftYear = (delta) => {
    const [y, m] = currentMonth.split('-').map(Number);
    setCurrentMonth(`${y + delta}-${String(m).padStart(2, '0')}`);
  };

  const prefix = scope === 'day' ? currentDate
    : scope === 'month' ? currentMonth
    : currentMonth.slice(0, 4);

  // 一次掃過 transactions 完成:篩選 + 累加 inc/exp + 按分類聚合
  // (useMemo:僅在 transactions / prefix 變動時重算)
  const { txns, inc, exp, incData, expData, incTotal, expTotal } = React.useMemo(() => {
    const _txns = state.transactions.filter((t) => t.date.startsWith(prefix));
    let _inc = 0, _exp = 0;
    const incByCat = {};
    const expByCat = {};
    for (const t of _txns) {
      if (!isRealFlow(t)) continue;
      const cat = t.category || '未分類';
      if (t.type === 'income') {
        _inc += t.amount;
        incByCat[cat] = (incByCat[cat] || 0) + t.amount;
      } else if (t.type === 'expense') {
        _exp += t.amount;
        expByCat[cat] = (expByCat[cat] || 0) + t.amount;
      }
    }
    const _incData = Object.entries(incByCat).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]);
    const _expData = Object.entries(expByCat).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]);
    return {
      txns: _txns, inc: _inc, exp: _exp,
      incData: _incData, expData: _expData,
      incTotal: _inc, expTotal: _exp,
    };
  }, [state.transactions, prefix]);

  // 依目前選擇,決定主資料來源
  const mainData = chartType === 'expense' ? expData : incData;
  const mainTotal = chartType === 'expense' ? expTotal : incTotal;

  // === 上月/上年同期對比（F） ===
  const prevPrefix = (() => {
    if (scope === 'day') {
      // 昨天
      const d = new Date(currentDate + 'T00:00:00');
      d.setDate(d.getDate() - 1);
      return `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}`;
    }
    if (scope === 'month') {
      const [y, m] = currentMonth.split('-').map(Number);
      const d = new Date(y, m - 2, 1); // 上個月
      return `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}`;
    } else {
      const y = parseInt(currentMonth.slice(0, 4));
      return String(y - 1);
    }
  })();
  let prevInc = 0, prevExp = 0;
  for (const t of state.transactions) {
    if (!t.date.startsWith(prevPrefix)) continue;
    if (!isRealFlow(t)) continue;
    if (t.type === 'income') prevInc += t.amount;
    else if (t.type === 'expense') prevExp += t.amount;
  }
  const expDiffPct = prevExp > 0 ? ((exp - prevExp) / prevExp) * 100 : null;
  const incDiffPct = prevInc > 0 ? ((inc - prevInc) / prevInc) * 100 : null;

  // === Top 5 單筆最大支出（J） ===
  const top5Exp = [...txns]
    .filter((t) => t.type === 'expense' && isRealFlow(t))
    .sort((a, b) => b.amount - a.amount)
    .slice(0, 5);

  // === 每日/每月趨勢（E/G）===
  // month 模式：逐日；year 模式：逐月
  const trendData = (() => {
    if (scope === 'month') {
      const [y, m] = currentMonth.split('-').map(Number);
      const daysInMonth = new Date(y, m, 0).getDate();
      const arr = Array.from({ length: daysInMonth }, (_, i) => ({ label: i + 1, exp: 0, inc: 0 }));
      txns.forEach((t) => {
        if (!isRealFlow(t)) return;
        const d = parseInt(t.date.slice(8, 10));
        if (t.type === 'expense') arr[d - 1].exp += t.amount;
        else if (t.type === 'income') arr[d - 1].inc += t.amount;
      });
      return arr;
    } else {
      const arr = Array.from({ length: 12 }, (_, i) => ({ label: i + 1, exp: 0, inc: 0 }));
      txns.forEach((t) => {
        if (!isRealFlow(t)) return;
        const mo = parseInt(t.date.slice(5, 7));
        if (t.type === 'expense') arr[mo - 1].exp += t.amount;
        else if (t.type === 'income') arr[mo - 1].inc += t.amount;
      });
      return arr;
    }
  })();
  const trendMax = Math.max(...trendData.map((d) => chartType === 'expense' ? d.exp : d.inc), 1);

  // === 下鑽：某大類的子類佔比（I）===
  const subcatData = drillCat ? (() => {
    const bySub = {};
    txns.filter((t) => t.type === chartType && isRealFlow(t) && (t.category || '未分類') === drillCat).forEach((t) => {
      const k = t.subCategory || '（無子類）';
      bySub[k] = (bySub[k] || 0) + t.amount;
    });
    return Object.entries(bySub).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]);
  })() : null;
  const subcatTotal = subcatData ? subcatData.reduce((s, [, v]) => s + v, 0) : 0;

  // === 轉帳單獨統計（L）===
  let transferTotal = 0, feeTotal = 0, transferCount = 0;
  for (const t of txns) {
    if (t.transferRole === 'out') { transferTotal += t.amount; transferCount++; }
    else if (t.transferRole === 'fee') { feeTotal += t.amount; }
  }

  // 點分類進明細（H）
  const handleClickCategory = (cat) => {
    if (onGoToTxn) onGoToTxn({ month: scope === 'month' ? currentMonth : null, category: cat, type: chartType });
  };

  const renderDonut = (data, total, opts = {}) => {
    const { onSliceClick, highlighted, centerLabel, centerValue } = opts;
    if (total === 0) {
      return (
        <svg style={{ width: 240, height: 240 }} viewBox="0 0 100 100">
          <circle cx="50" cy="50" r="30.5" fill="none" stroke="var(--border)" strokeWidth="7" />
          <text x="50" y="54" textAnchor="middle" fontSize="5" fill="var(--text-faint)" style={{ letterSpacing: '0.3px' }}>沒有資料</text>
        </svg>
      );
    }
    const cx = 50, cy = 50;
    // 圓環半徑:中線 30.5,環厚 7(比舊版 35/25 更秀氣)
    const ringR = 30.5;
    const ringW = 7;
    const r = ringR + ringW / 2;     // 外緣半徑(用於 label 計算等)= 34
    const innerR = ringR - ringW / 2; // 內緣半徑 = 27

    let maxIdx = 0;
    data.forEach(([, v], i) => { if (v > data[maxIdx][1]) maxIdx = i; });

    // 切片之間留白氣口:依切片數動態調整
    // 圓角末端會延伸 ringW/2 ≈ 3.5,需要氣口足夠大才看得到留白
    // 切片 ≤ 4 時用 round + 18° 氣口(可見氣口約 2.4 視覺單位,精緻);多切片時用 butt + 3°
    const useRoundCap = data.length <= 4;
    const gapDeg = data.length > 1 ? (useRoundCap ? 18 : 3) : 0;
    const totalGap = gapDeg * data.length;
    const availableDeg = 360 - totalGap;

    let startDeg = -90;
    const slices = [];
    data.forEach(([cat, val], i) => {
      const sweepDeg = (val / total) * availableDeg;
      const endDeg = startDeg + sweepDeg;
      slices.push({ cat, val, startDeg, endDeg, sweepDeg, idx: i });
      startDeg = endDeg + gapDeg;
    });

    const polar = (cxv, cyv, rv, deg) => {
      const rad = (deg * Math.PI) / 180;
      return [cxv + rv * Math.cos(rad), cyv + rv * Math.sin(rad)];
    };

    // 用 stroke + linecap=round 畫環,自然帶圓角末端;單片用 circle dasharray 就好
    // 為了對應 path 算可點擊區、保留高亮位移,還是用 path 描邊,但 strokeLinecap='round' 提供圓角
    // 路徑只需要中線弧:M 起 A 終
    const arcStroke = (sd, ed) => {
      const [x1, y1] = polar(cx, cy, ringR, sd);
      const [x2, y2] = polar(cx, cy, ringR, ed);
      const large = ed - sd > 180 ? 1 : 0;
      return `M ${x1} ${y1} A ${ringR} ${ringR} 0 ${large} 1 ${x2} ${y2}`;
    };

    return (
      <svg style={{ width: 240, height: 240, overflow: 'visible' }} viewBox="0 0 100 100">
        <defs>
          {/* 整體淡光暈:給選中切片用 */}
          <filter id="donutGlow" x="-30%" y="-30%" width="160%" height="160%">
            <feGaussianBlur stdDeviation="0.8" result="blur" />
            <feMerge>
              <feMergeNode in="blur" />
              <feMergeNode in="SourceGraphic" />
            </feMerge>
          </filter>
          {/* 中央數字的微陰影 */}
          <filter id="centerTextShadow" x="-20%" y="-20%" width="140%" height="140%">
            <feGaussianBlur in="SourceAlpha" stdDeviation="0.4" />
            <feOffset dx="0" dy="0.3" result="offsetblur" />
            <feComponentTransfer>
              <feFuncA type="linear" slope="0.18" />
            </feComponentTransfer>
            <feMerge>
              <feMergeNode />
              <feMergeNode in="SourceGraphic" />
            </feMerge>
          </filter>
        </defs>

        {slices.map((s) => {
          const color = CHART_COLORS[s.idx % CHART_COLORS.length];
          const isHi = highlighted != null && highlighted === s.cat;
          const isDim = highlighted != null && highlighted !== s.cat;
          const isOut = isHi || (highlighted == null && s.idx === maxIdx);
          const midDeg = (s.startDeg + s.endDeg) / 2;
          const offset = isOut ? 2.5 : 0;
          const [tx, ty] = polar(0, 0, offset, midDeg);
          // 單一分類佔 100% 時 → 整圈
          const isFullCircle = s.sweepDeg >= 360 - 0.01;
          const labelR = ringR;
          const [lx, ly] = polar(cx + tx, cy + ty, labelR, midDeg);
          const pct = (s.val / total) * 100;
          const showLabel = pct >= 6;
          return (
            <g
              key={s.cat}
              transform={`translate(${tx}, ${ty})`}
              opacity={isDim ? 0.3 : 1}
              filter={isOut ? 'url(#donutGlow)' : undefined}
              style={{ cursor: onSliceClick ? 'pointer' : 'default', transition: 'opacity 0.2s, transform 0.2s' }}
              onClick={onSliceClick ? () => onSliceClick(s.cat) : undefined}
            >
              {isFullCircle ? (
                <circle cx={cx} cy={cy} r={ringR} fill="none" stroke={color} strokeWidth={ringW} />
              ) : (
                <path
                  d={arcStroke(s.startDeg, s.endDeg)}
                  fill="none"
                  stroke={color}
                  strokeWidth={ringW}
                  strokeLinecap={useRoundCap ? 'round' : 'butt'}
                />
              )}
              {showLabel && (
                <text
                  x={lx - tx}
                  y={ly - ty + 1.2}
                  textAnchor="middle"
                  fontSize="3.4"
                  fontWeight="700"
                  fill="#ffffff"
                  style={{ pointerEvents: 'none', letterSpacing: '0.2px' }}
                >
                  {pct.toFixed(0)}%
                </text>
              )}
            </g>
          );
        })}

        {/* 中央資訊:標題小字 + 主數值粗大字,層次清楚 */}
        <text
          x="50" y="46"
          textAnchor="middle"
          fontSize="4.2"
          fill="var(--text-faint)"
          style={{ letterSpacing: '0.6px' }}
        >
          {centerLabel || (chartType === 'expense' ? '總支出' : '總收入')}
        </text>
        <text
          x="50" y="58"
          textAnchor="middle"
          fontSize="10"
          fontWeight="700"
          fill="var(--text)"
          filter="url(#centerTextShadow)"
          style={{ letterSpacing: '-0.3px', fontFamily: "'Space Grotesk', sans-serif" }}
        >
          {centerValue != null ? fmt(centerValue) : fmt(total)}
        </text>
      </svg>
    );
  };

  // 每日/每月趨勢柱狀圖（E/G）
  const renderTrendChart = (data, max, type) => {
    const W = 320, H = 120, padL = 10, padR = 10, padT = 12, padB = 18;
    const chartW = W - padL - padR;
    const chartH = H - padT - padB;
    const barW = chartW / data.length;
    const color = type === 'expense' ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--mint)';
    return (
      <svg viewBox={`0 0 ${W} ${H}`} style={{ width: '100%', height: 120 }}>
        {data.map((d, i) => {
          const val = type === 'expense' ? d.exp : d.inc;
          const h = val > 0 ? (val / max) * chartH : 0;
          const x = padL + i * barW;
          const y = padT + chartH - h;
          return (
            <g key={i}>
              {h > 0 && (
                <rect
                  x={x + 1}
                  y={y}
                  width={barW - 2}
                  height={h}
                  fill={color}
                  opacity={0.8}
                  rx={2}
                />
              )}
              {/* 底部標籤：每 5 個或首尾顯示 */}
              {(data.length <= 12 || i === 0 || i === data.length - 1 || (i + 1) % 5 === 0) && (
                <text
                  x={x + barW / 2}
                  y={H - 4}
                  textAnchor="middle"
                  fontSize="9"
                  fill="var(--text-faint)"
                >
                  {d.label}
                </text>
              )}
            </g>
          );
        })}
      </svg>
    );
  };

  // 預設區塊順序：summary, chart, trend, compare, top5, transfer
  const order = blockOrder || ['summary', 'period', 'chart', 'compare', 'top5', 'transfer'];

  return (
    <div style={styles.page}>
      <div style={styles.pageHeader}>
        <h1 style={styles.pageTitle}>統計</h1>
        <EditOrderButton editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />
      </div>

      <EditModeBanner editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />

      <div style={styles.pageScroll}>
      {order.map((blockKey, idx) => {
        const blockProps = {
          onReorder: setPageOrder,
          blockKey,
          editMode,
          isFirst: idx === 0,
          isLast: idx === order.length - 1,
          onMoveUp: () => moveBlock && moveBlock(blockKey, -1),
          onMoveDown: () => moveBlock && moveBlock(blockKey, 1),
        };

        if (blockKey === 'period') {
          const navTitle = scope === 'day'
            ? (() => {
                const [y, m, d] = currentDate.split('-');
                const wd = ['日', '一', '二', '三', '四', '五', '六'][new Date(currentDate + 'T00:00:00').getDay()];
                return `${y}/${m}/${d} (${wd})`;
              })()
            : scope === 'month'
              ? `${currentMonth.slice(0, 4)}年 ${parseInt(currentMonth.slice(5, 7))}月`
              : `${currentMonth.slice(0, 4)}年`;
          const onNavPrev = () => {
            if (editMode) return;
            if (scope === 'day') shiftDay(-1);
            else if (scope === 'month') shiftMonth(-1);
            else shiftYear(-1);
          };
          const onNavNext = () => {
            if (editMode) return;
            if (scope === 'day') shiftDay(1);
            else if (scope === 'month') shiftMonth(1);
            else shiftYear(1);
          };
          return (
            <Block key="period" {...blockProps} title="時間範圍">
              <div style={styles.scopeToggle}>
                <button
                  style={{ ...styles.scopeBtn, ...(scope === 'day' ? styles.scopeBtnActive : {}) }}
                  onClick={() => !editMode && setScope('day')}
                >日</button>
                <button
                  style={{ ...styles.scopeBtn, ...(scope === 'month' ? styles.scopeBtnActive : {}) }}
                  onClick={() => !editMode && setScope('month')}
                >月</button>
                <button
                  style={{ ...styles.scopeBtn, ...(scope === 'year' ? styles.scopeBtnActive : {}) }}
                  onClick={() => !editMode && setScope('year')}
                >年</button>
              </div>

              <div style={styles.monthHeader}>
                <div style={styles.monthNav} onClick={onNavPrev}>‹</div>
                <div style={styles.monthTitle}>{navTitle}</div>
                <div style={styles.monthNav} onClick={onNavNext}>›</div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'summary') {
          return (
            <Block key="summary" {...blockProps} title="收支總覽">
              <div style={styles.summaryRow}>
                <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
                  <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>收入</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: 'var(--mint-text)' }}>{fmt(inc)}</div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
                  <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>支出</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>{fmt(exp)}</div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
                  <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>結餘</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: (inc - exp) < 0 ? "var(--pink)" : (inc - exp) > 0 ? "var(--mint)" : "var(--text)" }}>{fmtSigned(inc - exp)}</div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'chart') {
          // 顯示資料：若 drillCat 有值，顯示子類別；否則顯示大類
          const displayData = drillCat ? subcatData : mainData;
          const displayTotal = drillCat ? subcatTotal : mainTotal;
          const selectedData = selectedCat
            ? displayData.find(([c]) => c === selectedCat)
            : null;
          const centerLabel = drillCat
            ? drillCat
            : (selectedCat || (chartType === 'expense' ? '總支出' : '總收入'));
          const centerValue = selectedData ? selectedData[1] : displayTotal;

          return (
            <Block
              key="chart"
              {...blockProps}
              title={drillCat ? `${drillCat} · 子類佔比` : (chartType === 'expense' ? '支出分類佔比' : '收入分類佔比')}
              headerRight={drillCat ? (
                <span style={styles.linkMint} onClick={() => { setDrillCat(null); setSelectedCat(null); }}>
                  ← 返回
                </span>
              ) : null}
            >
              {/* 支出/收入切換（D）*/}
              {!drillCat && (
                <div style={styles.recentFilterBar}>
                  <span
                    style={{ ...styles.recentFilterChip, ...(chartType === 'expense' ? styles.recentFilterChipActive : {}) }}
                    onClick={() => { setChartType('expense'); setSelectedCat(null); }}
                  >支出</span>
                  <span
                    style={{ ...styles.recentFilterChip, ...(chartType === 'income' ? styles.recentFilterChipActive : {}) }}
                    onClick={() => { setChartType('income'); setSelectedCat(null); }}
                  >收入</span>
                </div>
              )}

              <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', padding: '12px 0 20px' }}>
                {renderDonut(displayData, displayTotal, {
                  highlighted: selectedCat,
                  centerLabel,
                  centerValue,
                  onSliceClick: (cat) => setSelectedCat(selectedCat === cat ? null : cat),
                })}
              </div>

              {displayData.length > 0 ? (
                <div style={styles.legendList}>
                  {displayData.map(([cat, val], i) => {
                    const color = CHART_COLORS[i % CHART_COLORS.length];
                    const pct = ((val / displayTotal) * 100).toFixed(1);
                    const isSel = selectedCat === cat;
                    return (
                      <div
                        key={cat}
                        style={{
                          ...styles.legendRow,
                          background: isSel ? 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.08)' : 'transparent',
                          opacity: selectedCat && !isSel ? 0.4 : 1,
                          cursor: 'pointer',
                          borderRadius: 8,
                          padding: '4px 8px',
                        }}
                        onClick={() => setSelectedCat(isSel ? null : cat)}
                        onDoubleClick={() => {
                          // 雙擊：大類模式下鑽；子類模式跳明細
                          if (!drillCat) { setDrillCat(cat); setSelectedCat(null); }
                          else if (onGoToTxn) onGoToTxn({ month: scope === 'month' ? currentMonth : null, category: drillCat, subCategory: cat, type: chartType });
                        }}
                      >
                        <div style={{ ...styles.legendDot, background: color }} />
                        <div style={styles.legendIcon}>
                          {drillCat ? catIcon(chartType, drillCat) : catIcon(chartType, cat)}
                        </div>
                        <span style={styles.legendName}>{cat}</span>
                        <span style={styles.legendPct}>{pct}%</span>
                        <span style={styles.legendAmt}>{fmt(val)}</span>
                      </div>
                    );
                  })}
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', textAlign: 'center', marginTop: 8 }}>
                    {drillCat ? '雙擊子類 → 進明細' : '雙擊分類 → 看子類'}
                  </div>
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div style={styles.empty}>沒有資料</div>
              )}
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'trend') {
          // 日模式不顯示趨勢圖（單日沒意義）
          if (scope === 'day') return null;
          return (
            <Block key="trend" {...blockProps} title={scope === 'month' ? '每日支出趨勢' : '每月支出趨勢'}>
              <div style={{ padding: '8px 4px 4px' }}>
                {renderTrendChart(trendData, trendMax, chartType)}
              </div>
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', padding: '0 6px' }}>
                <span>{scope === 'month' ? '日' : '月'}</span>
                <span>最高 {fmt(trendMax)}</span>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'compare') {
          const curVal = chartType === 'expense' ? exp : inc;
          const prevVal = chartType === 'expense' ? prevExp : prevInc;
          const diff = curVal - prevVal;
          const diffPct = chartType === 'expense' ? expDiffPct : incDiffPct;
          const prevLabel = scope === 'day' ? '昨日' : scope === 'month' ? '上月' : '去年';
          // 支出增加=壞(紅)、減少=好(綠)；收入反之
          const isGood = chartType === 'expense' ? diff < 0 : diff > 0;
          const diffColor = diff === 0 ? 'var(--text-faint)' : (isGood ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--pink)');
          return (
            <Block key="compare" {...blockProps} title={`${prevLabel}同期對比`}>
              <div style={styles.compareRow}>
                <div style={styles.compareBox}>
                  <div style={styles.compareLabel}>本期{chartType === 'expense' ? '支出' : '收入'}</div>
                  <div style={styles.compareVal}>{fmt(curVal)}</div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.compareBox}>
                  <div style={styles.compareLabel}>{prevLabel}</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.compareVal, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>{fmt(prevVal)}</div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.compareBox}>
                  <div style={styles.compareLabel}>變化</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.compareVal, color: diffColor }}>
                    {diff > 0 ? '+' : ''}{fmt(diff)}
                    {diffPct != null && (
                      <span style={{ fontSize: 11, marginLeft: 4 }}>
                        ({diff >= 0 ? '+' : ''}{diffPct.toFixed(1)}%)
                      </span>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
              {prevVal === 0 && (
                <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', textAlign: 'center', marginTop: 8 }}>
                  {prevLabel}沒有資料
                </div>
              )}
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'top5') {
          if (top5Exp.length === 0) return null;
          return (
            <Block key="top5" {...blockProps} title="單筆最大支出 Top 5">
              <div style={styles.txnList}>
                {top5Exp.map((t, i) => {
                  const acct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === t.accountId);
                  return (
                    <div key={t.id} style={styles.txn} onClick={() => onClickTxn && onClickTxn(t)}>
                      <div style={{ ...styles.txnIcon, background: 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.1)' }}>
                        <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>#{i + 1}</span>
                      </div>
                      <div style={styles.txnInfo}>
                        <div style={styles.txnCat}>
                          {t.subCategory ? `${t.category || '未分類'} › ${t.subCategory}` : (t.category || '未分類')}
                        </div>
                        <div style={styles.txnMeta}>
                          {t.date.replace(/-/g, '/')}{acct?.name ? ` · ${acct.name}` : ''}
                          {t.note ? ` · ${t.note}` : ''}
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      <div style={{ ...styles.txnAmt, color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>-{fmt(t.amount)}</div>
                    </div>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'transfer') {
          if (transferCount === 0) return null;
          return (
            <Block key="transfer" {...blockProps} title="轉帳動態">
              <div style={styles.compareRow}>
                <div style={styles.compareBox}>
                  <div style={styles.compareLabel}>轉帳筆數</div>
                  <div style={styles.compareVal}>{transferCount}</div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.compareBox}>
                  <div style={styles.compareLabel}>搬移金額</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.compareVal, color: 'var(--accent-text)' }}>{fmt(transferTotal)}</div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.compareBox}>
                  <div style={styles.compareLabel}>手續費合計</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.compareVal, color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>{fmt(feeTotal)}</div>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', textAlign: 'center', marginTop: 8 }}>
                轉帳不計入支出/收入統計
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        return null;
      })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 設定頁 ============
function SettingsPage({
  state, setState, toast, toastRich, onReset, onCleanupHistory,
  lastBackupAt, setLastBackupAt,
  backupReminderDays, setBackupReminderDays,
  driveFolderUrl, setDriveFolderUrl,
  setConfirmDialog,
  editMode, setEditMode, onSubSheetChange,
  noteColor, setNoteColor,
  theme, setTheme,
  blockOrder, moveBlock, setPageOrder,
}) {
  const [showThirdParty, setShowThirdParty] = useState(false);
  const [showDriveSetup, setShowDriveSetup] = useState(false);
  const [showCleanupSheet, setShowCleanupSheet] = useState(false);
  const [showFilterDeleteSheet, setShowFilterDeleteSheet] = useState(false);
  const [showReminderSetup, setShowReminderSetup] = useState(false);
  const [dangerLocked, setDangerLocked] = useState(true); // 危險區預設鎖定
  const [driveInput, setDriveInput] = useState(driveFolderUrl);
  const [expandedStat, setExpandedStat] = useState(null); // 資料統計哪一列展開 ('txn' | 'account' | 'cat' | 'sub' | null)

  // 追蹤任何子 sheet 是否打開,通知父層用以隱藏 bottom nav
  const anySubSheetOpen = showThirdParty || showCleanupSheet || showFilterDeleteSheet;
  useEffect(() => {
    if (onSubSheetChange) onSubSheetChange(anySubSheetOpen);
  }, [anySubSheetOpen, onSubSheetChange]);
  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      if (onSubSheetChange) onSubSheetChange(false);
    };
  }, [onSubSheetChange]);

  // 快照（localStorage 內存最多 10 個）
  const SNAPSHOT_KEY = 'ledger_snapshots_v1';
  const SNAPSHOT_MAX = 10;
  const [snapshots, setSnapshots] = useState(() => {
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem(SNAPSHOT_KEY);
      return raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : [];
    } catch { return []; }
  });
  const [showSnapshots, setShowSnapshots] = useState(false);
  const [snapshotsLocked, setSnapshotsLocked] = useState(true); // 快照管理預設鎖定,防誤觸還原/刪除
  const [renamingSnapId, setRenamingSnapId] = useState(null); // 正在編輯名稱的快照 id
  const [renameInput, setRenameInput] = useState('');
  const [snapshotNameInput, setSnapshotNameInput] = useState('');
  const [showSnapshotNameDialog, setShowSnapshotNameDialog] = useState(false);
  // 新快照要儲存的類別（勾選）
  const [snapshotScopes, setSnapshotScopes] = useState({
    transactions: true,
    accounts: true,
    categories: true,
    accountTypes: true,
  });

  // 各彈跳視窗的左右滑返回
  const driveSetupSwipe = useSwipeToClose(() => setShowDriveSetup(false));
  const reminderSetupSwipe = useSwipeToClose(() => setShowReminderSetup(false));
  const snapshotNameSwipe = useSwipeToClose(() => setShowSnapshotNameDialog(false));
  const snapshotsSwipe = useSwipeToClose(() => setShowSnapshots(false));

  const persistSnapshots = (list) => {
    setSnapshots(list);
    try { localStorage.setItem(SNAPSHOT_KEY, JSON.stringify(list)); } catch (e) {
      toast('儲存失敗（空間不足？）');
    }
  };

  const createSnapshot = (customName) => {
    // 至少要勾一項
    const scopes = snapshotScopes;
    const anyChecked = scopes.transactions || scopes.accounts || scopes.categories || scopes.accountTypes;
    if (!anyChecked) {
      toast('至少要選一個類別');
      return;
    }
    // 已達上限:禁止儲存,提示先刪除舊的
    if (snapshots.length >= SNAPSHOT_MAX) {
      setConfirmDialog({
        title: '快照已達上限',
        bigNumber: { value: `${SNAPSHOT_MAX} / ${SNAPSHOT_MAX}`, label: '個快照' },
        message: '請先從「管理快照」刪除不需要的舊快照,\n再嘗試儲存新快照。',
        confirmText: '我知道了',
        singleAction: true,
        onConfirm: () => {},
      });
      return;
    }
    const now = new Date();
    const defaultName = `${now.getFullYear()}/${String(now.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}/${String(now.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')} ${String(now.getHours()).padStart(2, '0')}:${String(now.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')} 手動快照`;
    const data = {};
    if (scopes.transactions) {
      data.transactions = state.transactions;
      // holdings/trades 跟 transactions 強耦合,一起存避免資料錯亂
      data.holdings = state.holdings;
      data.trades = state.trades;
    }
    if (scopes.accounts) data.accounts = state.accounts;
    if (scopes.categories) data.categories = state.categories;
    if (scopes.accountTypes) data.accountTypes = state.accountTypes;
    const snap = {
      id: 'snap_' + Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 6),
      name: (customName && customName.trim()) || defaultName,
      createdAt: now.getTime(),
      data,
      scopes: { ...scopes },
      summary: {
        txnCount: scopes.transactions ? state.transactions.length : null,
        holdingCount: scopes.transactions ? state.holdings.length : null,
        tradeCount: scopes.transactions ? state.trades.length : null,
        acctCount: scopes.accounts ? state.accounts.length : null,
        catCount: scopes.categories ? ((state.categories.expense?.length || 0) + (state.categories.income?.length || 0)) : null,
        acctTypeCount: scopes.accountTypes ? state.accountTypes.length : null,
      },
    };
    // 新的在前，超過上限砍最舊的
    const next = [snap, ...snapshots].slice(0, SNAPSHOT_MAX);
    persistSnapshots(next);
    // 成功提示:用 toastRich 強化視覺
    if (toastRich) {
      toastRich({
        title: '已儲存快照',
        amount: '✓',
        amountColor: 'var(--mint-text)',
        lines: [
          `「${snap.name}」`,
          `${next.length} / ${SNAPSHOT_MAX} 個快照`,
        ],
      }, 2400);
    } else {
      toast(`已儲存快照：${snap.name}`);
    }
  };

  const restoreSnapshot = (snap) => {
    const scopes = snap.scopes || { transactions: true, accounts: true, categories: true, accountTypes: true };
    // 用 changes 格式呈現「現有 → 快照」的差異
    const changes = [];
    if (scopes.transactions && snap.data.transactions) {
      const cur = state.transactions.length;
      const next = snap.data.transactions.length;
      // 持股變化:舊快照沒有 holdings/trades 欄位 → 視為 0(該時間點還沒這功能,還原會清空)
      const curH = state.holdings.length;
      const nextH = Array.isArray(snap.data.holdings) ? snap.data.holdings.length : 0;
      const curT = state.trades.length;
      const nextT = Array.isArray(snap.data.trades) ? snap.data.trades.length : 0;
      const txnChanged = cur !== next;
      const stockChanged = curH !== nextH || curT !== nextT;
      changes.push({
        icon: 'list',
        label: '交易紀錄',
        from: `現有 ${cur} 筆${(curH > 0 || curT > 0) ? ` (持股 ${curH})` : ''}`,
        to: `快照 ${next} 筆${(nextH > 0 || nextT > 0) ? ` (持股 ${nextH})` : (curH > 0 || curT > 0) ? ' (持股 0)' : ''}`,
        changed: txnChanged || stockChanged,
      });
    }
    if (scopes.accounts && snap.data.accounts) {
      const cur = state.accounts.length;
      const next = snap.data.accounts.length;
      changes.push({
        icon: 'bank',
        label: '帳戶',
        from: `現有 ${cur} 個`,
        to: `快照 ${next} 個`,
        changed: cur !== next,
      });
    }
    if (scopes.categories && snap.data.categories) {
      const curCount = (state.categories.expense?.length || 0) + (state.categories.income?.length || 0);
      const nextCount = (snap.data.categories.expense?.length || 0) + (snap.data.categories.income?.length || 0);
      changes.push({
        icon: 'note',
        label: '分類設定',
        from: `現有 ${curCount} 項`,
        to: `快照 ${nextCount} 項`,
        changed: curCount !== nextCount,
      });
    }
    if (scopes.accountTypes && snap.data.accountTypes) {
      const cur = state.accountTypes.length;
      const next = snap.data.accountTypes.length;
      changes.push({
        icon: 'briefcase',
        label: '帳戶類型',
        from: `現有 ${cur} 種`,
        to: `快照 ${next} 種`,
        changed: cur !== next,
      });
    }
    setConfirmDialog({
      title: '還原快照',
      target: { label: '快照', name: snap.name },
      changes,
      changesHint: '現有資料將被快照取代,箭頭右側(快照版本)會生效。',
      confirmText: '確認還原',
      danger: true,
      onConfirm: () => {
        setState((s) => {
          const next = { ...s };
          if (scopes.transactions && snap.data.transactions) {
            next.transactions = snap.data.transactions;
            // holdings/trades 跟 transactions 強耦合:有就還原,沒有(舊快照)就清空
            // 「快照即當時時間點」原則:舊快照當時可能還沒這個功能,還原後就該是空的
            next.holdings = Array.isArray(snap.data.holdings) ? snap.data.holdings : [];
            next.trades = Array.isArray(snap.data.trades) ? snap.data.trades : [];
          }
          if (scopes.accounts && snap.data.accounts) next.accounts = snap.data.accounts;
          if (scopes.categories && snap.data.categories) next.categories = snap.data.categories;
          if (scopes.accountTypes && snap.data.accountTypes) next.accountTypes = snap.data.accountTypes;
          return next;
        });
        // 成功提示:用 toastRich 強化視覺
        const snapDate = new Date(snap.createdAt);
        const dateStr = `${snapDate.getFullYear()}/${String(snapDate.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}/${String(snapDate.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')} ${String(snapDate.getHours()).padStart(2, '0')}:${String(snapDate.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0')}`;
        const changedLabels = changes.filter(c => c.changed).map(c => c.label);
        if (toastRich) {
          toastRich({
            title: '已還原快照',
            amount: '✓',
            amountColor: 'var(--mint-text)',
            lines: [
              `「${snap.name}」`,
              `快照時間 · ${dateStr}`,
              changedLabels.length > 0 ? `已更新:${changedLabels.join('、')}` : '資料已同步',
            ],
          }, 2600);
        } else {
          toast(`已還原快照：${snap.name}`);
        }
        setShowSnapshots(false);
      },
    });
  };

  const startRenameSnapshot = (snap) => {
    setRenamingSnapId(snap.id);
    setRenameInput(snap.name);
  };

  const cancelRenameSnapshot = () => {
    setRenamingSnapId(null);
    setRenameInput('');
  };

  const saveRenameSnapshot = () => {
    const newName = renameInput.trim();
    if (!newName) {
      toast('名稱不能為空');
      return;
    }
    const target = snapshots.find((s) => s.id === renamingSnapId);
    if (!target || target.name === newName) {
      cancelRenameSnapshot();
      return;
    }
    const nextList = snapshots.map((s) =>
      s.id === renamingSnapId ? { ...s, name: newName } : s
    );
    persistSnapshots(nextList);
    cancelRenameSnapshot();
    if (toastRich) {
      toastRich({
        title: '已更新名稱',
        amount: '✓',
        amountColor: 'var(--mint-text)',
        lines: [`「${newName}」`],
      }, 1600);
    } else {
      toast('已更新名稱');
    }
  };

  const deleteSnapshot = (snap) => {
    setConfirmDialog({
      title: '刪除快照',
      target: { label: '快照', name: snap.name },
      message: '確定要刪除這個快照?',
      warning: '此操作無法復原',
      confirmText: '刪除',
      danger: true,
      onConfirm: () => {
        const nextList = snapshots.filter((s) => s.id !== snap.id);
        persistSnapshots(nextList);
        if (toastRich) {
          toastRich({
            title: '已刪除快照',
            amount: '✓',
            amountColor: 'var(--pink-text)',
            lines: [
              `「${snap.name}」`,
              `剩餘 ${nextList.length} 個快照`,
            ],
          }, 1180);
        } else {
          toast('已刪除快照');
        }
      },
    });
  };

  const updateLastBackup = () => {
    const now = Date.now();
    setLastBackupAt(now);
    try { localStorage.setItem('ledger_last_backup', String(now)); } catch {}
  };

  // 一鍵套用個人帳戶範本
  const applyAccountTemplate = () => {
    setConfirmDialog({
      title: '載入個人帳戶範本',
      message: `將新增 ${PERSONAL_ACCOUNT_TEMPLATE.length} 個帳戶到目前的帳戶列表\n\n（不會刪除現有帳戶，只是加上去）\n確定載入嗎？`,
      confirmText: '載入',
      danger: false,
      onConfirm: () => {
        const newAccounts = PERSONAL_ACCOUNT_TEMPLATE.map((a) => ({
          id: 'a_' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2, 10),
          name: a.name,
          type: a.type,
          initAmount: a.initAmount,
        }));
        setState((s) => ({ ...s, accounts: [...s.accounts, ...newAccounts] }));
        toast(`已載入 ${newAccounts.length} 個帳戶`);
      },
    });
  };

  // 同步預設分類（把 DEFAULT_CATEGORIES 裡有、但目前資料沒有的分類/子分類補進來，不動已有的）
  const syncDefaultCategories = () => {
    // 先算出會補幾個（大分類 + 子分類），讓使用者知道差多少
    let addCats = 0;
    let addSubs = 0;
    ['expense', 'income'].forEach((type) => {
      const defs = DEFAULT_CATEGORIES[type] || [];
      const cur = state.categories[type] || [];
      defs.forEach((defCat) => {
        const curCat = cur.find((c) => c.label === defCat.label);
        if (!curCat) {
          addCats++;
          addSubs += (defCat.subs || []).length;
        } else {
          (defCat.subs || []).forEach((s) => {
            if (!(curCat.subs || []).includes(s)) addSubs++;
          });
        }
      });
    });

    if (addCats === 0 && addSubs === 0) {
      toast('分類已是最新，沒有需要補的項目');
      return;
    }

    setConfirmDialog({
      title: '同步預設分類',
      message: `會補上缺少的 ${addCats} 個大分類、${addSubs} 個子分類\n\n已有的分類／子分類不會被刪除或變動，只是把預設裡有、你這邊沒有的補進來\n\n確定同步嗎？`,
      confirmText: '同步',
      danger: false,
      onConfirm: () => {
        setState((s) => {
          const nextCats = { expense: [], income: [] };
          ['expense', 'income'].forEach((type) => {
            const defs = DEFAULT_CATEGORIES[type] || [];
            const cur = s.categories[type] || [];
            // 先保留所有現有的（順序不動），同時補足各自缺少的子分類
            const merged = cur.map((curCat) => {
              const defCat = defs.find((d) => d.label === curCat.label);
              if (!defCat) return curCat;
              const existSubs = curCat.subs || [];
              const missingSubs = (defCat.subs || []).filter((s) => !existSubs.includes(s));
              return missingSubs.length ? { ...curCat, subs: [...existSubs, ...missingSubs] } : curCat;
            });
            // 再加上現有資料裡沒有的大分類（加在最後）
            defs.forEach((defCat) => {
              if (!merged.find((c) => c.label === defCat.label)) {
                merged.push(JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(defCat)));
              }
            });
            nextCats[type] = merged;
          });
          return { ...s, categories: nextCats };
        });
        toast(`已補上 ${addCats} 個大分類、${addSubs} 個子分類`);
      },
    });
  };

  // 要納入匯出/匯入的偏好設定 localStorage 鍵
  // 設計原則:會影響「使用者熟悉的 app 樣貌」的偏好都包含;裝置/過渡狀態不包含
  const EXPORTABLE_PREF_KEYS = [
    'ledger_theme_v1',
    'ledger_note_color_v1',
    'ledger_note_pref_v1',
    'ledger_block_order_v12',
    'ledger_account_order',
    'ledger_period_order',
    'ledger_day_order',
    'ledger_thirdparty_order',
    'ledger_dp_selected',
    'ledger_dp_weekend',
    'ledger_list_sort_v1',
    'ledger_recent_filter',
    'ledger_fee_cat',
    'ledger_fee_sub',
  ];
  const collectPreferences = () => {
    const prefs = {};
    EXPORTABLE_PREF_KEYS.forEach((k) => {
      try {
        const v = localStorage.getItem(k);
        if (v !== null) prefs[k] = v;
      } catch {}
    });
    return prefs;
  };
  const restorePreferences = (prefs) => {
    if (!prefs || typeof prefs !== 'object') return;
    EXPORTABLE_PREF_KEYS.forEach((k) => {
      if (prefs[k] !== undefined && prefs[k] !== null) {
        try { localStorage.setItem(k, prefs[k]); } catch {}
      }
    });
  };

  const buildExportPayload = () => JSON.stringify({
    transactions: state.transactions,
    accounts: state.accounts,
    categories: state.categories,
    accountTypes: state.accountTypes,
    holdings: state.holdings,
    trades: state.trades,
    preferences: collectPreferences(),
    exportedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    exportVersion: 3,
  }, null, 2);

  const doExport = () => {
    const data = buildExportPayload();
    try {
      const blob = new Blob([data], { type: 'application/json' });
      const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
      const a = document.createElement('a');
      a.href = url;
      a.download = `記帳備份_${todayStr()}.json`;
      document.body.appendChild(a);
      a.click();
      document.body.removeChild(a);
      URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
      updateLastBackup();
      toast('已匯出 JSON，請至「下載」資料夾查看');
    } catch {
      toast('匯出失敗');
    }
  };

  // 顯示 JSON 文字讓使用者手動複製(沙盒環境救援用,clipboard API 也可能被擋)
  const [exportTextDialog, setExportTextDialog] = useState(null);
  const doCopyJSON = () => {
    const data = buildExportPayload();
    setExportTextDialog(data);
  };

  const doExportCSV = () => {
    const rows = [['日期', '類型', '大分類', '子分類', '金額', '帳戶', '備註']];
    state.transactions.forEach((t) => {
      const acct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === t.accountId)?.name || '';
      rows.push([
        t.date,
        t.type === 'income' ? '收入' : '支出',
        t.category || '',
        t.subCategory || '',
        t.amount,
        acct,
        t.note || '',
      ]);
    });
    const csv = '\uFEFF' + rows.map((r) => r.map((c) => `"${String(c).replace(/"/g, '""')}"`).join(',')).join('\n');
    try {
      const blob = new Blob([csv], { type: 'text/csv;charset=utf-8' });
      const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
      const a = document.createElement('a');
      a.href = url;
      a.download = `記帳_${todayStr()}.csv`;
      document.body.appendChild(a);
      a.click();
      document.body.removeChild(a);
      URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
      toast('已匯出 CSV，請至「下載」資料夾查看');
    } catch {
      toast('匯出失敗');
    }
  };

  // 匯入 JSON
  const fileInputRef = React.useRef(null);
  const doImport = () => {
    fileInputRef.current?.click();
  };
  // 共用匯入邏輯,讓檔案匯入和文字匯入都能用
  const applyImportFromText = (text) => {
    try {
      const data = JSON.parse(text);
      if (!data.transactions || !Array.isArray(data.transactions)) {
        toast('檔案格式錯誤');
        return false;
      }
      const hasPrefs = data.preferences && typeof data.preferences === 'object' && Object.keys(data.preferences).length > 0;
      const holdingCount = Array.isArray(data.holdings) ? data.holdings.length : 0;
      const baseMsg = `檔案含 ${data.transactions.length} 筆紀錄${holdingCount > 0 ? ` (持股 ${holdingCount} 檔)` : ''}、${(data.accounts || []).length} 個帳戶`;
      const prefMsg = hasPrefs ? '\n\n會一併還原偏好設定(主題、排序、預設手續費分類等)' : '';
      setConfirmDialog({
        title: '匯入備份',
        message: `${baseMsg}${prefMsg}\n\n匯入後會「覆蓋」目前的資料,無法還原\n確定繼續嗎?`,
        confirmText: '匯入',
        danger: true,
        onConfirm: () => {
          // 用函式型 setState 確保不會被 React batch 吃掉
          // 並把所有 6 個欄位完整覆蓋(holdings/trades 沒有就清空,「備份即當時時間點」)
          setState(() => ({
            transactions: Array.isArray(data.transactions) ? data.transactions : [],
            accounts: Array.isArray(data.accounts) ? data.accounts : [],
            categories: data.categories || JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(DEFAULT_CATEGORIES)),
            accountTypes: Array.isArray(data.accountTypes) && data.accountTypes.length ? data.accountTypes : [...DEFAULT_ACCOUNT_TYPES],
            holdings: Array.isArray(data.holdings) ? data.holdings : [],
            trades: Array.isArray(data.trades) ? data.trades : [],
          }));
          if (hasPrefs) {
            restorePreferences(data.preferences);
          }
          toast('已匯入備份');
          setShowPasteImport(false);
          setPasteImportText('');
        },
      });
      return true;
    } catch {
      toast('檔案讀取失敗');
      return false;
    }
  };
  const handleFileImport = (e) => {
    const file = e.target.files?.[0];
    if (!file) return;
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = (ev) => {
      applyImportFromText(ev.target.result);
    };
    reader.readAsText(file);
    e.target.value = ''; // 清空以便下次選同檔案可再觸發
  };

  // 貼上 JSON 文字匯入
  const [showPasteImport, setShowPasteImport] = useState(false);
  const [pasteImportText, setPasteImportText] = useState('');

  // 開啟 Drive 資料夾
  const openDriveFolder = () => {
    if (!driveFolderUrl) {
      setShowDriveSetup(true);
      return;
    }
    try {
      window.open(driveFolderUrl, '_blank');
    } catch {
      toast('無法開啟，請確認網址');
    }
  };

  const saveDriveUrl = () => {
    const url = driveInput.trim();
    if (url && !/^https?:\/\//.test(url)) {
      toast('請輸入完整網址（含 https://）');
      return;
    }
    setDriveFolderUrl(url);
    try { localStorage.setItem('ledger_drive_folder', url); } catch {}
    setShowDriveSetup(false);
    toast(url ? '已儲存資料夾連結' : '已清除資料夾連結');
  };

  // 備份提醒邏輯
  const daysSinceBackup = lastBackupAt
    ? Math.floor((Date.now() - lastBackupAt) / 86400000)
    : null;
  const needsBackup = daysSinceBackup === null || daysSinceBackup >= backupReminderDays;
  const lastBackupText = lastBackupAt
    ? new Date(lastBackupAt).toLocaleDateString('zh-TW', { year: 'numeric', month: '2-digit', day: '2-digit' })
    : '從未備份';

  const updateReminderDays = (days) => {
    setBackupReminderDays(days);
    try { localStorage.setItem('ledger_backup_reminder_days', String(days)); } catch {}
    setShowReminderSetup(false);
    toast(`已設定每 ${days} 天提醒備份`);
  };

  return (
    <div style={styles.page}>
      <div style={styles.pageHeader}>
        <h1 style={styles.pageTitle}>設定</h1>
        <EditOrderButton editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />
      </div>

      <EditModeBanner editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />

      <div style={styles.pageScroll}>
      {/* 備份提醒卡（需要備份時顯示） */}
      {needsBackup && state.transactions.length > 0 && (
        <div style={styles.backupReminder} onClick={doExport}>
          <div style={{ width: 28, height: 28, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center' }}>
            <TypeIcon name="warning" size={22} color="#f5a04a" />
          </div>
          <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600, color: '#f5a04a', marginBottom: 2 }}>
              {daysSinceBackup === null ? '建議進行首次備份' : `已 ${daysSinceBackup} 天未備份`}
            </div>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>
              點此立即匯出 JSON 備份
            </div>
          </div>
          <div style={styles.settingsArrow}>›</div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 7 塊可排序設定區 */}
      {(blockOrder || ['backup-local', 'backup-ext', 'drive', 'reminder', 'account', 'dataStat', 'cleanup', 'danger']).map((blockKey, idx) => {
        const order = blockOrder || ['backup-local', 'backup-ext', 'drive', 'reminder', 'account', 'dataStat', 'cleanup', 'danger'];
        const blockProps = {
          onReorder: setPageOrder,
          blockKey,
          editMode,
          isFirst: idx === 0,
          isLast: idx === order.length - 1,
          onMoveUp: () => moveBlock && moveBlock(blockKey, -1),
          onMoveDown: () => moveBlock && moveBlock(blockKey, 1),
        };

        if (blockKey === 'backup-local') {
          return (
            <Block key="backup-local" {...blockProps} title="本地備份">
              {/* 儲存快照 */}
              <div style={styles.settingsItem} onClick={() => {
                if (editMode) return;
                if (snapshots.length >= SNAPSHOT_MAX) {
                  setConfirmDialog({
                    title: '快照已達上限',
                    bigNumber: { value: `${SNAPSHOT_MAX} / ${SNAPSHOT_MAX}`, label: '個快照' },
                    message: '請先從「管理快照」刪除不需要的舊快照,\n再嘗試儲存新快照。',
                    confirmText: '我知道了',
                    singleAction: true,
                    onConfirm: () => {},
                  });
                  return;
                }
                setSnapshotNameInput('');
                setSnapshotScopes({ transactions: true, accounts: true, categories: true, accountTypes: true });
                setShowSnapshotNameDialog(true);
              }}>
                <div style={styles.settingsIcon}><TypeIcon name="box" size={20} color="var(--mint-text)" /></div>
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={styles.settingsLabel}>儲存快照</div>
                  <div style={{
                    fontSize: 11,
                    color: snapshots.length >= SNAPSHOT_MAX ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--text-faint)',
                    fontWeight: snapshots.length >= SNAPSHOT_MAX ? 600 : 400,
                    marginTop: 2,
                  }}>
                    {snapshots.length >= SNAPSHOT_MAX
                      ? `已達上限(${snapshots.length} / ${SNAPSHOT_MAX})`
                      : `在 App 內保存目前狀態`}
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.settingsArrow}>›</div>
              </div>
              {/* 管理快照 */}
              <div style={styles.settingsItem} onClick={() => { if (!editMode) { setSnapshotsLocked(true); setRenamingSnapId(null); setShowSnapshots(true); } }}>
                <div style={styles.settingsIcon}><TypeIcon name="clock" size={20} color="var(--accent-text)" /></div>
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={styles.settingsLabel}>管理快照</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 2 }}>
                    {snapshots.length > 0 ? `編輯在 App 的快照檔案` : '尚未建立任何快照'}
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8 }}>
                  <span style={{
                    fontSize: 10,
                    color: snapshots.length >= SNAPSHOT_MAX * 0.9 ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--text-faint)',
                    fontWeight: snapshots.length >= SNAPSHOT_MAX * 0.9 ? 600 : 400,
                    fontVariantNumeric: 'tabular-nums',
                    lineHeight: 1,
                  }}>
                    {snapshots.length} / {SNAPSHOT_MAX}
                  </span>
                  <span style={{ ...styles.settingsArrow, lineHeight: 1 }}>›</span>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'backup-ext') {
          return (
            <Block key="backup-ext" {...blockProps} title="外存備份">
              {/* 匯出備份檔 */}
              <div style={styles.settingsItem} onClick={() => !editMode && doExport()}>
                <div style={styles.settingsIcon}><TypeIcon name="download" size={20} color="var(--accent-text)" /></div>
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={styles.settingsLabel}>匯出備份檔</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 2 }}>
                    直接存 JSON檔 到手機「 下載／download 」資料夾
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.settingsArrow}>›</div>
              </div>

              {/* 匯入備份檔 */}
              <div style={styles.settingsItem} onClick={() => !editMode && doImport()}>
                <div style={styles.settingsIcon}><TypeIcon name="folder" size={20} color="#a8c8f5" /></div>
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={styles.settingsLabel}>匯入備份檔</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 2 }}>
                    用 JSON檔 還原資料 ( 會覆蓋現有 )
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.settingsArrow}>›</div>
              </div>

              {/* 複製 JSON 代碼 */}
              <div style={styles.settingsItem} onClick={() => !editMode && doCopyJSON()}>
                <div style={styles.settingsIcon}><TypeIcon name="clipboard" size={20} color="var(--mint-text)" /></div>
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={styles.settingsLabel}>複製 JSON 代碼</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 2 }}>
                    拷貝文字代碼資料
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.settingsArrow}>›</div>
              </div>

              {/* 貼上 JSON 代碼 */}
              <div style={styles.settingsItem} onClick={() => !editMode && setShowPasteImport(true)}>
                <div style={styles.settingsIcon}><TypeIcon name="edit" size={20} color="#a8c8f5" /></div>
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={styles.settingsLabel}>貼上 JSON 代碼</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 2 }}>
                    還原文字代碼資料 ( 會覆蓋現有 )
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.settingsArrow}>›</div>
              </div>
              <input ref={fileInputRef} type="file" accept=".json,application/json" style={{ display: 'none' }} onChange={handleFileImport} />
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'drive') {
          return null;
        }

        if (blockKey === 'reminder') {
          return null;
        }

        if (blockKey === 'account') {
          return (
            <Block key="account" {...blockProps} title="帳號連結">
              <div style={styles.settingsItem} onClick={() => !editMode && setShowThirdParty(true)}>
                <div style={styles.settingsIcon}><TypeIcon name="link" size={20} color="#a8c8f5" /></div>
                <div style={styles.settingsLabel}>串連第三方連結</div>
                <div style={styles.settingsArrow}>›</div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'dataStat') {
          const catCount = (state.categories.expense?.length || 0) + (state.categories.income?.length || 0);
          const subCount =
            (state.categories.expense || []).reduce((sum, c) => sum + (c.subs?.length || 0), 0) +
            (state.categories.income || []).reduce((sum, c) => sum + (c.subs?.length || 0), 0);

          // 各 row 的細項計算
          const txnByType = {
            income: state.transactions.filter((t) => t.type === 'income' && !t.transferRole).length,
            expense: state.transactions.filter((t) => t.type === 'expense' && !t.transferRole).length,
            transfer: state.transactions.filter((t) => t.transferRole === 'out').length, // 一對轉出/轉入算一筆
          };

          const acctByType = (state.accountTypes || []).map((at) => ({
            label: at.label,
            color: at.color,
            count: state.accounts.filter((a) => a.type === at.value).length,
          })).filter((x) => x.count > 0);

          const statRows = [
            {
              key: 'txn',
              icon: 'clipboard', color: 'var(--text-dim)',
              label: '總紀錄筆數',
              value: state.transactions.length,
              details: [
                { label: '支出', color: 'var(--pink-text)', count: txnByType.expense },
                { label: '收入', color: 'var(--mint-text)', count: txnByType.income },
                { label: '轉帳', color: 'var(--accent-text)', count: txnByType.transfer },
              ],
            },
            {
              key: 'account',
              icon: 'bank', color: '#a8c8f5',
              label: '帳戶數',
              value: state.accounts.length,
              details: acctByType.map((x) => ({ label: x.label, color: x.color, count: x.count })),
            },
            {
              key: 'cat',
              icon: 'bag', color: 'var(--mint-text)',
              label: '大分類',
              value: catCount,
              details: [
                { label: '支出', color: 'var(--pink-text)', count: state.categories.expense?.length || 0 },
                { label: '收入', color: 'var(--mint-text)', count: state.categories.income?.length || 0 },
              ],
            },
            {
              key: 'sub',
              icon: 'list', color: 'var(--accent-text)',
              label: '子分類',
              value: subCount,
              details: [
                { label: '支出', color: 'var(--pink-text)', count: (state.categories.expense || []).reduce((s, c) => s + (c.subs?.length || 0), 0) },
                { label: '收入', color: 'var(--mint-text)', count: (state.categories.income || []).reduce((s, c) => s + (c.subs?.length || 0), 0) },
              ],
            },
          ];

          return (
            <Block key="dataStat" {...blockProps} title="資料統計">
              {statRows.map((row) => {
                const isExpanded = expandedStat === row.key;
                const canExpand = row.details && row.details.length > 0 && row.value > 0;
                return (
                  <React.Fragment key={row.key}>
                    <div
                      style={{
                        ...styles.statItem,
                        cursor: canExpand ? 'pointer' : 'default',
                        ...(isExpanded ? { marginBottom: 0, borderBottomLeftRadius: 0, borderBottomRightRadius: 0 } : {}),
                      }}
                      onClick={() => canExpand && setExpandedStat(isExpanded ? null : row.key)}
                    >
                      <div style={styles.statIcon}><TypeIcon name={row.icon} size={16} color={row.color} /></div>
                      <div style={styles.statLabel}>{row.label}</div>
                      <div style={styles.statValue}>{row.value} 筆</div>
                      {canExpand && (
                        <div style={{
                          marginLeft: 6,
                          fontSize: 10,
                          color: 'var(--text-faint)',
                          transition: 'transform 0.15s',
                          transform: isExpanded ? 'rotate(-90deg)' : 'rotate(0deg)',
                        }}>◀</div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                    {isExpanded && (
                      <div style={{
                        background: 'var(--bg-card)',
                        borderBottomLeftRadius: 10,
                        borderBottomRightRadius: 10,
                        marginTop: -4,
                        marginBottom: 4,
                        padding: '4px 14px 8px',
                        borderTop: '1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.04)',
                      }}>
                        {row.details.map((d, di) => (
                          <div key={di} style={{
                            display: 'flex',
                            alignItems: 'center',
                            padding: '5px 0 5px 26px',
                            fontSize: 11,
                          }}>
                            {d.color && (
                              <span style={{
                                width: 6, height: 6, borderRadius: 3,
                                background: d.color, marginRight: 8, flexShrink: 0,
                              }} />
                            )}
                            <span style={{ flex: 1, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>{d.label}</span>
                            <span style={{
                              color: 'var(--text)',
                              fontFamily: "'Space Grotesk', sans-serif",
                              fontVariantNumeric: 'tabular-nums',
                            }}>{d.count} 筆</span>
                          </div>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </React.Fragment>
                );
              })}
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'appearance') {
          return (
            <Block key="appearance" {...blockProps} title="外觀">
              <div style={{ padding: '4px 4px 8px' }}>
                {/* 主題切換 */}
                <div style={{
                  display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between',
                }}>
                  <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 2 }}>
                    <div style={{ fontSize: 14, color: 'var(--text)', fontWeight: 500 }}>主題</div>
                    <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>
                      切換深色或淺色風格
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div style={{
                    display: 'flex',
                    background: 'var(--bg-card)',
                    border: '1px solid var(--border)',
                    borderRadius: 10,
                    padding: 3,
                    gap: 2,
                  }}>
                    {[
                      { val: 'dark', label: '深色' },
                      { val: 'light', label: '淺色' },
                    ].map((opt) => {
                      const active = theme === opt.val;
                      return (
                        <button
                          key={opt.val}
                          onClick={() => !editMode && setTheme(opt.val)}
                          style={{
                            padding: '6px 14px',
                            border: 'none',
                            borderRadius: 7,
                            background: active ? 'var(--mint)' : 'transparent',
                            color: active ? '#1a1a1a' : 'var(--text-dim)',
                            fontSize: 12,
                            fontWeight: active ? 700 : 500,
                            cursor: 'pointer',
                            transition: 'all 0.15s',
                          }}
                        >
                          {opt.label}
                        </button>
                      );
                    })}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'cleanup') {
          return (
            <Block key="cleanup" {...blockProps} title="清理歷史紀錄">
              <div
                style={{ ...styles.settingsItem, cursor: 'pointer', alignItems: 'flex-start', padding: '12px 14px' }}
                onClick={() => !editMode && setShowCleanupSheet(true)}
              >
                <div style={styles.settingsIcon}>
                  <TypeIcon name="calendar" size={20} color="var(--mint-text)" />
                </div>
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={styles.settingsLabel}>依日期清除舊紀錄</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 2, lineHeight: 1.5 }}>
                    移除某個日期之前的交易,降低資料量
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.settingsArrow}>›</div>
              </div>
              <div
                style={{ ...styles.settingsItem, cursor: 'pointer', alignItems: 'flex-start', padding: '12px 14px' }}
                onClick={() => !editMode && setShowFilterDeleteSheet(true)}
              >
                <div style={styles.settingsIcon}>
                  <TypeIcon name="search" size={20} color="var(--accent-text)" />
                </div>
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={styles.settingsLabel}>條件篩選刪除</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 2, lineHeight: 1.5 }}>
                    依帳戶、分類、備註等條件精確刪除紀錄
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.settingsArrow}>›</div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'danger') {
          return (
            <Block
              key="danger"
              {...blockProps}
              title="危險區"
              headerRight={
                <div style={styles.lockRow}>
                  <span style={{ ...styles.lockLabel, color: dangerLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--pink)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 4 }}>
                    <TypeIcon name={dangerLocked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'} size={12} color={dangerLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--pink)'} />
                    {dangerLocked ? '鎖定中' : '已解鎖'}
                  </span>
                  <div
                    style={{ ...styles.toggleTrack, background: dangerLocked ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--pink)' }}
                    onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); if (!editMode) setDangerLocked((v) => !v); }}
                  >
                    <div style={{ ...styles.toggleThumb, transform: dangerLocked ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(18px)' }} />
                  </div>
                </div>
              }
            >
              <div
                style={{
                  ...styles.settingsItem,
                  borderColor: 'var(--pink)',
                  opacity: dangerLocked ? 0.4 : 1,
                  cursor: dangerLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
                  alignItems: 'flex-start',
                  padding: '14px 14px',
                }}
                onClick={() => !editMode && !dangerLocked && onReset()}
              >
                <div style={styles.settingsIcon}><TypeIcon name="warning" size={22} color="var(--pink-text)" /></div>
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.settingsLabel, color: 'var(--pink-text)', fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 600, marginBottom: 8 }}>清除所有資料</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text)', opacity: 0.75, lineHeight: 1.7 }}>
                    <div style={{ marginBottom: 2 }}>
                      <span style={{ color: 'var(--pink-text)', opacity: 1, fontWeight: 600 }}>移除</span>
                      <span style={{ margin: '0 8px', opacity: 0.55 }}>·</span>
                      <span>交易紀錄</span>
                      <span style={{ margin: '0 6px', opacity: 0.45 }}>／</span>
                      <span>帳戶</span>
                      <span style={{ margin: '0 6px', opacity: 0.45 }}>／</span>
                      <span>分類</span>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <span style={{ color: 'var(--mint-text)', opacity: 1, fontWeight: 600 }}>保留</span>
                      <span style={{ margin: '0 8px', opacity: 0.55 }}>·</span>
                      <span>快照備份</span>
                      <span style={{ margin: '0 6px', opacity: 0.45 }}>／</span>
                      <span>介面排序</span>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.settingsArrow}>›</div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        return null;
      })}
      </div>

      {showThirdParty && (
        <ThirdPartySheet onClose={() => setShowThirdParty(false)} toast={toast} />
      )}

      {showCleanupSheet && (
        <CleanupHistorySheet
          state={state}
          onClose={() => setShowCleanupSheet(false)}
          onCleanup={onCleanupHistory}
          setConfirmDialog={setConfirmDialog}
        />
      )}

      {showFilterDeleteSheet && (
        <FilterDeleteSheet
          state={state}
          setState={setStateWithSync}
          onClose={() => setShowFilterDeleteSheet(false)}
          setConfirmDialog={setConfirmDialog}
          toast={toast}
          toastRich={toastRich}
        />
      )}

      {/* Drive 資料夾設定彈窗 */}
      {showDriveSetup && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowDriveSetup(false)}>
          <div style={styles.pickerCard} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()} {...driveSetupSwipe}>
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>設定 Google Drive 資料夾</div>
            <div style={{ padding: '14px 16px' }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', lineHeight: 1.7, marginBottom: 10 }}>
                1. 到 Google Drive 建立備份用資料夾<br />
                2. 右鍵 → 共用 → 複製連結<br />
                3. 把連結貼到下方
              </div>
              <input
                type="text"
                style={styles.field}
                value={driveInput}
                onChange={(e) => setDriveInput(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="https://drive.google.com/drive/folders/..."
                autoFocus
              />
              <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 8 }}>
                留空可以清除設定
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8, padding: '0 16px 16px' }}>
              <button
                style={{ ...styles.deleteBtn, flex: 1, marginTop: 0 }}
                onClick={() => setShowDriveSetup(false)}
              >取消</button>
              <button
                style={{ ...styles.saveBtn, flex: 1, background: 'var(--mint)', color: 'var(--on-mint)', marginTop: 0 }}
                onClick={saveDriveUrl}
              >儲存</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 顯示 JSON 文字讓使用者手動複製(沙盒環境救援) */}
      {exportTextDialog !== null && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setExportTextDialog(null)}>
          <div style={styles.pickerCard} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>備份 JSON</div>
            <div style={{ padding: '14px 16px' }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', lineHeight: 1.7, marginBottom: 10 }}>
                長按下方文字 → 全選 → 複製,貼到 LINE Keep / 記事本 / 另一個瀏覽器分頁的「貼上 JSON 匯入」
              </div>
              <textarea
                readOnly
                style={{
                  ...styles.field,
                  minHeight: 180,
                  fontFamily: 'monospace',
                  fontSize: 11,
                  resize: 'vertical',
                }}
                value={exportTextDialog}
                onFocus={(e) => e.target.select()}
                onClick={(e) => e.target.select()}
              />
              <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 8 }}>
                共 {exportTextDialog.length.toLocaleString()} 字元
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8, padding: '0 16px 16px' }}>
              <button
                style={{ ...styles.deleteBtn, flex: 1, marginTop: 0 }}
                onClick={() => setExportTextDialog(null)}
              >關閉</button>
              <button
                style={{ ...styles.saveBtn, flex: 1, background: 'var(--mint)', color: 'var(--on-mint)', marginTop: 0 }}
                onClick={async () => {
                  try {
                    await navigator.clipboard.writeText(exportTextDialog);
                    toast('已複製到剪貼簿');
                  } catch {
                    toast('請手動長按文字複製');
                  }
                }}
              >嘗試複製</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 貼上 JSON 文字匯入對話框(沙盒環境救援用) */}
      {showPasteImport && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => { setShowPasteImport(false); setPasteImportText(''); }}>
          <div style={styles.pickerCard} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>貼上 JSON 匯入</div>
            <div style={{ padding: '14px 16px' }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', lineHeight: 1.7, marginBottom: 10 }}>
                把備份 JSON 文字貼到下方,可從 LINE Keep / 記事本複製
              </div>
              <textarea
                style={{
                  ...styles.field,
                  minHeight: 140,
                  fontFamily: 'monospace',
                  fontSize: 11,
                  resize: 'vertical',
                }}
                value={pasteImportText}
                onChange={(e) => setPasteImportText(e.target.value)}
                placeholder='{"transactions":[...],"accounts":[...]...}'
              />
              <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 8 }}>
                {pasteImportText.length > 0 ? `已貼上 ${pasteImportText.length.toLocaleString()} 字元` : '尚未貼上內容'}
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8, padding: '0 16px 16px' }}>
              <button
                style={{ ...styles.deleteBtn, flex: 1, marginTop: 0 }}
                onClick={() => { setShowPasteImport(false); setPasteImportText(''); }}
              >取消</button>
              <button
                style={{
                  ...styles.saveBtn,
                  flex: 1,
                  background: pasteImportText.trim() ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--bg-card-alt)',
                  color: pasteImportText.trim() ? 'var(--on-mint)' : 'var(--text-faint)',
                  marginTop: 0,
                  opacity: pasteImportText.trim() ? 1 : 0.5,
                }}
                disabled={!pasteImportText.trim()}
                onClick={() => applyImportFromText(pasteImportText.trim())}
              >匯入</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 提醒頻率設定彈窗 */}
      {showReminderSetup && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowReminderSetup(false)}>
          <div style={styles.pickerCard} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()} {...reminderSetupSwipe}>
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>備份提醒頻率</div>
            <div style={styles.pickerList}>
              {[3, 7, 14, 30].map((d) => (
                <div className="picker-item"
                  key={d}
                  style={{
                    ...styles.pickerItem,
                    ...(backupReminderDays === d ? { background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.08)' } : {}),
                  }}
                  onClick={() => updateReminderDays(d)}
