                        callGlobalToastRich({
                          variant: 'info_card',
                          titleSegments: [
                            { text: '「', color: 'var(--text-dim)' },
                            { text: txn._deletedAccountName, color: 'var(--text)', weight: 700 },
                            { text: '」帳戶', color: 'var(--text-dim)' },
                          ],
                          subtitle: '建立時間為',
                          highlight: timeText,
                          highlightColor: 'var(--blue)',
                        }, 2147483647);
                      }
                    }}
                    style={{
                      display: 'inline-flex',
                      alignItems: 'center',
                      justifyContent: 'center',
                      width: 16, height: 16,
                      marginLeft: 4,
                      color: 'var(--text-faint)',
                      cursor: 'pointer',
                      verticalAlign: 'middle',
                      WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
                    }}
                    title="建立時間"
                  >
                    <svg width="13" height="13" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
                      <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9.5" />
                      <line x1="12" y1="11" x2="12" y2="16.5" />
                      <circle cx="12" cy="8" r="0.7" fill="currentColor" />
                    </svg>
                  </span>
                </>
              ) : (
                <span>{acct ? acct.name : ''}</span>
              )}
              {roleTag && <span>  {roleTag}</span>}
            </>
          ) : (
            catLabel
          )}
        </div>
        <div style={styles.txnMeta}>
          {dateShort}
          {isTransferRole ? (
            // 轉帳的 meta 行顯示對方帳戶
            peerName ? (
              <>
                {' '}{peerName}
                {(peerVirtual || peerDeleted) && (
                  <span style={{
                    color: peerDeleted ? 'var(--text-faint)' : 'var(--mint)',
                    fontSize: 10,
                    fontWeight: 500,
                    marginLeft: 4,
                    padding: '0px 5px',
                    borderRadius: 3,
                    background: peerDeleted ? 'rgba(140, 140, 140, 0.12)' : 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.12)',
                  }}>{peerDeleted ? '帳號已刪' : '虛擬'}</span>
                )}
              </>
            ) : null
          ) : acct ? (
            <>
              {' '}{acct.name}
              {acct.virtual && (
                <span style={{
                  color: 'var(--mint)',
                  fontSize: 10,
                  fontWeight: 500,
                  marginLeft: 4,
                  padding: '0px 5px',
                  borderRadius: 3,
                  background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.12)',
                }}>虛擬</span>
              )}
            </>
          ) : txn._deletedAccountName ? (
            <>
              {' '}{txn._deletedAccountName}
              <span style={{
                    color: 'var(--text-faint)',
                    fontSize: 10,
                    fontWeight: 500,
                    marginLeft: 4,
                    padding: '0px 5px',
                    borderRadius: 3,
                    background: 'rgba(140, 140, 140, 0.12)',
                  }}>{'帳號已刪'}</span>
              <span
                onClick={(e) => {
                  e.stopPropagation();
                  {
                        const ts = txn._deletedAccountCreatedAt;
                        let timeText = '建立時間未知';
                        if (ts) {
                          const d = new Date(ts);
                          const Y = d.getFullYear();
                          const M = String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0');
                          const D = String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
                          const h = String(d.getHours()).padStart(2, '0');
                          const m = String(d.getMinutes()).padStart(2, '0');
                          timeText = `${Y}/${M}/${D} ${h}:${m}`;
                        }
                        callGlobalToastRich({
                          variant: 'info_card',
                          titleSegments: [
                            { text: '「', color: 'var(--text-dim)' },
                            { text: txn._deletedAccountName, color: 'var(--text)', weight: 700 },
                            { text: '」帳戶', color: 'var(--text-dim)' },
                          ],
                          subtitle: '建立時間為',
                          highlight: timeText,
                          highlightColor: 'var(--blue)',
                        }, 2147483647);
                      }
                }}
                style={{
                  display: 'inline-flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  width: 16, height: 16,
                  marginLeft: 4,
                  color: 'var(--text-faint)',
                  cursor: 'pointer',
                  verticalAlign: 'middle',
                  WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
                }}
                title="建立時間"
              >
                <svg width="13" height="13" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="1.8" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
                  <circle cx="12" cy="12" r="9.5" />
                  <line x1="12" y1="11" x2="12" y2="16.5" />
                  <circle cx="12" cy="8" r="0.7" fill="currentColor" />
                </svg>
              </span>
            </>
          ) : null}
          {txn.note && !isTransferRole && (
            <span style={noteListColor ? { color: noteListColor } : undefined}>
              {' · '}{txn.note}
            </span>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style={{ ...styles.txnAmt, color: amtColor }}>
        {isExp ? '-' : '+'}{fmt(txn.amount)}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
});

// ============ 新增/編輯交易 Sheet ============
// ============ 日期選擇器（自訂深色主題）============
function DatePicker({ value, onChange, onClose }) {
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(onClose);
  const today = todayStr();
  const [viewYM, setViewYM] = useState(() => (value || today).slice(0, 7)); // YYYY-MM
  // 日曆顏色主題（存 localStorage，AddTxnSheet 的日期區塊齒輪會改這些值）
  const [weekendColor, setWeekendColor] = useState(() => {
    try { return localStorage.getItem('ledger_dp_weekend') || 'var(--pink)'; } catch { return 'var(--pink)'; }
  });
  const [selectedColor, setSelectedColor] = useState(() => {
    try { return localStorage.getItem('ledger_dp_selected') || 'var(--mint)'; } catch { return 'var(--mint)'; }
  });
  const updateWeekendColor = (c) => { setWeekendColor(c); try { localStorage.setItem('ledger_dp_weekend', c); } catch {} };
  const updateSelectedColor = (c) => { setSelectedColor(c); try { localStorage.setItem('ledger_dp_selected', c); } catch {} };

  const [y, m] = viewYM.split('-').map(Number);
  const firstDay = new Date(y, m - 1, 1);
  const daysInMonth = new Date(y, m, 0).getDate();
  const startWeekday = firstDay.getDay(); // 0=Sun
  const cells = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < startWeekday; i++) cells.push(null);
  for (let d = 1; d <= daysInMonth; d++) cells.push(d);
  // 補空格到 42 格(6 週 × 7 天),固定日曆高度避免按鈕跳動
  while (cells.length < 42) cells.push(null);

  const [slideDir, setSlideDir] = useState(0); // -1 左滑、+1 右滑、0 無
  const [animKey, setAnimKey] = useState(0);

  const shiftMonth = (delta) => {
    let ny = y, nm = m + delta;
    if (nm < 1) { nm = 12; ny -= 1; }
    if (nm > 12) { nm = 1; ny += 1; }
    setSlideDir(delta);
    setAnimKey((k) => k + 1);
    setViewYM(`${ny}-${String(nm).padStart(2, '0')}`);
    try { navigator.vibrate?.(8); } catch {}
  };

  const selectDate = (d) => {
    const iso = `${y}-${String(m).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(d).padStart(2, '0')}`;
    onChange(iso);
    onClose();
  };

  const selected = value || today;
  const [sy, sm, sd] = selected.split('-').map(Number);
  const isSelected = (d) => y === sy && m === sm && d === sd;
  const isToday = (d) => {
    const [ty, tm, td] = today.split('-').map(Number);
    return y === ty && m === tm && d === td;
  };

  // 選中日期的禮拜幾
  const selectedDateObj = new Date(`${selected}T00:00:00`);
  const selectedWeekday = ['日', '一', '二', '三', '四', '五', '六'][selectedDateObj.getDay()];

  // 顏色選項
  const colorOptions = [
    { name: '薄荷綠', value: 'var(--mint)', preview: '#7ee0c0' },
    { name: '粉紅', value: 'var(--pink)', preview: '#f5b5c0' },
    { name: '紫', value: 'var(--accent)', preview: '#8f7ff0' },
    { name: '橘', value: '#f5a04a', preview: '#f5a04a' },
    { name: '黃', value: '#f5d84a', preview: '#f5d84a' },
    { name: '藍', value: '#6aa8f0', preview: '#6aa8f0' },
  ];

  return (
    <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={onClose}>
      <div
        style={{
          ...styles.datePickerCard,
          transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
          transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
        }}
        ref={swipe.ref}
        onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
      >
        <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
          <div style={{ width: 30 }} />
          <div style={styles.sheetTitle}>
            <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 500, marginRight: 8 }}>目前選擇</span>
            <span style={{ color: selectedColor, fontWeight: 700 }}>
              {sy}/{String(sm).padStart(2, '0')}/{String(sd).padStart(2, '0')} 週{selectedWeekday}
            </span>
          </div>
          <div style={{ width: 30 }} />
        </div>

        {/* 月份切換 */}
        <div style={styles.dpMonthBar}>
          <button className="dp-nav-btn" style={styles.dpNav} onClick={() => shiftMonth(-1)}>‹</button>
          <div
            key={'title-' + animKey}
            style={{
              ...styles.dpMonthTitle,
              animation: slideDir !== 0 ? `dpSlide${slideDir > 0 ? 'Right' : 'Left'} 0.22s cubic-bezier(0.2, 0.8, 0.2, 1)` : undefined,
            }}
          >{y} 年 {m} 月</div>
          <button className="dp-nav-btn" style={styles.dpNav} onClick={() => shiftMonth(1)}>›</button>
        </div>

        {/* 星期標籤 */}
        <div style={styles.dpWeekRow}>
          {['日', '一', '二', '三', '四', '五', '六'].map((w, i) => (
            <div key={w} style={{ ...styles.dpWeekLabel, color: i === 0 || i === 6 ? weekendColor : 'var(--text-faint)' }}>{w}</div>
          ))}
        </div>

        {/* 日期格 */}
        <div
          key={animKey}
          style={{
            ...styles.dpGrid,
            animation: slideDir !== 0 ? `dpSlide${slideDir > 0 ? 'Right' : 'Left'} 0.22s cubic-bezier(0.2, 0.8, 0.2, 1)` : undefined,
          }}
        >
          {cells.map((d, i) => {
            if (d === null) return <div key={'e' + i} style={{ aspectRatio: '1 / 1' }} />;
            const sel = isSelected(d);
            const today_ = isToday(d);
            const weekday = (startWeekday + d - 1) % 7;
            const isWeekend = weekday === 0 || weekday === 6;
            return (
              <div
                key={d}
                style={{
                  ...styles.dpDay,
                  ...(sel ? { background: selectedColor, color: 'var(--on-mint)', fontWeight: 700 } : {}),
                  ...(!sel && today_ ? { outline: `1.5px solid ${selectedColor}`, outlineOffset: '-1.5px', color: selectedColor } : {}),
                  ...(!sel && isWeekend ? { color: weekendColor } : {}),
                }}
                onClick={() => selectDate(d)}
              >
                {d}
              </div>
            );
          })}
        </div>

        <button style={{ ...styles.saveBtn, background: selectedColor, color: 'var(--on-mint)', marginTop: 14 }} onClick={() => selectDate(parseInt(today.slice(8)))}>回到今天</button>
        <button style={{ ...styles.deleteBtn, marginTop: 6 }} onClick={onClose}>取消</button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 備註樣式設定 sheet ============
function NotePrefSheet({ pref, onClose, setConfirmDialog, toastRich }) {
  const swipe = useSwipeToCloseAny(onClose);
  const [textColor, setTextColor] = useState(pref.textColor || '');
  const [bgColor, setBgColor] = useState(pref.bgColor || '');
  const [applyToInput, setApplyToInput] = useState(pref.applyToInput !== false);
  const [applyToList, setApplyToList] = useState(pref.applyToList !== false);

  const TEXT_PRESETS = ['', '#f5b5c0', '#7ee0c0', '#8f7ff0', '#f5d84a', '#f5a04a', '#6aa8f0', '#e88a8a'];
  const BG_PRESETS = ['', '#1a1c20', '#3a2828', '#283a28', '#28323a', '#3a2838', '#f5f5f0', '#fde4e8'];

  const apply = () => {
    const newPref = { textColor, bgColor, applyToInput, applyToList };
    const doApply = () => {
      try { localStorage.setItem(NOTE_PREF_KEY, JSON.stringify(newPref)); } catch {}
      notePrefBroadcast(newPref);
      onClose();
      if (toastRich) {
        toastRich({
          title: '已套用備註樣式',
          amount: '✓',
          amountColor: 'var(--mint-text)',
          lines: [
            applyToInput && applyToList ? '記帳時 + 瀏覽時' :
            applyToInput ? '僅記帳時' :
            applyToList ? '僅瀏覽時' : '兩者都未啟用',
          ],
        });
      }
    };
    if (!setConfirmDialog) { doApply(); return; }
    setConfirmDialog({
      title: '套用備註樣式',
      message: '確定要套用目前的備註樣式嗎?\n會覆蓋現有設定。',
      confirmText: '套用',
      onConfirm: doApply,
    });
  };
  const reset = () => {
    if (!setConfirmDialog) return;
    setConfirmDialog({
      title: '重設備註樣式',
      messageList: {
        before: '確定要還原成預設樣式嗎?',
        items: ['文字色', '背景色', '套用範圍'],
        after: '都會回到原本的設定。',
      },
      confirmText: '重設',
      danger: true,
      onConfirm: () => {
        setTextColor(''); setBgColor(''); setApplyToInput(true); setApplyToList(true);
        const defaultPref = { textColor: '', bgColor: '', applyToInput: true, applyToList: true };
        try { localStorage.setItem(NOTE_PREF_KEY, JSON.stringify(defaultPref)); } catch {}
        try { localStorage.removeItem(NOTE_COLOR_KEY); } catch {}
        noteColorBroadcast('');
        notePrefBroadcast(defaultPref);
        onClose();
        if (toastRich) {
          toastRich({
            title: '已重設備註樣式',
            amount: '✓',
            amountColor: 'var(--mint-text)',
            lines: ['文字色 / 背景色 / 套用範圍 已還原預設'],
          });
        }
      },
    });
  };

  // 共用色票按鈕渲染 (active 用中央打勾表示)
  const ColorSwatch = ({ value, active, onClick, isText }) => {
    // 判断色票亮暗以選拾打勾色
    const isLight = value && /^#[a-f0-9]{6}$/i.test(value) ? (
      parseInt(value.slice(1, 3), 16) * 0.299 +
      parseInt(value.slice(3, 5), 16) * 0.587 +
      parseInt(value.slice(5, 7), 16) * 0.114
    ) > 160 : false;
    const checkColor = !value ? 'var(--mint)' : (isLight ? '#1a1a1a' : '#fff');
    return (
      <button
        onClick={onClick}
        style={{
          aspectRatio: '1',
          borderRadius: isText ? '50%' : 10,
          border: '1px solid var(--border)',
          background: value || 'transparent',
          cursor: 'pointer',
          display: 'flex',
          alignItems: 'center',
          justifyContent: 'center',
          padding: 0,
          position: 'relative',
        }}
      >
        {active && (
          <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="60%" height="60%" fill="none" stroke={checkColor} strokeWidth="3.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
            <polyline points="4 12 10 18 20 6" />
          </svg>
        )}
        {!value && !active && (
          <span style={{ fontSize: 14, color: 'var(--text-faint)', lineHeight: 1 }}>—</span>
        )}
      </button>
    );
  };

  // 自訂色按鈕 (彩虹漸層 + 色票適配)
  const [pickerFor, setPickerFor] = useState(null); // 'text' | 'bg' | null

  const CustomColorBtn = ({ value, fieldKey, isText }) => {
    return (
      <button
        onClick={() => setPickerFor(fieldKey)}
        style={{
          aspectRatio: '1',
          borderRadius: isText ? '50%' : 10,
          border: '1px solid var(--border)',
          background: value || 'conic-gradient(from 0deg, #f5b5c0, #f5d84a, #7ee0c0, #6aa8f0, #8f7ff0, #f5b5c0)',
          cursor: 'pointer',
          padding: 0,
          position: 'relative',
          overflow: 'hidden',
        }}
        title="自訂色"
      />
    );
  };

  const ToggleRow = ({ label, sublabel, val, set }) => (
    <div
      onClick={() => set((v) => !v)}
      style={{
        display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between',
        padding: '8px 12px',
        background: 'var(--bg-card)',
        borderRadius: 8,
        cursor: 'pointer',
        flex: 1,
        gap: 6,
      }}
    >
      <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', minWidth: 0 }}>
        <span style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text)', fontWeight: 600 }}>{label}</span>
        {sublabel && (
          <span style={{ fontSize: 10, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 1 }}>{sublabel}</span>
        )}
      </div>
      <div style={{
        width: 32, height: 18, borderRadius: 9,
        background: val ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--border)',
        position: 'relative',
        flexShrink: 0,
        transition: 'background 0.2s',
      }}>
        <div style={{
          position: 'absolute', top: 2, left: 2,
          width: 14, height: 14, borderRadius: '50%',
          background: '#fff',
          transition: 'transform 0.2s',
          transform: val ? 'translateX(14px)' : 'translateX(0)',
        }} />
      </div>
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <div
      data-picker-backdrop="true"
      style={{
        position: 'fixed', inset: 0,
        background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.4)',
        zIndex: 350,
        display: 'flex',
        alignItems: 'flex-end',
      }}
      onClick={onClose}
    >
      <div
        {...swipe}
        style={{
          width: '100%',
          background: 'var(--bg)',
          borderTopLeftRadius: 18,
          borderTopRightRadius: 18,
          padding: '10px 14px calc(12px + env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0px))',
          boxShadow: '0 -10px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.5)',
          transform: `translateY(${swipe.dragY}px)`,
          transition: swipe.dragY === 0 ? 'transform 0.2s' : 'none',
          animation: swipe.dragY === 0 ? 'slideUp 0.2s ease-out' : 'none',
        }}
        onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
      >
        {/* 拖拉條 */}
        <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', marginBottom: 6 }}>
          <div style={{ width: 36, height: 4, borderRadius: 2, background: 'var(--border)' }} />
        </div>

        <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--text)', marginBottom: 10, textAlign: 'center' }}>
          備註樣式設定
        </div>

        {/* 文字色 */}
        <div style={{ marginBottom: 8 }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 5, fontWeight: 600 }}>文字顏色</div>
          <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(9, 1fr)', gap: 5, alignItems: 'center' }}>
            {TEXT_PRESETS.map((v) => (
              <ColorSwatch key={v || 'def'} value={v} active={textColor === v} onClick={() => setTextColor(v)} isText />
            ))}
            <CustomColorBtn value={textColor && !TEXT_PRESETS.includes(textColor) ? textColor : ''} fieldKey="text" isText />
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 背景色 */}
        <div style={{ marginBottom: 10 }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 5, fontWeight: 600 }}>框背景色</div>
          <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(9, 1fr)', gap: 5, alignItems: 'center' }}>
            {BG_PRESETS.map((v) => (
              <ColorSwatch key={v || 'def'} value={v} active={bgColor === v} onClick={() => setBgColor(v)} />
            ))}
            <CustomColorBtn value={bgColor && !BG_PRESETS.includes(bgColor) ? bgColor : ''} fieldKey="bg" />
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 套用範圍(2 個 toggle 並排) */}
        <div style={{ marginBottom: 10 }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 5, fontWeight: 600 }}>套用範圍</div>
          <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 5 }}>
            <ToggleRow label="記帳時" sublabel="新增/編輯備註欄" val={applyToInput} set={setApplyToInput} />
            <ToggleRow label="瀏覽時" sublabel="明細頁的備註" val={applyToList} set={setApplyToList} />
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 預覽 */}
        <div style={{
          padding: '8px 12px',
          background: bgColor || 'var(--bg-card)',
          borderRadius: 8,
          marginBottom: 10,
          border: '1px dashed var(--border)',
          minHeight: 36,
          display: 'flex',
          alignItems: 'center',
        }}>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 10, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginRight: 8 }}>預覽</span>
          <span style={{ color: textColor || 'var(--text)', fontSize: 13 }}>
            記下他們今天一起吃拉麵
          </span>
        </div>

        {/* 按鈕 */}
        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8 }}>
          <button
            onClick={reset}
            style={{
              flex: 1, padding: '10px',
              border: '1px solid var(--border)',
              borderRadius: 10,
              background: 'transparent',
              color: 'var(--text-dim)',
              fontSize: 13,
              cursor: 'pointer',
            }}
          >重設</button>
          <button
            onClick={apply}
            style={{
              flex: 2, padding: '10px',
              border: 'none',
              borderRadius: 10,
              background: 'var(--mint)',
              color: 'var(--on-mint)',
              fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700,
              cursor: 'pointer',
            }}
          >套用</button>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* 自製 HSL color picker */}
      {pickerFor && (
        <ColorPickerDialog
          initial={pickerFor === 'text' ? (textColor || '#7ee0c0') : (bgColor || '#2a2d34')}
          onCancel={() => setPickerFor(null)}
          onConfirm={(c) => {
            if (pickerFor === 'text') setTextColor(c);
            else setBgColor(c);
            setPickerFor(null);
          }}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 自製 HSL Color Picker ============
function ColorPickerDialog({ initial, onCancel, onConfirm }) {
  const swipe = useSwipeToCloseAny(onCancel);
  // 解析 initial 成 HSL
  const parseHex = (hex) => {
    if (!hex || !/^#[0-9a-f]{6}$/i.test(hex)) return { h: 180, s: 50, l: 50 };
    const r = parseInt(hex.slice(1, 3), 16) / 255;
    const g = parseInt(hex.slice(3, 5), 16) / 255;
    const b = parseInt(hex.slice(5, 7), 16) / 255;
    const max = Math.max(r, g, b);
    const min = Math.min(r, g, b);
    const l = (max + min) / 2;
    let h = 0, s = 0;
    if (max !== min) {
      const d = max - min;
      s = l > 0.5 ? d / (2 - max - min) : d / (max + min);
      if (max === r) h = (g - b) / d + (g < b ? 6 : 0);
      else if (max === g) h = (b - r) / d + 2;
      else h = (r - g) / d + 4;
      h *= 60;
    }
    return { h: Math.round(h), s: Math.round(s * 100), l: Math.round(l * 100) };
  };

  const hslToHex = (h, s, l) => {
    s /= 100; l /= 100;
    const k = (n) => (n + h / 30) % 12;
    const a = s * Math.min(l, 1 - l);
    const f = (n) => l - a * Math.max(-1, Math.min(k(n) - 3, Math.min(9 - k(n), 1)));
    const toHex = (x) => Math.round(x * 255).toString(16).padStart(2, '0');
    return '#' + toHex(f(0)) + toHex(f(8)) + toHex(f(4));
  };

  const init = parseHex(initial);
  const [h, setH] = useState(init.h);
  const [s, setS] = useState(init.s);
  const [l, setL] = useState(init.l);
  const [hexInput, setHexInput] = useState(initial);

  const currentHex = hslToHex(h, s, l);

  React.useEffect(() => {
    setHexInput(currentHex);
  }, [h, s, l]);

  const onHexChange = (val) => {
    setHexInput(val);
    if (/^#[0-9a-f]{6}$/i.test(val)) {
      const parsed = parseHex(val);
      setH(parsed.h);
      setS(parsed.s);
      setL(parsed.l);
    }
  };

  // 預設色票快選
  const QUICK_COLORS = [
    '#f5b5c0', '#7ee0c0', '#8f7ff0', '#f5d84a',
    '#f5a04a', '#6aa8f0', '#e88a8a', '#1a1c20',
    '#2a2d34', '#3a2828', '#283a28', '#28323a',
    '#3a2838', '#f5f5f0', '#fde4e8', '#ffffff',
  ];

  return (
    <div
      data-picker-backdrop="true"
      style={{
        position: 'fixed', inset: 0,
        background: 'rgba(0,0,0,0.6)',
        backdropFilter: 'blur(4px)',
        WebkitBackdropFilter: 'blur(4px)',
        zIndex: 500,
        display: 'flex',
        alignItems: 'center',
        justifyContent: 'center',
        animation: 'fadeIn 0.15s ease-out',
      }}
      onClick={onCancel}
    >
      <div
        {...swipe}
        onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
        style={{
          width: 'calc(100% - 32px)',
          maxWidth: 360,
          background: 'var(--bg)',
          borderRadius: 18,
          padding: 18,
          boxShadow: '0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.5)',
          transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX || 0}px) translateY(${swipe.dragY}px)`,
          transition: swipe.dragY === 0 ? 'transform 0.2s' : 'none',
          animation: swipe.dragY === 0 ? 'centerAlertPop 0.25s cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1)' : 'none',
        }}
      >
        {/* 大預覽塊 */}
        <div style={{
          width: '100%', height: 80,
          background: currentHex,
          borderRadius: 12,
          marginBottom: 14,
          border: '1px solid var(--border)',
          display: 'flex',
          alignItems: 'center',
          justifyContent: 'center',
          fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700, fontFamily: "'Space Grotesk', sans-serif",
          color: l > 60 ? '#1a1a1a' : '#fff',
          letterSpacing: '1px',
        }}>
          {currentHex.toUpperCase()}
        </div>

        {/* 色相 slider */}
        <div style={{ marginBottom: 10 }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 4 }}>色相 H · {h}°</div>
          <input
            type="range"
            onTouchStart={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
            onTouchMove={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
            min="0" max="360"
            value={h}
            onChange={(e) => setH(Number(e.target.value))}
            style={{
              width: '100%', height: 22,
              appearance: 'none',
              WebkitAppearance: 'none',
              background: 'linear-gradient(to right, #ff0000, #ffff00, #00ff00, #00ffff, #0000ff, #ff00ff, #ff0000)',
              borderRadius: 11,
              outline: 'none',
              cursor: 'pointer',
            }}
          />
        </div>

        {/* 飽和度 slider */}
        <div style={{ marginBottom: 10 }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 4 }}>飽和度 S · {s}%</div>
          <input
            type="range"
            onTouchStart={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
            onTouchMove={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
            min="0" max="100"
            value={s}
            onChange={(e) => setS(Number(e.target.value))}
            style={{
              width: '100%', height: 22,
              appearance: 'none',
              WebkitAppearance: 'none',
              background: `linear-gradient(to right, ${hslToHex(h, 0, l)}, ${hslToHex(h, 100, l)})`,
              borderRadius: 11,
              outline: 'none',
              cursor: 'pointer',
            }}
          />
        </div>

        {/* 明度 slider */}
        <div style={{ marginBottom: 12 }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 4 }}>明度 L · {l}%</div>
          <input
            type="range"
            onTouchStart={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
            onTouchMove={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
            min="0" max="100"
            value={l}
            onChange={(e) => setL(Number(e.target.value))}
            style={{
              width: '100%', height: 22,
              appearance: 'none',
              WebkitAppearance: 'none',
              background: `linear-gradient(to right, #000, ${hslToHex(h, s, 50)}, #fff)`,
              borderRadius: 11,
              outline: 'none',
              cursor: 'pointer',
            }}
          />
        </div>

        {/* HEX 輸入 */}
        <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8, marginBottom: 12 }}>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', flexShrink: 0 }}>HEX</span>
          <input
            type="text"
            onTouchStart={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
            value={hexInput}
            onChange={(e) => onHexChange(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="#7ee0c0"
            maxLength={7}
            style={{
              flex: 1,
              padding: '8px 10px',
              background: 'var(--bg-card)',
              border: '1px solid var(--border)',
              borderRadius: 8,
              color: 'var(--text)',
              fontSize: 13,
              fontFamily: "'Space Grotesk', sans-serif",
              outline: 'none',
              textTransform: 'uppercase',
            }}
          />
        </div>

        {/* 快選色 */}
        <div style={{ marginBottom: 14 }}>
          <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 5 }}>快速選色</div>
          <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(8, 1fr)', gap: 5 }}>
            {QUICK_COLORS.map((c) => (
              <button
                key={c}
                onClick={() => onHexChange(c)}
                style={{
                  aspectRatio: '1',
                  borderRadius: 8,
                  border: currentHex.toLowerCase() === c.toLowerCase() ? '2px solid var(--mint)' : '1px solid var(--border)',
                  background: c,
                  cursor: 'pointer',
                  padding: 0,
                }}
              />
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* 按鈕 */}
        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8 }}>
          <button
            onClick={onCancel}
            style={{
              flex: 1, padding: '11px',
              border: '1px solid var(--border)',
              borderRadius: 10,
              background: 'transparent',
              color: 'var(--text-dim)',
              fontSize: 13,
              cursor: 'pointer',
            }}
          >取消</button>
          <button
            onClick={() => onConfirm(currentHex)}
            style={{
              flex: 2, padding: '11px',
              border: 'none',
              borderRadius: 10,
              background: 'var(--mint)',
              color: 'var(--on-mint)',
              fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 700,
              cursor: 'pointer',
            }}
          >確定</button>
        </div>

        <style>{`
          input[type="range"]::-webkit-slider-thumb {
            -webkit-appearance: none;
            appearance: none;
            width: 22px;
            height: 22px;
            border-radius: 50%;
            background: #fff;
            border: 2px solid rgba(0,0,0,0.3);
            cursor: pointer;
            box-shadow: 0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,0.4);
          }
          input[type="range"]::-moz-range-thumb {
            width: 22px;
            height: 22px;
            border-radius: 50%;
            background: #fff;
            border: 2px solid rgba(0,0,0,0.3);
            cursor: pointer;
            box-shadow: 0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,0.4);
          }
        `}</style>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 計算機鍵盤 (底部 sheet) ============
function CalculatorSheet({ expr, onChange, mainColor, onMainColor, onClose }) {
  const swipe = useSwipeToCloseAny(onClose);
  // 是否還是「初始狀態」(剛打開,尚未動過鍵盤)
  // 第一次按數字鍵時,把現有值蓋掉重新輸入;按運算子則保留繼續算
  const [pristine, setPristine] = useState(true);

  // 觸覺回饋:依按鍵類型給不同震動長度
  const haptic = (key) => {
    try {
      if (!navigator.vibrate) return;
      if (key === '=' || key === 'C') navigator.vibrate(20);  // 重要操作重震
      else if (['+', '-', '*', '/', '%', 'BACK'].includes(key)) navigator.vibrate(12); // 運算子中震
      else navigator.vibrate(8); // 數字輕震
    } catch {}
  };

  const press = (key) => {
    haptic(key);
    let cur = expr || '';

    if (key === 'C') {
      onChange('');
      setPristine(false);
      return;
    }
    if (key === 'BACK') {
      onChange(cur.slice(0, -1));
      setPristine(false);
      return;
    }
    if (key === '=') {
      const result = evalExpr(cur);
      if (result !== null) onChange(String(result));
      setPristine(false);
      return;
    }
    if (key === '%') {
      // 解析:找出「最後一段數字」與它前面的「運算子 + 基準數」
      // 規則:
      //   單獨數字: A %        → A / 100
      //   A + B %:               → A + (A * B / 100)
      //   A - B %:               → A - (A * B / 100)
      //   A * B %:               → A * B / 100
      //   A / B %:               → A / B / 100  (理論值,實作為 A / (B/100) 較常見?用 A * 100 / B 反而怪。直接用 A / B / 100)
      setPristine(false);
      if (!cur || /[+\-*/]$/.test(cur)) return; // 結尾沒數字
      const m = cur.match(/^(.*?)([+\-*/])([0-9.]+)$/);
      if (!m) {
        // 純粹一個數字 → 直接除 100
        const n = parseFloat(cur);
        if (!isNaN(n)) onChange(String(n / 100));
        return;
      }
      const [, prefix, op, lastNum] = m;
      const lastN = parseFloat(lastNum);
      if (isNaN(lastN)) return;
      // 找 prefix 的值當基準
      const baseVal = evalExpr(prefix);
      if (baseVal === null) return;
      let result;
      if (op === '+') result = baseVal + (baseVal * lastN / 100);
      else if (op === '-') result = baseVal - (baseVal * lastN / 100);
      else if (op === '*') result = baseVal * lastN / 100;
      else if (op === '/') result = baseVal / lastN / 100;
      if (!Number.isFinite(result)) return;
      // 4 位小數
      onChange(String(Math.round(result * 10000) / 10000));
      return;
    }
    if (['+', '-', '*', '/'].includes(key)) {
      // 運算子:保留現有值,離開 pristine
      setPristine(false);
      // 結尾為運算子 → 替換
      if (/[+\-*/]$/.test(cur)) {
        onChange(cur.slice(0, -1) + key);
        return;
      }
      if (cur === '') return; // 開頭不允許運算子
      onChange(cur + key);
      return;
    }
    // 以下為數字 / . / 00:若 pristine,先清空再輸入
    const startFresh = pristine;
    setPristine(false);
    const base = startFresh ? '' : cur;

    if (key === '.') {
      const m = base.match(/[0-9.]*$/);
      const lastNum = m ? m[0] : '';
      if (lastNum.includes('.')) return;
      if (lastNum === '') onChange(base + '0.');
      else onChange(base + '.');
      return;
    }
    if (key === '00') {
      const m = base.match(/[0-9.]*$/);
      const lastNum = m ? m[0] : '';
      if (lastNum === '' || lastNum === '0') {
        onChange(base === '' ? '0' : base);
      } else {
        onChange(base + '00');
      }
      return;
    }
    // 數字 0-9
    const m = base.match(/[0-9.]*$/);
    const lastNum = m ? m[0] : '';
    if (lastNum === '0') {
      onChange(base.slice(0, -1) + key);
    } else {
      onChange(base + key);
    }
  };

  const btnBase = {
    border: 'none',
    background: 'var(--bg-card)',
    color: 'var(--text)',
    fontSize: 22,
    fontWeight: 500,
    padding: '14px 0',
    borderRadius: 12,
    cursor: 'pointer',
    fontFamily: "'Space Grotesk', sans-serif",
    WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
    transition: 'transform 0.08s ease-out, background 0.08s ease-out',
    userSelect: 'none',
  };
  const opBtn = { ...btnBase, color: mainColor, fontWeight: 600 };
  const fnBtn = { ...btnBase, color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontSize: 18 };
  // 主色 RGB 解析(用於 :active 變色,把 mainColor 轉成淡覆蓋)
  const activeBgVar = '--calc-active-bg';

  return (
    <div
      data-picker-backdrop="true"
      {...swipe}
      style={{
        position: 'fixed', inset: 0,
        background: 'transparent',
        zIndex: 350,
        display: 'flex',
        alignItems: 'flex-end',
      }}
      onClick={onClose}
    >
      <div
        style={{
          width: '100%',
          background: 'var(--bg)',
          borderTopLeftRadius: 18,
          borderTopRightRadius: 18,
          padding: '14px 12px calc(12px + env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0px))',
          boxShadow: '0 -10px 40px rgba(0,0,0,0.5)',
          transform: `translateY(${swipe.dragY}px)`,
          transition: swipe.dragY === 0 ? 'transform 0.2s' : 'none',
          animation: swipe.dragY === 0 ? 'slideUp 0.2s ease-out' : 'none',
          touchAction: 'none',
        }}
        onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
      >
        {/* 鍵盤 4×5 grid */}
        <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(4, 1fr)', gap: 6 }}>
          <button className="calc-btn calc-btn-fn" style={fnBtn} onClick={() => press('C')}>C</button>
          <button className="calc-btn calc-btn-fn" style={fnBtn} onClick={() => press('BACK')}>⌫</button>
          <button className="calc-btn calc-btn-op" style={opBtn} onClick={() => press('%')}>%</button>
          <button className="calc-btn calc-btn-op" style={opBtn} onClick={() => press('/')}>÷</button>

          <button className="calc-btn" style={btnBase} onClick={() => press('7')}>7</button>
          <button className="calc-btn" style={btnBase} onClick={() => press('8')}>8</button>
          <button className="calc-btn" style={btnBase} onClick={() => press('9')}>9</button>
          <button className="calc-btn calc-btn-op" style={opBtn} onClick={() => press('*')}>×</button>

          <button className="calc-btn" style={btnBase} onClick={() => press('4')}>4</button>
          <button className="calc-btn" style={btnBase} onClick={() => press('5')}>5</button>
          <button className="calc-btn" style={btnBase} onClick={() => press('6')}>6</button>
          <button className="calc-btn calc-btn-op" style={opBtn} onClick={() => press('-')}>−</button>

          <button className="calc-btn" style={btnBase} onClick={() => press('1')}>1</button>
          <button className="calc-btn" style={btnBase} onClick={() => press('2')}>2</button>
          <button className="calc-btn" style={btnBase} onClick={() => press('3')}>3</button>
          <button className="calc-btn calc-btn-op" style={opBtn} onClick={() => press('+')}>+</button>

          <button className="calc-btn" style={{ ...btnBase, gridColumn: 'span 2' }} onClick={() => press('0')}>0</button>
          <button className="calc-btn" style={btnBase} onClick={() => press('.')}>.</button>
          <button
            className="calc-btn calc-btn-eq"
            style={{ ...opBtn, background: mainColor, color: onMainColor || '#1a1a1a', fontWeight: 700 }}
            onClick={() => press('=')}
          >=</button>
        </div>

        {/* 完成 */}
        <button
          className="calc-btn calc-btn-eq"
          onClick={() => {
            haptic('=');
            // 結束時若還是表達式,自動算一次
            const result = evalExpr(expr || '');
            if (result !== null) onChange(String(result));
            onClose();
          }}
          style={{
            width: '100%',
            marginTop: 10,
            padding: '14px 0',
            background: mainColor,
            color: onMainColor || '#1a1a1a',
            border: 'none',
            borderRadius: 12,
            fontSize: 15,
            fontWeight: 700,
            cursor: 'pointer',
            fontFamily: 'inherit',
          }}
        >
          完成
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// 共用:計算表達式
function evalExpr(expr) {
  try {
    if (!/^[0-9+\-*/.]*$/.test(expr)) return null;
    if (!expr) return 0;
    const clean = expr.replace(/[+\-*/]+$/, '');
    if (!clean) return 0;
    const result = Function('"use strict"; return (' + clean + ')')();
    if (!Number.isFinite(result)) return null;
    // 最多 4 位小數,去除多餘 0
    return Math.round(result * 10000) / 10000;
  } catch { return null; }
}

// 共用:把表達式轉成顯示用(× ÷ −)
function fmtExprDisplay(expr) {
  if (!expr) return '';
  return expr.replace(/\*/g, '×').replace(/\//g, '÷').replace(/-/g, '−');
}

function AddTxnSheet({ state, type, setType, editing, defaultDate, onSave, onDelete, toast, toastRich, alertCenter, noteColor, onClose, editMode, setEditMode, blockOrder, moveBlock, onManageCategory, onManageAccount, onAddSubCategory, setConfirmDialog, onOpenStockEntry }) {
  const [showCalculator, setShowCalculator] = useState(false);
  const [showNotePref, setShowNotePref] = useState(false);
  const [showOtherTypeSheet, setShowOtherTypeSheet] = useState(false);
  const notePref = useNotePref();
  // 保險:若 blockOrder 缺失或為空,使用預設順序
  const DEFAULT_ADD_TXN_ORDER = ['amount', 'typeToggle', 'date', 'category', 'subCategory', 'note', 'account'];
  const DEFAULT_TRANSFER_ORDER = ['amount', 'typeToggle', 'date', 'fromAccount', 'toAccount', 'note'];
  const DEFAULT_LEND_ORDER = ['amount', 'typeToggle', 'date', 'fromAccount', 'note', 'expectDate'];
  const isTransfer = type === 'transfer';
  const isLend = type === 'lend';
  const rawOrder = isTransfer
    ? DEFAULT_TRANSFER_ORDER
    : isLend
    ? DEFAULT_LEND_ORDER
    : ((blockOrder && blockOrder.length > 0) ? blockOrder : DEFAULT_ADD_TXN_ORDER);
  // 舊版 blockOrder 可能沒有 'note',這裡自動補上(放在 subCategory 後 / account 前較合理)
  const effectiveOrder = rawOrder.includes('note')
    ? rawOrder
    : (() => {
        const out = [...rawOrder];
        const accountIdx = out.indexOf('account');
        if (accountIdx >= 0) out.splice(accountIdx, 0, 'note');
        else out.push('note');
        return out;
      })();
  const [amount, setAmount] = useState(editing ? String(editing.amount) : '0');
  // 編輯時所有欄位預設鎖定（防止誤觸）
  const [fieldsLocked, setFieldsLocked] = useState(!!editing);
  // 編輯轉帳時:必須勾選確認才能儲存(避免使用者無意間連動更動了另一筆紀錄)
  const [transferAcked, setTransferAcked] = useState(false);
  const [category, setCategory] = useState(editing?.category || state.categories[type]?.[0]?.label || '');
  const [subCategory, setSubCategory] = useState(editing?.subCategory || state.categories[type]?.[0]?.subs?.[0] || '');
  const [accountId, setAccountId] = useState(editing?.accountId || state.accounts[0]?.id);
  const [note, setNote] = useState(editing?.note || '');
  const [date, setDate] = useState(editing?.date || defaultDate || todayStr());
  // 轉帳相關 state
  const editingTransfer = editing && editing.transferId;
  const transferGroup = editingTransfer ? state.transactions.filter((t) => t.transferId === editing.transferId) : null;
  const editOut = transferGroup ? transferGroup.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'out') : null;
  const editIn = transferGroup ? transferGroup.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'in') : null;
  const editFee = transferGroup ? transferGroup.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'fee') : null;
  // 任一端是已刪虛擬帳戶 → 整筆紀錄成為「歷史快照」,金額/手續費也應鎖死,避免變更後造成資產不平衡
  const transferDeletedVirtual = editingTransfer && (
    !!editOut?._deletedAccountName || !!editIn?._deletedAccountName
  );

  // 代墊相關 state
  const editingLend = editing && editing.lendId;
  const lendGroup = editingLend ? state.transactions.filter((t) => t.lendId === editing.lendId) : null;
  const editLendOut = lendGroup ? lendGroup.find((t) => t.transferRole === 'lend_out') : null;
  // editLendOut.lendMeta 有 expectDate/debtor

  // 轉帳預設:轉出 = 第一個非系統帳戶,轉入 = 第二個非系統帳戶(避開轉出)
  const realAccounts = state.accounts.filter((a) => !a.isSystem);
  const defaultFromId = realAccounts[0]?.id;
  const defaultToId = realAccounts.find((a) => a.id !== defaultFromId)?.id || '';

  const [fromAccountId, setFromAccountId] = useState(
    editOut?.accountId || editLendOut?.accountId || defaultFromId
  );
  const [toAccountId, setToAccountId] = useState(editIn?.accountId || defaultToId);
  const [fee, setFee] = useState(editFee ? String(editFee.amount) : '0');
  const [showFromSheet, setShowFromSheet] = useState(false);
  const [showToSheet, setShowToSheet] = useState(false);

  // 代墊欄位 state
  const [expectDate, setExpectDate] = useState(editLendOut?.lendMeta?.expectDate || '');
  const [debtor, setDebtor] = useState(editLendOut?.lendMeta?.debtor || '');
  const [showExpectDateSheet, setShowExpectDateSheet] = useState(false);
  // 手續費分類(可在齒輪中修改,有 localStorage 記憶)
  const [feeCategory, setFeeCategory] = useState(() => {
    if (editFee) return editFee.category;
    try { return localStorage.getItem('ledger_fee_cat') || '手續費用'; } catch { return '手續費用'; }
  });
  const [feeSubCategory, setFeeSubCategory] = useState(() => {
    if (editFee) return editFee.subCategory;
    try { return localStorage.getItem('ledger_fee_sub') || '轉帳（手續費）'; } catch { return '轉帳（手續費）'; }
  });
  const [showFeeCatPicker, setShowFeeCatPicker] = useState(false);
  const [feeCatStep, setFeeCatStep] = useState(1); // 1=選大分類, 2=選子分類
  const [feeCatStepCat, setFeeCatStepCat] = useState(null); // 第二階顯示哪個大分類
  const updateFeeCat = (cat, sub) => {
    setFeeCategory(cat);
    setFeeSubCategory(sub);
    try {
      localStorage.setItem('ledger_fee_cat', cat);
      localStorage.setItem('ledger_fee_sub', sub);
    } catch {}
  };
  const openFeeCatPicker = () => {
    // 若已有子分類,直接進第二階(顯示當前大分類的子分類列表)
    if (feeCategory && feeSubCategory) {
      setFeeCatStepCat(feeCategory);
      setFeeCatStep(2);
    } else {
      setFeeCatStep(1);
      setFeeCatStepCat(null);
    }
    setShowFeeCatPicker(true);
  };
  const [showDatePicker, setShowDatePicker] = useState(false);
  const [showCategorySheet, setShowCategorySheet] = useState(false);
  const [showSubCategorySheet, setShowSubCategorySheet] = useState(false);
  const [showAccountSheet, setShowAccountSheet] = useState(false);
  const [showSubInput, setShowSubInput] = useState(false);
  const [subInputValue, setSubInputValue] = useState('');
  const [showDateColorSettings, setShowDateColorSettings] = useState(false);
  // 日期欄位顯示用的顏色（從 localStorage 讀；供頭部文字著色用）
  const [weekendColor, setWeekendColor] = useState(() => {
    try { return localStorage.getItem('ledger_dp_weekend') || 'var(--pink)'; } catch { return 'var(--pink)'; }
  });
  const [selectedDateColor, setSelectedDateColor] = useState(() => {
    try { return localStorage.getItem('ledger_dp_selected') || 'var(--mint)'; } catch { return 'var(--mint)'; }
  });
  const updateWeekendColor = (c) => { setWeekendColor(c); try { localStorage.setItem('ledger_dp_weekend', c); } catch {} };
  const updateSelectedDateColor = (c) => { setSelectedDateColor(c); try { localStorage.setItem('ledger_dp_selected', c); } catch {} };
  const dateColorOptions = [
    { name: '薄荷綠', value: 'var(--mint)', preview: '#7ee0c0' },
    { name: '粉紅', value: 'var(--pink)', preview: '#f5b5c0' },
    { name: '紫', value: 'var(--accent)', preview: '#8f7ff0' },
    { name: '橘', value: '#f5a04a', preview: '#f5a04a' },
    { name: '黃', value: '#f5d84a', preview: '#f5d84a' },
    { name: '藍', value: '#6aa8f0', preview: '#6aa8f0' },
  ];

  const cats = state.categories[type] || [];

  // 編輯現有轉帳時,把 type 切為 transfer(只在初次 mount 時)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (editingTransfer && type !== 'transfer') {
      setType('transfer');
    }
    // eslint-disable-next-line react-hooks/exhaustive-deps
  }, []);

  const changeType = (newType) => {
    setType(newType);
    if (newType === 'transfer' || newType === 'lend') return; // 轉帳、代墊不需要 category
    const firstCat = state.categories[newType][0];
    setCategory(firstCat?.label || '');
    setSubCategory(firstCat?.subs?.[0] || '');
  };

  // handleSave for 轉帳
  const handleSaveTransfer = () => {
    const evalResult = /[+\-*/]/.test(amount) ? evalExpr(amount) : parseFloat(amount);
    const amt = (evalResult === null || isNaN(evalResult)) ? 0 : evalResult;
    if (!amt) { (alertCenter || toast)('尚未輸入金額'); return; }
    if (amt < 0) { (alertCenter || toast)('金額必須大於 0'); return; }
    if (amt === 0) { (alertCenter || toast)('金額不能為 0'); return; }
    if (/[+\-*/]/.test(amount)) setAmount(String(amt));
    if (!fromAccountId) { toast && toast('尚未選擇轉出帳戶'); return; }
    if (!toAccountId) { toast && toast('尚未選擇轉入帳戶'); return; }
    if (fromAccountId === toAccountId) { toast && toast('轉出與轉入帳戶不能相同'); return; }
    const feeAmt = parseFloat(fee) || 0;

    const doSave = () => {
      onSave({
        _transfer: {
          transferId: editing?.transferId,
          amount: amt,
          fee: feeAmt > 0 ? feeAmt : 0,
          feeCategory,
          feeSubCategory,
          fromId: fromAccountId,
          toId: toAccountId,
          date,
          note: note.trim(),
          createdAt: editing?.createdAt,
        },
      });
    };

    // 編輯轉帳時顯示完整變更總覽（所有欄位都列出）
    if (editing && setConfirmDialog) {
      const acctName = (id) => state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === id)?.name || '(未知)';
      const fmtNum = (n) => Number(n).toLocaleString('en-US');
      const oldAmt = editOut?.amount ?? 0;
      const oldFee = editFee?.amount ?? 0;
      const oldFrom = editOut?.accountId;
      const oldTo = editIn?.accountId;
      const oldDate = editOut?.date || editing.date;

      const fieldMap = {
        amount: (() => {
          const changed = oldAmt !== amt;
          const d = amt - oldAmt;
          return {
            icon: 'coin', label: '轉帳金額',
            from: fmtNum(oldAmt), to: fmtNum(amt),
            changed,
            diff: changed ? (d > 0 ? '+' : '') + fmtNum(d) : null,
          };
        })(),
        date: {
          icon: 'calendar', label: '日期',
          from: oldDate, to: date,
          changed: oldDate !== date,
        },
        fromAccount: {
          icon: 'bank', label: '轉出帳戶',
          from: acctName(oldFrom), to: acctName(fromAccountId),
          changed: oldFrom !== fromAccountId,
        },
        toAccount: {
          icon: 'bank', label: '轉入帳戶',
          from: acctName(oldTo), to: acctName(toAccountId),
          changed: oldTo !== toAccountId,
        },
        // 手續費跟著轉入帳戶一起顯示（原頁面佈局也是放在轉入帳戶後面）
        fee: (() => {
          const changed = oldFee !== feeAmt;
          const d = feeAmt - oldFee;
          return {
            icon: 'coin', label: '手續費',
            from: fmtNum(oldFee), to: fmtNum(feeAmt),
            changed,
            diff: changed ? (d > 0 ? '+' : '') + fmtNum(d) : null,
          };
        })(),
        note: (() => {
          const oldNote = (editOut?.note || '').trim();
          const newNote = note.trim();
          return {
            icon: 'note', label: '備註',
            from: oldNote || '(空白)',
            to: newNote || '(空白)',
            changed: oldNote !== newNote,
          };
        })(),
      };
      // 轉帳的排序寫死 DEFAULT_TRANSFER_ORDER(['amount', 'typeToggle', 'date', 'fromAccount', 'toAccount', 'note'])
      // 手續費插在 toAccount 後面
      const TRANSFER_CONFIRM_ORDER = ['amount', 'date', 'fromAccount', 'toAccount', 'fee', 'note'];
      const changes = TRANSFER_CONFIRM_ORDER
        .map((k) => fieldMap[k])
        .filter(Boolean);

      const anyChanged = changes.some((c) => c.changed);
      setConfirmDialog({
        title: anyChanged ? '確認變更內容' : '確認儲存',
        changes,
        confirmText: anyChanged ? '確定變更' : '確定',
        danger: true,
        onConfirm: doSave,
      });
      return;
    }

    doSave();
  };

  // handleSave for 代墊
  const handleSaveLend = () => {
    const evalResult = /[+\-*/]/.test(amount) ? evalExpr(amount) : parseFloat(amount);
    const amt = (evalResult === null || isNaN(evalResult)) ? 0 : evalResult;
    if (!amt) { (alertCenter || toast)('尚未輸入金額'); return; }
    if (amt < 0) { (alertCenter || toast)('金額必須大於 0'); return; }
    if (amt === 0) { (alertCenter || toast)('金額不能為 0'); return; }
    if (/[+\-*/]/.test(amount)) setAmount(String(amt));
    if (!fromAccountId) { toast && toast('尚未選擇付款帳戶'); return; }
    onSave({
      _lend: {
        lendId: editing?.lendId,
        amount: amt,
        fromId: fromAccountId,
        date,
        note: note.trim(),
        expectDate: expectDate || '',
        debtor: debtor.trim() || '',
        createdAt: editing?.createdAt,
      },
    });
  };

  const handleSave = () => {
    // 若 amount 還是表達式(含運算子),先求值
    const evalResult = /[+\-*/]/.test(amount) ? evalExpr(amount) : parseFloat(amount);
    const amt = (evalResult === null || isNaN(evalResult)) ? 0 : evalResult;
    if (!amt) {
      (alertCenter || toast)('尚未輸入金額');
      return;
    }
    if (amt < 0) {
      (alertCenter || toast)('金額必須大於 0');
      return;
    }
    if (amt === 0) {
      (alertCenter || toast)('金額不能為 0');
      return;
    }
    // 同步把運算結果寫回 amount(下次再用就不是表達式了)
    if (/[+\-*/]/.test(amount)) {
      setAmount(String(amt));
    }
    if (!accountId) {
      toast && toast('尚未選擇帳戶');
      return;
    }
    if (!category) {
      toast && toast('尚未選擇大分類');
      return;
    }

    const doSave = () => {
      onSave({
        id: editing?.id || uid(),
        type,
        amount: amt,
        date,
        note: note.trim(),
        category,
        subCategory: subCategory || '',
        accountId,
        createdAt: editing?.createdAt || Date.now(),
      });
    };

    // 編輯模式：跳出變更總覽確認（所有欄位都列出）
    if (editing && setConfirmDialog) {
      const acctName = (id) => state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === id)?.name || '(未知)';
      const fmtNum = (n) => Number(n).toLocaleString('en-US');

      // 每個欄位定義成字典，依頁面 blockOrder 動態組合
      const fieldMap = {
        amount: (() => {
          const changed = editing.amount !== amt;
          const diff = amt - editing.amount;
          return {
            icon: 'coin', label: '金額',
            from: fmtNum(editing.amount), to: fmtNum(amt),
            changed,
            diff: changed ? (diff > 0 ? '+' : '') + fmtNum(diff) : null,
          };
        })(),
        date: {
          icon: 'calendar', label: '日期',
          from: editing.date, to: date,
          changed: editing.date !== date,
        },
        account: {
          icon: 'bank', label: '收支帳戶',
          from: acctName(editing.accountId), to: acctName(accountId),
          changed: editing.accountId !== accountId,
        },
        category: {
          icon: 'bag', label: '大分類',
          from: editing.category || '(無)', to: category || '(無)',
          changed: (editing.category || '') !== (category || ''),
        },
        subCategory: {
          icon: 'list', label: '子分類',
          from: editing.subCategory || '(無)', to: subCategory || '(無)',
          changed: (editing.subCategory || '') !== (subCategory || ''),
        },
        note: {
          icon: 'note', label: '備註',
          from: (editing.note || '').trim() || '(空白)',
          to: note.trim() || '(空白)',
          changed: (editing.note || '').trim() !== note.trim(),
        },
      };
      // 依頁面排序產出,過濾掉 blockOrder 裡的 typeToggle 等非欄位
      const changes = effectiveOrder
        .map((k) => fieldMap[k])
        .filter(Boolean);

      const anyChanged = changes.some((c) => c.changed);
      setConfirmDialog({
        title: anyChanged ? '確認變更內容' : '確認儲存',
        changes,
        confirmText: anyChanged ? '確定變更' : '確定',
        danger: true,
        onConfirm: doSave,
      });
      return;
    }

    doSave();
  };

  const mainColor = type === 'income' ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--pink)';
  const onMainColor = type === 'income' ? 'var(--on-mint)' : 'var(--on-pink)';
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(onClose, { skipInPickerBackdrop: true });
  const catPickerSwipe = useSwipeBack(() => setShowCategorySheet(false));
  const subPickerSwipe = useSwipeBack(() => setShowSubCategorySheet(false));
  const accountPickerSwipe = useSwipeBack(() => setShowAccountSheet(false));
  const fromPickerSwipe = useSwipeBack(() => setShowFromSheet(false));
  const toPickerSwipe = useSwipeBack(() => setShowToSheet(false));
  const subInputSwipe = useSwipeBack(() => setShowSubInput(false));
  const dateColorSwipe = useSwipeBack(() => setShowDateColorSettings(false));
  // 手續費分類 picker:第二階時滑動返回到第一階,第一階滑動關閉
  const feeCatPickerSwipe = useSwipeBack(() => {
    if (feeCatStep === 2) {
      setFeeCatStep(1);
      setFeeCatStepCat(null);
    } else {
      setShowFeeCatPicker(false);
    }
  });

  // 日期選擇器覆蓋層
  if (showDatePicker) {
    return (
      <DatePicker
        value={date}
        onChange={setDate}
        onClose={() => setShowDatePicker(false)}
      />
    );
  }

  // 預計收回日期選擇器(代墊用)
  if (showExpectDateSheet) {
    return (
      <DatePicker
        value={expectDate || todayStr()}
        onChange={setExpectDate}
        onClose={() => setShowExpectDateSheet(false)}
      />
    );
  }

  return (
    <div
      data-sheet="true"
      style={{
        ...styles.sheet,
        transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
        transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
      }}
      ref={swipe.ref}
    >
      <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
        <div style={{ width: 80 }} />
        <div style={{ ...styles.sheetTitle, color: 'var(--text)' }}>
          {editing
            ? (isTransfer ? '編輯轉帳紀錄' : isLend ? '編輯代墊紀錄' : '編輯收支紀錄')
            : (isTransfer ? '新增轉帳' : isLend ? '新增代墊' : '新增收支紀錄')}
        </div>
        <div style={{ minWidth: 80, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'flex-end' }}>
          <EditOrderButton editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />
        </div>
      </div>

      <EditModeBanner editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />

      {/* 編輯模式下:統一的欄位鎖定切換(計算機開啟時隱藏避免遮金額) */}
      {editing && !showCalculator && (
        <div
          onClick={() => !editMode && setFieldsLocked((v) => !v)}
          style={{
            display: 'flex',
            alignItems: 'center',
            justifyContent: 'space-between',
            margin: '0 0 10px',
            padding: '10px 14px',
            background: fieldsLocked ? 'rgba(255,180,180,0.06)' : 'rgba(126,224,192,0.08)',
            border: `1px solid ${fieldsLocked ? 'rgba(255,180,180,0.22)' : 'rgba(126,224,192,0.3)'}`,
            borderRadius: 10,
            cursor: editMode ? 'default' : 'pointer',
            userSelect: 'none',
          }}
        >
          <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8, fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>
            <TypeIcon name={fieldsLocked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'} size={16} color={fieldsLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)'} />
            <span>{fieldsLocked ? '鎖定中' : '已解鎖'}</span>
            <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)', fontSize: 12 }}>
              · {fieldsLocked ? '點此解鎖後可編輯欄位' : '點此鎖定欄位'}
            </span>
          </span>
          <div
            style={{
              width: 36, height: 20, borderRadius: 10,
              background: fieldsLocked ? 'var(--border)' : 'var(--mint)',
              position: 'relative',
              transition: 'background 0.2s',
              flexShrink: 0,
            }}
          >
            <div
              style={{
                position: 'absolute',
                top: 2,
                left: fieldsLocked ? 2 : 18,
                width: 16, height: 16, borderRadius: '50%',
                background: '#fff',
                transition: 'left 0.2s',
              }}
            />
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      <div style={styles.sheetScroll} data-scroll-container>
      {/* 可排序區塊 */}
      {effectiveOrder.map((blockKey, idx) => {
        const blockProps = {
          key: blockKey,
          blockKey,
          editMode,
          isFirst: idx === 0,
          isLast: idx === effectiveOrder.length - 1,
          onMoveUp: () => moveBlock(blockKey, -1),
          onMoveDown: () => moveBlock(blockKey, 1),
        };

        if (blockKey === 'amount') {
          // 偵測 amount 是否為計算式(含運算子)
          const hasOperator = /[+\-*/]/.test(amount);
          // 格式化顯示
          const formatAmount = (raw) => {
            if (!raw || raw === '0') return '';
            if (hasOperator) {
              // 計算式:把運算子轉成顯示符號,數字部分加千分位
              return raw
                .split(/([+\-*/])/)
                .map((part) => {
                  if (/[+\-*/]/.test(part)) {
                    return ' ' + fmtExprDisplay(part) + ' ';
                  }
                  // 數字,加千分位(若有小數點則保留)
                  if (!part) return '';
                  const [intPart, decPart] = part.split('.');
                  const withComma = intPart ? Number(intPart).toLocaleString('en-US') : '';
                  return decPart !== undefined ? `${withComma}.${decPart}` : withComma;
                })
                .join('');
            }
            // 純數字
            const [intPart, decPart] = raw.split('.');
            const withComma = Number(intPart || 0).toLocaleString('en-US');
            return decPart !== undefined ? `${withComma}.${decPart}` : withComma;
          };
          const displayAmount = formatAmount(amount);
          // 字體自適應
          const amtLen = displayAmount.length || 1;
          const dynFontSize = amtLen <= 6 ? 48
            : amtLen <= 8 ? 40
            : amtLen <= 10 ? 32
            : amtLen <= 12 ? 26
            : amtLen <= 16 ? 22
            : 18;
          // 編輯時統一使用 fieldsLocked;若任一端是已刪虛擬,金額永久鎖
          const isLocked = (!!editing && fieldsLocked) || transferDeletedVirtual;
          return (
            <Block {...blockProps} title="金額">
              <div
                style={{
                  ...styles.amountBoxCompact,
                  position: 'relative',
                  cursor: isLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
                  opacity: isLocked ? 0.55 : 1,
                }}
                onTouchEnd={(e) => {
                  if (isLocked) return;
                  e.preventDefault();
                  setShowCalculator(true);
                }}
                onClick={() => {
                  if (isLocked) return;
                  setShowCalculator(true);
                }}
              >
                <div
                  style={{
                    color: amount && amount !== '0' ? mainColor : 'var(--text-faint)',
                    background: 'transparent',
                    width: '100%',
                    height: '100%',
                    display: 'flex',
                    alignItems: 'center',
                    justifyContent: 'center',
                    fontSize: dynFontSize,
                    fontWeight: 700,
                    fontFamily: "'Space Grotesk', sans-serif",
                    letterSpacing: '-0.5px',
                    transition: 'font-size 0.15s',
                    padding: '0 12px',
                    textAlign: 'center',
                    wordBreak: 'break-all',
                    // 計算機開啟且尚未輸入金額時 → 慢速脈動提示
                    animation: showCalculator && (!amount || amount === '0')
                      ? 'amountPulse 1.4s ease-in-out infinite'
                      : 'none',
                  }}
                >
                  {displayAmount || '0'}
                </div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'typeToggle' && !editing) {
          // 「其他」分組:轉帳、代墊、(股票結算待開放)
          const otherTypes = ['transfer'];
          const isOther = otherTypes.includes(type);
          const otherLabel = type === 'transfer' ? '轉帳' : '其他';
          return (
            <Block {...blockProps} title="類型" inline>
              <div style={styles.typeToggle}>
                {/* 支出 */}
                <button
                  onClick={() => { if (!editMode) changeType('expense'); }}
                  style={{
                    ...styles.typeBtn,
                    ...(type === 'expense' ? { background: 'var(--pink)', color: 'var(--on-pink)' } : {}),
                  }}
                >支出</button>
                {/* 收入 */}
                <button
                  onClick={() => { if (!editMode) changeType('income'); }}
                  style={{
                    ...styles.typeBtn,
                    ...(type === 'income' ? { background: 'var(--mint)', color: 'var(--on-mint)' } : {}),
                  }}
                >收入</button>
                {/* 其他(轉帳/代墊/股票)— 點開 sheet 選 */}
                <button
                  onClick={() => { if (!editMode) setShowOtherTypeSheet(true); }}
                  style={{
                    ...styles.typeBtn,
                    ...(isOther ? { background: 'var(--accent)', color: 'var(--on-accent)' } : {}),
                    display: 'inline-flex',
                    alignItems: 'center',
                    justifyContent: 'center',
                    gap: 4,
                  }}
                >
                  {isOther ? otherLabel : '其他'}
                  <span style={{ fontSize: 10, opacity: 0.8 }}>▾</span>
                </button>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'category') {
          const currentCat = cats.find((c) => c.label === category);
          const catLocked = !!editing && fieldsLocked;
          return (
            <Block
              {...blockProps}
              title="大分類"
              inline
              headerRight={<span style={{ ...styles.gearBtn, opacity: catLocked ? 0.3 : 1 }} onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); !editMode && !catLocked && onManageCategory(type); }}>⚙️</span>}
            >
              <div
                style={{ ...styles.selectFieldCompact, opacity: catLocked ? 0.55 : 1, cursor: catLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer' }}
                onClick={() => !editMode && !catLocked && setShowCategorySheet(true)}
              >
                {currentCat ? (
                  <>
                    <div style={{ ...styles.selectFieldIconSm, background: type === 'income' ? 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.15)' : 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.15)' }}>
                      <TypeIcon name={currentCat.icon} size={16} color={mainColor} />
                    </div>
                    <div style={styles.selectFieldLabelCompact}>{currentCat.label}</div>
                  </>
                ) : (
                  <div style={styles.selectFieldPlaceholder}>選擇大分類</div>
                )}
                <div style={styles.selectFieldArrow}>›</div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'subCategory') {
          const currentCat = cats.find((c) => c.label === category);
          const subLocked = !!editing && fieldsLocked;
          return (
            <Block
              {...blockProps}
              title="子分類"
              inline
              headerRight={
                <span
                  style={{ ...styles.gearBtn, opacity: currentCat && !subLocked ? 1 : 0.3 }}
                  onClick={(e) => {
                    e.stopPropagation();
                    if (!editMode && currentCat && !subLocked) onManageCategory(type, category);
                  }}
                >⚙️</span>
              }
            >
              <div
                style={{ ...styles.selectFieldCompact, opacity: subLocked ? 0.55 : 1, cursor: subLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer' }}
                onClick={() => !editMode && !subLocked && setShowSubCategorySheet(true)}
              >
                {subCategory ? (
                  <>
                    <div style={{ ...styles.selectFieldIconSm, background: type === 'income' ? 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.15)' : 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.15)' }}>
                      <TypeIcon name={currentCat?.icon || 'note'} size={16} color={mainColor} />
                    </div>
                    <div style={styles.selectFieldLabelCompact}>{subCategory}</div>
                  </>
                ) : (
                  <div style={styles.selectFieldPlaceholder}>選擇子分類（選填）</div>
                )}
                <div style={styles.selectFieldArrow}>›</div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'note') {
          const noteLocked = !!editing && fieldsLocked;
          // 套用偏好(僅當 applyToInput=true 時)
          const inputBg = (notePref.applyToInput && notePref.bgColor) ? notePref.bgColor : 'var(--bg-card)';
          const inputColor = (notePref.applyToInput && notePref.textColor) ? notePref.textColor : (noteColor || 'var(--text)');
          return (
            <Block
              {...blockProps}
              title="備註"
              inline
              headerRight={<span style={{ ...styles.gearBtn, opacity: (noteLocked || editMode) ? 0.3 : 1 }} onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); if (!editMode && !noteLocked) setShowNotePref(true); }}>⚙️</span>}
            >
              <div style={{ position: 'relative', width: '100%' }}>
                <textarea
                  value={note}
                  onChange={(e) => setNote(e.target.value)}
                  onInput={(e) => {
                    e.target.style.height = 'auto';
                    e.target.style.height = Math.min(e.target.scrollHeight, 160) + 'px';
                  }}
                  ref={(el) => {
                    if (el && note) {
                      el.style.height = 'auto';
                      el.style.height = Math.min(el.scrollHeight, 160) + 'px';
                    }
                  }}
                  placeholder="選填（ 上限 100 字 ）"
                  disabled={noteLocked}
                  maxLength={100}
                  rows={1}
                  style={{
                    ...styles.selectFieldCompact,
                    border: 'none',
                    outline: 'none',
                    background: inputBg,
                    color: inputColor,
                    fontSize: 14,
                    width: '100%',
                    opacity: noteLocked ? 0.55 : 1,
                    cursor: noteLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'text',
                    resize: 'none',
                    height: 44,
                    minHeight: 44,
                    maxHeight: 160,
                    fontFamily: 'inherit',
                    lineHeight: '22px',
                    padding: '11px 12px',
                    boxSizing: 'border-box',
                    overflow: 'hidden',
                    display: 'block',
                  }}
                />
                {note.length > 0 && !noteLocked && (
                  <div style={{
                    position: 'absolute',
                    bottom: 4,
                    right: 10,
                    fontSize: 10,
                    color: note.length >= 90 ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--text-faint)',
                    pointerEvents: 'none',
                    fontVariantNumeric: 'tabular-nums',
                    fontWeight: note.length >= 90 ? 600 : 400,
                  }}>
                    {note.length} / 100
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'account') {
          const currentAcct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === accountId);
          const currentTypeMeta = currentAcct ? state.accountTypes.find((t) => t.value === currentAcct.type) : null;
          const acctLocked = !!editing && fieldsLocked;
          return (
            <Block
              {...blockProps}
              title="收支帳戶"
              inline
              headerRight={<span style={{ ...styles.gearBtn, opacity: acctLocked ? 0.3 : 1 }} onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); !editMode && !acctLocked && onManageAccount(); }}>⚙️</span>}
            >
              {state.accounts.length === 0 ? (
                <div style={styles.emptyAccountHint} onClick={() => !editMode && !acctLocked && onManageAccount()}>
                  尚未建立帳戶，點這裡或 ⚙️ 新增
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div
                  style={{ ...styles.selectFieldCompact, opacity: acctLocked ? 0.55 : 1, cursor: acctLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer' }}
                  onClick={() => !editMode && !acctLocked && setShowAccountSheet(true)}
                >
                  {currentAcct ? (
                    <>
                      <div style={{ ...styles.selectFieldIconSm, background: currentTypeMeta?.color || '#f5c29c' }}>
                        <TypeIcon name={currentTypeMeta?.icon || 'box'} size={16} color="#fff" />
                      </div>
                      <div style={styles.selectFieldLabelCompact}>
                        {currentAcct.name}
                      </div>
                      <span style={styles.selectFieldSubInline}>
                        {(() => { const b = calcBalance(currentAcct, state.transactions); return b.toLocaleString(); })()}
                      </span>
                    </>
                  ) : (
                    <div style={styles.selectFieldPlaceholder}>選擇帳戶</div>
                  )}
                  <div style={styles.selectFieldArrow}>›</div>
                </div>
              )}
            </Block>
          );
        }

        // 轉帳:轉出帳戶 / 代墊:付款帳戶
        if (blockKey === 'fromAccount') {
          const currentAcct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === fromAccountId);
          const currentTypeMeta = currentAcct ? state.accountTypes.find((t) => t.value === currentAcct.type) : null;
          // 轉出帳戶端是已刪虛擬:從 editOut(out 紀錄)查 _deletedAccountName
          // 永久鎖定該欄位,不被全域解鎖按鈕影響
          const isDeletedFrom = editingTransfer && editOut?._deletedAccountName;
          const deletedFromName = isDeletedFrom ? editOut._deletedAccountName : '';
          // 齒輪只受全域鎖影響(去帳戶管理頁面),不受 isDeletedFrom 影響
          const gearLocked = !!editing && fieldsLocked;
          // fromLocked:全域鎖、自己端已刪虛擬、或對方端已刪虛擬(都要鎖,避免改帳戶後對方無法配對)
          const fromLocked = gearLocked || isDeletedFrom || transferDeletedVirtual;
          const blockTitle = isLend ? '付款帳戶' : '轉出帳戶';
          const placeholder = isLend ? '選擇付款帳戶' : '選擇轉出帳戶';
          return (
            <Block
              {...blockProps}
              title={blockTitle}
              inline
              headerRight={<span style={{ ...styles.gearBtn, opacity: gearLocked ? 0.3 : 1 }} onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); !editMode && !gearLocked && onManageAccount(); }}>⚙️</span>}
            >
              {state.accounts.length === 0 ? (
                <div style={styles.emptyAccountHint} onClick={() => !editMode && !fromLocked && onManageAccount()}>
                  尚未建立帳戶，點這裡或 ⚙️ 新增
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div
                  style={{ ...styles.selectFieldCompact, opacity: fromLocked ? 0.55 : 1, cursor: fromLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer' }}
                  onClick={() => !editMode && !fromLocked && setShowFromSheet(true)}
                >
                  {isDeletedFrom ? (
                    <>
                      <div style={{ ...styles.selectFieldIconSm, background: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>
                        <TypeIcon name="box" size={16} color="#fff" />
                      </div>
                      <div style={styles.selectFieldLabelCompact}>{deletedFromName}</div>
                      <span style={{
                        color: 'var(--text-faint)',
                        fontSize: 10,
                        fontWeight: 500,
                        marginLeft: 6,
                        padding: '1px 6px',
                        borderRadius: 4,
                        background: 'rgba(140, 140, 140, 0.12)',
                      }}>{'帳號已刪'}</span>
                    </>
                  ) : currentAcct ? (
                    <>
                      <div style={{ ...styles.selectFieldIconSm, background: currentTypeMeta?.color || '#f5c29c' }}>
                        <TypeIcon name={currentTypeMeta?.icon || 'box'} size={16} color="#fff" />
                      </div>
                      <div style={styles.selectFieldLabelCompact}>{currentAcct.name}</div>
                      <span style={styles.selectFieldSubInline}>
                        {(() => { const b = calcBalance(currentAcct, state.transactions); return b.toLocaleString(); })()}
                      </span>
                    </>
                  ) : (
                    <div style={styles.selectFieldPlaceholder}>{placeholder}</div>
                  )}
                  <div style={styles.selectFieldArrow}>›</div>
                </div>
              )}
            </Block>
          );
        }

        // 轉帳:轉入帳戶 + 手續費用(合併)
        if (blockKey === 'toAccount') {
          const currentAcct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === toAccountId);
          const currentTypeMeta = currentAcct ? state.accountTypes.find((t) => t.value === currentAcct.type) : null;
          const sameAcct = fromAccountId && toAccountId && fromAccountId === toAccountId;
          // 轉入帳戶端是已刪虛擬:從 editIn(in 紀錄)查 _deletedAccountName
          const isDeletedTo = editingTransfer && editIn?._deletedAccountName;
          const deletedToName = isDeletedTo ? editIn._deletedAccountName : '';
          // 齒輪只受全域鎖影響,不受 isDeletedTo 影響
          const toGearLocked = !!editing && fieldsLocked;
          const toLocked = toGearLocked || isDeletedTo || transferDeletedVirtual;
          const feeGearLocked = !!editing && fieldsLocked;
          const feeLockedNow = (!!editing && fieldsLocked) || transferDeletedVirtual;
          return (
            <>
              {/* 轉入帳戶:inline 排版(跟轉出帳戶一致) */}
              <Block
                {...blockProps}
                title="轉入帳戶"
                inline
                headerRight={<span style={{ ...styles.gearBtn, opacity: toGearLocked ? 0.3 : 1 }} onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); !editMode && !toGearLocked && onManageAccount(); }}>⚙️</span>}
              >
                {state.accounts.length === 0 ? (
                  <div style={styles.emptyAccountHint} onClick={() => !editMode && !toLocked && onManageAccount()}>
                    尚未建立帳戶，點這裡或 ⚙️ 新增
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <div
                    style={{ ...styles.selectFieldCompact, opacity: toLocked ? 0.55 : 1, cursor: toLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer', ...(sameAcct ? { borderColor: 'var(--pink)' } : {}) }}
                    onClick={() => !editMode && !toLocked && setShowToSheet(true)}
                  >
                    {isDeletedTo ? (
                      <>
                        <div style={{ ...styles.selectFieldIconSm, background: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>
                          <TypeIcon name="box" size={16} color="#fff" />
                        </div>
                        <div style={styles.selectFieldLabelCompact}>{deletedToName}</div>
                        <span style={{
                          color: 'var(--text-faint)',
                          fontSize: 10,
                          fontWeight: 500,
                          marginLeft: 6,
                          padding: '1px 6px',
                          borderRadius: 4,
                          background: 'rgba(140, 140, 140, 0.12)',
                        }}>{'帳號已刪'}</span>
                      </>
                    ) : currentAcct ? (
                      <>
                        <div style={{ ...styles.selectFieldIconSm, background: currentTypeMeta?.color || '#f5c29c' }}>
                          <TypeIcon name={currentTypeMeta?.icon || 'box'} size={16} color="#fff" />
                        </div>
                        <div style={styles.selectFieldLabelCompact}>{currentAcct.name}</div>
                        <span style={styles.selectFieldSubInline}>
                          {(() => { const b = calcBalance(currentAcct, state.transactions); return b.toLocaleString(); })()}
                        </span>
                      </>
                    ) : (
                      <div style={styles.selectFieldPlaceholder}>選擇轉入帳戶</div>
                    )}
                    <div style={styles.selectFieldArrow}>›</div>
                  </div>
                )}
              </Block>
              {sameAcct && (
                <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--pink-text)', marginTop: -4, marginBottom: 6, padding: '0 14px' }}>
