                  轉出與轉入帳戶不能相同
                </div>
              )}

              {/* 手續費用:inline 排版(跟轉入帳戶一致),齒輪=改分類 */}
              {state.accounts.length > 0 && (() => {
                // 找出手續費分類的圖示(用 catIcon 查 expense/手續費分類)
                const feeCatData = (state.categories.expense || []).find((c) => c.label === feeCategory);
                return (
                  <Block
                    blockKey="fee"
                    editMode={editMode}
                    title="手續費用"
                    inline
                    headerRight={<span style={{ ...styles.gearBtn, opacity: feeGearLocked ? 0.3 : 1 }} onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); !editMode && !feeGearLocked && openFeeCatPicker(); }}>⚙️</span>}
                  >
                    <div style={{ ...styles.selectFieldCompact, opacity: feeLockedNow ? 0.55 : 1 }}>
                      {/* 左側:分類圖示 + 子分類名稱(點擊開齒輪) */}
                      <div
                        style={{ ...styles.selectFieldIconSm, background: 'var(--accent)', cursor: feeLockedNow ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer' }}
                        onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); !editMode && !feeLockedNow && openFeeCatPicker(); }}
                      >
                        <TypeIcon name="coin" size={16} color="#fff" />
                      </div>
                      <div
                        style={{ ...styles.selectFieldLabelCompact, cursor: feeLockedNow ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer', flex: 'none', maxWidth: '55%', overflow: 'hidden', textOverflow: 'ellipsis', whiteSpace: 'nowrap' }}
                        onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); !editMode && !feeLockedNow && openFeeCatPicker(); }}
                      >
                        {feeSubCategory || feeCategory}
                      </div>
                      {/* 右側:金額輸入 */}
                      <input
                        type="text"
                        inputMode="decimal"
                        readOnly={feeLockedNow}
                        style={{
                          flex: 1,
                          background: 'transparent',
                          border: 'none',
                          outline: 'none',
                          color: 'var(--text)',
                          fontSize: 15,
                          textAlign: 'right',
                          padding: 0,
                          margin: 0,
                          fontFamily: "'Space Grotesk', sans-serif",
                          minWidth: 0,
                          height: '100%',
                          boxSizing: 'border-box',
                          cursor: feeLockedNow ? 'not-allowed' : 'text',
                        }}
                        value={fee}
                        onChange={(e) => {
                          if (feeLockedNow) return;
                          const v = e.target.value;
                          if (v === '' || /^\d*\.?\d*$/.test(v)) setFee(v);
                        }}
                        onFocus={(e) => { if (feeLockedNow) { e.target.blur(); return; } if (fee === '0') setFee(''); e.target.select(); }}
                        onClick={(e) => { if (!feeLockedNow) e.target.select(); }}
                        onBlur={() => { if (fee === '') setFee('0'); }}
                        placeholder="0"
                        disabled={editMode}
                      />
                    </div>
                  </Block>
                );
              })()}
            </>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'date') {
          const [y, m, d] = date.split('-');
          const dObj = new Date(`${date}T00:00:00`);
          const wd = ['日', '一', '二', '三', '四', '五', '六'][dObj.getDay()];
          const dayOfWeek = dObj.getDay();
          const isWeekend = dayOfWeek === 0 || dayOfWeek === 6;
          const dateLabel = `${y}/${String(m).padStart(2, '0')}/${String(d).padStart(2, '0')}`;
          const dateLocked = !!editing && fieldsLocked;
          return (
            <Block
              {...blockProps}
              title="日期"
              inline
              headerRight={
                <span
                  style={{ ...styles.gearBtn, opacity: dateLocked ? 0.3 : 1 }}
                  onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); !editMode && !dateLocked && setShowDateColorSettings(true); }}
                >⚙️</span>
              }
            >
              <div
                style={{ ...styles.selectFieldCompact, opacity: dateLocked ? 0.55 : 1, cursor: dateLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer' }}
                onClick={() => !editMode && !dateLocked && setShowDatePicker(true)}
              >
                <div style={styles.selectFieldLabelCompact}>
                  {dateLabel}
                  <span style={{ color: isWeekend ? weekendColor : 'var(--text-dim)', marginLeft: 6, fontSize: 13 }}>
                    ({wd})
                  </span>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.selectFieldArrow}>›</div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'expectDate') {
          // 代墊專用:預計收回日期
          const dateLabel = expectDate ? expectDate.replace(/-/g, '/') : '';
          const wd = expectDate ? ['日','一','二','三','四','五','六'][new Date(expectDate).getDay()] : '';
          return (
            <Block {...blockProps} title="預計收回" inline>
              <div
                style={{ ...styles.selectFieldCompact, cursor: 'pointer' }}
                onClick={() => !editMode && setShowExpectDateSheet(true)}
              >
                <div style={styles.selectFieldLabelCompact}>
                  {expectDate ? (
                    <>
                      {dateLabel}
                      <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginLeft: 6, fontSize: 13 }}>({wd})</span>
                    </>
                  ) : (
                    <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>選填</span>
                  )}
                </div>
                {expectDate && (
                  <button
                    onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); setExpectDate(''); }}
                    style={{
                      background: 'transparent', border: 'none', color: 'var(--text-faint)',
                      fontSize: 18, cursor: 'pointer', marginRight: 4, padding: '0 4px',
                    }}
                  >×</button>
                )}
                <div style={styles.selectFieldArrow}>›</div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'note') {
          return null;
        }

        return null;
      })}

      {/* 編輯轉帳時:儲存前必須勾選的關聯紀錄提醒 */}
      {editing && isTransfer && editingTransfer && (
        <div
          onClick={() => !editMode && setTransferAcked((v) => !v)}
          style={{
            margin: '12px 0 0',
            padding: '12px 14px',
            background: transferAcked ? 'rgba(126,224,192,0.08)' : 'rgba(143,127,240,0.08)',
            border: `1px solid ${transferAcked ? 'rgba(126,224,192,0.35)' : 'rgba(143,127,240,0.30)'}`,
            borderRadius: 10,
            cursor: editMode ? 'default' : 'pointer',
            userSelect: 'none',
            display: 'flex',
            alignItems: 'flex-start',
            gap: 10,
            transition: 'background 0.2s, border-color 0.2s',
          }}
        >
          {/* checkbox */}
          <div style={{
            width: 20, height: 20, borderRadius: 5,
            border: `2px solid ${transferAcked ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--accent-text)'}`,
            background: transferAcked ? 'var(--mint)' : 'transparent',
            display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
            flexShrink: 0,
            marginTop: 1,
            transition: 'all 0.18s',
          }}>
            {transferAcked && (
              <svg width="13" height="13" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--on-mint)" strokeWidth="3.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
                <polyline points="5 12 10 17 19 8" />
              </svg>
            )}
          </div>
          {/* 文字 */}
          <div style={{ flex: 1, fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text)', lineHeight: 1.55 }}>
            <div style={{ fontWeight: 600, marginBottom: 3 }}>
              這是一組轉帳(共 {transferGroup ? transferGroup.length : 2} 筆關聯轉帳紀錄)
            </div>
            <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>
              我已了解 <span style={{ color: 'var(--mint-text)', fontWeight: 600 }}>修改後儲存</span>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>/</span>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--pink-text)', fontWeight: 600 }}>選擇刪除</span> 後,會同步 <span style={{ color: 'var(--mint-text)', fontWeight: 600 }}>更新</span>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>/</span>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--pink-text)', fontWeight: 600 }}>刪除</span> 所有關聯紀錄
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 儲存按鈕(固定在最下面,不參與排序) */}
      <button
        style={{
          ...styles.saveBtn,
          background: isTransfer ? 'var(--accent)' : mainColor,
          color: isTransfer ? 'var(--on-accent)' : (onMainColor || '#1a1a1a'),
          marginTop: 10,
          opacity: (editing && isTransfer && editingTransfer && !transferAcked) ? 0.4 : 1,
          cursor: (editing && isTransfer && editingTransfer && !transferAcked) ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
        }}
        onClick={() => {
          if (editMode) return;
          // 編輯轉帳時必須先勾選確認
          if (editing && isTransfer && editingTransfer && !transferAcked) {
            (alertCenter || toast)('請先勾選確認後再儲存');
            return;
          }
          isTransfer ? handleSaveTransfer() : isLend ? handleSaveLend() : handleSave();
        }}
      >
        儲存
      </button>

      {editing && (
        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8, marginTop: 6 }}>
          <button
            style={{
              ...styles.deleteBtn,
              flex: 1,
              marginTop: 0,
              opacity: (isTransfer && editingTransfer && !transferAcked) ? 0.4 : 1,
              cursor: (isTransfer && editingTransfer && !transferAcked) ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
            }}
            onClick={() => {
              if (editMode) return;
              if (isTransfer && editingTransfer && !transferAcked) {
                (alertCenter || toast)('請先勾選確認後再刪除');
                return;
              }
              onDelete(editing.id);
            }}
          >刪除</button>
          <button
            style={{
              flex: 1,
              padding: '12px',
              background: 'var(--bg-card)',
              border: '1px solid var(--text-dim)',
              borderRadius: 10,
              color: 'var(--text)',
              fontSize: 15,
              fontWeight: 500,
              cursor: 'pointer',
            }}
            onClick={onClose}
          >取消</button>
        </div>
      )}
      </div>

      {/* 計算機鍵盤(點金額時跳出) */}
      {showCalculator && (
        <CalculatorSheet
          expr={amount === '0' ? '' : amount}
          onChange={(v) => setAmount(v === '' ? '0' : v)}
          mainColor={mainColor}
          onMainColor={onMainColor}
          onClose={() => setShowCalculator(false)}
        />
      )}

      {/* 備註樣式設定 sheet */}
      {showNotePref && (
        <NotePrefSheet
          pref={notePref}
          onClose={() => setShowNotePref(false)}
          setConfirmDialog={setConfirmDialog}
          toastRich={toastRich}
        />
      )}

      {/* 其他類型選擇 sheet(轉帳 / 代墊 / 股票) */}
      {showOtherTypeSheet && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowOtherTypeSheet(false)}>
          <div
            style={{ ...styles.pickerCard, maxWidth: 320 }}
            onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
          >
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>選擇類型</div>
            <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 8, padding: '8px 12px 16px' }}>
              {/* 轉帳 */}
              <button
                style={{
                  display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 14,
                  padding: '14px 16px', borderRadius: 12,
                  background: type === 'transfer' ? 'var(--accent-bg, rgba(143,127,240,0.12))' : 'var(--bg-card-2, rgba(127,127,127,0.06))',
                  border: type === 'transfer' ? '1.5px solid var(--accent)' : '1.5px solid transparent',
                  color: 'var(--text)', cursor: 'pointer', textAlign: 'left',
                }}
                onClick={() => { changeType('transfer'); setShowOtherTypeSheet(false); }}
              >
                <div style={{
                  width: 36, height: 36, borderRadius: 10, background: 'var(--accent)',
                  display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', flexShrink: 0,
                }}>
                  <TypeIcon name="bolt" size={20} color="var(--on-accent)" />
                </div>
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 600 }}>轉帳</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginTop: 2 }}>
                    在帳戶之間搬移資金
                  </div>
                </div>
              </button>

              {/* 股票結算 — 點下去開「選擇投資帳戶」流程 */}
              <button
                onClick={() => {
                  if (onOpenStockEntry) onOpenStockEntry();
                }}
                style={{
                  display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 14,
                  padding: '14px 16px', borderRadius: 12,
                  background: 'var(--bg-card-2, rgba(127,127,127,0.04))',
                  border: '1.5px solid transparent',
                  color: 'var(--text)', cursor: 'pointer', textAlign: 'left',
                }}
              >
                <div style={{
                  width: 36, height: 36, borderRadius: 10,
                  background: '#9ae0d4', // invest 類型色
                  display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', flexShrink: 0,
                }}>
                  <TypeIcon name="chart" size={20} color="#fff" />
                </div>
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 600 }}>股票結算</div>
                  <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginTop: 2 }}>
                    買進、賣出、估市值
                  </div>
                </div>
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 分類選單 */}
      {showCategorySheet && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowCategorySheet(false)}>
          <div
            style={{
              ...styles.pickerCard,
              transform: `translateX(${catPickerSwipe.dragX}px)`,
              transition: catPickerSwipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.2s' : 'none',
            }}
            ref={catPickerSwipe.ref}
            onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
          >
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--text)' }}>請選擇 </span>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--blue)' }}>大分類</span>
            </div>
            {/* 新增大分類:跟子分類 picker 工具列風格一致(灰底 + 綠色 + ＋ 圖示) */}
            <div
              style={{
                background: 'var(--bg)',
                borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border)',
              }}
            >
              <div
                style={{
                  padding: '11px 12px',
                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  gap: 6,
                  fontSize: 13,
                  fontWeight: 600,
                  color: 'var(--mint-text)',
                  cursor: 'pointer',
                  WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
                }}
                onClick={() => {
                  setShowCategorySheet(false);
                  onManageCategory(type, '__new__');
                }}
              >
                <span style={{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 400, lineHeight: 1 }}>＋</span>
                <span>新增大分類</span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={styles.pickerList}>
              {cats.map((c) => (
                <div className="picker-item"
                  key={c.label}
                  style={{
                    ...styles.pickerItem,
                    ...(category === c.label ? { background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.08)' } : {}),
                  }}
                  onClick={() => {
                    setCategory(c.label);
                    setSubCategory(c.subs?.[0] || '');
                    setShowCategorySheet(false);
                    // 選完大分類後一律彈子分類選單（空白也要彈，讓使用者可新增）
                    setTimeout(() => setShowSubCategorySheet(true), 150);
                  }}
                >
                  <div style={{ ...styles.pickerItemIcon, background: type === 'income' ? 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.15)' : 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.15)' }}>
                    <TypeIcon name={c.icon} size={16} color={mainColor} />
                  </div>
                  <div style={styles.pickerItemLabel}>{c.label}</div>
                  {category === c.label && <div style={{ color: mainColor, fontSize: 14 }}>✓</div>}
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 子分類選單 */}
      {showSubCategorySheet && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowSubCategorySheet(false)}>
          <div
            style={{
              ...styles.pickerCard,
              transform: `translateX(${subPickerSwipe.dragX}px)`,
              transition: subPickerSwipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.2s' : 'none',
            }}
            ref={subPickerSwipe.ref}
            onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
          >
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--text)' }}>請選擇 </span>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>{category || ''}</span>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--text)' }}> </span>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--blue)' }}>子分類</span>
            </div>
            {/* 頂部工具列:左「不使用」+ 右「新增」並排,跟下方真正的子分類列表視覺分開 */}
            <div
              style={{
                display: 'flex',
                alignItems: 'stretch',
                background: 'var(--bg)',
                borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border)',
              }}
            >
              {/* 左:不使用子分類 */}
              <div
                style={{
                  flex: 1,
                  padding: '11px 12px',
                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  gap: 6,
                  fontSize: 13,
                  fontWeight: 500,
                  color: !subCategory ? 'var(--mint-text)' : 'var(--text-faint)',
                  background: !subCategory ? 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.10)' : 'transparent',
                  cursor: 'pointer',
                  WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
                  transition: 'background 0.15s',
                }}
                onClick={() => {
                  setSubCategory('');
                  setShowSubCategorySheet(false);
                }}
              >
                <span style={{ fontSize: 14, opacity: 0.8 }}>⊘</span>
                <span>不使用子分類</span>
                {!subCategory && <span style={{ marginLeft: 2, fontSize: 13 }}>✓</span>}
              </div>
              {/* 中間細直線 */}
              <div style={{ width: 1, background: 'var(--border)' }} />
              {/* 右:新增子分類 */}
              <div
                style={{
                  flex: 1,
                  padding: '11px 12px',
                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  gap: 6,
                  fontSize: 13,
                  fontWeight: 600,
                  color: 'var(--mint-text)',
                  cursor: 'pointer',
                  WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
                }}
                onClick={() => {
                  setShowSubCategorySheet(false);
                  setSubInputValue('');
                  setTimeout(() => setShowSubInput(true), 100);
                }}
              >
                <span style={{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 400, lineHeight: 1 }}>＋</span>
                <span>新增子分類</span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={styles.pickerList}>
              {(() => {
                const cc = cats.find((c) => c.label === category);
                const subs = cc?.subs || [];
                if (subs.length === 0) {
                  return (
                    <div style={{ ...styles.pickerEmpty }}>
                      此分類暫無子分類，點上方「＋ 新增子分類」建立
                    </div>
                  );
                }
                return subs.map((s) => (
                  <div className="picker-item"
                    key={s}
                    style={{
                      ...styles.pickerItem,
                      ...(subCategory === s ? { background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.08)' } : {}),
                    }}
                    onClick={() => {
                      setSubCategory(s);
                      setShowSubCategorySheet(false);
                    }}
                  >
                    <div style={{ ...styles.pickerItemIcon, background: type === 'income' ? 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.15)' : 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.15)' }}>
                      <TypeIcon name={cc?.icon || 'note'} size={16} color={mainColor} />
                    </div>
                    <div style={styles.pickerItemLabel}>{s}</div>
                    {subCategory === s && <div style={{ color: mainColor, fontSize: 14 }}>✓</div>}
                  </div>
                ));
              })()}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 帳戶選單 */}
      {showAccountSheet && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowAccountSheet(false)}>
          <div
            style={{
              ...styles.pickerCard,
              transform: `translateX(${accountPickerSwipe.dragX}px)`,
              transition: accountPickerSwipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.2s' : 'none',
            }}
            ref={accountPickerSwipe.ref}
            onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
          >
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>請選擇帳戶</div>
            {/* 新增帳戶:跟其他 picker 工具列風格一致(灰底 + 綠色 + ＋ 圖示) */}
            <div
              style={{
                background: 'var(--bg)',
                borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border)',
              }}
            >
              <div
                style={{
                  padding: '11px 12px',
                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  gap: 6,
                  fontSize: 13,
                  fontWeight: 600,
                  color: 'var(--mint-text)',
                  cursor: 'pointer',
                  WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
                }}
                onClick={() => {
                  setShowAccountSheet(false);
                  onManageAccount('__new__');
                }}
              >
                <span style={{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 400, lineHeight: 1 }}>＋</span>
                <span>新增帳戶</span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={styles.pickerList}>
              {(() => {
                const regular = state.accounts.filter((a) => !a.virtual);
                const virtuals = state.accounts.filter((a) => a.virtual);
                const renderRow = (a) => {
                  const tm = state.accountTypes.find((t) => t.value === a.type) || { icon: 'box', color: '#f5c29c' };
                  const bal = calcBalance(a, state.transactions);
                  return (
                    <div className="picker-item"
                      key={a.id}
                      style={{
                        ...styles.pickerItem,
                        ...(accountId === a.id ? { background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.08)' } : {}),
                      }}
                      onClick={() => {
                        setAccountId(a.id);
                        setShowAccountSheet(false);
                      }}
                    >
                      <div style={{ ...styles.pickerItemIcon, background: tm.color || '#f5c29c' }}>
                        <TypeIcon name={tm.icon || 'box'} size={16} color="#fff" />
                      </div>
                      <div style={styles.pickerItemLabel}>
                        <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>
                          {a.name}
                          {a.virtual && (
                            <span style={{
                              color: 'var(--mint)',
                              fontSize: 10,
                              fontWeight: 500,
                              marginLeft: 6,
                              padding: '1px 5px',
                              borderRadius: 3,
                              background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.12)',
                            }}>虛擬</span>
                          )}
                        </span>
                        <span style={styles.pickerItemSub}>{bal.toLocaleString()}</span>
                      </div>
                      {accountId === a.id && <div style={{ color: mainColor, fontSize: 14 }}>✓</div>}
                    </div>
                  );
                };
                return (
                  <>
                    {regular.length > 0 && virtuals.length > 0 && (
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', padding: '6px 14px 4px', fontWeight: 500 }}>一般帳戶</div>
                    )}
                    {regular.map(renderRow)}
                    {virtuals.length > 0 && (
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', padding: '8px 14px 4px', fontWeight: 500, marginTop: regular.length > 0 ? 4 : 0 }}>
                        <span style={{ color: 'var(--mint)', fontWeight: 600 }}>虛擬帳戶</span>
                      </div>
                    )}
                    {virtuals.map(renderRow)}
                  </>
                );
              })()}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 轉出帳戶選擇器 */}
      {showFromSheet && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowFromSheet(false)}>
          <div
            style={{
              ...styles.pickerCard,
              transform: `translateX(${fromPickerSwipe.dragX}px)`,
              transition: fromPickerSwipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.2s' : 'none',
            }}
            ref={fromPickerSwipe.ref}
            onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
          >
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>請選擇轉出帳戶</div>
            <div style={styles.pickerList}>
              {(() => {
                const regular = state.accounts.filter((a) => !a.virtual);
                const virtuals = state.accounts.filter((a) => a.virtual);
                const renderRow = (a) => {
                  const tm = state.accountTypes.find((t) => t.value === a.type) || { icon: 'box', color: '#f5c29c' };
                  const bal = calcBalance(a, state.transactions);
                  return (
                    <div className="picker-item"
                      key={a.id}
                      style={{ ...styles.pickerItem, ...(fromAccountId === a.id ? { background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.08)' } : {}) }}
                      onClick={() => {
                        // 轉出有優先權:選任何帳戶都允許
                        setFromAccountId(a.id);
                        // 若新轉出 = 目前轉入,自動把轉入往下移一格(沒下一個就循環);排除系統帳戶
                        if (a.id === toAccountId) {
                          const realList = state.accounts.filter((x) => !x.isSystem);
                          const idx = realList.findIndex((x) => x.id === a.id);
                          if (idx >= 0 && realList.length > 1) {
                            const nextIdx = (idx + 1) % realList.length;
                            setToAccountId(realList[nextIdx].id);
                          }
                        }
                        setShowFromSheet(false);
                      }}
                    >
                      <div style={{ ...styles.pickerItemIcon, background: tm.color || '#f5c29c' }}>
                        <TypeIcon name={tm.icon || 'box'} size={16} color="#fff" />
                      </div>
                      <div style={styles.pickerItemLabel}>
                        <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>
                          {a.name}
                          {a.virtual && (
                            <span style={{
                              color: 'var(--mint)',
                              fontSize: 10,
                              fontWeight: 500,
                              marginLeft: 6,
                              padding: '1px 5px',
                              borderRadius: 3,
                              background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.12)',
                            }}>虛擬</span>
                          )}
                        </span>
                        <span style={styles.pickerItemSub}>{bal.toLocaleString()}</span>
                      </div>
                      {fromAccountId === a.id && <div style={{ color: 'var(--accent-text)', fontSize: 14 }}>✓</div>}
                    </div>
                  );
                };
                return (
                  <>
                    {regular.length > 0 && virtuals.length > 0 && (
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', padding: '6px 14px 4px', fontWeight: 500 }}>一般帳戶</div>
                    )}
                    {regular.map(renderRow)}
                    {virtuals.length > 0 && (
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', padding: '8px 14px 4px', fontWeight: 500, marginTop: regular.length > 0 ? 4 : 0 }}>
                        <span style={{ color: 'var(--mint)', fontWeight: 600 }}>虛擬帳戶</span>
                      </div>
                    )}
                    {virtuals.map(renderRow)}
                  </>
                );
              })()}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 轉入帳戶選擇器 */}
      {showToSheet && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowToSheet(false)}>
          <div
            style={{
              ...styles.pickerCard,
              transform: `translateX(${toPickerSwipe.dragX}px)`,
              transition: toPickerSwipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.2s' : 'none',
            }}
            ref={toPickerSwipe.ref}
            onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
          >
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>請選擇轉入帳戶</div>
            <div style={styles.pickerList}>
              {(() => {
                const regular = state.accounts.filter((a) => !a.virtual);
                const virtuals = state.accounts.filter((a) => a.virtual);
                const renderRow = (a) => {
                  const tm = state.accountTypes.find((t) => t.value === a.type) || { icon: 'box', color: '#f5c29c' };
                  const bal = calcBalance(a, state.transactions);
                  const isSameAsFrom = fromAccountId === a.id;
                  return (
                    <div className="picker-item"
                      key={a.id}
                      style={{
                        ...styles.pickerItem,
                        ...(toAccountId === a.id ? { background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.08)' } : {}),
                        ...(isSameAsFrom ? { opacity: 0.35, cursor: 'not-allowed', pointerEvents: 'none' } : {}),
                      }}
                      onClick={() => {
                        if (isSameAsFrom) return;
                        setToAccountId(a.id);
                        setShowToSheet(false);
                      }}
                    >
                      <div style={{ ...styles.pickerItemIcon, background: tm.color || '#f5c29c' }}>
                        <TypeIcon name={tm.icon || 'box'} size={16} color="#fff" />
                      </div>
                      <div style={styles.pickerItemLabel}>
                        <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', flexWrap: 'wrap' }}>
                          {a.name}
                          {a.virtual && (
                            <span style={{
                              color: 'var(--mint)',
                              fontSize: 10,
                              fontWeight: 500,
                              marginLeft: 6,
                              padding: '1px 5px',
                              borderRadius: 3,
                              background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.12)',
                            }}>虛擬</span>
                          )}
                        </span>
                        <span style={styles.pickerItemSub}>{bal.toLocaleString()}</span>
                        {isSameAsFrom && (
                          <span style={{ display: 'block', fontSize: 10, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 2 }}>
                            已是轉出帳戶
                          </span>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      {toAccountId === a.id && !isSameAsFrom && <div style={{ color: 'var(--accent-text)', fontSize: 14 }}>✓</div>}
                    </div>
                  );
                };
                return (
                  <>
                    {regular.length > 0 && virtuals.length > 0 && (
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', padding: '6px 14px 4px', fontWeight: 500 }}>一般帳戶</div>
                    )}
                    {regular.map(renderRow)}
                    {virtuals.length > 0 && (
                      <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', padding: '8px 14px 4px', fontWeight: 500, marginTop: regular.length > 0 ? 4 : 0 }}>
                        <span style={{ color: 'var(--mint)', fontWeight: 600 }}>虛擬帳戶</span>
                      </div>
                    )}
                    {virtuals.map(renderRow)}
                  </>
                );
              })()}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 手續費分類選擇器(兩階:大分類 → 子分類) */}
      {showFeeCatPicker && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowFeeCatPicker(false)}>
          <div
            style={{
              ...styles.pickerCard,
              transform: `translateX(${feeCatPickerSwipe.dragX}px)`,
              transition: feeCatPickerSwipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.2s' : 'none',
            }}
            ref={feeCatPickerSwipe.ref}
            onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
          >
            {/* 標題列:step 1 無返回 / step 2 有明顯返回按鈕 */}
            <div style={{ ...styles.pickerTitle, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8, padding: '12px 12px 12px 12px' }}>
              {feeCatStep === 2 ? (
                <button
                  style={{
                    background: 'var(--bg-card)',
                    border: '1px solid var(--border)',
                    borderRadius: 10,
                    color: 'var(--text)',
                    padding: '6px 12px 6px 8px',
                    fontSize: 14,
                    fontWeight: 500,
                    cursor: 'pointer',
                    display: 'flex',
                    alignItems: 'center',
                    gap: 2,
                  }}
                  onClick={() => { setFeeCatStep(1); setFeeCatStepCat(null); }}
                >
                  <span style={{ fontSize: 18, lineHeight: 1 }}>‹</span>
                  <span>返回</span>
                </button>
              ) : (
                <div style={{ width: 66 }} />
              )}
              <span style={{ flex: 1, textAlign: 'center', fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 600 }}>
                {feeCatStep === 1 ? (
                  <>選擇 <span style={{ color: '#f5d84a' }}>大分類</span></>
                ) : (
                  <>群組 <span style={{ color: '#f5d84a' }}>子分類</span></>
                )}
              </span>
              <div style={{ width: 66 }} />
            </div>

            {/* 目前選擇提示(青色底避免和選中項紫色混淆) */}
            <div style={{
              margin: '4px 16px 10px',
              padding: '10px 12px',
              background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.10)',
              border: '1px solid rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.35)',
              borderRadius: 10,
              fontSize: 13,
            }}>
              <div style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontSize: 11, marginBottom: 3 }}>目前選擇</div>
              <div style={{ color: 'var(--mint-text)', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: 14 }}>
                {feeCategory}{feeSubCategory ? ` > ${feeSubCategory}` : ''}
              </div>
            </div>

            {/* 內容列表 */}
            <div style={{ ...styles.pickerList, maxHeight: '55vh', padding: '0 8px 12px' }}>
              {feeCatStep === 1 ? (
                // 第一階:大分類列表
                (state.categories.expense || []).map((cat) => {
                  const isCurrent = feeCategory === cat.label;
                  const hasSubs = (cat.subs || []).length > 0;
                  return (
                    <div className="picker-item"
                      key={cat.label}
                      style={{
                        ...styles.pickerItem,
                        padding: '14px 14px',
                        marginBottom: 6,
                        borderRadius: 10,
                        ...(isCurrent ? { background: 'rgba(143, 127, 240, 0.12)', border: '1px solid rgba(143, 127, 240, 0.4)' } : { background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.02)' }),
                      }}
                      onClick={() => {
                        if (hasSubs) {
                          setFeeCatStepCat(cat.label);
                          setFeeCatStep(2);
                        } else {
                          updateFeeCat(cat.label, '');
                          setShowFeeCatPicker(false);
                        }
                      }}
                    >
                      <div style={{ ...styles.pickerItemLabel, fontSize: 15 }}>
                        {cat.label}
                      </div>
                      {isCurrent && <div style={{ color: 'var(--accent-text)', fontSize: 16, marginRight: 6 }}>✓</div>}
                      {hasSubs && (
                        <>
                          <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)', fontSize: 12, marginRight: 4 }}>
                            {cat.subs.length} 項
                          </span>
                          <div style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)', fontSize: 18 }}>›</div>
                        </>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  );
                })
              ) : (
                // 第二階:子分類列表
                (() => {
                  const catObj = (state.categories.expense || []).find((c) => c.label === feeCatStepCat);
                  if (!catObj) return null;
                  return (
                    <>
                      {/* (不指定子分類) */}
                      <div className="picker-item"
                        style={{
                          ...styles.pickerItem,
                          padding: '14px 14px',
                          marginBottom: 6,
                          borderRadius: 10,
                          ...(feeCategory === feeCatStepCat && !feeSubCategory ? { background: 'rgba(143, 127, 240, 0.12)', border: '1px solid rgba(143, 127, 240, 0.4)' } : { background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.02)' }),
                        }}
                        onClick={() => { updateFeeCat(feeCatStepCat, ''); setShowFeeCatPicker(false); }}
                      >
                        <div style={{ ...styles.pickerItemLabel, color: '#6aa8f0', fontSize: 15 }}>
                          (不指定子分類)
                        </div>
                        {feeCategory === feeCatStepCat && !feeSubCategory && <div style={{ color: 'var(--accent-text)', fontSize: 16 }}>✓</div>}
                      </div>
                      {(catObj.subs || []).map((sub) => {
                        const isCurrent = feeCategory === feeCatStepCat && feeSubCategory === sub;
                        return (
                          <div className="picker-item"
                            key={sub}
                            style={{
                              ...styles.pickerItem,
                              padding: '14px 14px',
                              marginBottom: 6,
                              borderRadius: 10,
                              ...(isCurrent ? { background: 'rgba(143, 127, 240, 0.12)', border: '1px solid rgba(143, 127, 240, 0.4)' } : { background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.02)' }),
                            }}
                            onClick={() => { updateFeeCat(feeCatStepCat, sub); setShowFeeCatPicker(false); }}
                          >
                            <div style={{ ...styles.pickerItemLabel, fontSize: 15 }}>{sub}</div>
                            {isCurrent && <div style={{ color: 'var(--accent-text)', fontSize: 16 }}>✓</div>}
                          </div>
                        );
                      })}
                    </>
                  );
                })()
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 子分類輸入彈窗 */}
      {showSubInput && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowSubInput(false)}>
          <div
            style={{
              ...styles.pickerCard,
              transform: `translateX(${subInputSwipe.dragX}px)`,
              transition: subInputSwipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.2s' : 'none',
            }}
            ref={subInputSwipe.ref}
            onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
          >
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>新增子分類到「{category}」</div>
            <div style={{ padding: '14px 16px' }}>
              <input
                type="text"
                style={styles.field}
                value={subInputValue}
                onChange={(e) => setSubInputValue(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="請輸入子分類名稱"
                autoFocus
                maxLength={20}
              />
            </div>
            <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8, padding: '0 16px 16px' }}>
              <button
                style={{ ...styles.deleteBtn, flex: 1, marginTop: 0 }}
                onClick={() => setShowSubInput(false)}
              >取消</button>
              <button
                style={{ ...styles.saveBtn, flex: 1, background: 'var(--mint)', color: 'var(--on-mint)', marginTop: 0 }}
                onClick={() => {
                  const val = subInputValue.trim();
                  if (!val) return alert('請輸入名稱');
                  const cc = cats.find((c) => c.label === category);
                  const existingSubs = cc?.subs || [];
                  if (existingSubs.includes(val)) return alert('此子分類已存在');
                  onAddSubCategory && onAddSubCategory(type, category, val);
                  setSubCategory(val);
                  setShowSubInput(false);
                }}
              >確定</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 日期顏色設定彈窗 */}
      {showDateColorSettings && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowDateColorSettings(false)}>
          <div
            style={{
              ...styles.pickerCard,
              transform: `translateX(${dateColorSwipe.dragX}px)`,
              transition: dateColorSwipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.2s' : 'none',
            }}
            ref={dateColorSwipe.ref}
            onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
          >
            <div style={styles.pickerTitle}>日曆顏色設定</div>
            <div style={{ padding: '12px 16px' }}>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 8 }}>選中日期顏色</div>
              <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(6, 1fr)', gap: 8, marginBottom: 16 }}>
                {dateColorOptions.map((c) => {
                  const sel = selectedDateColor === c.value;
                  return (
                    <div
                      key={c.value}
                      onClick={() => updateSelectedDateColor(c.value)}
                      style={{
                        aspectRatio: '1',
                        borderRadius: 12,
                        background: c.preview,
                        cursor: 'pointer',
                        position: 'relative',
                      }}
                    >
                      {sel && (
                        <div style={{
                          position: 'absolute',
                          top: -4, right: -4,
                          width: 18, height: 18,
                          borderRadius: '50%',
                          background: 'var(--mint)',
                          color: '#fff',
                          fontSize: 12,
                          fontWeight: 700,
                          display: 'flex',
                          alignItems: 'center',
                          justifyContent: 'center',
                          boxShadow: '0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,0.18)',
                        }}>✓</div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
              <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginBottom: 8 }}>週末日期顏色</div>
              <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(6, 1fr)', gap: 8 }}>
                {dateColorOptions.map((c) => {
                  const sel = weekendColor === c.value;
                  return (
                    <div
                      key={c.value}
                      onClick={() => updateWeekendColor(c.value)}
                      style={{
                        aspectRatio: '1',
                        borderRadius: 12,
                        background: c.preview,
                        cursor: 'pointer',
                        position: 'relative',
                      }}
                    >
                      {sel && (
                        <div style={{
                          position: 'absolute',
                          top: -4, right: -4,
                          width: 18, height: 18,
                          borderRadius: '50%',
                          background: 'var(--mint)',
                          color: '#fff',
                          fontSize: 12,
                          fontWeight: 700,
                          display: 'flex',
                          alignItems: 'center',
                          justifyContent: 'center',
                          boxShadow: '0 1px 3px rgba(0,0,0,0.18)',
                        }}>✓</div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  );
                })}
              </div>
              {/* 一鍵全部隨機 */}
              <div
                onClick={() => {
                  const a = dateColorOptions[Math.floor(Math.random() * dateColorOptions.length)];
                  let b = dateColorOptions[Math.floor(Math.random() * dateColorOptions.length)];
                  while (b.value === a.value && dateColorOptions.length > 1) {
                    b = dateColorOptions[Math.floor(Math.random() * dateColorOptions.length)];
                  }
                  updateSelectedDateColor(a.value);
                  updateWeekendColor(b.value);
                }}
                style={{
                  marginTop: 16,
                  padding: '10px 14px',
                  borderRadius: 12,
                  background: 'var(--bg-input)',
                  border: '1px dashed var(--border)',
                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'center',
                  gap: 8,
                  cursor: 'pointer',
                  userSelect: 'none',
                }}
              >
                <span style={{ fontSize: 16 }}>🎨</span>
                <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 600, color: 'var(--text)' }}>一鍵隨機配色</span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ padding: '0 16px 16px' }}>
              <button
                style={{ ...styles.saveBtn, background: 'var(--mint)', color: 'var(--on-mint)' }}
                onClick={() => setShowDateColorSettings(false)}
              >完成</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 期間明細 Sheet（本日/本週/本月/本年）============
function PeriodDetailSheet({ state, setState, catIcon, periodKey, onClose, onClickTxn, setConfirmDialog, toastRich, toast }) {
  const today = todayStr();
  const now = new Date();
  const toIso = (d) => `${d.getFullYear()}-${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}`;

  let title = '', range = '', predicate = () => false;

  if (periodKey === 'today') {
    title = '本日花費';
    range = today.replace(/-/g, '/');
    predicate = (d) => d === today;
  } else if (periodKey === 'week') {
    const dow = now.getDay();
    const ws = new Date(now); ws.setDate(now.getDate() - dow);
    const we = new Date(ws); we.setDate(ws.getDate() + 6);
    const s = toIso(ws), e = toIso(we);
    title = '本週花費';
    range = `${s.replace(/-/g, '/')} ~ ${e.replace(/-/g, '/')}`;
    predicate = (d) => d >= s && d <= e;
  } else if (periodKey === 'month') {
    const ym = today.slice(0, 7);
    const lastDay = new Date(parseInt(ym.slice(0, 4)), parseInt(ym.slice(5, 7)), 0).getDate();
    title = '本月花費';
    range = `${ym.replace('-', '/')}/01 ~ ${ym.replace('-', '/')}/${String(lastDay).padStart(2, '0')}`;
    predicate = (d) => d.startsWith(ym);
  } else if (periodKey === 'year') {
    const y = today.slice(0, 4);
    title = '本年花費';
    range = `${y}/01/01 ~ ${y}/12/31`;
    predicate = (d) => d.startsWith(y);
  }

  const txns = state.transactions
    .filter((t) => predicate(t.date))
    .sort((a, b) => b.date.localeCompare(a.date) || (b.createdAt || 0) - (a.createdAt || 0));

  let inc = 0, exp = 0;
  for (const t of txns) {
    if (!isRealFlow(t)) continue;
    if (t.type === 'income') inc += t.amount;
    else if (t.type === 'expense') exp += t.amount;
  }

  // 按日分組
  const groups = {};
  txns.forEach((t) => {
    (groups[t.date] ||= []).push(t);
  });
  const groupKeys = Object.keys(groups).sort((a, b) => b.localeCompare(a));

  const [editMode, setEditMode] = React.useState(false);
  // 多選刪除模式
  const [selectMode, setSelectMode] = React.useState(false);
  const [selectedIds, setSelectedIds] = React.useState(() => new Set());
  const exitSelectMode = () => { setSelectMode(false); setSelectedIds(new Set()); };
  // 左右滑:選擇模式時=退出選擇,否則=關閉 sheet(共用同一個 hook,避免 dragX 雙重定義)
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(selectMode ? exitSelectMode : onClose, { skipInPickerBackdrop: true });
  const toggleSelect = (id) => {
    setSelectedIds((prev) => {
      const next = new Set(prev);
      if (next.has(id)) next.delete(id); else next.add(id);
      return next;
    });
  };
  const enterSelectModeWith = (id) => { setSelectMode(true); setSelectedIds(new Set([id])); };
  const selectableCount = txns.length;
  const allSelected = selectableCount > 0 && selectedIds.size === selectableCount;
  const toggleAll = () => {
    if (allSelected) setSelectedIds(new Set());
    else setSelectedIds(new Set(txns.map((t) => t.id)));
  };
  // 批量刪除
  const doBatchDelete = () => {
    const ids = Array.from(selectedIds);
    if (ids.length === 0) return;
    const sel = state.transactions.filter((t) => ids.includes(t.id));
    const transferIds = new Set();
    const settleIds = new Set();
    sel.forEach((t) => {
      if (t.transferId) transferIds.add(t.transferId);
      if (t.settleId) settleIds.add(t.settleId);
    });
    const actuallyDeleteIds = new Set(ids);
    state.transactions.forEach((t) => {
      if (t.transferId && transferIds.has(t.transferId)) actuallyDeleteIds.add(t.id);
      if (t.settleId && settleIds.has(t.settleId)) actuallyDeleteIds.add(t.id);
    });
    // 預測股票買進 cascade 連動清掉的 sell + settle 紀錄,加入 actuallyDeleteIds 一起顯示
    const cascadeIds = expandStockBuyCascade(state, actuallyDeleteIds);
    if (cascadeIds.size > 0) {
      for (const id of cascadeIds) actuallyDeleteIds.add(id);
    }
    const delCount = actuallyDeleteIds.size;
    const includesTransfer = transferIds.size > 0;
    const includesSettle = settleIds.size > 0;
    const expandedCount = delCount - ids.length;
    const listText = buildBatchDeletePreview(state.transactions, selectedIds, actuallyDeleteIds);
    if (!setConfirmDialog) return;
    // message:只有「為什麼會多刪幾筆」的提示,不再寫總數(target list 已表達)
    let linkMsg;
    if (expandedCount > 0) {
      if (includesTransfer && includesSettle) {
        linkMsg = '同組轉帳與股票結算將一併刪除。';
      } else if (includesSettle) {
        linkMsg = '本金歸還與損益屬同一組,將一併刪除。';
      } else if (includesTransfer) {
        linkMsg = '轉帳兩端紀錄屬同一組,將一併刪除。';
      }
    }
    // 偵測股票買進影響:若刪除會讓某 holding 完全消失,加警告
    const stockImpact = detectStockBuyImpact(state, actuallyDeleteIds);
    if (stockImpact.msg) {
      linkMsg = (linkMsg ? linkMsg + '\n\n' : '') + stockImpact.msg;
    }
    setConfirmDialog({
      title: stockImpact.anyHoldingDestroyed ? '刪除股票買進'
        : includesSettle && includesTransfer ? '刪除多筆紀錄'
        : includesSettle ? '刪除股票結算'
        : includesTransfer ? '刪除轉帳'
        : `刪除 ${ids.length} 筆交易`,
      target: { label: '將刪除', name: listText, multiline: true },
      message: linkMsg,
      warning: '此操作無法復原',
      confirmText: stockImpact.anyHoldingDestroyed ? '仍要刪除持股' : '刪除',
      highlightWords: stockImpact.highlightWords,
      danger: true,
      onConfirm: () => {
        setState && setState((s) => ({
          ...s,
          transactions: s.transactions.filter((t) => !actuallyDeleteIds.has(t.id)),
        }));
        if (toastRich) {
          toastRich({ title: `已刪除 ${delCount} 筆`, amount: '✓', amountColor: 'var(--pink-text)' }, 1200);
        } else if (toast) {
          toast(`已刪除 ${delCount} 筆`);
        }
        exitSelectMode();
      },
    });
  };

  const [blockOrder, setBlockOrder] = React.useState(() => {
    const defaults = ['summary', 'list'];
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem('ledger_period_order');
      if (raw) {
        const saved = JSON.parse(raw);
        const defSet = new Set(defaults);
        const filtered = Array.isArray(saved) ? saved.filter((k) => defSet.has(k)) : [];
        const missing = defaults.filter((k) => !filtered.includes(k));
        return [...filtered, ...missing];
      }
    } catch {}
    return defaults;
  });
  React.useEffect(() => {
    try { localStorage.setItem('ledger_period_order', JSON.stringify(blockOrder)); } catch {}
  }, [blockOrder]);
  const moveBlock = (key, dir) => {
    setBlockOrder((prev) => {
      const i = prev.indexOf(key);
      if (i < 0) return prev;
      const j = i + dir;
      if (j < 0 || j >= prev.length) return prev;
      const next = [...prev];
      [next[i], next[j]] = [next[j], next[i]];
      return next;
    });
  };

  return (
    <div
      data-sheet="true"
      style={{
        ...styles.sheet,
        transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
        transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
      }}
      ref={swipe.ref}
    >
      <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
        {selectMode ? (
          <>
            <div style={{ width: 50 }} />
            <div style={styles.sheetTitle}>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>已選</span>
              <span style={{ marginLeft: 6, fontVariantNumeric: 'tabular-nums' }}>{selectedIds.size}</span>
              <span style={{ marginLeft: 4, fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 500, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>/{selectableCount}</span>
            </div>
            <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'flex-end' }}>
              <span
                style={{
                  fontSize: 14,
                  fontWeight: 600,
                  color: 'var(--pink-text)',
                  cursor: 'pointer',
                  padding: '6px 14px',
                  borderRadius: 16,
                  border: '1.5px solid var(--pink)',
                  background: 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.08)',
                  userSelect: 'none',
                  WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
                }}
                onClick={exitSelectMode}
              >取消</span>
            </div>
          </>
        ) : (
          <>
            <div style={{ width: 50 }} />
            <div style={styles.sheetTitle}>{title}</div>
            <div style={{ minWidth: 50, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'flex-end' }}>
              <EditOrderButton editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />
            </div>
          </>
        )}
      </div>

      <EditModeBanner editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />

      <div style={styles.sheetScroll} data-scroll-container>
      <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontSize: 13, marginBottom: 14 }}>
        {range}
      </div>

      {blockOrder.map((blockKey, idx) => {
        const blockProps = {
          blockKey,
          editMode,
          isFirst: idx === 0,
          isLast: idx === blockOrder.length - 1,
          onMoveUp: () => moveBlock(blockKey, -1),
          onMoveDown: () => moveBlock(blockKey, 1),
          onReorder: (newOrder) => setBlockOrder(newOrder),
          inline: true,
        };
        if (blockKey === 'summary') {
          return (
            <Block key="summary" {...blockProps}>
              <div style={styles.summaryRow}>
                <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
                  <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>收入</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: 'var(--mint-text)' }}>{fmt(inc)}</div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
                  <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>支出</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>{fmt(exp)}</div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
                  <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>結餘</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: (inc - exp) < 0 ? "var(--pink)" : (inc - exp) > 0 ? "var(--mint)" : "var(--text)" }}>{fmtSigned(inc - exp)}</div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }
        if (blockKey === 'list') {
          return (
            <Block key="list" {...blockProps}>
              {txns.length ? (
                <div style={styles.txnList}>
                  {groupKeys.map((date) => {
                    const days = groups[date];
                    const dInc = days.filter((t) => isRealFlow(t) && t.type === 'income').reduce((s, t) => s + t.amount, 0);
                    const dExp = days.filter((t) => isRealFlow(t) && t.type === 'expense').reduce((s, t) => s + t.amount, 0);
                    const wd = ['日', '一', '二', '三', '四', '五', '六'][new Date(date).getDay()];
                    return (
                      <React.Fragment key={date}>
                        <div style={styles.groupDate}>
                          <span>{date.replace(/-/g, '/')} · 週{wd}</span>
                          <span style={styles.groupDateAmt}>
                            {dInc > 0 && <span style={{ color: 'var(--mint-text)' }}>+{fmt(dInc)} </span>}
                            {dExp > 0 && <span style={{ color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>-{fmt(dExp)}</span>}
                          </span>
                        </div>
                        {days.map((t) => (
                          <TxnRow
                            key={t.id}
                            txn={t}
                            state={state}
                            catIcon={catIcon}
                            selectMode={selectMode}
                            selected={selectedIds.has(t.id)}
                            onClick={() => {
                              if (editMode) return;
                              if (selectMode) toggleSelect(t.id);
                              else onClickTxn(t);
                            }}
                            onLongPress={() => {
                              if (editMode || selectMode) return;
                              enterSelectModeWith(t.id);
                            }}
                          />
                        ))}
                      </React.Fragment>
                    );
                  })}
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div style={styles.empty}>這段期間還沒有紀錄</div>
              )}
            </Block>
          );
        }
        return null;
      })}
      </div>

      {selectMode && (
        <div style={{
          position: 'fixed', bottom: 0, left: 0, right: 0,
          maxWidth: 480, margin: '0 auto',
          padding: '10px 14px calc(12px + env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0px))',
          background: 'rgba(20, 22, 25, 0.96)',
          backdropFilter: 'blur(20px)',
          WebkitBackdropFilter: 'blur(20px)',
          borderTop: '1px solid var(--border)',
          display: 'flex', gap: 8, zIndex: 60,
          boxShadow: '0 -12px 24px rgba(0,0,0,0.3)',
        }}>
          <button
            style={{
              flex: '0 0 auto', padding: '10px 16px',
              background: 'var(--bg-card)', color: 'var(--text)',
              border: '1px solid var(--border)', borderRadius: 10,
              fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer',
              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 6,
            }}
            onClick={toggleAll}
            disabled={selectableCount === 0}
          >
            <div style={{
              width: 18, height: 18, borderRadius: 9,
              border: `1.5px solid ${allSelected ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--text-faint)'}`,
              background: allSelected ? 'var(--mint)' : 'transparent',
              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
            }}>
              {allSelected && (
                <svg width="10" height="10" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="#1a1a1a" strokeWidth="4" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
                  <polyline points="20 6 9 17 4 12" />
                </svg>
              )}
            </div>
            <span>{allSelected ? '取消全選' : '全選'}</span>
          </button>
          <button
            style={{
              flex: 1, padding: '10px 16px',
              background: selectedIds.size > 0 ? 'var(--pink)' : 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.25)',
              color: selectedIds.size > 0 ? '#1a1a1a' : 'var(--text-faint)',
              border: 'none', borderRadius: 10,
              fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 700,
              cursor: selectedIds.size > 0 ? 'pointer' : 'default',
              display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', gap: 6,
              transition: 'background 0.15s, color 0.15s',
            }}
            onClick={() => selectedIds.size > 0 && doBatchDelete()}
            disabled={selectedIds.size === 0}
          >
            <TypeIcon name="trash" size={14} color={selectedIds.size > 0 ? '#1a1a1a' : 'var(--text-faint)'} />
            <span>刪除 {selectedIds.size > 0 ? `(${selectedIds.size})` : ''}</span>
          </button>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 當日明細 Sheet（點日期條進來）============
function DayDetailSheet({ state, catIcon, date, onClose, onClickTxn, onAdd }) {
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(onClose, { skipInPickerBackdrop: true });

  const txns = state.transactions
    .filter((t) => t.date === date)
    .sort((a, b) => (b.createdAt || 0) - (a.createdAt || 0));

  let inc = 0, exp = 0;
  for (const t of txns) {
    if (!isRealFlow(t)) continue;
    if (t.type === 'income') inc += t.amount;
    else if (t.type === 'expense') exp += t.amount;
  }

  const d = new Date(date);
  const wd = ['日', '一', '二', '三', '四', '五', '六'][d.getDay()];
  const isToday = date === todayStr();

  const [editMode, setEditMode] = React.useState(false);
  const [blockOrder, setBlockOrder] = React.useState(() => {
    const defaults = ['summary', 'list'];
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem('ledger_day_order');
      if (raw) {
        const saved = JSON.parse(raw);
        const defSet = new Set(defaults);
        const filtered = Array.isArray(saved) ? saved.filter((k) => defSet.has(k)) : [];
        const missing = defaults.filter((k) => !filtered.includes(k));
        return [...filtered, ...missing];
      }
    } catch {}
    return defaults;
  });
  React.useEffect(() => {
    try { localStorage.setItem('ledger_day_order', JSON.stringify(blockOrder)); } catch {}
  }, [blockOrder]);
  const moveBlock = (key, dir) => {
    setBlockOrder((prev) => {
      const i = prev.indexOf(key);
      if (i < 0) return prev;
      const j = i + dir;
      if (j < 0 || j >= prev.length) return prev;
      const next = [...prev];
      [next[i], next[j]] = [next[j], next[i]];
      return next;
    });
  };

  return (
    <div
      data-sheet="true"
      style={{
        ...styles.sheet,
        transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
        transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
      }}
      ref={swipe.ref}
    >
      <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
        <div style={{ width: 50 }} />
        <div style={styles.sheetTitle}>
          {isToday ? '今日明細' : '當日明細'}
        </div>
        <div style={{ minWidth: 50, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'flex-end' }}>
          <EditOrderButton editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />
        </div>
      </div>

      <EditModeBanner editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />

      <div style={styles.sheetScroll} data-scroll-container>
      <div style={{ textAlign: 'center', color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontSize: 14, marginBottom: 14 }}>
        {date.replace(/-/g, '/')} · 週{wd}
      </div>

      {blockOrder.map((blockKey, idx) => {
        const blockProps = {
          blockKey,
          editMode,
          isFirst: idx === 0,
          isLast: idx === blockOrder.length - 1,
          onMoveUp: () => moveBlock(blockKey, -1),
          onMoveDown: () => moveBlock(blockKey, 1),
          onReorder: (newOrder) => setBlockOrder(newOrder),
          inline: true,
        };
        if (blockKey === 'summary') {
          return (
            <Block key="summary" {...blockProps}>
              <div style={styles.summaryRow}>
                <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
                  <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>收入</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: 'var(--mint-text)' }}>{fmt(inc)}</div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
                  <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>支出</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>{fmt(exp)}</div>
                </div>
                <div style={styles.summaryBox}>
                  <div style={styles.summaryLabel}>結餘</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.summaryValue, color: (inc - exp) < 0 ? "var(--pink)" : (inc - exp) > 0 ? "var(--mint)" : "var(--text)" }}>{fmtSigned(inc - exp)}</div>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: '1fr 1fr', gap: 8, marginTop: 14 }}>
                <button style={styles.addIncBtn} onClick={() => !editMode && onAdd('income', date)}>＋ 新增收入</button>
                <button style={styles.addExpBtn} onClick={() => !editMode && onAdd('expense', date)}>＋ 新增支出</button>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }
        if (blockKey === 'list') {
          return (
            <Block key="list" {...blockProps}>
              {txns.length ? (
                <div style={styles.txnList}>
                  {txns.map((t) => (
                    <TxnRow key={t.id} txn={t} state={state} catIcon={catIcon} onClick={() => !editMode && onClickTxn(t)} />
                  ))}
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div style={styles.empty}>這天還沒有紀錄<br />點上方按鈕記一筆</div>
              )}
            </Block>
          );
        }
        return null;
      })}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 分類管理 Sheet ============
function CategoryManageSheet({ state, setState, toast, toastRich, catType, initialLabel, onClose, setConfirmDialog }) {
  const list = state.categories[catType] || [];
  const isNewMode = initialLabel === '__new__';
  const initialIdx = (!isNewMode && initialLabel) ? list.findIndex((c) => c.label === initialLabel) : -1;
  const [editingIdx, setEditingIdx] = useState(
    isNewMode ? 'new' : (initialIdx >= 0 ? initialIdx : null)
  );
  const commonIconsInit = catType === 'income'
    ? 'briefcase' : 'plate';
  const [label, setLabel] = useState(initialIdx >= 0 ? list[initialIdx].label : '');
  // 編輯既有分類時預設鎖定名稱(避免誤改),新增模式不鎖
  const [nameLocked, setNameLocked] = useState(initialIdx >= 0);
  // 圖示也預設鎖定(編輯既有分類時避免誤觸選到別的圖示)
  const [iconLocked, setIconLocked] = useState(initialIdx >= 0);
  const [icon, setIcon] = useState(
    isNewMode ? commonIconsInit : (initialIdx >= 0 ? list[initialIdx].icon : 'note')
  );
  // 子分類輸入彈窗：mode 為 'new' 或 'edit'，editingSubIdx 用於 edit
  const [subInputMode, setSubInputMode] = useState(null); // null | 'new' | 'edit'
  const [subInputValue, setSubInputValue] = useState('');
  const [subEditIdx, setSubEditIdx] = useState(null);
  // 編輯子分類時,預設鎖定避免誤改;新增模式則一律解鎖
  const [subInputLocked, setSubInputLocked] = useState(false);
  const subInputSwipe = useSwipeToClose(() => setSubInputMode(null));
  const [editMode, setEditMode] = useState(false);
  const [subEditMode, setSubEditMode] = useState(false); // 子分類排序模式
  // 進入排序模式時 snapshot 原順序;若使用者左右滑離開未按完成 → 還原
  const subsSnapshotRef = React.useRef(null);
  // 從編輯返回時對應 row 淡黃閃爍
  const [flashLabel, setFlashLabel] = useState(null);
  // 暫存 — 在 cancel 時設定,等列表 row mount 完才轉成 flashLabel 觸發動畫
  const pendingFlashRef = React.useRef(null);

  // 列表捲動位置記憶 — 點分類進入編輯時 startEdit() 記住,
  // 退回列表時 effect 還原
  const scrollContainerRef = React.useRef(null);
  const savedScrollTopRef = React.useRef(0);
  const prevEditingIdxRef = React.useRef(editingIdx);
  React.useEffect(() => {
    const wasEditing = prevEditingIdxRef.current !== null;
    const isEditing = editingIdx !== null;
    if (wasEditing && !isEditing) {
      // rAF 確保 DOM 已切回列表後再執行還原 + 觸發閃爍
      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        if (scrollContainerRef.current) {
          scrollContainerRef.current.scrollTop = savedScrollTopRef.current;
        }
        if (pendingFlashRef.current) {
          setFlashLabel(pendingFlashRef.current);
          pendingFlashRef.current = null;
        }
      });
    }
    prevEditingIdxRef.current = editingIdx;
  }, [editingIdx]);

  React.useEffect(() => {
    if (!flashLabel) return;
    const t = setTimeout(() => setFlashLabel(null), 1100);
    return () => clearTimeout(t);
  }, [flashLabel]);

  const enterSubEditMode = () => {
    if (editingIdx !== null && editingIdx !== 'new') {
      subsSnapshotRef.current = [...(list[editingIdx].subs || [])];
    }
    setSubEditMode(true);
  };

  const exitSubEditMode = (restore) => {
    if (restore && subsSnapshotRef.current && editingIdx !== null && editingIdx !== 'new') {
      const snapshot = subsSnapshotRef.current;
      setState((s) => {
        const newCats = [...s.categories[catType]];
        newCats[editingIdx] = { ...newCats[editingIdx], subs: snapshot };
        return { ...s, categories: { ...s.categories, [catType]: newCats } };
      });
    }
    subsSnapshotRef.current = null;
    setSubEditMode(false);
  };

  const typeLabel = catType === 'income' ? '收入' : '支出';

  const moveSub = (i, delta) => {
    if (editingIdx === null || editingIdx === 'new') return;
    const subs = list[editingIdx].subs || [];
    const newIdx = i + delta;
    if (newIdx < 0 || newIdx >= subs.length) return;
    setState((s) => {
      const newCats = [...s.categories[catType]];
      const arr = [...(newCats[editingIdx].subs || [])];
      [arr[i], arr[newIdx]] = [arr[newIdx], arr[i]];
      newCats[editingIdx] = { ...newCats[editingIdx], subs: arr };
      return { ...s, categories: { ...s.categories, [catType]: newCats } };
    });
  };

  const reorderSubs = (newOrder) => {
    if (editingIdx === null || editingIdx === 'new') return;
    setState((s) => {
      const newCats = [...s.categories[catType]];
      const subs = newCats[editingIdx].subs || [];
      const set = new Set(subs);
      const reordered = newOrder.filter((x) => set.has(x));
      subs.forEach((x) => { if (!newOrder.includes(x)) reordered.push(x); });
      newCats[editingIdx] = { ...newCats[editingIdx], subs: reordered };
      return { ...s, categories: { ...s.categories, [catType]: newCats } };
    });
  };

  const commonIcons = catType === 'income'
    ? ['briefcase', 'salary', 'bag', 'cash', 'gift', 'chart', 'bank', 'card', 'coin', 'gem', 'spark', 'target', 'home', 'building', 'cap', 'book', 'phone', 'list', 'calendar', 'box', 'note']
    : ['plate', 'cart', 'shopping', 'coffee', 'home', 'building', 'car', 'fuel', 'bed', 'bolt', 'phone', 'card', 'hospital', 'movie', 'game', 'music', 'gift', 'cap', 'book', 'paw', 'note'];

  const startAdd = () => {
    setEditingIdx('new');
    setLabel('');
    setIcon(commonIcons[0]);
    setNameLocked(false); // 新增模式不鎖定
    setIconLocked(false);
  };

  const startEdit = (i) => {
    // 進編輯前,先記住列表捲動位置(setState 後內容會被替換,scrollTop 會變 0)
    if (scrollContainerRef.current) {
      savedScrollTopRef.current = scrollContainerRef.current.scrollTop;
    }
    setEditingIdx(i);
    setLabel(list[i].label);
    setIcon(list[i].icon);
    setNameLocked(true); // 編輯既有分類時預設鎖定名稱(避免誤改)
    setIconLocked(true); // 圖示也預設鎖定
    setSubEditMode(false);
  };

  const cancel = (flashTarget = null) => {
    if (flashTarget) pendingFlashRef.current = flashTarget;
    setEditingIdx(null);
    setLabel('');
    setNameLocked(false);
    setIconLocked(false);
    setSubEditMode(false);
  };

  // 左右滑返回:在編輯/新增表單中 → 回到列表;在列表 → 關閉 sheet
  // 若處於子分類排序模式,先還原原順序(放棄變更),再回到列表
  const swipeBack = () => {
    const currentLabel = (editingIdx !== null && editingIdx !== 'new' && list[editingIdx])
      ? list[editingIdx].label
      : null;
    if (subEditMode) {
      exitSubEditMode(true);
      cancel(currentLabel);
      return;
    }
    if (editingIdx !== null) {
      cancel(currentLabel);
    } else {
      onClose();
    }
  };
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(swipeBack, { skipInPickerBackdrop: true });

  const save = () => {
    const t = label.trim();
    if (!t) return alert('請輸入分類名稱');
    if (editingIdx === 'new') {
      setState((s) => ({
        ...s,
        categories: {
          ...s.categories,
          [catType]: [...s.categories[catType], { label: t, icon, subs: [] }],
        },
      }));
      toastRich({
        title: `已新增${typeLabel}分類`,
        amount: '✓',
        amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
        lines: [`「${t}」`],
      });
    } else {
      const oldLabel = list[editingIdx].label;
      const oldIcon = list[editingIdx].icon;
      const oldSubs = list[editingIdx].subs || [];
      const labelChanged = t !== oldLabel;
      const iconChanged = icon !== oldIcon;

      // 沒任何變更 → 用 toastRich 強化提示
      if (!labelChanged && !iconChanged) {
        toastRich({
          title: '沒有任何變更',
          amount: '✓',
          icon: 'info',
          amountColor: 'var(--text-faint)',
          lines: [`「${oldLabel}」資料未調整`],
        }, 1400);
        cancel(oldLabel);
        return;
      }

      setState((s) => {
        const newCats = [...s.categories[catType]];
        newCats[editingIdx] = { label: t, icon, subs: oldSubs };
        // 連動更新現有交易的分類名稱
        const newTxns = labelChanged
          ? s.transactions.map((x) =>
              x.type === catType && x.category === oldLabel ? { ...x, category: t } : x
            )
          : s.transactions;
        return {
          ...s,
          categories: { ...s.categories, [catType]: newCats },
          transactions: newTxns,
        };
      });
      toastRich(labelChanged ? {
        titleSegments: [
          '已更新', '\n',
          typeLabel,
          ' ',
          { text: '大分類', color: 'var(--blue)' },
          ' ',
          '名稱',
        ],
        amount: '✓',
        amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
        lines: [`「${oldLabel}」 → 「${t}」`],
      } : {
        title: `已更新${typeLabel}分類`,
        amount: '✓',
        amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
        lines: [`「${t}」`],
      }, labelChanged ? 3500 : 1180);
      cancel(t);
      return;
    }
    cancel(t);
  };

  const remove = (i) => {
    const target = list[i].label;
    const affected = state.transactions.filter((x) => x.type === catType && x.category === target).length;
    if (setConfirmDialog) {
      setConfirmDialog({
        title: `刪除 ${typeLabel}分類 名稱`,
        target: { label: '名稱', name: target },
        message: affected > 0
          ? `將影響 ${affected} 筆 收支紀錄\n但這些紀錄不會被刪除\n只會清空 大分類與子分類欄位`
          : `目前沒有紀錄使用此分類`,
        highlightWords: ['大分類與子分類欄位'],
        confirmText: '刪除',
        danger: true,
        onConfirm: () => {
          setState((s) => ({
            ...s,
            categories: {
              ...s.categories,
              [catType]: s.categories[catType].filter((_, idx) => idx !== i),
            },
          }));
          cancel();
          toastRich({
            title: `已刪除${typeLabel}分類`,
            amount: '✓',
            amountColor: 'var(--pink)',
            lines: [`「${target}」`, affected > 0 ? `${affected} 筆紀錄已清除分類欄位` : null].filter(Boolean),
          });
        },
      });
    }
  };

  const moveCat = (i, delta) => {
    const newIdx = i + delta;
    if (newIdx < 0 || newIdx >= list.length) return;
    setState((s) => {
      const arr = [...s.categories[catType]];
      [arr[i], arr[newIdx]] = [arr[newIdx], arr[i]];
      return { ...s, categories: { ...s.categories, [catType]: arr } };
    });
  };

  const reorderCats = (newLabelOrder) => {
    setState((s) => {
      const arr = s.categories[catType] || [];
      const map = new Map(arr.map((c) => [c.label, c]));
      const reordered = newLabelOrder.map((lbl) => map.get(lbl)).filter(Boolean);
      arr.forEach((c) => { if (!newLabelOrder.includes(c.label)) reordered.push(c); });
      return { ...s, categories: { ...s.categories, [catType]: reordered } };
    });
  };

  return (
    <div
      data-sheet="true"
      style={{
        ...styles.sheet,
        transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
        transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
      }}
      ref={swipe.ref}
    >
      <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
        <div style={{ width: 50 }} />
        <div style={styles.sheetTitle}>
