          {editingIdx === null ? (
            // 列表模式:支出/收入 大分類 管理
            <>
              <span style={{ color: catType === 'income' ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--pink)' }}>
                {typeLabel}
              </span>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--blue)', marginLeft: 6, fontWeight: 600 }}>
                大分類
              </span>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontWeight: 500, marginLeft: 6 }}>
                管理
              </span>
            </>
          ) : editingIdx === 'new' ? (
            // 新增模式
            <>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontWeight: 500 }}>
                新增
              </span>
              <span style={{ color: catType === 'income' ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--pink)', marginLeft: 4 }}>
                {typeLabel}
              </span>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontWeight: 500, marginLeft: 2 }}>
                大分類
              </span>
            </>
          ) : (
            // 編輯模式:編輯大分類:〈名稱〉
            <>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontWeight: 500 }}>
                編輯
              </span>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--blue)', marginLeft: 4, fontWeight: 600 }}>
                大分類
              </span>
              <span style={{ color: 'var(--text)', marginLeft: 6, fontWeight: 700 }}>
                {list[editingIdx]?.label || ''}
              </span>
            </>
          )}
        </div>
        <div style={{ minWidth: 50, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'flex-end' }}>
          {editingIdx === null && <EditOrderButton editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />}
        </div>
      </div>

      <EditModeBanner editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />

      <div style={styles.sheetScroll} data-scroll-container ref={scrollContainerRef}>
      <div
        key={editingIdx === null ? 'list' : `edit-${editingIdx}`}
        style={{
          animation: editingIdx === null
            ? 'pushBack 0.32s ease-out'
            : 'pushEnter 0.32s ease-out',
        }}
      >
      {editingIdx !== null ? (
        <>
          <div style={{ ...styles.fieldLabel, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
            <span>名稱</span>
            {editingIdx !== 'new' && editingIdx !== null && (
              <div
                onClick={() => setNameLocked(!nameLocked)}
                style={{ ...styles.lockRow, cursor: 'pointer', userSelect: 'none' }}
              >
                <span style={{ ...styles.lockLabel, color: nameLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 4 }}>
                  <TypeIcon name={nameLocked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'} size={12} color={nameLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)'} />
                  {nameLocked ? '鎖定中' : '已解鎖'}
                </span>
                <div
                  style={{ ...styles.toggleTrack, background: nameLocked ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--mint)' }}
                >
                  <div style={{ ...styles.toggleThumb, transform: nameLocked ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(18px)' }} />
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
          <input
            type="text"
            style={{
              ...styles.field,
              opacity: nameLocked && editingIdx !== 'new' && editingIdx !== null ? 0.55 : 1,
              cursor: nameLocked && editingIdx !== 'new' && editingIdx !== null ? 'not-allowed' : 'text',
            }}
            value={label}
            onChange={(e) => setLabel(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="例如:飲料"
            maxLength={10}
            disabled={nameLocked && editingIdx !== 'new' && editingIdx !== null}
          />

          <div style={{ ...styles.fieldLabel, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
            <span>圖示</span>
            {editingIdx !== 'new' && editingIdx !== null && (
              <div
                onClick={() => setIconLocked(!iconLocked)}
                style={{ ...styles.lockRow, cursor: 'pointer', userSelect: 'none' }}
              >
                <span style={{ ...styles.lockLabel, color: iconLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 4 }}>
                  <TypeIcon name={iconLocked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'} size={12} color={iconLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)'} />
                  {iconLocked ? '鎖定中' : '已解鎖'}
                </span>
                <div
                  style={{ ...styles.toggleTrack, background: iconLocked ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--mint)' }}
                >
                  <div style={{ ...styles.toggleThumb, transform: iconLocked ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(18px)' }} />
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
          <div style={{
            ...styles.iconGrid,
            opacity: iconLocked && editingIdx !== 'new' && editingIdx !== null ? 0.55 : 1,
            pointerEvents: iconLocked && editingIdx !== 'new' && editingIdx !== null ? 'none' : 'auto',
          }}>
            {commonIcons.map((ic) => {
              const selected = icon === ic;
              return (
                <div
                  key={ic}
                  tabIndex={-1}
                  style={{
                    ...styles.iconCell,
                    ...(selected ? { outline: '1.5px solid var(--mint)', outlineOffset: '-1.5px', background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.1)' } : {}),
                  }}
                  onClick={() => setIcon(ic)}
                >
                  <TypeIcon name={ic} size={24} color={selected ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--text-dim)'} />
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>

          {/* 子分類管理（只在編輯現有分類時顯示） */}
          {editingIdx !== 'new' && editingIdx !== null && (
            <>
              <div style={{ ...styles.fieldLabel, marginTop: 16, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
                <span>子分類</span>
                <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8 }}>
                  {(list[editingIdx].subs || []).length > 1 && (
                    <EditOrderButton editMode={subEditMode} setEditMode={(v) => v ? enterSubEditMode() : exitSubEditMode(false)} />
                  )}
                  {!subEditMode && (
                    <button
                      style={{
                        display: 'inline-flex',
                        alignItems: 'center',
                        gap: 5,
                        padding: '5px 11px',
                        fontSize: 12,
                        fontWeight: 600,
                        color: 'var(--mint)',
                        background: 'rgba(126,224,192,0.10)',
                        border: '1px solid rgba(126,224,192,0.35)',
                        borderRadius: 999,
                        cursor: 'pointer',
                        userSelect: 'none',
                        transition: 'background 0.15s, transform 0.1s',
                        WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
                      }}
                      onClick={() => {
                        setSubInputMode('new');
                        setSubInputValue('');
                        setSubEditIdx(null);
                        setSubInputLocked(false);
                      }}
                    >
                      <svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="3" strokeLinecap="round">
                        <line x1="12" y1="5" x2="12" y2="19" />
                        <line x1="5" y1="12" x2="19" y2="12" />
                      </svg>
                      新增
                    </button>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>
              {subEditMode && <EditModeBanner editMode={subEditMode} setEditMode={(v) => v ? enterSubEditMode() : exitSubEditMode(false)} />}
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 6 }}>
                {(list[editingIdx].subs || []).length === 0 ? (
                  <div style={styles.pickerEmpty}>尚未建立子分類</div>
                ) : (
                  (list[editingIdx].subs || []).map((s, si) => {
                    const subs = list[editingIdx].subs || [];
                    return (
                    <Block
                      key={s + si}
                      blockKey={s}
                      editMode={subEditMode}
                      isFirst={si === 0}
                      isLast={si === subs.length - 1}
                      onMoveUp={() => moveSub(si, -1)}
                      onMoveDown={() => moveSub(si, 1)}
                      onReorder={(newOrder) => reorderSubs(newOrder)}
                      inline
                      compactInline
                    >
                    <div style={styles.subRow}>
                      <div style={{ flex: 1, fontSize: 14, color: 'var(--text)' }}>{s}</div>
                      {!subEditMode && (
                        <>
                      <div
                        style={styles.subRowBtn}
                        onClick={() => {
                          setSubInputMode('edit');
                          setSubInputValue(s);
                          setSubEditIdx(si);
                          setSubInputLocked(true);
                        }}
                      >編輯</div>
                      <div
                        style={{ ...styles.subRowBtn, color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}
                        onClick={() => {
                          if (setConfirmDialog) {
                            // 計算受影響筆數
                            const affected = state.transactions.filter(
                              (x) => x.type === catType && x.category === list[editingIdx].label && x.subCategory === s
                            ).length;
                            const parentLabel = list[editingIdx].label;
                            setConfirmDialog({
                              title: '刪除 子分類 名稱',
                              target: { label: '名稱', name: s },
                              message: affected > 0
                                ? `將影響 ${affected} 筆 收支紀錄\n但這些紀錄不會被刪除\n只會清空 子分類欄位`
                                : `目前沒有紀錄使用此子分類`,
                              highlightWords: ['子分類欄位'],
                              confirmText: '刪除',
                              danger: true,
                              onConfirm: () => {
                                setState((st) => {
                                  const newCats = [...st.categories[catType]];
                                  newCats[editingIdx] = {
                                    ...newCats[editingIdx],
                                    subs: (newCats[editingIdx].subs || []).filter((_, idx) => idx !== si),
                                  };
                                  // 清掉使用此子分類的交易
                                  const newTxns = st.transactions.map((x) =>
                                    x.type === catType && x.category === list[editingIdx].label && x.subCategory === s
                                      ? { ...x, subCategory: '' } : x
                                  );
                                  return { ...st, categories: { ...st.categories, [catType]: newCats }, transactions: newTxns };
                                });
                                toastRich({
                                  title: '已刪除子分類',
                                  amount: '✓',
                                  amountColor: 'var(--pink)',
                                  lines: [`「${s}」`, affected > 0 ? `${affected} 筆紀錄已清除子分類欄位` : null].filter(Boolean),
                                });
                              },
                            });
                          }
                        }}
                      >刪除</div>
                        </>
                      )}
                    </div>
                    </Block>
                    );
                  })
                )}
              </div>
            </>
          )}

          <button style={{ ...styles.saveBtn, background: 'var(--mint)', color: 'var(--on-mint)', marginTop: 16 }} onClick={save}>儲存</button>
          <button style={{ ...styles.deleteBtn, marginTop: 6 }} onClick={() => cancel(editingIdx !== 'new' && list[editingIdx] ? list[editingIdx].label : null)}>取消</button>
          {editingIdx !== 'new' && (
            <button style={{ ...styles.deleteBtn, marginTop: 6 }} onClick={() => remove(editingIdx)}>刪除此分類</button>
          )}
        </>
      ) : (
        <>
          <div style={{ ...styles.txnList, gap: 4 }}>
            {list.map((c, i) => (
              <Block
                key={c.label}
                blockKey={c.label}
                editMode={editMode}
                isFirst={i === 0}
                isLast={i === list.length - 1}
                onMoveUp={() => moveCat(i, -1)}
                onMoveDown={() => moveCat(i, 1)}
                onReorder={(newOrder) => reorderCats(newOrder)}
                inline
                compactInline
              >
                <div
                  style={{
                    ...styles.txn,
                    border: '1px dashed var(--border)',
                    borderRadius: 10,
                    padding: '6px 10px',
                    ...(flashLabel === c.label ? { animation: 'returnFlash 0.9s ease' } : {}),
                  }}
                >
                  <div style={styles.txnIcon}>
                    <TypeIcon name={c.icon} size={22} color="var(--text)" />
                  </div>
                  <div style={styles.txnInfo} onClick={() => !editMode && startEdit(i)}>
                    <div style={styles.txnCat}>
                      {c.label}
                      {c.subs?.length > 0 && (
                        <span style={{ marginLeft: 8, fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', fontWeight: 400 }}>
                          子分類 {c.subs.length} 筆
                        </span>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)', fontSize: 18, marginLeft: 4 }} onClick={() => !editMode && startEdit(i)}>›</div>
                </div>
              </Block>
            ))}
          </div>
          {!editMode && (
            <div style={{ height: 12 }} />
          )}
        </>
      )}
      </div>
      </div>

      {/* 釘在底部的「＋ 新增分類」按鈕（僅列表模式顯示） */}
      {editingIdx === null && !editMode && (
        <div style={{ ...styles.stickyFooterBar, padding: '6px 0 0' }}>
          <button
            style={{
              ...styles.saveBtn,
              background: 'var(--mint)',
              color: 'var(--on-mint)',
              marginTop: 0,
              width: '100%',
              padding: '14px 0 calc(14px + env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0px))',
              borderRadius: 12,
            }}
            onClick={startAdd}
          >
            ＋ 新增{typeLabel}分類
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* 子分類輸入彈窗（取代 window.prompt） */}
      {subInputMode && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.pickerBackdrop} onClick={() => setSubInputMode(null)}>
          <div style={styles.pickerCard} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()} {...subInputSwipe}>
            <div style={{ ...styles.pickerTitle, fontSize: 17, fontWeight: 700, padding: '14px 16px 12px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', gap: 8 }}>
              <span>{subInputMode === 'new' ? '新增子分類' : '修改子分類名稱'}</span>
              {/* 編輯模式才顯示鎖定 toggle */}
              {subInputMode === 'edit' && (
                <div
                  onClick={() => setSubInputLocked((v) => !v)}
                  style={{ ...styles.lockRow, cursor: 'pointer', userSelect: 'none' }}
                >
                  <span style={{ ...styles.lockLabel, color: subInputLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 4 }}>
                    <TypeIcon name={subInputLocked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'} size={12} color={subInputLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)'} />
                    {subInputLocked ? '鎖定中' : '已解鎖'}
                  </span>
                  <div
                    style={{ ...styles.toggleTrack, background: subInputLocked ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--mint)' }}
                  >
                    <div style={{ ...styles.toggleThumb, transform: subInputLocked ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(18px)' }} />
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
            <div style={{ padding: '14px 16px' }}>
              <input
                type="text"
                style={{
                  ...styles.field,
                  ...(subInputLocked ? { opacity: 0.6, cursor: 'not-allowed' } : {}),
                }}
                value={subInputValue}
                onChange={(e) => setSubInputValue(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="請輸入子分類名稱"
                maxLength={20}
                readOnly={subInputLocked}
              />
            </div>
            <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8, padding: '0 16px 16px' }}>
              <button
                style={{ ...styles.deleteBtn, flex: 1, marginTop: 0 }}
                onClick={() => setSubInputMode(null)}
              >取消</button>
              <button
                style={{
                  ...styles.saveBtn,
                  flex: 1,
                  background: 'var(--mint)',
                  color: 'var(--on-mint)',
                  marginTop: 0,
                  opacity: subInputLocked ? 0.4 : 1,
                  cursor: subInputLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
                }}
                onClick={() => {
                  if (subInputLocked) {
                    toast('請先解鎖才能儲存');
                    return;
                  }
                  const val = subInputValue.trim();
                  if (!val) return alert('請輸入名稱');
                  const currentSubs = list[editingIdx].subs || [];
                  if (subInputMode === 'new') {
                    if (currentSubs.includes(val)) return alert('此子分類已存在');
                    setState((s) => {
                      const newCats = [...s.categories[catType]];
                      newCats[editingIdx] = { ...newCats[editingIdx], subs: [...(newCats[editingIdx].subs || []), val] };
                      return { ...s, categories: { ...s.categories, [catType]: newCats } };
                    });
                    toastRich({
                      title: '已新增子分類',
                      amount: '✓',
                      amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
                      lines: [`「${val}」`, list[editingIdx].label],
                    });
                  } else {
                    // edit mode
                    const oldVal = currentSubs[subEditIdx];
                    if (val === oldVal) { setSubInputMode(null); return; }
                    if (currentSubs.includes(val)) return alert('此子分類已存在');
                    setState((st) => {
                      const newCats = [...st.categories[catType]];
                      const subs = [...(newCats[editingIdx].subs || [])];
                      subs[subEditIdx] = val;
                      newCats[editingIdx] = { ...newCats[editingIdx], subs };
                      const newTxns = st.transactions.map((x) =>
                        x.type === catType && x.category === list[editingIdx].label && x.subCategory === oldVal
                          ? { ...x, subCategory: val } : x
                      );
                      return { ...st, categories: { ...st.categories, [catType]: newCats }, transactions: newTxns };
                    });
                    toastRich({
                      titleSegments: [
                        '已更新', '\n',
                        typeLabel,
                        ' ',
                        { text: '子分類', color: 'var(--blue)' },
                        ' ',
                        '名稱',
                      ],
                      amount: '✓',
                      amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
                      lines: [`「${oldVal}」 → 「${val}」`, list[editingIdx].label],
                    }, 3500);
                  }
                  setSubInputMode(null);
                }}
              >確定</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 帳戶類型管理 Sheet ============
function AccountTypeManageSheet({ state, setState, toast, toastRich, onClose, setConfirmDialog }) {
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(onClose, { skipInPickerBackdrop: true });
  const list = state.accountTypes || [];
  const [editingIdx, setEditingIdx] = useState(null); // 'new' | index | null
  const [label, setLabel] = useState('');
  const [icon, setIcon] = useState(TYPE_ICONS[0]);
  const [color, setColor] = useState(TYPE_COLORS[0]); // 底色
  const [palette, setPalette] = useState('pastel'); // 'pastel' | 'solid'
  const [shade, setShade] = useState(0); // -50 ~ +50（調深淺）
  const [editMode, setEditMode] = useState(false);
  // 防誤觸：編輯現有類型時預設鎖定,新增時解鎖
  const [labelLocked, setLabelLocked] = useState(false);
  const [iconLocked, setIconLocked] = useState(false);

  const reorderTypes = (newValueOrder) => {
    setState((s) => {
      const arr = s.accountTypes || [];
      const map = new Map(arr.map((t) => [t.value, t]));
      const reordered = newValueOrder.map((v) => map.get(v)).filter(Boolean);
      arr.forEach((t) => { if (!newValueOrder.includes(t.value)) reordered.push(t); });
      return { ...s, accountTypes: reordered };
    });
  };

  const startAdd = () => {
    setEditingIdx('new');
    setLabel('');
    setIcon(TYPE_ICONS[0]);
    setColor(TYPE_COLORS[0]);
    setPalette('pastel');
    setShade(0);
    setLabelLocked(false);
    setIconLocked(false);
  };

  const startEdit = (i) => {
    setEditingIdx(i);
    setLabel(list[i].label);
    setIcon(list[i].icon || TYPE_ICONS[0]);
    setColor(list[i].color || TYPE_COLORS[0]);
    setPalette('pastel');
    setShade(0);
    setLabelLocked(true);
    setIconLocked(true);
  };

  const cancel = () => {
    setEditingIdx(null);
    setLabel('');
  };

  const save = () => {
    const t = label.trim();
    if (!t) return alert('請輸入類型名稱');
    const finalColor = adjustShade(color, shade);
    if (editingIdx === 'new') {
      const newValue = 'type_' + Date.now().toString(36);
      setState((s) => ({
        ...s,
        accountTypes: [...s.accountTypes, { value: newValue, label: t, icon, color: finalColor }],
      }));
      if (toastRich) {
        toastRich({
          title: '已新增類型',
          amount: '✓',
          amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
          lines: [`「${t}」`],
        }, 1400);
      } else {
        toast('已新增');
      }
      cancel();
      return;
    }

    // 編輯模式:檢查是否有實際變更
    const original = list[editingIdx];
    if (!original) { cancel(); return; }
    const labelChanged = t !== original.label;
    const iconChanged = icon !== (original.icon || TYPE_ICONS[0]);
    const colorChanged = finalColor !== (original.color || TYPE_COLORS[0]);

    // 沒任何變更 → 用 toastRich 強化提示
    if (!labelChanged && !iconChanged && !colorChanged) {
      if (toastRich) {
        toastRich({
          title: '沒有任何變更',
          amount: '✓',
          icon: 'info',
          amountColor: 'var(--text-faint)',
          lines: [`「${original.label}」資料未調整`],
        }, 1400);
      } else {
        toast('沒有任何變更');
      }
      cancel();
      return;
    }

    setState((s) => {
      const arr = [...s.accountTypes];
      arr[editingIdx] = { ...arr[editingIdx], label: t, icon, color: finalColor };
      return { ...s, accountTypes: arr };
    });
    const changedParts = [];
    if (labelChanged) changedParts.push('名稱');
    if (iconChanged) changedParts.push('圖示');
    if (colorChanged) changedParts.push('顏色');
    if (toastRich) {
      toastRich(labelChanged ? {
        titleSegments: [
          '已更新', '\n',
          { text: '帳戶類型', color: 'var(--blue)' },
          ' ',
          changedParts.join('、'),
        ],
        amount: '✓',
        amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
        lines: [`「${original.label}」 → 「${t}」`],
      } : {
        title: `已更新 ${changedParts.join('、')}`,
        amount: '✓',
        amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
        lines: [`「${t}」`],
      }, labelChanged ? 3500 : 1400);
    } else {
      toast(`已更新 ${changedParts.join('、')}`);
    }
    cancel();
  };

  const remove = (i) => {
    const target = list[i];
    const used = state.accounts.some((a) => a.type === target.value);
    const msg = used
      ? `有帳戶正在使用「${target.label}」類型，刪除後那些帳戶的類型會變成空。確定刪除？`
      : `確定刪除「${target.label}」類型？`;
    if (setConfirmDialog) {
      setConfirmDialog({
        title: '刪除帳戶類型',
        message: msg,
        confirmText: '刪除',
        danger: true,
        onConfirm: () => {
          setState((s) => ({
            ...s,
            accountTypes: s.accountTypes.filter((_, idx) => idx !== i),
          }));
          cancel();
          toast('已刪除');
        },
      });
    }
  };

  const moveType = (i, delta) => {
    const newIdx = i + delta;
    if (newIdx < 0 || newIdx >= list.length) return;
    setState((s) => {
      const arr = [...s.accountTypes];
      [arr[i], arr[newIdx]] = [arr[newIdx], arr[i]];
      return { ...s, accountTypes: arr };
    });
  };

  return (
    <div
      data-sheet="true"
      style={{
        ...styles.sheet,
        transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
        transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
      }}
      ref={swipe.ref}
    >
      <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
        <div style={{ width: 50 }} />
        <div style={styles.sheetTitle}>帳戶類型管理</div>
        <div style={{ minWidth: 50, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'flex-end' }}>
          {editingIdx === null && <EditOrderButton editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />}
        </div>
      </div>

      <EditModeBanner editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />

      <div style={styles.sheetScroll} data-scroll-container>
      {editingIdx !== null ? (
        <>
          <div style={{ ...styles.fieldLabel, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
            <span>類型名稱</span>
            <div style={styles.lockRow}>
              <span style={{ ...styles.lockLabel, color: labelLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 4 }}>
                <TypeIcon name={labelLocked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'} size={12} color={labelLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)'} />
                {labelLocked ? '鎖定中' : '已解鎖'}
              </span>
              <div
                style={{ ...styles.toggleTrack, background: labelLocked ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--mint)' }}
                onClick={() => setLabelLocked((v) => !v)}
              >
                <div style={{ ...styles.toggleThumb, transform: labelLocked ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(18px)' }} />
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          <input
            type="text"
            style={{ ...styles.field, opacity: labelLocked ? 0.55 : 1 }}
            value={label}
            onChange={(e) => setLabel(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="例如：股票、基金、加密貨幣"
            readOnly={labelLocked}
            maxLength={10}
          />

          <div style={{ ...styles.fieldLabel, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
            <span>圖示</span>
            <div style={styles.lockRow}>
              <span style={{ ...styles.lockLabel, color: iconLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 4 }}>
                <TypeIcon name={iconLocked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'} size={12} color={iconLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)'} />
                {iconLocked ? '鎖定中' : '已解鎖'}
              </span>
              <div
                style={{ ...styles.toggleTrack, background: iconLocked ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--mint)' }}
                onClick={() => setIconLocked((v) => !v)}
              >
                <div style={{ ...styles.toggleThumb, transform: iconLocked ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(18px)' }} />
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div style={{ ...styles.iconGrid, opacity: iconLocked ? 0.55 : 1, pointerEvents: iconLocked ? 'none' : 'auto' }}>
            {TYPE_ICONS.map((ic) => {
              const selected = icon === ic;
              const finalColor = adjustShade(color, shade);
              return (
                <div
                  key={ic}
                  tabIndex={-1}
                  style={{
                    ...styles.iconCell,
                    ...(selected
                      ? { background: finalColor, outline: '2px solid #fff', outlineOffset: '-2px' }
                      : {}),
                  }}
                  onClick={() => setIcon(ic)}
                >
                  <TypeIcon name={ic} size={36} color={selected ? '#fff' : 'var(--text-dim)'} />
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>

          <div style={{ ...styles.sectionLabel, marginTop: 14 }}>
            <span>顏色</span>
            <div style={styles.colorTargetSwitch}>
              <div
                style={{
                  ...styles.colorTargetBtn,
                  ...(palette === 'pastel' ? styles.colorTargetBtnActive : {}),
                }}
                onClick={() => setPalette('pastel')}
              >柔和</div>
              <div
                style={{
                  ...styles.colorTargetBtn,
                  ...(palette === 'solid' ? styles.colorTargetBtnActive : {}),
                }}
                onClick={() => setPalette('solid')}
              >純色</div>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div style={styles.colorGrid}>
            {(palette === 'pastel' ? TYPE_COLORS : SOLID_COLORS).map((co) => {
              const isSelected = color === co;
              return (
                <div
                  key={co}
                  tabIndex={-1}
                  style={{
                    ...styles.colorCell,
                    background: co,
                    ...(isSelected ? { outline: '2px solid #fff', outlineOffset: '-2px', transform: 'scale(1.1)' } : {}),
                  }}
                  onClick={() => setColor(co)}
                />
              );
            })}
          </div>

          {/* 深淺拉桿 */}
          <div style={{ ...styles.sectionLabel, marginTop: 14, marginBottom: 6 }}>
            <span>深淺</span>
            <span style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>
              {shade > 0 ? `亮 +${shade}%` : shade < 0 ? `暗 ${shade}%` : '原色'}
            </span>
          </div>
          <div style={styles.shadeRow} onTouchStart={(e) => e.stopPropagation()} onTouchMove={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
            <span style={styles.shadeLabelDim}>暗</span>
            <input
              type="range"
              min="-100"
              max="100"
              step="2"
              value={shade}
              onChange={(e) => {
                const v = parseInt(e.target.value);
                if (v !== shade && navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(3);
                setShade(v);
              }}
              onTouchStart={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
              onTouchMove={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
              style={{ ...styles.shadeSlider, accentColor: adjustShade(color, shade) }}
            />
            <span style={styles.shadeLabelDim}>亮</span>
          </div>

          <button style={{ ...styles.saveBtn, background: 'var(--mint)', color: 'var(--on-mint)', marginTop: 20 }} onClick={save}>儲存</button>
          <button style={{ ...styles.deleteBtn, marginTop: 6 }} onClick={cancel}>取消</button>
          {editingIdx !== 'new' && (
            <button style={{ ...styles.deleteBtn, marginTop: 6 }} onClick={() => remove(editingIdx)}>刪除此類型</button>
          )}
        </>
      ) : (
        <>
          <div style={styles.txnList}>
            {list.map((t, i) => (
              <Block
                key={t.value}
                blockKey={t.value}
                editMode={editMode}
                isFirst={i === 0}
                isLast={i === list.length - 1}
                onMoveUp={() => moveType(i, -1)}
                onMoveDown={() => moveType(i, 1)}
                onReorder={(newOrder) => reorderTypes(newOrder)}
                inline
              >
                <div style={styles.txn}>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.acctListIcon, background: t.color || '#f5c29c' }}>
                    <TypeIcon name={t.icon || 'box'} size={22} color="#fff" />
                  </div>
                  <div style={styles.txnInfo} onClick={() => !editMode && startEdit(i)}>
                    <div style={styles.txnCat}>{t.label}</div>
                  </div>
                  <div style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)', fontSize: 18, marginLeft: 4 }} onClick={() => !editMode && startEdit(i)}>›</div>
                </div>
              </Block>
            ))}
          </div>
          {!editMode && (
            <div style={{ height: 12 }} />
          )}
        </>
      )}
      </div>

      {/* 釘在底部的「＋ 新增帳戶類型」按鈕（僅列表模式顯示） */}
      {editingIdx === null && !editMode && (
        <div style={styles.stickyFooterBar}>
          <button
            style={{
              ...styles.saveBtn,
              background: 'var(--mint)',
              color: 'var(--on-mint)',
              marginTop: 0,
              width: '100%',
              padding: '14px 0 calc(14px + env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0px))',
              borderRadius: 12,
            }}
            onClick={startAdd}
          >
            ＋ 新增帳戶類型
          </button>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 帳戶管理 Sheet ============
// ============ 帳戶明細 Sheet（顯示該帳戶當月交易）============
function AccountDetailSheet({ state, catIcon, account, onClose, onClickTxn, onSell, onBuyHolding, onSellHolding, onUpdateMarketValue, onOpenHolding }) {
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(onClose, { skipInPickerBackdrop: true });
  const [currentMonth, setCurrentMonth] = useState(todayStr().slice(0, 7));
  const [showFilter, setShowFilter] = useState(false);
  const filterSwipe = useSwipeToClose(() => setShowFilter(false));
  // 進階篩選（啟用後取代月份模式）
  const [filterMode, setFilterMode] = useState(false);
  const [fStart, setFStart] = useState(todayStr().slice(0, 7) + '-01');
  const [fEnd, setFEnd] = useState(todayStr());
  const [fType, setFType] = useState('all'); // all/income/expense
  const [fKeyword, setFKeyword] = useState('');

  const shiftMonth = (delta) => {
    const [y, m] = currentMonth.split('-').map(Number);
    let ny = y, nm = m + delta;
    if (nm < 1) { nm = 12; ny -= 1; }
    if (nm > 12) { nm = 1; ny += 1; }
    setCurrentMonth(`${ny}-${String(nm).padStart(2, '0')}`);
  };

  const typeMeta = state.accountTypes.find((t) => t.value === account.type) || { label: '其他', icon: 'box', color: '#f5c29c' };
  const balance = calcBalance(account, state.transactions);

  // 決定顯示哪些交易
  let txns;
  if (filterMode) {
    txns = state.transactions
      .filter((t) => t.accountId === account.id)
      .filter((t) => t.date >= fStart && t.date <= fEnd)
      .filter((t) => fType === 'all' ? true : t.type === fType)
      .filter((t) => {
        if (!fKeyword.trim()) return true;
        const kw = fKeyword.trim().toLowerCase();
        return (t.category || '').toLowerCase().includes(kw) || (t.note || '').toLowerCase().includes(kw);
      })
      .sort((a, b) => b.date.localeCompare(a.date) || (b.createdAt || 0) - (a.createdAt || 0));
  } else {
    txns = txnsInMonth(account, state.transactions, currentMonth);
  }

  // 統計
  const sumIncome = txns.filter((t) => t.type === 'income').reduce((s, t) => s + t.amount, 0);
  const sumExpense = txns.filter((t) => t.type === 'expense').reduce((s, t) => s + t.amount, 0);

  const applyFilter = () => {
    setFilterMode(true);
    setShowFilter(false);
  };

  const clearFilter = () => {
    setFilterMode(false);
    setShowFilter(false);
  };

  const [editMode, setEditMode] = useState(false);
  const [blockOrder, setBlockOrder] = useState(() => {
    const defaults = ['hero', 'holdings', 'monthBar', 'summary', 'list'];
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem('ledger_account_order');
      if (raw) {
        const saved = JSON.parse(raw);
        const defSet = new Set(defaults);
        const filtered = Array.isArray(saved) ? saved.filter((k) => defSet.has(k)) : [];
        // 缺的 block 依序按 defaults 中的位置插入(而不是直接堆到後面)
        const missing = defaults.filter((k) => !filtered.includes(k));
        if (missing.length === 0) return filtered;
        // 對每個缺的 block,找出它在 defaults 中的下一個已存在的 block,插入到它前面
        const result = [...filtered];
        for (const miss of missing) {
          const defIdx = defaults.indexOf(miss);
          // 找 defaults 中此位置之後第一個已在 result 裡的
          let nextKey = null;
          for (let i = defIdx + 1; i < defaults.length; i++) {
            if (result.includes(defaults[i])) { nextKey = defaults[i]; break; }
          }
          if (nextKey) {
            const insertAt = result.indexOf(nextKey);
            result.splice(insertAt, 0, miss);
          } else {
            result.push(miss); // 找不到下一個就放最後
          }
        }
        return result;
      }
    } catch {}
    return defaults;
  });
  React.useEffect(() => {
    try { localStorage.setItem('ledger_account_order', JSON.stringify(blockOrder)); } catch {}
  }, [blockOrder]);
  const moveBlock = (key, dir) => {
    setBlockOrder((prev) => {
      const i = prev.indexOf(key);
      if (i < 0) return prev;
      const j = i + dir;
      if (j < 0 || j >= prev.length) return prev;
      const next = [...prev];
      [next[i], next[j]] = [next[j], next[i]];
      return next;
    });
  };

  return (
    <div
      data-sheet="true"
      style={{
        ...styles.sheet,
        transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
        transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
      }}
      ref={swipe.ref}
    >
      <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
        <div style={{ width: 50 }} />
        <div style={styles.sheetTitle}>{account.name}</div>
        <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 4, minWidth: 50, justifyContent: 'flex-end' }}>
          {!editMode && (
            <button
              style={{
                ...styles.editOrderBtn,
                display: 'flex',
                alignItems: 'center',
                justifyContent: 'center',
              }}
              onClick={() => setShowFilter(true)}
              aria-label="搜尋"
            >
              <TypeIcon name="search" size={16} color="var(--text-dim)" />
            </button>
          )}
          <EditOrderButton editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />
        </div>
      </div>

      <EditModeBanner editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />

      <div style={styles.sheetScroll} data-scroll-container>
      {blockOrder.map((blockKey, idx) => {
        const blockProps = {
          blockKey,
          editMode,
          isFirst: idx === 0,
          isLast: idx === blockOrder.length - 1,
          onMoveUp: () => moveBlock(blockKey, -1),
          onMoveDown: () => moveBlock(blockKey, 1),
          onReorder: (newOrder) => setBlockOrder(newOrder),
          inline: true,
        };

        if (blockKey === 'hero') {
          return (
            <Block key="hero" {...blockProps}>
              <div style={styles.acctHeroCard}>
                <div style={{ ...styles.acctListIcon, background: typeMeta.color || '#f5c29c', width: 52, height: 52 }}>
                  <TypeIcon name={typeMeta.icon || 'box'} size={26} color="#fff" />
                </div>
                <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                  <div style={styles.acctHeroMeta}>{typeMeta.label}</div>
                  <div style={styles.acctHeroBalance}>{balance.toLocaleString()}</div>
                  <div style={styles.acctHeroInit}>
                    初始 {(() => { const ia = account.initAmount || 0; return ia.toLocaleString(); })()}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        // 持股區塊(僅 invest 帳戶)
        if (blockKey === 'holdings' && account.type === 'invest' && (account.investSubType || 'stock') === 'stock') {
          const myHoldings = state.holdings.filter((h) => h.accountId === account.id);
          const activeHoldings = myHoldings.filter((h) => holdingShares(h, state.trades) > 0);

          return (
            <Block key="holdings" {...blockProps}>
              {/* 區塊內標題(因為拿掉了 Block 的 inline title,改用區塊內標籤,讓內容滿版) */}
              <div style={{
                fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontWeight: 500,
                marginBottom: 8, paddingLeft: 4,
              }}>
                持股
              </div>
              {/* 持股列表(精簡:每張卡片只 symbol + 股數 + 市值,點開進詳情) */}
              {activeHoldings.length === 0 ? (
                <div style={{
                  padding: '24px 16px',
                  textAlign: 'center',
                  color: 'var(--text-faint)',
                  fontSize: 13,
                }}>
                  尚未持有任何股票
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 8 }}>
                  {activeHoldings.map((h) => {
                    const shares = holdingShares(h, state.trades);
                    const market = h.marketValue || 0;
                    return (
                      <div
                        key={h.id}
                        onClick={() => onOpenHolding && onOpenHolding(h)}
                        style={{
                          padding: '14px',
                          borderRadius: 12,
                          background: 'var(--bg-card)',
                          border: '1px solid var(--border)',
                          cursor: 'pointer',
                          display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 12,
                        }}
                      >
                        <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                          <div style={{ fontSize: 16, fontWeight: 700 }}>{h.symbol}</div>
                          <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginTop: 4 }}>
                            {shares.toLocaleString()} 股
                          </div>
                        </div>
                        <div style={{ textAlign: 'right' }}>
                          {market > 0 ? (
                            <>
                              <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>市值</div>
                              <div style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 600 }}>{fmt(market)}</div>
                            </>
                          ) : (
                            <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--mint-text)' }}>點此編輯市值</div>
                          )}
                        </div>
                        <div style={{ fontSize: 18, color: 'var(--text-faint)' }}>›</div>
                      </div>
                    );
                  })}
                </div>
              )}

              {/* + 買進按鈕 */}
              <button
                onClick={() => onBuyHolding && onBuyHolding(account, null)}
                style={{
                  marginTop: 10, width: '100%',
                  padding: '12px',
                  background: 'var(--mint)', color: '#fff',
                  border: 'none', borderRadius: 12,
                  fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600,
                  cursor: 'pointer',
                }}
              >+ 買進股票</button>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'monthBar') {
          return (
            <Block key="monthBar" {...blockProps}>
              {filterMode ? (
                <div style={styles.filterBadge}>
                  <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                    <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)' }}>篩選結果</div>
                    <div style={{ fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text)' }}>
                      {fStart.replace(/-/g, '/')} ~ {fEnd.replace(/-/g, '/')}
                      {fType !== 'all' && ` · ${fType === 'income' ? '收入' : '支出'}`}
                      {fKeyword && ` · "${fKeyword}"`}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <div style={styles.filterClearBtn} onClick={() => !editMode && clearFilter()}>✕</div>
                </div>
              ) : (
                <div style={styles.acctMonthBar}>
                  <div style={styles.dpNav} onClick={() => !editMode && shiftMonth(-1)}>‹</div>
                  <div style={styles.dpMonthTitle}>
                    {currentMonth.slice(0, 4)} 年 {parseInt(currentMonth.slice(5, 7))} 月
                  </div>
                  <div style={styles.dpNav} onClick={() => !editMode && shiftMonth(1)}>›</div>
                </div>
              )}
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'summary') {
          return (
            <Block key="summary" {...blockProps}>
              <div style={styles.acctMonthSummary}>
                <div>
                  <div style={styles.acctSumLabel}>收入</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.acctSumVal, color: 'var(--mint-text)' }}>+{sumIncome.toLocaleString()}</div>
                </div>
                <div>
                  <div style={styles.acctSumLabel}>支出</div>
                  <div style={{ ...styles.acctSumVal, color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>−{sumExpense.toLocaleString()}</div>
                </div>
                <div>
                  <div style={styles.acctSumLabel}>淨額</div>
                  <div style={styles.acctSumVal}>
                    {sumIncome - sumExpense >= 0 ? '+' : ''}{(sumIncome - sumExpense).toLocaleString()}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </Block>
          );
        }

        if (blockKey === 'list') {
          return (
            <Block key="list" {...blockProps}>
              {txns.length === 0 ? (
                <div style={styles.emptyAccountHint}>{filterMode ? '無符合條件的交易' : '本月暫無交易'}</div>
              ) : (
                <div style={styles.txnList}>
                  {txns.map((t) => (
                    <TxnRow
                      key={t.id}
                      txn={t}
                      state={state}
                      catIcon={catIcon}
                      onClick={() => !editMode && onClickTxn(t)}
                    />
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </Block>
          );
        }

        return null;
      })}
      </div>

      {/* 篩選彈窗 */}
      {showFilter && (
        <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.actionMenuBackdrop} onClick={() => setShowFilter(false)} {...filterSwipe}>
          <div style={styles.filterCard} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
            <div style={styles.actionMenuTitle}>篩選條件</div>

            <div style={styles.fieldLabel}>起始日期</div>
            <input
              type="date"
              style={styles.field}
              value={fStart}
              onChange={(e) => setFStart(e.target.value)}
            />

            <div style={styles.fieldLabel}>結束日期</div>
            <input
              type="date"
              style={styles.field}
              value={fEnd}
              onChange={(e) => setFEnd(e.target.value)}
            />

            <div style={styles.fieldLabel}>類型</div>
            <div style={styles.typeToggle}>
              {[
                { v: 'all', l: '全部' },
                { v: 'expense', l: '支出' },
                { v: 'income', l: '收入' },
              ].map((opt) => (
                <button
                  key={opt.v}
                  onClick={() => setFType(opt.v)}
                  style={{
                    ...styles.typeBtn,
                    ...(fType === opt.v
                      ? opt.v === 'income' ? { background: 'var(--mint)', color: 'var(--on-mint)' }
                      : opt.v === 'expense' ? { background: 'var(--pink)', color: 'var(--on-pink)' }
                      : { background: 'var(--accent)', color: '#fff' }
                      : {}),
                  }}
                >{opt.l}</button>
              ))}
            </div>

            <div style={styles.fieldLabel}>關鍵字（非必填）</div>
            <input
              type="text"
              style={styles.field}
              value={fKeyword}
              onChange={(e) => setFKeyword(e.target.value)}
              placeholder="搜尋分類或備註"
            />

            <button style={{ ...styles.saveBtn, background: 'var(--mint)', color: 'var(--on-mint)', marginTop: 20 }} onClick={applyFilter}>套用</button>
            <button style={{ ...styles.deleteBtn, marginTop: 6 }} onClick={() => setShowFilter(false)}>取消</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

function AccountsSheet({ state, setState, toast, toastRich, onClose, initialEditId, onOpenDetail, setConfirmDialog, fadingAccountIds: fadingProp, setFadingAccountIds: setFadingProp }) {
  // 如果父層沒傳就用本地的(避免 crash)
  const [localFading, setLocalFading] = useState(() => new Set());
  const fadingAccountIds = fadingProp || localFading;
  const setFadingAccountIds = setFadingProp || setLocalFading;
  const wantNew = initialEditId === '__new__';
  const initial = (!wantNew && initialEditId) ? state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === initialEditId) : null;
  const isEmpty = state.accounts.length === 0;
  const firstType = (state.accountTypes[0]?.value) || 'cash';
  // 有 initialEditId='__new__' → 直接新增；有具體 id → 編輯該帳戶；沒帳戶 → 新增模式；否則顯示列表
  const [editingId, setEditingId] = useState(wantNew ? 'new' : (initial ? initial.id : (isEmpty ? 'new' : null)));
  const [name, setName] = useState(initial ? initial.name : '');
  const [type, setType] = useState(initial ? initial.type : firstType);
  const [initAmount, setInitAmount] = useState(initial && initial.initAmount != null ? String(initial.initAmount) : '');
  // 虛擬帳戶:創建時決定,之後鎖死。刪除時不會帶走相關紀錄(僅在結餘 = 0 時)。
  const [virtual, setVirtual] = useState(initial ? !!initial.virtual : false);
  // 投資子類型:'general' = 一般投資 / 'stock' = 股票投資(顯示持股 UI)
  // 預設 stock(維持既有體驗);只在 type === 'invest' 時生效
  const [investSubType, setInvestSubType] = useState(initial ? (initial.investSubType || 'stock') : 'stock');
  const [showAdvanced, setShowAdvanced] = useState(false);
  const [showTypeManage, setShowTypeManage] = useState(false);
  const [actionMenu, setActionMenu] = useState(null); // 選中的帳戶（彈動作選單）
  // 一般帳戶刪除模式選擇:{ acct, expenseCount, incomeCount, transferGroups, balance, allRelatedTxnIds, transferIds } | null
  const [deleteModeChoice, setDeleteModeChoice] = useState(null);
  // 對話框打開時預設鎖定,使用者要先解鎖才能點選兩個刪除選項(防誤觸)
  const [deleteModeLocked, setDeleteModeLocked] = useState(true);
  const [editMode, setEditMode] = useState(false); // 排序模式
  const actionMenuSwipe = useSwipeToClose(() => setActionMenu(null));
  // 列表捲動位置記憶 — 點帳戶進入編輯時 startEdit() 同步記住,
  // 退回列表時透過 effect 還原(等內容換回列表後再設 scrollTop)
  const scrollContainerRef = React.useRef(null);
  const savedScrollTopRef = React.useRef(0);
  const prevEditingIdRef = React.useRef(editingId);
  React.useEffect(() => {
    const wasEditing = prevEditingIdRef.current;
    const isEditing = editingId;
    if (wasEditing && !isEditing && scrollContainerRef.current) {
      // 從編輯切回列表 → 還原位置(用 rAF 確保 DOM 已更新)
      requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        if (scrollContainerRef.current) {
          scrollContainerRef.current.scrollTop = savedScrollTopRef.current;
        }
      });
    }
    prevEditingIdRef.current = editingId;
  }, [editingId]);
  // 防誤觸：預設「編輯現有帳戶」時鎖住，「新增」時解鎖
  const [nameLocked, setNameLocked] = useState(() => !!initial);
  const [amountLocked, setAmountLocked] = useState(() => !!initial);
  const [typeLocked, setTypeLocked] = useState(() => !!initial);
  // 投資模式鎖定:切換會影響持股 UI 跟總資產計算,所以加鎖防誤觸
  const [subTypeLocked, setSubTypeLocked] = useState(() => !!initial);
  // 虛擬標籤鎖定(視覺一致性,讓進階選項所有切換項都有相同的鎖頭 UI)
  const [virtualLocked, setVirtualLocked] = useState(() => !!initial);

  // 依 DOM 順序重排帳戶
  const reorderAccounts = (newIdOrder) => {
    setState((s) => {
      const map = new Map(s.accounts.map((a) => [a.id, a]));
      const reordered = newIdOrder.map((id) => map.get(id)).filter(Boolean);
      // 加上任何漏網的（理論上不會發生）
      s.accounts.forEach((a) => { if (!newIdOrder.includes(a.id)) reordered.push(a); });
      return { ...s, accounts: reordered };
    });
  };
  const moveAccount = (id, dir) => {
    setState((s) => {
      const i = s.accounts.findIndex((a) => a.id === id);
      if (i < 0) return s;
      const j = i + dir;
      if (j < 0 || j >= s.accounts.length) return s;
      const next = [...s.accounts];
      [next[i], next[j]] = [next[j], next[i]];
      return { ...s, accounts: next };
    });
  };

  const startAdd = () => {
    setEditingId('new');
    setName('');
    setType(firstType);
    setInitAmount('');
    setVirtual(false);
    setInvestSubType('stock'); // 預設股票模式
    // 新增時預設解鎖，方便立即輸入
    setNameLocked(false);
    setAmountLocked(false);
    setTypeLocked(false);
    setSubTypeLocked(false);
    setVirtualLocked(false);
  };

  const startEdit = (a) => {
    // 同步記住列表捲動位置(這個必須在 setState 之前,否則內容會被替換,scrollTop 變 0)
    if (scrollContainerRef.current) {
      savedScrollTopRef.current = scrollContainerRef.current.scrollTop;
    }
    setEditingId(a.id);
    setName(a.name);
    setType(a.type);
    setInitAmount(a.initAmount != null ? String(a.initAmount) : '');
    setVirtual(!!a.virtual);
    setInvestSubType(a.investSubType || 'stock'); // 既有資料沒此欄位時當 stock
    // 編輯現有帳戶時預設鎖定,避免誤觸
    setNameLocked(true);
    setAmountLocked(true);
    setTypeLocked(true);
    setSubTypeLocked(true);
    setVirtualLocked(true);
  };

  const cancel = () => {
    // 若還沒有任何帳戶（第一次進來必須建立），直接關閉 sheet
    if (state.accounts.length === 0) {
      onClose();
      return;
    }
    setEditingId(null);
    setName('');
  };

  const save = () => {
    if (!name.trim()) return alert('請輸入帳戶名稱');
    const amt = initAmount.trim() === '' ? 0 : parseFloat(initAmount);
    let initAmt = isNaN(amt) ? 0 : amt;
    // 負債類型:初始金額一律存為負數(不管使用者輸入正數或負數)
    if (type === 'debt' && initAmt !== 0) {
      initAmt = -Math.abs(initAmt);
    }
    const trimmedName = name.trim();

    // 檢查名稱是否與其他帳戶重複(編輯時排除自己)
    const dupAcct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.name === trimmedName && a.id !== editingId && !a.isSystem);
    if (dupAcct) {
      if (toastRich) {
        toastRich({
          title: '名稱已被使用',
          amount: '✓', // 觸發 checkmark badge 模式;實際 icon 由 icon prop 決定
          icon: 'warn',
          amountColor: 'var(--pink)',
          lines: [`「${trimmedName}」`, '請改用其他名稱'],
        }, 1800);
      } else {
        alert(`名稱「${trimmedName}」已被使用`);
      }
      return;
    }

    if (editingId === 'new') {
      const newAcct = { id: 'a_' + uid().slice(2, 10), name: trimmedName, type, initAmount: initAmt, createdAt: Date.now() };
      if (virtual) newAcct.virtual = true;
      if (type === 'invest') newAcct.investSubType = investSubType;
      setState((s) => ({ ...s, accounts: [...s.accounts, newAcct] }));
      if (toastRich) {
        toastRich({
          title: '已新增帳戶',
          amount: '✓',
          amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
          lines: [`「${trimmedName}」`],
        }, 1400);
      } else {
        toast('已新增');
      }
      cancel();
      return;
    }
    // 編輯模式:檢查是否有實際變更
    const original = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === editingId);
    if (!original) { cancel(); return; }
    const newName = name.trim();
    const nameChanged = newName !== original.name;
    const typeChanged = type !== original.type;
    const initAmtChanged = initAmt !== (original.initAmount || 0);
    const subTypeChanged = type === 'invest' && investSubType !== (original.investSubType || 'stock');
    const virtualChanged = !!virtual !== !!original.virtual;

    // 沒任何變更 → 用 toastRich 強化提示,讓使用者明確知道沒有東西被改動
    if (!nameChanged && !typeChanged && !initAmtChanged && !subTypeChanged && !virtualChanged) {
      if (toastRich) {
        toastRich({
          title: '沒有任何變更',
          amount: '✓',  // 觸發徽章模式
          icon: 'info',  // 但用 ⓘ 圖示取代勾勾
          amountColor: 'var(--text-faint)',
          lines: [`「${original.name}」資料未調整`],
        }, 1400);
      } else {
        toast('沒有任何變更');
      }
      cancel();
      return;
    }

    // 計算受影響的紀錄數
    const relatedTxnCount = state.transactions.filter((t) => t.accountId === editingId).length;

    // 實際儲存的動作
    const doSave = () => {
      setState((s) => ({
        ...s,
        accounts: s.accounts.map((a) => {
          if (a.id !== editingId) return a;
          const updated = { ...a, name: newName, type, initAmount: initAmt };
          if (type === 'invest') {
            updated.investSubType = investSubType;
          } else {
            delete updated.investSubType; // 換成非 invest 類型時清掉
          }
          // 虛擬標籤
          if (virtual) {
            updated.virtual = true;
          } else {
            delete updated.virtual;
          }
          return updated;
        }),
      }));
      // 變更摘要 toast
      const changedParts = [];
      if (nameChanged) changedParts.push('名稱');
      if (typeChanged) changedParts.push('類型');
      if (initAmtChanged) changedParts.push('初始金額');
      if (subTypeChanged) changedParts.push('投資模式');
      if (virtualChanged) changedParts.push('虛擬標籤');
      if (toastRich) {
        toastRich(nameChanged ? {
          titleSegments: [
            '已更新', '\n',
            { text: '帳戶', color: 'var(--blue)' },
            ' ',
            changedParts.join('、'),
          ],
          amount: '✓',
          amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
          lines: [`「${original.name}」 → 「${newName}」`],
        } : {
          title: `已更新 ${changedParts.join('、')}`,
          amount: '✓',
          amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
          lines: [`「${newName}」`],
        }, nameChanged ? 3500 : 1400);
      } else {
        toast(`已更新 ${changedParts.join('、')}`);
      }
      cancel();
    };

    // 改了初始金額 → 跳確認對話框(這是有金融意義的操作)
    if (initAmtChanged && setConfirmDialog) {
      const oldAmt = original.initAmount || 0;
      const diff = initAmt - oldAmt;
      // 差額顯示帶正負號(包含 0 的情況也保險處理)
      const diffStr = diff >= 0 ? `+${fmt(diff)}` : `-${fmt(diff)}`;
      const bullets = [
        `• 原始金額 ${fmt(oldAmt)} → ${fmt(initAmt)} (差額 ${diffStr})`,
        relatedTxnCount > 0
          ? `• 此帳戶有 ${relatedTxnCount} 筆紀錄,當前餘額會跟著變動`
          : `• 此帳戶目前沒有紀錄,變更後直接反映在餘額`,
        '• 此動作無法復原',
      ];
      setConfirmDialog({
        title: '變更 初始金額',
        target: { label: '帳戶', name: original.name },
        message: `確定要變更「${original.name}」的初始金額?\n${bullets.join('\n')}`,
        confirmText: '確定變更',
        danger: true,
        onConfirm: doSave,
      });
      return;
    }

    // 只改了名稱/類型 → 直接存
    doSave();
  };

  const remove = (id) => {
    const acct = state.accounts.find((a) => a.id === id);
    const acctName = acct ? acct.name : '此帳戶';
    const isVirtual = !!acct?.virtual;
    const balance = acct ? calcBalance(acct, state.transactions) : 0;
    // 算受影響筆數
    const directTxns = state.transactions.filter((t) => t.accountId === id);
    const transferIds = new Set(directTxns.filter((t) => t.transferId).map((t) => t.transferId));
    // 轉帳組:不只 directTxns,連帶該 transferId 整組(因為刪除一邊會讓另一邊變孤兒)
    const allRelatedTxnIds = new Set(directTxns.map((t) => t.id));
    state.transactions.forEach((t) => {
      if (t.transferId && transferIds.has(t.transferId)) {
        allRelatedTxnIds.add(t.id);
      }
    });
    const expenseCount = directTxns.filter((t) => t.type === 'expense' && !t.transferId).length;
    const incomeCount = directTxns.filter((t) => t.type === 'income' && !t.transferId).length;
    const transferGroups = transferIds.size;

    if (!setConfirmDialog) {
      // fallback
      setState((s) => ({
        ...s,
        accounts: s.accounts.filter((a) => a.id !== id),
        transactions: s.transactions.filter((t) => !allRelatedTxnIds.has(t.id)),
      }));
      cancel();
      toast('已刪除');
      return;
    }

    if (directTxns.length === 0) {
      // 沒紀錄 — 簡單確認
      setConfirmDialog({
        title: '刪除帳戶',
        message: `確定刪除「${acctName}」?\n\n• 此帳戶目前沒有任何紀錄\n• 起始餘額 ${fmt(acct?.initAmount || 0)} 也會一併移除\n• 此動作無法復原`,
        confirmText: '刪除',
        danger: true,
        onConfirm: () => {
          setState((s) => ({ ...s, accounts: s.accounts.filter((a) => a.id !== id) }));
          cancel();
          toast('已刪除');
        },
        beforeConfirm: () => {
          setFadingAccountIds((prev) => { const next = new Set(prev); next.add(id); return next; });
          return new Promise((resolve) => setTimeout(resolve, 280));
        },
      });
    } else {
      // 有紀錄 — 開二選一對話框讓使用者選刪除模式
      // 選項 1:完整刪除(現有行為)— 帳戶+紀錄全刪
      // 選項 2:保留紀錄刪除 — 帳戶移除但紀錄烙印「(已刪)」標,統計不變
      setDeleteModeLocked(true); // 每次打開都重置回鎖定
      setDeleteModeChoice({
        acct,
        acctName,
        expenseCount,
        incomeCount,
        transferGroups,
        balance,
        allRelatedTxnIds,
        directCount: directTxns.length,
        id,
      });
    }
  };

  // 二選一對話框的兩個執行動作(被「有紀錄」分支呼叫)
  // 動作 A:完整刪除 — 帳戶+紀錄全刪(原本的行為)
  const performFullDelete = (info) => {
    const { id, allRelatedTxnIds } = info;
    setDeleteModeChoice(null);
    setFadingAccountIds((prev) => { const next = new Set(prev); next.add(id); return next; });
    setTimeout(() => {
      setState((s) => ({
        ...s,
        accounts: s.accounts.filter((a) => a.id !== id),
        transactions: s.transactions.filter((t) => !allRelatedTxnIds.has(t.id)),
      }));
      cancel();
      toast('已刪除帳戶與相關紀錄');
    }, 280);
  };
  // 動作 B:保留紀錄刪除 — 帳戶刪除,紀錄烙印「(已刪)」標,統計不變
  const performKeepRecordsDelete = (info) => {
    const { id, acctName, acct } = info;
    setDeleteModeChoice(null);
    setFadingAccountIds((prev) => { const next = new Set(prev); next.add(id); return next; });
    setTimeout(() => {
      setState((s) => {
      const acctCreatedAt = acct?.createdAt || null;
      // 把帳戶名稱「烙印」到相關紀錄上(直接屬於本帳戶的 + 對方端)
      // 用 _deletedAccountName / _deletedPeerName 既有機制
      const newTxns = s.transactions.map((t) => {
        if (t.accountId === id) {
          // 一般帳戶刪除:不只「不設」virtual,還要「主動清除」殘留標記
          // 避免上層 spread 不覆蓋既有屬性的問題
          const patched = {
            ...t,
            _deletedAccountName: acctName,
            ...(acctCreatedAt ? { _deletedAccountCreatedAt: acctCreatedAt } : {}),
          };
          if (acct?.virtual) {
            patched._deletedAccountVirtual = true;
          } else {
            // 一般帳戶:強制刪除可能殘留的 true 標記
            delete patched._deletedAccountVirtual;
          }
          return patched;
        }
        if (t.transferId && t.transferPeer) {
          if (t.transferPeer.fromId === id || t.transferPeer.toId === id) {
            const patched = {
              ...t,
              _deletedPeerName: acctName,
              ...(acctCreatedAt ? { _deletedPeerCreatedAt: acctCreatedAt } : {}),
            };
            if (acct?.virtual) {
              patched._deletedPeerVirtual = true;
            } else {
              delete patched._deletedPeerVirtual;
            }
            return patched;
          }
        }
        return t;
      });
      return {
        ...s,
        accounts: s.accounts.filter((a) => a.id !== id),
        transactions: newTxns,
      };
    });
    cancel();
    if (toastRich) {
      toastRich({
        title: '已刪除帳戶',
        amount: '✓',
        amountColor: 'var(--mint)',
        lines: [`「${acctName}」`, '歷史紀錄已保留'],
      }, 1800);
    } else {
      toast('已刪除,紀錄保留');
    }
    }, 280);
  };

  const moveAcct = (i, delta) => {
    const newIdx = i + delta;
    if (newIdx < 0 || newIdx >= state.accounts.length) return;
    setState((s) => {
      const arr = [...s.accounts];
      [arr[i], arr[newIdx]] = [arr[newIdx], arr[i]];
      return { ...s, accounts: arr };
    });
  };

  // swipe 返回邏輯:
  // - 若在編輯/新增表單中 → 取消表單，回到列表(而不是關閉整個 sheet)
  // - 若在列表 → 關閉 sheet
  // 注意:第一次進入且沒任何帳戶時,cancel() 會直接關閉 sheet,這是正確的
  const swipeBack = () => {
    if (editingId !== null) {
      cancel();
    } else {
      onClose();
    }
  };
  const swipe = useSwipeBack(swipeBack, { skipInPickerBackdrop: true });

  // 類型管理覆蓋層
  if (showTypeManage) {
    return (
      <AccountTypeManageSheet
        state={state}
        setState={setStateWithSync}
        toast={toast}
        toastRich={toastRich}
        onClose={() => setShowTypeManage(false)}
        setConfirmDialog={setConfirmDialog}
      />
    );
  }

  return (
    <div
      data-sheet="true"
      style={{
        ...styles.sheet,
        transform: `translateX(${swipe.dragX}px)`,
        transition: swipe.dragX === 0 ? 'transform 0.22s ease-out' : 'none',
      }}
      ref={swipe.ref}
    >
      <div style={styles.sheetHead}>
        <div style={{ width: 50 }} />
        <div style={styles.sheetTitle}>帳戶管理</div>
        <div style={{ minWidth: 50, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'flex-end' }}>
          {!editingId && <EditOrderButton editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />}
        </div>
      </div>

      <EditModeBanner editMode={editMode} setEditMode={setEditMode} />

      {/* 列表模式：總資產區釘在上面（不捲動） */}
      {!editingId && (() => {
        let totalAssets = 0, totalDebt = 0;
        state.accounts.forEach((a) => {
          // 投資帳戶且為股票模式 → 用市值計算;一般投資模式照舊用 calcBalance
          const isStockInvest = a.type === 'invest' && (a.investSubType || 'stock') === 'stock';
          const investSummary = isStockInvest
            ? investAccountSummary(a, state.holdings, state.trades)
            : null;
          const bal = investSummary && investSummary.totalCost > 0
            ? investSummary.totalMarket
            : calcBalance(a, state.transactions);
          // debt 帳戶:bal 為負才算負債(取絕對值);過度還款變正時算資產
          // 非 debt 帳戶:bal 為負才算負債(透支情境);其他算資產
          if (bal < 0) {
            totalDebt += Math.abs(bal);
          } else {
            totalAssets += bal;
          }
        });
        const net = totalAssets - totalDebt;
        return (
          <div style={styles.assetSummary}>
            <div style={styles.assetSumBox}>
              <div style={styles.assetSumLabel}>總資產</div>
              <div style={{ ...styles.assetSumValue, color: 'var(--mint-text)' }}>
                {totalAssets.toLocaleString()}
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={styles.assetSumDivider} />
            <div style={styles.assetSumBox}>
              <div style={styles.assetSumLabel}>總負債</div>
              <div style={{ ...styles.assetSumValue, color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>
                {totalDebt.toLocaleString()}
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={styles.assetSumDivider} />
            <div style={styles.assetSumBox}>
              <div style={styles.assetSumLabel}>淨資產</div>
              <div style={{ ...styles.assetSumValue, color: net < 0 ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--text)' }}>
                {net.toLocaleString()}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      })()}

      {/* 捲動區 */}
      <div style={styles.sheetScroll} data-scroll-container ref={scrollContainerRef}>

      {editingId ? (
        <>
          <div style={{ ...styles.block, padding: '10px 12px', marginBottom: 10 }}>
            <div style={{ ...styles.sectionLabel, marginTop: 0, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
              <span>帳戶類型</span>
              <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10 }}>
                <span style={styles.gearBtn} onClick={() => setShowTypeManage(true)}>⚙️</span>
                <div style={styles.lockRow}>
                  <span style={{ ...styles.lockLabel, color: typeLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 4 }}>
                    <TypeIcon name={typeLocked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'} size={12} color={typeLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)'} />
                    {typeLocked ? '鎖定中' : '已解鎖'}
                  </span>
                  <div
                    style={{ ...styles.toggleTrack, background: typeLocked ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--mint)' }}
                    onClick={() => setTypeLocked((v) => !v)}
                  >
                    <div style={{ ...styles.toggleThumb, transform: typeLocked ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(18px)' }} />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ ...styles.acctTypeGrid, opacity: typeLocked ? 0.55 : 1, pointerEvents: typeLocked ? 'none' : 'auto' }}>
              {state.accountTypes.map((t) => {
                const selected = type === t.value;
                return (
                  <div
                    key={t.value}
                    tabIndex={-1}
                    style={{
                      ...styles.acctTypeCell,
                      ...(selected
                        ? { outline: `1.5px solid ${t.color || 'var(--mint)'}`, outlineOffset: '-1.5px', background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.08)' }
                        : {}),
                    }}
                    onClick={() => setType(t.value)}
                  >
                    <div style={{ ...styles.acctTypeIconBox, background: t.color || 'var(--bg)' }}>
                      <TypeIcon name={t.icon || 'box'} size={16} color="#fff" />
                    </div>
                    <div style={styles.acctTypeLabel}>{t.label}</div>
                  </div>
                );
              })}
            </div>
          </div>

          <div style={{ ...styles.block, padding: '10px 12px', marginBottom: 10 }}>
            <div style={{ ...styles.fieldLabel, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginTop: 0 }}>
              <span>帳戶名稱</span>
              <div style={styles.lockRow}>
                <span style={{ ...styles.lockLabel, color: nameLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 4 }}>
                  <TypeIcon name={nameLocked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'} size={12} color={nameLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)'} />
                  {nameLocked ? '鎖定中' : '已解鎖'}
                </span>
                <div
                  style={{ ...styles.toggleTrack, background: nameLocked ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--mint)' }}
                  onClick={() => setNameLocked((v) => !v)}
                >
                  <div style={{ ...styles.toggleThumb, transform: nameLocked ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(18px)' }} />
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style={{ position: 'relative', width: '100%' }}>
              <input
                type="text"
                style={{ ...styles.field, opacity: nameLocked ? 0.55 : 1 }}
                value={name}
                onChange={(e) => setName(e.target.value)}
                readOnly={nameLocked}
                placeholder={
                  type === 'bank' ? '例如：玉山銀行、台新活存' :
                  type === 'card' ? '例如:中信卡、玉山現金回饋' :
                  type === 'cash' ? '例如:現金、零用金' :
                  type === 'epay' ? '例如:街口支付、LINE Pay' :
                  type === 'invest' ? '例如:元大證券、定存' :
                  '請輸入帳戶名稱'
                }
                maxLength={20}
              />
              {name.length > 0 && !nameLocked && (
                <div style={{
                  position: 'absolute',
                  bottom: 4,
                  right: 10,
                  fontSize: 10,
                  color: name.length >= 18 ? 'var(--pink)' : 'var(--text-faint)',
                  pointerEvents: 'none',
                  fontVariantNumeric: 'tabular-nums',
                  fontWeight: name.length >= 18 ? 600 : 400,
                }}>
                  {name.length} / 20
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>

          <div style={{ ...styles.block, padding: '10px 12px', marginBottom: 10 }}>
            <div style={{ ...styles.fieldLabel, display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginTop: 0 }}>
              <span>初始金額</span>
              <div style={styles.lockRow}>
                <span style={{ ...styles.lockLabel, color: amountLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 4 }}>
                  <TypeIcon name={amountLocked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'} size={12} color={amountLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)'} />
                  {amountLocked ? '鎖定中' : '已解鎖'}
                </span>
                <div
                  style={{ ...styles.toggleTrack, background: amountLocked ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--mint)' }}
                  onClick={() => setAmountLocked((v) => !v)}
                >
                  <div style={{ ...styles.toggleThumb, transform: amountLocked ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(18px)' }} />
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <input
              type="text"
              inputMode="decimal"
              style={{ ...styles.field, opacity: amountLocked ? 0.55 : 1 }}
              value={initAmount}
              onChange={(e) => {
                const v = e.target.value;
                if (v === '' || /^-?\d*\.?\d*$/.test(v)) setInitAmount(v);
              }}
              readOnly={amountLocked}
              placeholder="自行輸入金額（可留空）"
            />
          </div>

          {/* 進階選項:虛擬標籤 + 投資模式(invest 類型才顯示投資模式) */}
          <div style={{ marginBottom: 10 }}>
              {/* 摺疊觸發器 */}
              <div
                onClick={() => setShowAdvanced((v) => !v)}
                style={{
                  display: 'flex',
                  alignItems: 'center',
                  justifyContent: 'space-between',
                  padding: '10px 12px',
                  cursor: 'pointer',
                  WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
                  userSelect: 'none',
                }}
              >
                <span style={{ fontSize: 13, color: 'var(--text-dim)', fontWeight: 500 }}>
                  進階選項
                </span>
                <span style={{
                  fontSize: 12,
                  color: 'var(--text-faint)',
                  transform: showAdvanced ? 'rotate(180deg)' : 'rotate(0deg)',
                  transition: 'transform 0.2s',
                  display: 'inline-block',
                }}>▾</span>
              </div>

              {/* 展開內容 */}
              {showAdvanced && (
                <div style={{ ...styles.block, padding: '10px 12px', marginTop: 4, display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 12 }}>
                  {/* 投資模式選擇:只在 type === 'invest' 顯示 */}
                  {type === 'invest' && (
                    <div>
                      <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 8 }}>
                        <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 600, color: 'var(--text)' }}>
                          投資模式
                        </span>
                        <div style={styles.lockRow}>
                          <span style={{ ...styles.lockLabel, color: subTypeLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 4 }}>
                            <TypeIcon name={subTypeLocked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'} size={12} color={subTypeLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)'} />
                            {subTypeLocked ? '鎖定中' : '已解鎖'}
                          </span>
                          <div
                            style={{ ...styles.toggleTrack, background: subTypeLocked ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--mint)' }}
                            onClick={() => setSubTypeLocked((v) => !v)}
                          >
                            <div style={{ ...styles.toggleThumb, transform: subTypeLocked ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(18px)' }} />
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                      <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8, opacity: subTypeLocked ? 0.55 : 1, pointerEvents: subTypeLocked ? 'none' : 'auto' }}>
                        {[
                          { value: 'stock', label: '股票模式' },
                          { value: 'general', label: '一般模式' },
                        ].map((opt) => (
                          <div
                            key={opt.value}
                            onClick={() => { if (!subTypeLocked) setInvestSubType(opt.value); }}
                            style={{
                              flex: 1, textAlign: 'center',
                              padding: '10px 12px', borderRadius: 10,
                              fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600,
                              background: investSubType === opt.value ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--bg-card)',
                              color: investSubType === opt.value ? '#fff' : 'var(--text-dim)',
                              border: `1.5px solid ${investSubType === opt.value ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--border)'}`,
                              cursor: subTypeLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
                              userSelect: 'none',
                              transition: 'all 0.15s',
                            }}
                          >
                            {opt.label}
                          </div>
                        ))}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  )}

                  {/* 虛擬標籤 */}
                  <div>
                    <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between', marginBottom: 8 }}>
                      <span style={{ fontSize: 13, fontWeight: 600, color: 'var(--text)' }}>
                        虛擬標籤
                      </span>
                      <div style={styles.lockRow}>
                        <span style={{ ...styles.lockLabel, color: virtualLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 4 }}>
                          <TypeIcon name={virtualLocked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'} size={12} color={virtualLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--mint)'} />
                          {virtualLocked ? '鎖定中' : '已解鎖'}
                        </span>
                        <div
                          style={{ ...styles.toggleTrack, background: virtualLocked ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--mint)' }}
                          onClick={() => setVirtualLocked((v) => !v)}
                        >
                          <div style={{ ...styles.toggleThumb, transform: virtualLocked ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(18px)' }} />
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <div
                      style={{
                        display: 'flex',
                        alignItems: 'flex-start',
                        gap: 10,
                        cursor: virtualLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
                        userSelect: 'none',
                        WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
                        opacity: virtualLocked ? 0.55 : 1,
                      }}
