                      onClick={() => { if (!virtualLocked) setVirtual((v) => !v); }}
                    >
                      <div style={{
                        width: 20, height: 20, borderRadius: 5,
                        border: `2px solid ${virtual ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--border)'}`,
                        background: virtual ? 'var(--mint)' : 'transparent',
                        display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center',
                        flexShrink: 0,
                        marginTop: 2,
                        transition: 'all 0.15s',
                      }}>
                        {virtual && (
                          <svg width="12" height="12" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="var(--on-mint)" strokeWidth="3.5" strokeLinecap="round" strokeLinejoin="round">
                            <polyline points="5 12 10 17 19 8" />
                          </svg>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                        <div style={{ fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 600, color: 'var(--text)' }}>
                          設為虛擬帳戶
                        </div>
                        <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: 'var(--text-dim)', marginTop: 4, lineHeight: 1.6 }}>
                          標示為「虛擬」,提醒這個餘額不是現金,而是能用在代墊、暫時收支等概念性金流。適合「暫時支出但會回收」的錢,避免忘記它的存在。
                        </div>
                        <div style={{ fontSize: 11, color: 'var(--text-faint)', marginTop: 6, lineHeight: 1.5 }}>
                          例如:幫朋友刷卡買手機,等他還錢
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>

          <button style={{ ...styles.addIncBtn, width: '100%', marginTop: 20 }} onClick={save}>儲存</button>
          <button style={{ ...styles.deleteBtn, marginTop: 8 }} onClick={cancel}>取消</button>
          {editingId !== 'new' && (
            <button style={{ ...styles.deleteBtn, marginTop: 8 }} onClick={() => remove(editingId)}>刪除帳戶</button>
          )}
        </>
      ) : (
        <>
          <div style={{ display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 4 }}>
            {state.accounts.map((a, i) => {
              const typeMeta = state.accountTypes.find((t) => t.value === a.type) || { label: '其他', icon: 'box', color: '#f5c29c' };
              // 投資帳戶且為股票模式 → 顯示市值;否則用既有 calcBalance
              const isStockInvest = a.type === 'invest' && (a.investSubType || 'stock') === 'stock';
              const investSummary = isStockInvest
                ? investAccountSummary(a, state.holdings, state.trades)
                : null;
              const bal = investSummary && investSummary.totalCost > 0
                ? investSummary.totalMarket
                : calcBalance(a, state.transactions);
              const balColor = bal < 0 ? 'var(--pink)' : bal > 0 ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--text-faint)';
              const balDisplay = bal.toLocaleString();
              const isFading = fadingAccountIds.has(a.id);
              // 只在淡出時包 wrapper(平常不包,避免影響拖曳邏輯找父節點)
              const blockEl = (
                <Block
                  blockKey={a.id}
                  editMode={editMode}
                  isFirst={i === 0}
                  isLast={i === state.accounts.length - 1}
                  onMoveUp={() => moveAccount(a.id, -1)}
                  onMoveDown={() => moveAccount(a.id, 1)}
                  onReorder={(newOrder) => reorderAccounts(newOrder)}
                  inline
                  compactInline
                >
                  <div
                    style={{
                      ...styles.txn,
                      border: '1px dashed var(--border)',
                      borderRadius: 10,
                      padding: '6px 10px',
                    }}
                    onClick={() => !editMode && setActionMenu(a)}
                  >
                    <div style={{ ...styles.acctListIcon, width: 36, height: 36, borderRadius: 10, background: typeMeta.color || '#f5c29c' }}>
                      <TypeIcon name={typeMeta.icon || 'box'} size={18} color="#fff" />
                    </div>
                    <div style={styles.txnInfo}>
                      <div style={styles.txnCat}>
                        {a.name}
                        {a.virtual && (
                          <span style={{
                            color: 'var(--mint)',
                            fontSize: 11,
                            fontWeight: 500,
                            marginLeft: 8,
                            padding: '1px 6px',
                            borderRadius: 4,
                            background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.12)',
                            verticalAlign: 'middle',
                          }}>虛擬</span>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      <div style={styles.txnMeta}>
                        {typeMeta.label} · 餘額 <span style={{ color: balColor, fontWeight: bal !== 0 ? 600 : 400 }}>{balDisplay}</span>
                        {investSummary && investSummary.totalCost > 0 && (
                          <span style={{
                            marginLeft: 8,
                            color: investSummary.totalPnl >= 0 ? 'var(--mint-text)' : 'var(--pink-text)',
                            fontWeight: 500,
                          }}>
                            {investSummary.totalPnl >= 0 ? '+' : ''}{((investSummary.totalPnl / investSummary.totalCost) * 100).toFixed(1)}%
                          </span>
                        )}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <div style={{ color: 'var(--text-faint)', fontSize: 18, marginLeft: 4 }}>›</div>
                  </div>
                </Block>
              );
              // 淡出時包 wrapper,正常時直接渲染 Block(避免破壞拖曳結構)
              if (isFading) {
                return (
                  <div
                    key={a.id}
                    style={{
                      opacity: 0,
                      transform: 'translateX(40px) scale(0.96)',
                      maxHeight: 0,
                      marginTop: 0,
                      marginBottom: 0,
                      overflow: 'hidden',
                      transition: 'opacity 0.25s ease-out, transform 0.25s ease-out, max-height 0.28s ease-out, margin 0.28s ease-out',
                      pointerEvents: 'none',
                    }}
                  >
                    {blockEl}
                  </div>
                );
              }
              return blockEl;
            })}
          </div>
          {!editMode && (
            <div style={{ height: 12 }} />
          )}
        </>
      )}
      </div>

      {/* 釘在底部的「＋ 新增帳戶」按鈕（僅列表模式顯示） */}
      {!editingId && !editMode && (
        <div style={styles.stickyFooterBar}>
          <button
            style={{
              ...styles.addIncBtn,
              width: '100%',
              padding: '14px 0 calc(14px + env(safe-area-inset-bottom, 0px))',
              borderRadius: 12,
            }}
            onClick={startAdd}
          >＋ 新增帳戶</button>
        </div>
      )}





      {/* 一般帳戶有紀錄時 — 二選一刪除模式對話框 */}
      {deleteModeChoice && (() => {
        const info = deleteModeChoice;
        const balanceText = info.balance !== 0 ? fmtSigned(info.balance) : '0';
        // 構築「完整刪除」第一條 bullet:依實際資料動態組成「支出 N 筆紀錄永久消失」
        const fullDeleteParts = [];
        if (info.expenseCount > 0) fullDeleteParts.push(`支出 ${info.expenseCount} 筆`);
        if (info.incomeCount > 0) fullDeleteParts.push(`收入 ${info.incomeCount} 筆`);
        if (info.transferGroups > 0) fullDeleteParts.push(`轉帳 ${info.transferGroups} 筆`);
        const fullDeleteFirstBullet = `${fullDeleteParts.join('、')} 紀錄永久消失`;
        // 共通事實樣式:位置/間距保留,但拿掉灰底,改用透明底+左邊細指示線淡化
        const commonFactStyle = {
          padding: '8px 12px',
          background: 'transparent',
          fontSize: 12,
          color: 'var(--text-dim)',
          marginTop: 10,
          marginBottom: 8,
        };
        return (
          <div
            data-picker-backdrop="true"
            style={styles.pickerBackdrop}
            onClick={() => setDeleteModeChoice(null)}
          >
            <div style={styles.pickerCard} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
              {/* 標題:純「刪除帳戶」+ 防誤觸鎖。帳戶名抽到下方 target 卡片 */}
              <div style={{
                ...styles.pickerTitle,
                fontSize: 17,
                fontWeight: 700,
                padding: '14px 18px',
                display: 'flex',
                alignItems: 'center',
                justifyContent: 'space-between',
                gap: 12,
                borderBottom: '1px solid var(--border)',
              }}>
                <span style={{ flex: 1, textAlign: 'left' }}>
                  <span style={{ color: 'var(--pink)', marginRight: 6 }}>刪除</span>
                  <span style={{ color: 'var(--text)' }}>帳戶</span>
                </span>
                <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8, flexShrink: 0 }}>
                  <span style={{ ...styles.lockLabel, color: deleteModeLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--pink)', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 4 }}>
                    <TypeIcon name={deleteModeLocked ? 'lock' : 'unlock'} size={12} color={deleteModeLocked ? 'var(--text-dim)' : 'var(--pink)'} />
                    {deleteModeLocked ? '鎖定中' : '已解鎖'}
                  </span>
                  <div
                    style={{ ...styles.toggleTrack, background: deleteModeLocked ? 'var(--bg-card)' : 'var(--pink)' }}
                    onClick={() => setDeleteModeLocked((v) => !v)}
                  >
                    <div style={{ ...styles.toggleThumb, transform: deleteModeLocked ? 'translateX(0)' : 'translateX(18px)' }} />
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Target 卡片:沿用 ConfirmDialog 的目標物件強調顯示 pattern */}
              <div style={{
                margin: '8px 16px 8px',
                padding: '10px 14px',
                background: 'rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.10)',
                border: '1px solid rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.25)',
                borderRadius: 10,
                display: 'flex',
                alignItems: 'center',
                gap: 10,
              }}>
                <div style={{
                  fontSize: 11,
                  color: 'var(--pink)',
                  fontWeight: 600,
                  letterSpacing: 0.5,
                  flexShrink: 0,
                  lineHeight: 1,
                }}>名稱</div>
                <div style={{
                  fontSize: 15,
                  color: 'var(--text)',
                  fontWeight: 600,
                  flex: 1,
                  overflow: 'hidden',
                  textOverflow: 'ellipsis',
                  whiteSpace: 'nowrap',
                  lineHeight: 1,
                }}>{info.acctName}</div>
              </div>

              {/* 兩個按鈕卡 */}
              <div style={{ padding: '0 14px 6px', display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: 10 }}>
                {/* 選項 1:保留紀錄刪除(推薦) */}
                <button
                  disabled={deleteModeLocked}
                  onClick={() => {
                    // 二次確認:用 ConfirmDialog 再問一次
                    setConfirmDialog && setConfirmDialog({
                      title: '確認 保留歷史紀錄',
                      target: { label: '名稱', name: info.acctName },
                      message: `將以「保留歷史紀錄」方式刪除帳戶。\n\n• 帳戶從清單移除\n• 收支紀錄完整保留並標示「帳號已刪」\n• 統計數字不受影響${info.balance !== 0 ? `\n• 帳戶餘額 ${balanceText} 從總資產扣除` : ''}\n\n確定要繼續嗎?`,
                      confirmText: '確認刪除',
                      danger: true,
                      onConfirm: () => performKeepRecordsDelete(info),
                    });
                  }}
                  style={{
                    width: '100%',
                    border: 'none',
                    background: 'rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.10)',
                    borderLeft: '3px solid var(--mint)',
                    borderRadius: 10,
                    padding: '14px 16px',
                    textAlign: 'left',
                    cursor: deleteModeLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
                    opacity: deleteModeLocked ? 0.5 : 1,
                    WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
                    fontFamily: 'inherit',
                    transition: 'opacity 0.2s',
                  }}
                >
                  <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8 }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--mint-text)' }}>保留歷史紀錄</span>
                    <span style={{
                      fontSize: 10, fontWeight: 700,
                      color: '#fff',
                      background: 'var(--mint)',
                      padding: '2px 7px',
                      borderRadius: 10,
                      letterSpacing: '0.3px',
                    }}>推薦</span>
                  </div>
                  {/* 共通事實:淡化處理 */}
                  <div style={commonFactStyle}>
                    帳戶從「帳戶清單」移除
                  </div>
                  {/* 差異點 bullets */}
                  <ul style={{
                    margin: 0,
                    paddingLeft: 16,
                    fontSize: 12,
                    color: 'var(--text-dim)',
                    lineHeight: 1.7,
                    listStyle: 'disc',
                  }}>
                    <li>收支紀錄保留,並標示「帳號已刪」</li>
                    <li>統計數字不受影響</li>
                    {info.balance !== 0 && (
                      <li>帳戶餘額 {balanceText} 從總資產扣除</li>
                    )}
                  </ul>
                </button>

                {/* 選項 2:完整刪除 */}
                <button
                  disabled={deleteModeLocked}
                  onClick={() => {
                    // 二次確認:用 ConfirmDialog 再問一次
                    setConfirmDialog && setConfirmDialog({
                      title: '確認 完整刪除',
                      target: { label: '名稱', name: info.acctName },
                      message: `將以「完整刪除」方式移除帳戶。\n\n• 帳戶與所有 ${info.directCount} 筆紀錄永久消失\n• 統計頁的歷史收支會跟著縮水\n• 此動作無法復原\n\n確定要繼續嗎?`,
                      confirmText: '確認刪除',
                      danger: true,
                      onConfirm: () => performFullDelete(info),
                    });
                  }}
                  style={{
                    width: '100%',
                    border: 'none',
                    background: 'rgba(217, 104, 121, 0.08)',
                    borderLeft: '3px solid var(--pink)',
                    borderRadius: 10,
                    padding: '14px 16px',
                    textAlign: 'left',
                    cursor: deleteModeLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
                    opacity: deleteModeLocked ? 0.5 : 1,
                    WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
                    fontFamily: 'inherit',
                    transition: 'opacity 0.2s',
                  }}
                >
                  <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 8 }}>
                    <span style={{ fontSize: 15, fontWeight: 700, color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}>完整刪除</span>
                  </div>
                  {/* 共通事實:淡化處理(跟另一選項一致) */}
                  <div style={commonFactStyle}>
                    帳戶從「帳戶清單」移除
                  </div>
                  {/* 差異點 bullets */}
                  <ul style={{
                    margin: 0,
                    paddingLeft: 16,
                    fontSize: 12,
                    color: 'var(--text-dim)',
                    lineHeight: 1.7,
                    listStyle: 'disc',
                  }}>
                    <li>{fullDeleteFirstBullet}</li>
                    <li>統計頁的歷史收支會跟著縮水</li>
                    <li>此動作無法復原</li>
                  </ul>
                </button>
              </div>

              {/* 取消(獨立一行) */}
              <div
                onClick={() => setDeleteModeChoice(null)}
                style={{
                  padding: '14px',
                  textAlign: 'center',
                  fontSize: 14,
                  fontWeight: 500,
                  color: 'var(--text-dim)',
                  cursor: 'pointer',
                  borderTop: '1px solid var(--border)',
                  WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
                }}
              >取消</div>
            </div>
          </div>
        );
      })()}

      {/* 帳戶動作浮動選單(置中懸浮) */}
      {actionMenu && (() => {
        const typeMeta = state.accountTypes.find((t) => t.value === actionMenu.type) || { label: '其他', icon: 'box', color: '#f5c29c' };
        const bal = calcBalance(actionMenu, state.transactions);
        const balColor = bal < 0 ? 'var(--pink)' : bal > 0 ? 'var(--mint)' : 'var(--text-faint)';
        const balDisplay = bal.toLocaleString();
        return (
          <div data-picker-backdrop="true" style={styles.centerDialogBackdrop} onClick={() => setActionMenu(null)} {...actionMenuSwipe}>
            <div style={styles.centerDialogCard} onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}>
              <div style={styles.centerDialogHeader}>
                <div style={styles.centerDialogHeaderName}>{actionMenu.name}</div>
                <div style={styles.centerDialogHeaderMeta}>
                  {typeMeta.label} · 餘額 <span style={{ color: balColor, fontWeight: bal !== 0 ? 600 : 400 }}>{balDisplay}</span>
                </div>
              </div>
              <div style={styles.centerDialogDivider} />
            <div
              style={styles.centerDialogItem}
              onClick={() => {
                const acct = actionMenu;
                setActionMenu(null);
                if (onOpenDetail) onOpenDetail(acct);
              }}
            >
              <span style={styles.actionMenuIcon}>
                <TypeIcon name="barchart" size={20} color="var(--mint-text)" />
              </span>
              <span>查詢帳戶明細</span>
            </div>
            <div style={styles.centerDialogDivider} />
            <div
              style={styles.centerDialogItem}
              onClick={() => {
                const acct = actionMenu;
                setActionMenu(null);
                startEdit(acct);
              }}
            >
              <span style={styles.actionMenuIcon}>
                <TypeIcon name="pencil" size={20} color="var(--accent-text)" />
              </span>
              <span>編輯帳戶資料</span>
            </div>
            <div style={styles.centerDialogDivider} />
            <div
              style={{ ...styles.centerDialogItem, color: 'var(--pink-text)' }}
              onClick={() => {
                const acct = actionMenu;
                setActionMenu(null);
                remove(acct.id);
              }}
            >
              <span style={styles.actionMenuIcon}>
                <TypeIcon name="trash" size={20} color="var(--pink-text)" />
              </span>
              <span>刪除這個帳戶</span>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        );
      })()}
    </div>
  );
}

// ============ 全域樣式 ============
function Style({ theme = 'dark' }) {
  const dark = `
        --bg: #141619;
        --bg-card: #1d1f24;
        --bg-elevated: #272a31;
        --bg-input: #2a2d34;
        --border: #33363e;
        --border-soft: #2a2d32;
        --text: #eff1f3;
        --text-dim: #9ba0a9;
        --text-faint: #5b6068;
        --mint: #7ee0c0;
        --mint-bg: rgba(126, 224, 192, 0.14);
        --pink: #f5b5c0;
        --pink-bg: rgba(245, 181, 192, 0.14);
        --blue: #a8c8f5;
        --accent: #8f7ff0;
        --accent-dim: rgba(143, 127, 240, 0.14);
        --dash: #e8b947;
        --highlight: #f5d84a;
        --on-highlight: #1a1a1a;
        --on-mint: #1a1a1a;
        --on-pink: #1a1a1a;
        --on-accent: #1a1a1a;
        --mint-text: #7ee0c0;
        --pink-text: #f5b5c0;
        --accent-text: #8f7ff0;
        --bottomnav-bg: rgba(20, 22, 25, 0.92);
        --toast-rich-bg: linear-gradient(180deg, #1e2024 0%, #16181b 100%);
        --toast-rich-shadow: 0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.8), 0 0 0 1px rgba(126,224,192,0.18), 0 0 40px rgba(126,224,192,0.08);
        --toast-backdrop: rgba(0,0,0,0.65);`;
  const light = `
        --bg: #f5f6f8;
        --bg-card: #ffffff;
        --bg-elevated: #ffffff;
        --bg-input: #eef0f3;
        --border: #dfe2e6;
        --border-soft: #e7e9ec;
        --text: #1a1c20;
        --text-dim: #5b6470;
        --text-faint: #9ca3af;
        --mint: #2faa83;
        --mint-bg: rgba(47, 170, 131, 0.14);
        --pink: #d96877;
        --pink-bg: rgba(217, 104, 119, 0.12);
        --blue: #5b8fd9;
        --accent: #6b5fd9;
        --accent-dim: rgba(107, 95, 217, 0.12);
        --dash: #c9962d;
        --highlight: #b25d00;
        --on-highlight: #ffffff;
        --on-mint: #ffffff;
        --on-pink: #ffffff;
        --on-accent: #ffffff;
        --mint-text: #2faa83;
        --pink-text: #d96877;
        --accent-text: #6b5fd9;
        --bottomnav-bg: rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.92);
        --toast-rich-bg: linear-gradient(180deg, #ffffff 0%, #f5f6f8 100%);
        --toast-rich-shadow: 0 20px 60px rgba(0,0,0,0.18), 0 0 0 1px rgba(47,170,131,0.25), 0 0 40px rgba(47,170,131,0.1);
        --toast-backdrop: rgba(0,0,0,0.35);`;
  return (
    <style>{`
      @import url('https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Noto+Sans+TC:wght@400;500;600;700&family=Space+Grotesk:wght@400;500;600;700&display=swap');
      :root {${theme === 'light' ? light : dark}
      }
      * {
        box-sizing: border-box;
        margin: 0;
        padding: 0;
        -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0,0,0,0) !important;
        -webkit-touch-callout: none;
        -webkit-user-select: none;
        user-select: none;
        -webkit-focus-ring-color: transparent !important;
      }
      html, body, #root {
        background: var(--bg);
        color: var(--text);
        font-family: 'Noto Sans TC', -apple-system, sans-serif;
        font-size: 15px;
        line-height: 1.5;
        min-height: 100vh;
      }
      input, textarea { -webkit-user-select: text; user-select: text; }
      button { font-family: inherit; cursor: pointer; border: none; background: none; }
      input, select, textarea { font-family: inherit; }
      /* 只針對表單元素與 button 清 outline，不動 div */
      button, input, select, textarea {
        outline: none !important;
        -webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0,0,0,0) !important;
      }
      button:focus, button:active, button:focus-visible,
      input:focus, select:focus, textarea:focus {
        outline: none !important;
        box-shadow: none !important;
      }
      input[type="date"]::-webkit-calendar-picker-indicator { filter: invert(0.6); }
      /* 隱藏 number input 的上下箭頭 */
      input[type="number"]::-webkit-inner-spin-button,
      input[type="number"]::-webkit-outer-spin-button {
        -webkit-appearance: none;
        margin: 0;
      }
      input[type="number"] { -moz-appearance: textfield; }
      @keyframes wiggle {
        0%, 100% { transform: translate(0, 0) rotate(0deg); }
        25% { transform: translate(-1px, 0) rotate(-0.3deg); }
        75% { transform: translate(1px, 0) rotate(0.3deg); }
      }
      @keyframes toastSlideIn {
        from { opacity: 0; transform: translate(-50%, -50%) scale(0.92); }
        to { opacity: 1; transform: translate(-50%, -50%) scale(1); }
      }
      @keyframes dpSlideRight {
        from { opacity: 0.4; transform: translateX(18px); }
        to { opacity: 1; transform: translateX(0); }
      }
      @keyframes dpSlideLeft {
        from { opacity: 0.4; transform: translateX(-18px); }
        to { opacity: 1; transform: translateX(0); }
      }
      /* 進入動畫:淡入 + 從下方輕推上來(層級切換的細緻感) */
      @keyframes pushEnter {
        from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); }
        to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
      }
      /* 返回動畫:淡入 + 從下方輕推上來(同樣方式,因為都是「進入新層」) */
      @keyframes pushBack {
        from { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(12px); }
        to { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0); }
      }
      /* 從編輯返回時對應 row 淡黃閃爍(結尾回到 bg-card 避免灰階過渡) */
      @keyframes returnFlash {
        0% { background: rgba(245, 220, 100, 0.32); }
        100% { background: var(--bg-card); }
      }
      /* 計算機開啟、金額還沒輸入時,數字慢速脈動,提示「準備輸入」 */
      @keyframes amountPulse {
        0%, 100% { opacity: 0.35; }
        50% { opacity: 1; }
      }
      .dp-nav-btn { border: none; padding: 0; transition: transform 0.1s, background 0.15s; -webkit-tap-highlight-color: transparent; }
      .dp-nav-btn:active { transform: scale(0.85); background: var(--mint-bg) !important; color: var(--mint-text) !important; }
      /* Picker 列項內縮分隔線(iOS Settings 風格)— 從 icon 後對齊,最後一列自動無線 */
      .picker-item { position: relative; }
      .picker-item:not(:last-child)::after {
        content: '';
        position: absolute;
        left: 54px; right: 16px; bottom: 0;
        height: 1px;
        background: var(--border);
        opacity: 0.6;
        pointer-events: none;
      }
      @keyframes toastBackdropFade {
        from { opacity: 0; }
        to { opacity: 1; }
      }
      @keyframes toastBadgePop {
        0% { transform: scale(0.3); opacity: 0; }
        50% { transform: scale(1.15); opacity: 1; }
        100% { transform: scale(1); opacity: 1; }
      }
      @keyframes toastBadgeRing {
        0% { transform: scale(0.6); opacity: 0.6; }
        100% { transform: scale(2.0); opacity: 0; }
      }
      @keyframes toastInfoSlideIn {
        0% { transform: translateY(8px); opacity: 0; }
        100% { transform: translateY(0); opacity: 1; }
      }
      @keyframes toastInfoBarGrow {
        0% { transform: scaleY(0); }
        100% { transform: scaleY(1); }
      }
      @keyframes toastInfoTitleRise {
        0% { transform: translateY(4px); opacity: 0; }
        100% { transform: translateY(0); opacity: 1; }
      }
      @keyframes toastInfoAmountFade {
        0% { opacity: 0; }
        60% { opacity: 0; }
        100% { opacity: 0.85; }
      }
      @keyframes toastDeletedFadeOut {
        0%   { opacity: 1; transform: scale(1); filter: blur(0px); color: var(--pink-text); letter-spacing: -0.8px; }
        20%  { opacity: 1; transform: scale(1); filter: blur(0px); color: var(--pink-text); letter-spacing: -0.8px; }
        100% { opacity: 0; transform: scale(0.85); filter: blur(3px); color: var(--text-faint); letter-spacing: 2px; }
      }
      /* 改名動畫:舊名劃紅線後向上飄走 */
      @keyframes toastRenameOldFly {
        0%   { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0) scale(1); filter: blur(0px); }
        45%  { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0) scale(1); filter: blur(0px); }
        100% { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(-22px) scale(0.85); filter: blur(2.5px); }
      }
      /* 改名動畫:紅線從左到右劃過 */
      @keyframes toastRenameStrike {
        0%   { width: 0%; opacity: 0; }
        10%  { opacity: 1; }
        50%  { width: 100%; opacity: 1; }
        90%  { width: 100%; opacity: 1; }
        100% { width: 100%; opacity: 0; }
      }
      /* 改名動畫:新名從下方淡入飄上 */
      @keyframes toastRenameNewFloat {
        0%   { opacity: 0; transform: translateY(14px) scale(0.92); }
        100% { opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0) scale(1); }
      }
      @keyframes slideUp {
        from { transform: translateY(100%); }
        to { transform: translateY(0); }
      }
      @keyframes fadeIn {
        from { opacity: 0; }
        to { opacity: 1; }
      }
      @keyframes centerAlertPop {
        0% { transform: scale(0.7); opacity: 0; }
        50% { transform: scale(1.05); opacity: 1; }
        100% { transform: scale(1); opacity: 1; }
      }
      /* 計算機按鍵按下視覺反饋 */
      .calc-btn:active {
        transform: scale(0.92);
        background: rgba(255,255,255,0.08) !important;
      }
      .calc-btn-op:active {
        background: rgba(255,255,255,0.12) !important;
      }
      .calc-btn-fn:active {
        background: rgba(255,255,255,0.06) !important;
      }
      .calc-btn-eq:active {
        filter: brightness(0.85);
      }
      .block-edit-anim { animation: wiggle 0.4s ease-in-out infinite; }
      .page-fade {
        background: var(--bg);
        min-height: 100vh;
        padding-bottom: 80px;
      }

      input[type="range"] {
        -webkit-appearance: none;
        appearance: none;
        background: transparent;
        touch-action: pan-x;
      }
      input[type="range"]::-webkit-slider-runnable-track {
        height: 6px;
        background: rgba(255,255,255,0.1);
        border-radius: 3px;
      }
      input[type="range"]::-webkit-slider-thumb {
        -webkit-appearance: none;
        width: 22px;
        height: 22px;
        background: #fff;
        border-radius: 50%;
        margin-top: -8px;
        box-shadow: 0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);
        cursor: pointer;
      }
      input[type="range"]::-moz-range-track {
        height: 6px;
        background: rgba(255,255,255,0.1);
        border-radius: 3px;
      }
      input[type="range"]::-moz-range-thumb {
        width: 22px;
        height: 22px;
        background: #fff;
        border-radius: 50%;
        border: none;
        box-shadow: 0 2px 6px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);
        cursor: pointer;
      }
    `}</style>
  );
}

// ============ 掛載到 DOM(瀏覽器入口)============
// 注意:Babel standalone 不支援 ES Modules export,所以 App 是一般 function
// index.html 用 React UMD + ReactDOM UMD,這裡用 ReactDOM.createRoot 掛載
const _container = document.getElementById('root');
if (_container) {
  const _root = ReactDOM.createRoot(_container);
  _root.render(React.createElement(App));
}
